# Question 101 — Post-Extubation Positional Hypoxia in Morbid Obesity / 拔管后体位性低氧血症（病态肥胖）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>48-year-old man</strong> is admitted to the hospital for management of acute respiratory failure. He has a 4-day history of fever, an increase in <strong>thick, yellow-green sputum production</strong>, and diffuse muscular aches. During the past 2 years, he has produced 2 to 3 tablespoons of yellow sputum daily. He has smoked two packs of cigarettes daily for 30 years. He is 183 cm (6 ft) tall and weighs 134 kg (295 lb); <strong>BMI is 40 kg/m²</strong>. On admission, his temperature is 38.6°C (101.5°F), pulse is 120/min, respirations are 30/min, and blood pressure is 170/100 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on room air shows <strong>an oxygen saturation of 60%</strong>. On admission, an AP portable x-ray shows bilateral diffuse interstitial infiltrates without consolidation. He does not respond to high-flow oxygen therapy. He is intubated and mechanically ventilated. Examination shows hyperresonance to percussion and wheezes bilaterally. Ceftriaxone and levofloxacin are administered, and his symptoms improve. On hospital day 4, he is extubated. His temperature is 37.6°C (99.7°F), pulse is 100/min, respirations are 22/min, and blood pressure is 150/96 mm Hg. <strong>Pulse oximetry while sitting shows an oxygen saturation greater than 95%</strong>. Six hours later, <strong>the patient's oxygen saturation is 86%</strong>. <strong>The patient is lying in bed</strong> and says he feels fine. Physical examination shows no wheezing, crackles, or rhonchi. There is no peripheral edema. A repeat chest x-ray shows improvement. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management to improve this patient's oxygen saturation?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management to improve this patient's oxygen saturation?</strong></p>
<p>A) Increase the oxygen concentration of inspired air<br />
B) Increase the positive end-expiratory pressure<br />
C) Place the patient in Trendelenburg position<br />
D) Place the patient's head on three pillows<br />
E) Return the patient to a sitting position</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>BMI 40 kg/m², weight 134 kg<br />
BMI 40 kg/m²，体重 134 kg</td>
<td>Morbid obesity displaces the diaphragm cephalad when supine, reducing FRC and causing V/Q mismatch<br />
病态肥胖仰卧时使膈肌向头侧移位，降低功能残气量，导致通气/血流比失调</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SpO2 &gt;95% while sitting on day 4<br />
第 4 天坐位时 SpO2 &gt;95%</td>
<td>Adequate oxygenation in upright position rules out persistent infection, PE, and pulmonary edema as ongoing causes<br />
直立位氧合正常，排除持续性感染、肺栓塞和肺水肿作为持续病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SpO2 86% six hours later, patient lying in bed<br />
6 小时后 SpO2 86%，患者处于卧位</td>
<td>Positional change from sitting to supine directly correlates with desaturation — the key diagnostic pivot<br />
体位从坐位变为仰卧与去饱和直接相关——核心诊断转折点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No wheezing, crackles, or rhonchi; no peripheral edema; CXR improved<br />
无喘鸣、湿啰音或痰鸣；无外周水肿；胸片好转</td>
<td>Absence of new pathology eliminates acute COPD exacerbation, pulmonary edema, and infection as causes<br />
无新发病理征象，排除 COPD 急性加重、肺水肿和感染为原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intubated and mechanically ventilated for several days<br />
经过数天气管插管机械通气</td>
<td>Prolonged mechanical ventilation causes respiratory muscle atrophy (ventilator-induced diaphragmatic dysfunction), impairing post-extubation ventilatory effort<br />
长时间机械通气导致呼吸肌萎缩（呼吸机相关膈肌功能障碍），损害拔管后通气努力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patient says he feels fine despite low SpO2<br />
尽管 SpO2 低，患者自觉状态良好</td>
<td>Subjective comfort with objective desaturation indicates a mechanical/postural cause rather than active cardiopulmonary decompensation<br />
主观舒适而客观低氧饱和度，提示机械性/体位性原因而非急性心肺失代偿</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Morbid obesity** combined with **post-extubation respiratory muscle atrophy** creates position-dependent ventilatory insufficiency that worsens dramatically when supine:

**病态肥胖**与**拔管后呼吸肌萎缩**共同造成体位依赖性通气不足，仰卧时显著加重：

- When supine, the weight of abdominal contents displaces the **diaphragm cephalad**, reducing functional residual capacity (FRC) and increasing alveolar collapse at lung bases\
  仰卧时腹腔内容物的重量使**膈肌向头侧移位**，降低功能残气量（FRC），增加肺基底部肺泡塌陷

- **Respiratory muscles atrophy** rapidly during controlled mechanical ventilation; weakened muscles cannot overcome the added chest wall restriction imposed by a 134 kg abdomen in the supine position\
  控制性机械通气期间**呼吸肌迅速萎缩**；虚弱的肌肉无法克服仰卧时 134 kg 腹部带来的额外胸壁阻力

- Sitting upright allows the diaphragm to descend freely under gravity, restores lung volumes, and improves **V/Q matching** without any new pharmacologic or mechanical intervention\
  坐直后膈肌在重力作用下可自由下降，恢复肺容量，改善**通气/血流匹配**，无需任何新的药物或机械干预

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In morbid obesity, FRC in the supine position may be reduced by up to 50% compared to upright sitting — enough to push baseline SpO2 from 95% to the 80s.

**解剖小窍门:** 病态肥胖患者仰卧位的功能残气量较坐位可减少高达 50%——足以使基线 SpO2 从 95% 降至 80% 左右。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Repositioning to Sitting / 正确答案 (E) — 恢复坐位

**Postural repositioning** is the simplest, most direct, and most evidence-backed intervention for position-dependent hypoxia in this post-extubation morbidly obese patient:

**体位调整**是针对此例拔管后病态肥胖患者体位依赖性低氧血症最简单、最直接、最有循证依据的干预：

- The patient demonstrated SpO2 \>95% in sitting position just six hours earlier — returning upright directly reverses the exact mechanism causing desaturation\
  患者仅 6 小时前坐位时 SpO2 \>95%——恢复直立位可直接逆转导致去饱和的确切机制

- Post-extubation pulmonary rehabilitation (sitting, standing, ambulation, coughing, physiotherapy) rebuilds diaphragmatic and accessory respiratory muscle strength over days\
  拔管后肺康复（坐立、站立、行走、咳嗽、呼吸理疗）可在数日内重建膈肌和辅助呼吸肌力量

- No new diagnosis or treatment is required — the cause is mechanical and the fix is positional\
  无需新的诊断或治疗——病因是机械性的，解决方案是体位性的

**Diagnosis:** Position-dependent hypoxia secondary to morbid obesity (reduced FRC when supine) and post-extubation respiratory muscle atrophy; confirmed by SpO2 \>95% sitting vs. 86% supine with no new cardiopulmonary pathology

**诊断:** 体位依赖性低氧血症，继发于病态肥胖（仰卧时 FRC 降低）和拔管后呼吸肌萎缩；坐位 SpO2 \>95% 对比仰卧 86%，无新发心肺疾患证实

**Treatment:** Return to sitting or upright position immediately; initiate pulmonary physiotherapy, incentive spirometry, coughing exercises, and progressive ambulation

**治疗:** 立即恢复坐位或直立位；开始呼吸理疗、激励性肺活量训练、咳嗽训练和渐进性下床活动

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Increase the oxygen concentration of inspired air<br />
A — 增加吸入气氧浓度</td>
<td>Treats the symptom (low SpO2) not the root cause (positional V/Q mismatch from obesity + muscle atrophy); does not rehabilitate respiratory mechanics<br />
治标（低 SpO2）不治本（肥胖+肌萎缩所致体位性通气/血流失调）；无法恢复呼吸力学</td>
<td>Supplemental O2 is temporizing; positional hypoxia requires positional correction, not more oxygen<br />
补充氧气是临时措施；体位性低氧需体位纠正，而非更多氧气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Increase the positive end-expiratory pressure<br />
B — 增加呼气末正压</td>
<td>PEEP/non-invasive positive pressure (BiPAP/CPAP) is indicated for pulmonary edema or COPD exacerbation; patient has no crackles, no edema, no respiratory distress, and CXR is improving<br />
PEEP/无创正压通气（BiPAP/CPAP）用于肺水肿或 COPD 急性加重；患者无湿啰音、无水肿、无呼吸窘迫，胸片改善中</td>
<td>No active bronchospasm or alveolar flooding to justify positive pressure ventilation<br />
无活动性支气管痉挛或肺泡积液，不需要正压通气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Place the patient in Trendelenburg position<br />
C — 将患者置于 Trendelenburg 体位（头低足高位）</td>
<td>Head-down tilt shifts abdominal contents further cephalad, compressing the diaphragm even more — worsens hypoxia in obese patients; used for hypotension or central line placement, not respiratory failure<br />
头低位使腹腔脏器进一步向头侧移位，更大程度压迫膈肌——加重肥胖患者低氧血症；用于低血压或中心静脉置管，不用于呼吸衰竭</td>
<td>This position directly worsens the exact mechanism (diaphragm compression) underlying this patient's hypoxia<br />
该体位直接加重此患者低氧血症的根本机制（膈肌受压）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Place the patient's head on three pillows<br />
D — 将患者头部垫三个枕头</td>
<td>Elevating only the head without elevating the torso does not decompress the diaphragm; appropriate for orthopnea in CHF when the torso is also elevated; no crackles, edema, or CHF history here<br />
仅抬高头部不抬高躯干无法减压膈肌；适用于 CHF 伴端坐呼吸（需同时抬高躯干）；本例无湿啰音、水肿或 CHF 病史</td>
<td>Heart failure requires crackles and edema to be considered; pillow elevation ≠ sitting upright<br />
心力衰竭需有湿啰音和水肿方可考虑；枕头抬高≠坐直</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Return the patient to a sitting position ✓<br />
E — 让患者恢复坐位 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — SpO2 was &gt;95% when sitting just hours ago; returning upright reverses obesity-driven diaphragm displacement and allows respiratory muscle recruitment without any added treatment<br />
正确——数小时前坐位时 SpO2 &gt;95%；恢复直立位逆转肥胖所致膈肌移位，促进呼吸肌募集，无需额外治疗</td>
<td>Directly reverses the positional mechanism; no new diagnosis or medication required<br />
直接逆转体位机制；无需新诊断或药物</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Choice A — when SpO2 drops, "give more oxygen" feels reflexively correct, but this patient has adequate lung function when upright; the problem is mechanical position, not oxygen delivery deficit.*

最有诱惑性的干扰项是 Choice A——SpO2 下降时"给更多氧气"在本能上看似正确，但该患者直立时肺功能正常；问题在于机械性体位，而非氧气输送不足。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Positional Hypoxia (Morbid Obesity) vs. Orthopnea (Congestive Heart Failure) / 体位性低氧（病态肥胖）vs. 端坐呼吸（充血性心力衰竭）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Positional Hypoxia — Morbid Obesity</strong><br />
<strong>体位性低氧——病态肥胖</strong></th>
<th><strong>Orthopnea — Congestive Heart Failure</strong><br />
<strong>端坐呼吸——充血性心力衰竭</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Primary mechanism<br />
主要机制</td>
<td>Supine → abdominal mass displaces diaphragm cephalad → reduced FRC → V/Q mismatch → hypoxia<br />
仰卧→腹部脂肪使膈肌向头侧移位→FRC下降→通气/血流失调→低氧血症</td>
<td>Supine → increased venous return → pulmonary venous congestion → interstitial/alveolar edema → impaired gas exchange<br />
仰卧→静脉回流增加→肺静脉淤血→间质/肺泡水肿→气体交换受损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lung auscultation<br />
肺部听诊</td>
<td>Clear — no crackles, no wheezes<br />
清音——无湿啰音、无喘鸣</td>
<td>Bilateral basilar fine crackles (rales)<br />
双肺底细湿啰音（水泡音）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peripheral edema<br />
外周水肿</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Bilateral pitting edema of lower extremities<br />
双下肢凹陷性水肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chest X-ray<br />
胸片</td>
<td>Normal or improving<br />
正常或改善</td>
<td>Pulmonary vascular congestion, Kerley B lines, pleural effusions, cardiomegaly<br />
肺血管淤血、Kerley B 线、胸腔积液、心脏增大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Best immediate treatment<br />
最佳即时治疗</td>
<td>Sit or stand upright; pulmonary physiotherapy; ambulation<br />
坐立或站立；呼吸理疗；下床活动</td>
<td>Diuresis (IV furosemide); upright positioning; supplemental O2<br />
利尿（静脉呋塞米）；坐直；补充氧气</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Role of pillow elevation<br />
枕头抬高的作用</td>
<td>Ineffective — torso must be fully upright to decompress diaphragm<br />
无效——须完全直立躯干才能减压膈肌</td>
<td>Helpful — reduces venous return and pulmonary congestion<br />
有效——减少静脉回流和肺充血</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A morbidly obese post-extubation patient who desaturates while lying flat but was fine while sitting requires only repositioning upright — the hypoxia is positional, not pathological.**

**病态肥胖拔管后患者平卧时低氧饱和度、坐位时正常，只需恢复直立位——低氧血症是体位性的，不是病理性的。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "PLACE" Post-Extubation Respiratory Recovery / 记忆钩 — "PLACE"拔管后呼吸恢复口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>hysiotherapy — respiratory exercises to rebuild atrophied ventilator muscles / 呼吸理疗——重建萎缩的呼吸机肌群<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ying flat is dangerous — supine halves FRC in morbid obesity / 平躺危险——仰卧使病态肥胖者 FRC 减半<br />
• <strong>A</strong>mbulate — walking recruits respiratory muscles and clears secretions / 下床活动——行走募集呼吸肌并清除分泌物<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ough — active exhalation exercises the diaphragm and prevents atelectasis / 咳嗽——主动呼气锻炼膈肌并预防肺不张<br />
• <strong>E</strong>rect position — upright sitting is the first-line fix for positional hypoxia / 直立位——坐直是体位性低氧的一线处理</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Post-Extubation Management and Obesity-Related Respiratory Physiology / 高频知识表 — 拔管后管理及肥胖相关呼吸生理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Indications for intubation<br />
气管插管指征</td>
<td>Apnea, hypoxia refractory to supplemental O2, hypercapnia with obtundation, failure to protect airway (absent gag/cough reflex, altered mental status)<br />
呼吸停止、吸氧后仍难治性低氧、伴意识障碍的高碳酸血症、气道保护失败（无呕吐/咳嗽反射、意识改变）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ventilator-induced diaphragmatic dysfunction (VIDD)<br />
呼吸机相关膈肌功能障碍（VIDD）</td>
<td>Controlled mechanical ventilation causes diaphragm atrophy within 18–69 hours; contractile force decreases by ~50% after 48–72 hours of full ventilatory support<br />
控制性机械通气在 18–69 小时内引起膈肌萎缩；完全通气支持 48–72 小时后收缩力下降约 50%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Obesity and supine FRC<br />
肥胖与仰卧位功能残气量</td>
<td>Intra-abdominal fat mass elevates diaphragm → FRC decreases → closing capacity exceeds FRC → dependent lung zones collapse → intrapulmonary shunt → refractory hypoxia<br />
腹腔脂肪使膈肌抬高→FRC下降→闭合容量超过FRC→依赖性肺区塌陷→肺内分流→难治性低氧血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to use non-invasive positive pressure (NIPPV) post-extubation<br />
拔管后何时使用无创正压通气</td>
<td>Indicated: cardiogenic pulmonary edema, COPD exacerbation with hypercapnia, hypoxic respiratory failure (selected cases). NOT indicated: positional/mechanical hypoxia without respiratory distress<br />
适应证：心源性肺水肿、COPD 急性加重伴高碳酸血症、低氧性呼吸衰竭（部分病例）。不适应：无呼吸窘迫的体位性/机械性低氧</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-extubation rehabilitation components<br />
拔管后康复内容</td>
<td>Upright positioning, early mobility/ambulation, incentive spirometry, cough training, diaphragmatic breathing exercises, chest physiotherapy<br />
直立体位、早期活动/行走、激励性肺活量训练、咳嗽训练、腹式呼吸训练、胸部理疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Trendelenburg position: uses and harms<br />
Trendelenburg 体位：用途与危害</td>
<td>Used for: hypotension, central venous access. Harmful in: respiratory failure (worsens diaphragm mechanics), elevated ICP, morbid obesity (marked FRC reduction)<br />
用于：低血压、中心静脉置管。有害情况：呼吸衰竭（加重膈肌力学障碍）、颅内压升高、病态肥胖（FRC 显著下降）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Obesity Hypoventilation Syndrome (OHS/Pickwickian syndrome):** BMI \>30 with chronic daytime hypercapnia (PaCO2 \>45 mmHg) not explained by another cause; suppressed central respiratory drive worsens during sleep; treated with CPAP/BiPAP long-term\
  **肥胖低通气综合征（OHS/Pickwick 综合征）:** BMI \>30 伴慢性日间高碳酸血症（PaCO2 \>45 mmHg），排除其他原因；中枢呼吸驱动受抑制，睡眠时加重；长期以 CPAP/BiPAP 治疗

- **Chronic bronchitis baseline:** This patient's 2-year history of daily productive yellow sputum meets the chronic bronchitis definition (productive cough \>3 months/year × \>2 years), explaining his severe initial presentation with acute-on-chronic COPD exacerbation\
  **慢性支气管炎基线:** 患者 2 年每日咳嗽咳痰史符合慢性支气管炎定义（每年咳痰 \>3 个月 × \>2 年），解释急性加重叠加慢性 COPD 的严重初始表现

- **VAP prevention bundle:** Head-of-bed elevation to 30–45° during mechanical ventilation prevents aspiration pneumonia — the same upright positioning principle is therapeutic post-extubation in obese patients\
  **VAP 预防捆绑措施:** 机械通气期间床头抬高 30–45° 预防误吸性肺炎——相同的直立位原则在肥胖拔管后患者中具有治疗作用

- **Key complication of morbid obesity post-op/post-ICU:** Increased risk of atelectasis, pneumonia, and prolonged ventilator dependence; early ambulation and physiotherapy reduce ICU length of stay and readmission rates\
  **病态肥胖术后/ICU 后的主要并发症:** 肺不张、肺炎和长时间呼吸机依赖风险增加；早期活动和理疗可减少 ICU 住院时间和再入院率

# Question 102 — HIV Post-Exposure Prophylaxis / 艾滋病职业暴露后预防

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>24-year-old female medical student</strong> sustains a <strong>deep laceration of her left index finger</strong> while assisting the surgeon during an operation on a patient with <strong>cervical cancer</strong>. The surgical patient has a history of <strong>multiple sexual partners</strong> and <strong>intravenous drug use</strong>; it is <strong>not yet known if she is HIV positive</strong>. Examination of the medical student shows a <strong>2-cm, bleeding laceration</strong>; the bleeding stops with compression. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management pending results of HIV testing on the surgical patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management pending HIV test results?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acyclovir therapy<br />
B) Antiretroviral therapy<br />
C) Corticosteroid therapy<br />
D) Nafcillin therapy<br />
E) No treatment is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<td>24-year-old female medical student<br />
24岁女性医学生</td>
<td>Healthcare worker = occupational HIV exposure scenario; PEP guidelines apply<br />

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Deep laceration of left index finger<br />

</tr>
<tr>

高危行为显著提高来源患者HIV阳性的可能性</td>

</tr>
<tr>

HIV检测结果待出</td>
<td>Key qualifier: management before knowing source status = empiric PEP is appropriate<br />
关键限定语：未知来源状态前的处理 = 经验性PEP是合适的</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Occupational HIV exposure** triggers a predictable cascade: virus inoculated into the wound undergoes **local replication** in tissue dendritic cells before **systemic dissemination** via lymphatics. The window between inoculation and systemic spread (estimated 24–72 hours) is the therapeutic target for **post-exposure prophylaxis (PEP)**:

**职业性HIV暴露**触发可预测的病理级联：接种到伤口的病毒先在组织树突状细胞中进行**局部复制**，再经淋巴管**全身播散**。接种与全身播散之间的窗口期（约24-72小时）正是**暴露后预防（PEP）**的治疗靶点：

- Two nucleoside/nucleotide reverse transcriptase inhibitors (NRTIs, e.g., tenofovir + emtricitabine) block reverse transcription of viral RNA into proviral DNA\
  两种核苷/核苷酸逆转录酶抑制剂（NRTIs，如替诺福韦+恩曲他滨）阻断病毒RNA逆转录为前病毒DNA

- An integrase strand transfer inhibitor (INSTI, e.g., dolutegravir or raltegravir) prevents integration of proviral DNA into the host genome\
  整合酶链转移抑制剂（INSTI，如度鲁特韦或雷特格韦）阻止前病毒DNA整合到宿主基因组

- The combined regimen suppresses viral replication long enough for immune clearance of initially infected cells\
  联合方案抑制病毒复制足够长时间，使免疫系统清除初始感染细胞

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Deeper wounds with larger inoculum carry higher risk; hollow-bore needles (blood-filled syringe) \> solid needles (suture needle) \> surface lacerations.

**解剖小窍门:** 伤口越深、接种量越大风险越高；空心针（充血注射器）\> 实心针（缝合针）\> 表面撕裂伤。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — HIV Post-Exposure Prophylaxis / 正确答案 (B) — 艾滋病暴露后预防

**Post-exposure prophylaxis (PEP)** with a multidrug antiretroviral regimen is the evidence-based standard of care for known or suspected occupational HIV exposure:

**暴露后预防（PEP）**采用多药抗逆转录病毒方案，是已知或疑似职业性HIV暴露的循证标准治疗：

- Initiate PEP as soon as possible — ideally within 1–2 hours, must be within 72 hours; PEP is not recommended beyond 72 hours\
  尽快启动PEP——理想情况下1-2小时内，必须在72小时内；超过72小时不推荐PEP

- Preferred regimen: tenofovir disoproxil fumarate (TDF) + emtricitabine (FTC) + dolutegravir (DTG) once daily for 28 days\
  首选方案：富马酸替诺福韦二吡呋酯（TDF）+ 恩曲他滨（FTC）+ 度鲁特韦（DTG）每日一次，疗程28天

- Promptly initiated PEP reduces risk of HIV seroconversion by approximately 81%\
  及时启动PEP可将HIV血清转化风险降低约81%

**Diagnosis:** Occupational HIV exposure is defined as percutaneous injury (needlestick or laceration) or mucous membrane/non-intact skin contact with blood or other potentially infectious materials from a source of unknown or confirmed HIV-positive status.

**诊断:** 职业性HIV暴露定义为经皮损伤（针刺或撕裂）或黏膜/非完整皮肤接触血液，或来自HIV状态未知或确认阳性来源患者的其他潜在感染性材料。

**Treatment:** Wound care (soap and water wash) → report incident → baseline HIV/HBV/HCV serology → start 28-day triple antiretroviral PEP empirically → source patient HIV testing expedited → serial HIV testing at 6 weeks, 3 months, 6 months post-exposure.

**治疗:** 伤口处理（肥皂水冲洗）→ 上报事故 → 基线HIV/HBV/HCV血清学 → 经验性启动28天三联抗病毒PEP → 加急来源患者HIV检测 → 暴露后6周、3个月、6个月连续HIV检测。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acyclovir therapy<br />
A — 阿昔洛韦治疗</td>
<td>Acyclovir inhibits viral thymidine kinase and DNA polymerase — herpesvirus-specific; has no activity against HIV reverse transcriptase or integrase<br />
阿昔洛韦抑制病毒胸腺嘧啶激酶和DNA聚合酶——疱疹病毒特异性；对HIV逆转录酶或整合酶无活性</td>
<td>Mechanism mismatch: anti-herpes ≠ anti-retroviral; would be correct only for HSV/VZV/CMV exposure<br />
机制不匹配：抗疱疹≠抗逆转录病毒；仅HSV/VZV/CMV暴露时正确</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Antiretroviral therapy ✓<br />
B — 抗逆转录病毒治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — multidrug ARV regimen (2 NRTIs + INSTI) is guideline-recommended PEP for occupational HIV exposure<br />
正确——多药ARV方案（2种NRTIs + INSTI）是职业性HIV暴露的指南推荐PEP</td>
<td>Only drug class with proven efficacy against HIV in the critical early replication window<br />
唯一在关键早期复制窗口期内对HIV有证实疗效的药物类别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Corticosteroid therapy<br />
C — 皮质类固醇治疗</td>
<td>Immunosuppression from corticosteroids impairs host immune response and would facilitate, not prevent, HIV establishment<br />
皮质类固醇的免疫抑制损害宿主免疫应答，促进而非预防HIV建立</td>
<td>Anti-inflammatory ≠ antiviral; corticosteroids actively worsen outcome in this scenario<br />
抗炎≠抗病毒；皮质类固醇在此场景中会主动恶化结局</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Nafcillin therapy<br />
D — 萘夫西林治疗</td>
<td>Nafcillin is an anti-staphylococcal beta-lactam antibiotic with zero antiviral activity; prophylactic antibiotics are not indicated for clean lacerations in healthy healthcare workers<br />
萘夫西林是抗葡萄球菌β-内酰胺类抗生素，无任何抗病毒活性；健康医护人员的清洁撕裂伤不需要预防性抗生素</td>
<td>Antibacterial ≠ antiviral; antibiotic prophylaxis reserved for contaminated wounds or immunocompromised hosts<br />
抗菌≠抗病毒；预防性抗生素用于污染伤口或免疫功能低下的宿主</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No treatment is indicated<br />
E — 无需治疗</td>
<td>While seroconversion risk is low (~0.25–0.35%), PEP is supported by high-quality evidence and should not be withheld for possible exposures — "low risk" ≠ "no action needed"<br />
虽然血清转化风险低（约0.25-0.35%），但PEP有高质量证据支持，可能暴露不应拒绝给予——"低风险"≠"无需处理"</td>
<td>Source has multiple high-risk factors; empiric PEP benefit-risk strongly favors treatment given its favorable safety profile<br />
来源患者有多个高危因素；鉴于PEP良好的安全性，经验性PEP的收益-风险比强烈支持治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E — test-takers may reason that seroconversion risk is low and source HIV status is unknown, but PEP guidelines explicitly cover "possible exposure" scenarios and empiric initiation while awaiting source testing is the standard of care.*

最容易被干扰的是E选项——考生可能认为血清转化风险低且来源HIV状态未知，但PEP指南明确涵盖"可能暴露"场景，在等待来源检测期间经验性启动是标准治疗。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Occupational HIV PEP vs. Antivirals for Other Pathogens / 职业性HIV暴露后预防与其他病原体抗病毒治疗对比

<strong>HIV暴露后预防（抗逆转录病毒）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Herpesvirus Exposure (Acyclovir)</strong><br />

<tr>
<td>Target pathogen<br />
靶病原体</td>

药物机制</td>

NRTIs阻断逆转录酶；INSTIs阻断整合酶</td>

首选方案</td>

TDF/FTC + 度鲁特韦 × 28天</td>

阿昔洛韦或伐昔洛韦（剂量因适应证而异）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Time window<br />
时间窗口</td>
<td>≤72 hours (start ASAP)<br />
≤72小时（尽快启动）</td>
<td>Varies; prophylaxis usually daily for duration of risk<br />
不同；预防通常每日一次直至风险期结束</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cross-activity?<br />
交叉活性？</td>
<td>ARVs have NO activity against herpesviruses<br />
ARVs对疱疹病毒无活性</td>
<td>Acyclovir has NO activity against HIV<br />
阿昔洛韦对HIV无活性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Follow-up testing<br />
随访检测</td>
<td>HIV Ag/Ab at 6w, 3m, 6m post-exposure<br />
暴露后6周、3个月、6个月HIV抗原/抗体检测</td>
<td>Clinical monitoring; serology if needed<br />
临床监测；必要时血清学检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**After occupational HIV exposure (needlestick or laceration from a high-risk source), immediately wash the wound with soap and water and start empiric multidrug antiretroviral PEP (2 NRTIs + integrase inhibitor) within 72 hours for 28 days.**

**职业性HIV暴露（来自高危来源的针刺或撕裂伤）后，立即用肥皂水冲洗伤口，并在72小时内经验性启动多药抗逆转录病毒PEP（2种NRTIs + 整合酶抑制剂），疗程28天。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — WASH PEP / 记忆钩 — WASH PEP 四步口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>W</strong>ash — Soap and water immediately; no squeezing or caustic agents / 立即用肥皂水冲洗；不要挤压伤口或用腐蚀性物质<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ssess — Evaluate source risk (viral load, high-risk behaviors) and exposure depth / 评估来源风险（病毒载量、高危行为）和暴露深度<br />
• <strong>S</strong>tart — Triple antiretroviral PEP within 72 hours (ideally ≤2 h); 28-day course / 72小时内（理想≤2小时）启动三联抗病毒PEP；疗程28天<br />
• <strong>H</strong>IV test — Baseline + serial testing at 6 weeks, 3 months, 6 months / 基线 + 6周、3个月、6个月连续HIV检测</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — HIV Post-Exposure Prophylaxis / 高频知识表 — 艾滋病暴露后预防

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Seroconversion risk without PEP<br />
未用PEP的血清转化风险</td>
<td>Percutaneous: ~0.25–0.35%; mucous membrane: ~0.09%; intact skin: negligible<br />
经皮：约0.25-0.35%；黏膜：约0.09%；完整皮肤：可忽略</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors for higher seroconversion<br />
血清转化风险升高因素</td>
<td>Hollow-bore needle, deep wound, visible blood on device, source with high viral load or terminal AIDS<br />
空心针、深部伤口、器械上可见血液、来源患者高病毒载量或终末期AIDS</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PEP timing rule<br />
PEP时机规则</td>
<td>Start within 72 hours — ideally within 1–2 hours; every hour of delay reduces efficacy; beyond 72 h, PEP is not recommended<br />
72小时内启动——理想1-2小时内；每延误一小时疗效降低；72小时后不推荐PEP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred PEP regimen<br />
首选PEP方案</td>
<td>TDF 300mg + FTC 200mg + dolutegravir 50mg once daily × 28 days; efficacy ~81% reduction in transmission<br />
TDF 300mg + FTC 200mg + 度鲁特韦50mg 每日一次 × 28天；疗效约降低81%传播风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Immediate wound management steps<br />
即时伤口处理步骤</td>
<td>Wash thoroughly with soap and water; do NOT squeeze or "milk" the wound; do NOT use bleach or caustic agents<br />
肥皂水彻底冲洗；不要挤压或"挤奶式"处理伤口；不要使用漂白剂或腐蚀性物质</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Baseline labs at time of exposure<br />
暴露时基线检测</td>
<td>HIV Ag/Ab combination test, HBsAg/anti-HBs, HCV Ab, pregnancy test (females), CBC, comprehensive metabolic panel<br />
HIV抗原/抗体联合检测、HBsAg/抗HBs、HCV抗体、妊娠试验（女性）、血常规、全套代谢</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reporting requirement<br />
报告要求</td>
<td>All occupational exposures must be reported per OSHA; ensures follow-up and workers' compensation eligibility if seroconversion occurs<br />
根据OSHA规定所有职业性暴露必须上报；确保随访及发生血清转化时的工伤补偿资格</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Co-exposure to HBV/HCV:** If source is also HBsAg-positive, check healthcare worker's HBV vaccination status — give HBIG + vaccine series if unvaccinated or non-immune; no post-exposure prophylaxis exists for HCV, only monitoring\
  **HBV/HCV合并暴露:** 若来源患者同时HBsAg阳性，检查医护人员HBV疫苗接种状态——未接种或无免疫者给予HBIG + 疫苗系列；HCV无暴露后预防药物，仅监测

- **PrEP vs. PEP distinction:** Pre-exposure prophylaxis (PrEP) = daily TDF/FTC for HIV-negative high-risk individuals BEFORE any exposure; post-exposure prophylaxis (PEP) = triple ARV regimen started AFTER a known or suspected exposure — mechanism is the same but context and timing differ\
  **PrEP与PEP区别:** 暴露前预防（PrEP）= HIV阴性高危人群在任何暴露前每日服用TDF/FTC；暴露后预防（PEP）= 已知或疑似暴露后启动三联ARV方案——机制相同但情境和时机不同

- **Acyclovir scope (why Choice A fails):** Acyclovir covers all herpesviruses (HSV-1/2, VZV, EBV, CMV at high doses) via thymidine kinase-dependent chain termination — a mechanism that exists only in herpesviruses, not in HIV retroviruses\
  **阿昔洛韦适用范围（A选项为何错误）:** 阿昔洛韦通过胸腺嘧啶激酶依赖的链终止覆盖所有疱疹病毒（HSV-1/2、VZV、EBV、高剂量CMV）——该机制仅存在于疱疹病毒，不存在于HIV逆转录病毒

- **Variant scenario — source tests HIV-negative:** If source patient's HIV test returns negative AND exposure was low-risk, PEP may be discontinued early; if source is known to be recently infected (acute HIV, high viremia), maintain full 28-day course regardless\
  **题目变式——来源检测HIV阴性:** 若来源患者HIV检测回报阴性且暴露为低风险，可提前停止PEP；若来源已知为近期感染（急性HIV、高病毒血症），无论如何维持完整28天疗程

# Question 103 — Velopharyngeal Insufficiency After Cleft Palate Repair / 腭裂修复术后腭咽闭合不全

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>10-month-old female infant</strong> is brought to the office by her parents for a follow-up examination <strong>3 weeks after undergoing staged repair of a left complete unilateral cleft lip and palate</strong>. The procedure and recovery were uncomplicated, and the infant was discharged home 2 days later. The parents report she is <strong>feeding well with a traditional bottle nipple</strong> and now also consumes some soft baby foods. She has <strong>not had fever, pain, or nasal regurgitation</strong>. She receives no medications. Today, she is at the 25th percentile for length and weight. Vital signs are normal. Physical examination discloses a <strong>well-healing surgical incision on the left upper vermilion and philtrum</strong>; the palate also appears to be healing well without wound dehiscence or palatal holes. This patient's parents should be informed that she is at increased risk for developing which of the following?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which complication is she at increased risk for?</strong></p>
<p>A) Chronic colonization with group A streptococcus<br />
B) Dyslexia<br />
C) Peritonsillar abscess<br />
D) Severe myopia<br />
E) Velopharyngeal insufficiency</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>10-month-old female, staged cleft lip and palate repair<br />
10月龄女婴，分期唇腭裂修复术</td>
<td>Identifies the index procedure and patient age — cleft palate repair is a known risk factor for VPI regardless of surgical success<br />
明确手术史——腭裂修复术后无论手术是否成功均存在VPI风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Left complete unilateral cleft lip and palate<br />
左侧完全性单侧唇腭裂</td>
<td>"Complete" means it extends through the nares; palatal involvement is the key driver of VPI risk<br />
"完全性"意味着裂隙贯穿鼻孔；腭部受累是VPI风险的核心驱动因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Feeding well, no nasal regurgitation currently<br />
目前喂养良好，无鼻腔反流</td>
<td>No current VPI symptoms — question asks about future risk, not present diagnosis<br />
目前无VPI症状——题目问的是未来风险，而非当前诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Well-healing incision without wound dehiscence or palatal holes<br />
切口愈合良好，无裂开或腭孔</td>
<td>Reassuring anatomic healing does NOT eliminate long-term VPI risk from shortened or scarred palate<br />
解剖愈合良好并不能消除因腭部短缩或瘢痕形成导致的远期VPI风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3 weeks post-repair, no fever or pain<br />
术后3周，无发热或疼痛</td>
<td>Early postoperative period is uneventful — the question pivots to long-term sequelae<br />
术后早期平稳——题目转向远期后遗症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Parents should be informed of increased risk<br />
家长应被告知风险</td>
<td>Counseling question — requires knowing the most common long-term complication of cleft palate repair<br />
咨询类问题——需要知道腭裂修复最常见的远期并发症</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Velopharyngeal insufficiency** results from the inability to properly close the **velopharyngeal port** — the anatomic sphincter separating the nasopharynx from the oropharynx during speech production:

**腭咽闭合不全**源于无法在言语产出时正确关闭**腭咽括约肌**——该结构将鼻咽腔与口咽腔分隔开：

- Cleft palate → palate is structurally shortened or scarred after repair → inadequate posterior reach to contact the posterior pharyngeal wall\
  腭裂→腭部结构性短缩或修复后瘢痕形成→腭部无法充分向后接触咽后壁

- During speech, air leaks into nasopharynx → hypernasal resonance, nasal emission, reduced speech intelligibility\
  言语时气流漏入鼻咽腔→鼻音过重、鼻腔漏气、言语清晰度下降

- VPI occurs even after successful anatomic repair because muscle function and palatal length may remain suboptimal\
  即使解剖修复成功，VPI仍可发生，因为肌肉功能和腭部长度仍可能不理想

- Incidence after cleft palate repair ranges from 20–30%, making it the most common long-term sequela\
  腭裂修复术后VPI发生率约20–30%，是最常见的远期后遗症

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The velum (soft palate) must elevate and retract posteriorly to contact Passavant's ridge on the posterior pharyngeal wall — if it falls short, VPI results.

**解剖小窍门:** 软腭必须上抬并向后回缩，接触咽后壁的Passavant嵴——若接触不足，即发生VPI。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Velopharyngeal Insufficiency / 正确答案 (E) — 腭咽闭合不全

**Velopharyngeal insufficiency (VPI)** is the most common long-term sequela of cleft palate, occurring even after technically successful surgical repair:

**腭咽闭合不全（VPI）**是腭裂最常见的远期后遗症，即使手术在技术层面成功也可能发生：

- VPI = functional failure of the velopharyngeal sphincter to close completely during speech\
  VPI = 言语时腭咽括约肌功能性闭合不完全

- Caused by shortened palate, palatal scarring, or residual muscular dysfunction post-repair\
  由腭部短缩、腭部瘢痕或修复后肌肉功能残余障碍引起

- Clinical presentation: hypernasal speech, nasal air emission, compensatory articulation errors (glottal stops)\
  临床表现：鼻音过重、鼻腔漏气、代偿性构音错误（声门爆破音）

- Speech problems emerge as the child begins to produce consonants — typically not apparent at 10 months\
  随着儿童开始发辅音，言语问题逐渐显现——通常在10月龄时尚不明显

**Diagnosis:** Nasopharyngoscopy and videofluoroscopy are gold-standard assessments; speech-language pathology evaluation is essential.

**诊断:** 鼻咽镜检查和视频透视检查是诊断金标准；言语语言病理学评估至关重要。

**Treatment:** Speech therapy for mild VPI; surgical intervention (pharyngeal flap, sphincter pharyngoplasty, or palatal re-repair) for moderate-to-severe VPI.

**治疗:** 轻度VPI行言语治疗；中重度VPI行手术干预（咽瓣手术、括约肌咽成形术或腭部再修复）。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Chronic colonization with group A streptococcus<br />
A — 慢性A族链球菌定植</td>
<td>GAS colonization is NOT increased in cleft lip/palate; evidence suggests S. aureus (not GAS) may be more prevalent<br />
唇腭裂患儿A族链球菌定植率并不升高；有证据表明金黄色葡萄球菌（而非A族链球菌）可能更常见</td>
<td>Organism specificity — GAS is a distractor; VPI is the well-established sequela<br />
病原体特异性——A族链球菌是干扰项；VPI才是明确的后遗症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Dyslexia<br />
B — 阅读障碍</td>
<td>Controversial association; some language delays occur with syndromic clefts, but dyslexia is not the primary established risk<br />
关联存在争议；综合征性唇腭裂可能有语言发育迟缓，但阅读障碍并非主要确定风险</td>
<td>Dyslexia is a written-language disorder; VPI is a well-documented structural speech sequela<br />
阅读障碍是书面语言障碍；VPI是有充分记录的结构性言语后遗症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Peritonsillar abscess<br />
C — 扁桃体周脓肿</td>
<td>Peritonsillar abscess follows tonsillitis; not a consequence of cleft repair<br />
扁桃体周脓肿继发于扁桃体炎，与腭裂修复无关</td>
<td>Anatomically unrelated complication — different tissue, different mechanism<br />
解剖上无关的并发症——不同组织、不同机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Severe myopia<br />
D — 严重近视</td>
<td>Myopia + cleft palate = Stickler syndrome, but this is rare and syndromic; question describes isolated cleft<br />
近视+腭裂=Stickler综合征，但这是罕见的综合征性病例；题目描述的是孤立性腭裂</td>
<td>Syndromic associations are rare exceptions; VPI is the universal sequela of cleft palate regardless of etiology<br />
综合征性关联是罕见例外；VPI是腭裂无论病因如何均存在的普遍后遗症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Velopharyngeal insufficiency ✓<br />
E — 腭咽闭合不全 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — VPI affects 20–30% of patients after cleft palate repair and is the most commonly counseled long-term risk<br />
正确——VPI影响约20–30%的腭裂修复术后患者，是最常需要告知的远期风险</td>
<td>Directly results from shortened/scarred palate; clinically manifests as hypernasality during speech development<br />
直接源于腭部短缩/瘢痕；在言语发育期临床表现为鼻音过重</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice B (dyslexia), as language problems in cleft patients are real but less established and less universal than VPI — the question specifically targets the most common, well-documented sequela.*

选项B（阅读障碍）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，唇腭裂患儿确实存在语言问题，但其关联尚存争议且不如VPI普遍——题目针对的是最常见、证据最充分的后遗症。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**After cleft palate repair, parents must be counseled that velopharyngeal insufficiency (VPI) — hypernasality from incomplete closure of the velopharyngeal port — is the most common long-term sequela, occurring in up to 30% of repaired patients.**

**腭裂修复术后，必须告知家长腭咽闭合不全（VPI）——因腭咽括约肌不能完全闭合所致的鼻音过重——是最常见的远期后遗症，发生率高达30%。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — VPI After Cleft: "SNAP" / 记忆钩 — 腭裂后VPI："SNAP":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>hortened palate — the structural root cause of VPI / 腭部短缩——VPI的结构性根本原因<br />
• <strong>N</strong>asopharynx leakage — air escapes upward during speech / 鼻咽腔漏气——言语时气流向上逸出<br />
• <strong>A</strong>rticulation errors (compensatory glottal stops) — child adapts to VPI / 构音错误（代偿性声门爆破音）——儿童对VPI的代偿<br />
• <strong>P</strong>haryngoplasty — surgical fix for moderate-to-severe VPI / 咽成形术——中重度VPI的手术解决方案</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cleft Lip and Palate Embryology, Repair, and Sequelae / 高频知识表 — 唇腭裂胚胎学、修复及后遗症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Embryologic origin of cleft lip<br />
唇裂的胚胎学起源</td>
<td>Failure of fusion of maxillary prominence with medial nasal prominence (week 5–7); upper lip and primary palate<br />
第5–7周上颌突与内侧鼻突融合失败；累及上唇和原发腭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Embryologic origin of cleft palate<br />
腭裂的胚胎学起源</td>
<td>Failure of fusion of palatine shelves (week 7–10); secondary palate (hard + soft palate)<br />
第7–10周腭板融合失败；继发腭（硬腭+软腭）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associated syndromes<br />
相关综合征</td>
<td>Patau syndrome (trisomy 13); Treacher Collins (midfacial hypoplasia); Stickler syndrome (myopia + cleft); Pierre Robin sequence (micrognathia + glossoptosis)<br />
Patau综合征（13三体）；Treacher Collins（中面部发育不全）；Stickler综合征（近视+腭裂）；Pierre Robin序列（小颌畸形+舌后坠）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Timing of repair<br />
手术修复时机</td>
<td>Cleft lip: 3–6 months ("rule of 10s" — 10 weeks, 10 lbs, Hgb 10); cleft palate: 9–12 months (before speech development)<br />
唇裂：3–6月龄（"10规则"——10周、10磅、血红蛋白10）；腭裂：9–12月龄（言语发育前）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Velopharyngeal insufficiency (VPI)<br />
腭咽闭合不全（VPI）</td>
<td>Most common sequela (20–30%); hypernasality, nasal emission, compensatory articulation; diagnosed by nasopharyngoscopy + videofluoroscopy<br />
最常见后遗症（20–30%）；鼻音过重、鼻腔漏气、代偿性构音；鼻咽镜+视频透视诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Other long-term complications<br />
其他远期并发症</td>
<td>Otitis media with effusion (Eustachian tube dysfunction); dental malocclusion; maxillary growth restriction; hearing loss; speech and language delays<br />
渗出性中耳炎（咽鼓管功能障碍）；牙列错殆；上颌骨生长受限；听力损失；言语语言发育迟缓</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eustachian tube dysfunction in cleft palate<br />
腭裂中的咽鼓管功能障碍</td>
<td>Tensor veli palatini muscle (opens Eustachian tube) is disrupted → recurrent otitis media → hearing loss → often requires myringotomy tubes<br />
腭帆张肌（开放咽鼓管）受损→复发性中耳炎→听力损失→常需鼓膜置管</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of hypernasality:** VPI is the most common cause; others include submucous cleft palate (bifid uvula + notched hard palate + diastasis of levator), neurologic disorders (palatal paresis), adenoidectomy in at-risk patients\
  **鼻音过重的鉴别:** VPI是最常见原因；其他包括黏膜下腭裂（悬雍垂裂+硬腭切迹+腭帆提肌分离）、神经系统疾病（腭肌麻痹）、高危患者行腺样体切除术后

- **Surgical variants for VPI:** Pharyngeal flap (static midline flap from posterior pharyngeal wall) vs. sphincter pharyngoplasty (dynamic lateral port narrowing) — choice depends on VPI pattern on nasopharyngoscopy\
  **VPI手术变式:** 咽瓣手术（来自咽后壁的静态正中瓣）vs. 括约肌咽成形术（动态侧方缩窄）——选择取决于鼻咽镜检查的VPI形态

- **Key complication of pharyngeal flap:** Obstructive sleep apnea (OSA) — flap narrows the velopharyngeal port and may cause airway obstruction during sleep; requires postoperative sleep monitoring\
  **咽瓣手术的关键并发症:** 阻塞性睡眠呼吸暂停（OSA）——咽瓣缩窄腭咽腔，睡眠时可能导致气道阻塞；需术后睡眠监测

- **Multidisciplinary care team:** Plastic surgery, speech-language pathology, orthodontics, ENT (for otitis media/hearing), genetics (syndromic evaluation), and psychology — cleft teams coordinate care throughout childhood\
  **多学科团队:** 整形外科、言语语言病理学、正畸科、耳鼻喉科（中耳炎/听力）、遗传学（综合征评估）、心理科——唇腭裂团队贯穿整个儿童期协调诊疗

# Question 104 — Schizophrenia / 精神分裂症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>22-year-old man</strong> is brought to the physician by his parents because he has become <strong>newly preoccupied with religion during the past year</strong>. He lives with his parents and attends a community college. <strong>Two months ago, he stopped attending his classes</strong>. His parents report that he spends most of the day in his room alone reading religious scripture. He shows no interest in activities he once enjoyed, no longer spends time with his friends, <strong>masturbates frequently and obviously</strong>, and spends most of the night <strong>walking around his room laughing and talking to himself</strong>. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, he has a depressed mood and animated affect. His speech is <strong>pressured</strong>, and responses to questions are <strong>tangential</strong>. He reports <strong>hearing a voice during the past 2 months</strong> that he believes is "the voice of God." He says that he feels confused and has <strong>thoughts about ending his life</strong> because he cannot understand if God truly wants him to become the next Messiah.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Delusional disorder<br />
B) Obsessive-compulsive disorder<br />
C) Schizoid personality disorder<br />
D) Schizophrenia<br />
E) Schizotypal personality disorder</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>22-year-old male, symptoms over 1 year<br />
22岁男性，症状持续超过1年</td>
<td>Peak onset in males is late teens to mid-20s; total duration &gt;6 months satisfies DSM-5 schizophrenia criterion<br />
男性发病高峰为青少年晚期至25岁；总病程&gt;6个月符合DSM-5精神分裂症标准</td>
</tr>

停止上大学课程</td>

工作/教育领域的显著功能损害是DSM-5必要标准，人格障碍中通常不具备</td>

言语紊乱——符合DSM-5活跃期第3条症状标准</td>
</tr>

<td>Hearing a voice ("voice of God") for 2 months<br />
听到声音（"上帝之声"）持续2个月</td>

听幻觉——符合DSM-5活跃期第2条症状标准；可与妄想性障碍相鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Believes he may be the next Messiah<br />
相信自己可能是下一位弥赛亚</td>
<td>Grandiose religious delusion — counts as the 1st DSM-5 active-phase symptom criterion<br />
夸大性宗教妄想——符合DSM-5活跃期第1条症状标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No interest in enjoyed activities, social withdrawal, suicidal ideation<br />
对原先爱好失去兴趣、社交退缩、自杀意念</td>
<td>Negative symptoms (anhedonia, avolition) plus suicidality — high-risk features of schizophrenia, especially in young males with early illness<br />
阴性症状（快感缺失、意志力减退）加自杀意念——精神分裂症高风险特征，尤其见于早期病程年轻男性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Schizophrenia** arises from **dopamine dysregulation** in two distinct pathways, combined with **glutamate (NMDA receptor) dysfunction** and structural brain changes that explain both positive and negative symptoms:

**精神分裂症**源于两条不同通路中的**多巴胺失调**，加之**谷氨酸（NMDA受体）功能障碍**和脑结构改变，共同解释了阳性和阴性症状：

- **Mesolimbic pathway** hyperdopaminergia → positive symptoms (hallucinations, delusions, disorganized behavior)\
  **中脑边缘通路**多巴胺过多 → 阳性症状（幻觉、妄想、行为紊乱）

- **Mesocortical pathway** hypodopaminergia → negative symptoms (flat affect, avolition, alogia, anhedonia)\
  **中脑皮质通路**多巴胺不足 → 阴性症状（情感平淡、意志力减退、言语贫乏、快感缺失）

- Structural: **enlarged lateral ventricles** and decreased prefrontal cortical volume on MRI\
  结构改变：MRI显示**侧脑室扩大**及前额叶皮质体积减少

- **NMDA receptor hypofunction** on inhibitory GABAergic interneurons → disinhibition of dopamine release (explains why PCP/ketamine mimic schizophrenia)\
  抑制性GABAergic中间神经元上的**NMDA受体功能低下** → 多巴胺释放去抑制（解释了PCP/氯胺酮为何可模拟精神分裂症）

- Heritability ~80%; concordance in identical twins ~50% — environment (obstetric complications, cannabis, urban upbringing) also contributes\
  遗传度约80%；同卵双生子一致率约50%——环境因素（产科并发症、大麻、城市成长）亦有贡献

**Pharmacologic corollary:** All antipsychotics share D2 receptor blockade in the mesolimbic pathway — this reduces positive symptoms. Negative symptoms respond poorly to D2 blockers.

**药理学推论:** 所有抗精神病药共同机制为阻断中脑边缘通路D2受体——可改善阳性症状。阴性症状对D2阻断剂反应较差。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Schizophrenia / 正确答案 (D) — 精神分裂症

**Schizophrenia** is a chronic psychotic disorder defined by ≥2 active-phase symptoms for ≥6 months total (including prodrome/residual), with significant functional impairment not attributable to substances or another medical condition:

**精神分裂症**是一种慢性精神病性障碍，定义为≥2项活跃期症状持续总计≥6个月（含前驱期/残留期），伴显著功能损害，且不能归因于物质或其他器质性疾病：

- The 5 active-phase symptoms are: Delusions, Hallucinations, Disorganized speech, Disorganized behavior, Negative symptoms — **at least 1 must be from the first three (D, H, or S)**\
  5项活跃期症状为：妄想、幻觉、言语紊乱、行为紊乱、阴性症状——**至少1项必须来自前三项（妄想、幻觉或言语紊乱）**

- This patient has ALL 5: Messiah delusion, auditory hallucination ("voice of God"), pressured/tangential speech, grossly disorganized behavior (masturbating publicly, talking to himself), and negative symptoms (anhedonia, social withdrawal)\
  本患者具备全部5项：弥赛亚妄想、听幻觉（"上帝之声"）、急促/切题性差言语、严重紊乱行为（公开手淫、自言自语）、阴性症状（快感缺失、社交退缩）

- Duration: religious preoccupation for 1 full year (prodrome) + active psychosis ≥2 months — well exceeds the 6-month minimum\
  病程：宗教先占观念持续整整1年（前驱期）+ 活跃期精神病≥2个月——远超6个月最低标准

**Diagnosis:** Rule out substance-induced psychosis (stimulants, cannabis, PCP), autoimmune encephalitis (anti-NMDAR antibodies), temporal lobe epilepsy, and mood disorder with psychotic features before diagnosing schizophrenia

**诊断:** 诊断精神分裂症前须排除物质诱导性精神病（兴奋剂、大麻、PCP）、自身免疫性脑炎（抗NMDAR抗体）、颞叶癫痫及伴精神病特征的心境障碍

**Treatment:** First-line atypical antipsychotics (risperidone, olanzapine, quetiapine, aripiprazole) target positive symptoms; clozapine reserved for treatment-resistant cases (≥2 failed trials); psychosocial rehabilitation and family therapy are essential adjuncts

**治疗:** 一线非典型抗精神病药（利培酮、奥氮平、喹硫平、阿立哌唑）针对阳性症状；氯氮平保留用于难治性病例（≥2种药物无效）；心理社会康复和家庭治疗是不可缺少的辅助手段

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Delusional disorder<br />
A — 妄想性障碍</td>
<td>Features only non-bizarre delusions ≥1 month with NO hallucinations and NO disorganized speech or behavior — this patient has all three additional features<br />
仅有非奇异性妄想≥1个月，无幻觉，无言语或行为紊乱——本患者三种附加特征均存在</td>
<td>Hallucinations and disorganized symptoms are explicitly exclusionary for delusional disorder<br />
幻觉和紊乱症状明确排除妄想性障碍诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Obsessive-compulsive disorder<br />
B — 强迫症</td>
<td>OCD involves ego-dystonic obsessions + neutralizing compulsions; no true hallucinations, delusions, or formal thought disorder<br />
强迫症涉及自我不和谐的强迫思维+中和性强迫行为；无真性幻觉、妄想或正式思维障碍</td>
<td>This patient's religious preoccupation has psychotic quality (fixed Messiah delusion + auditory hallucination), distinct from OCD's intrusive-but-recognized-as-unreal pattern<br />
本患者宗教先占观念具有精神病性质（固定的弥赛亚妄想+听幻觉），与强迫症"侵入性但自知虚假"的模式截然不同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Schizoid personality disorder<br />
C — 分裂样人格障碍</td>
<td>Cluster A PD with lifelong pervasive social detachment and restricted affect; NO delusions, NO hallucinations, NO disorganized speech — psychosis is absent by definition<br />
A组人格障碍，终身弥漫性社交疏离和情感受限；无妄想、无幻觉、无言语紊乱——定义上不存在精神病症状</td>
<td>Personality disorders are ego-syntonic lifelong patterns; acute onset of frank psychosis with hallucinations rules out any PD<br />
人格障碍是自我协调的终身模式；急性发作的明显精神病（含幻觉）可排除任何人格障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Schizophrenia ✓<br />
D — 精神分裂症 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — meets all DSM-5 criteria: ≥2 active-phase symptoms (delusions + hallucinations + disorganized speech + disorganized behavior + negative symptoms), total duration &gt;6 months, and significant functional decline (dropped out of college)<br />
正确——符合所有DSM-5标准：≥2项活跃期症状（妄想+幻觉+言语紊乱+行为紊乱+阴性症状），总病程&gt;6个月，显著功能下降（退学）</td>
<td>Only diagnosis that accounts for the full triad: positive symptoms + negative symptoms + functional impairment over the required duration<br />
唯一能解释完整三联征的诊断：阳性症状+阴性症状+符合病程要求的功能损害</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Schizotypal personality disorder<br />
E — 分裂型人格障碍</td>
<td>Cluster A PD with odd/eccentric behavior, magical thinking, ideas of reference, and social anxiety; may have brief transient psychotic episodes but NOT sustained delusions or prominent persistent hallucinations<br />
A组人格障碍，伴奇异/怪癖行为、魔法思维、牵连观念和社交焦虑；可有短暂精神病发作，但无持续妄想或显著持续幻觉</td>
<td>Sustained auditory hallucination + systematized grandiose delusion persisting over months constitutes frank psychosis — not compatible with schizotypal PD<br />
持续数月的听幻觉+系统化夸大妄想构成明显精神病发作——与分裂型人格障碍不相符</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is delusional disorder (A) because of the prominent religious delusion, but the co-occurring auditory hallucination and disorganized speech/behavior are explicitly incompatible with that diagnosis — those features mandate schizophrenia.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是妄想性障碍（A），因其存在显著宗教妄想，但同时出现的听幻觉和言语/行为紊乱与该诊断明确不符——这些特征必须诊断为精神分裂症。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Schizophrenia requires ≥2 of 5 active-phase symptoms for ≥6 months with functional decline — this patient's religious delusion, auditory hallucination, disorganized speech, disorganized behavior, and negative symptoms all simultaneously present, making the diagnosis unambiguous.**

**精神分裂症需要5项活跃期症状中≥2项持续≥6个月并伴功能下降——本患者宗教妄想、听幻觉、言语紊乱、行为紊乱和阴性症状同时具备，诊断明确无疑。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "HANDS" for Schizophrenia's 5 DSM-5 Active-Phase Criteria / 记忆钩 — "HANDS" 记忆精神分裂症5大DSM-5活跃期标准:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>allucinations — auditory most common; "hearing voices" is the classic presentation / 幻觉——以听幻觉最常见；"听到声音"是经典表现<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bnormal (disorganized) behavior — bizarre, purposeless, grossly inappropriate actions / 异常（紊乱）行为——怪异、无目的、严重不得体的行为<br />
• <strong>N</strong>egative symptoms — flat affect, Alogia, aVolition, Anhedonia (the "4 A's") / 阴性症状——情感平淡、言语贫乏、意志减退、快感缺失（"4个A"）<br />
• <strong>D</strong>elusions — fixed false beliefs; grandiose, paranoid, referential, or bizarre types / 妄想——固定的错误信念；夸大性、偏执性、牵连性或奇异性<br />
• <strong>S</strong>peech (disorganized) — tangential answers, loose associations, word salad in severe cases / 言语（紊乱）——切题性差、联想松弛、严重时出现词语杂拌</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Schizophrenia Spectrum Disorders / 高频知识表 — 精神分裂症谱系障碍

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Schizophrenia spectrum duration criteria<br />
精神分裂症谱系病程标准</td>
<td>Brief psychotic disorder: &lt;1 month (often with stressor); Schizophreniform: 1–6 months; Schizophrenia: ≥6 months — all three require the same active-phase symptom criteria<br />
短暂精神病性障碍：&lt;1个月（常有应激源）；精神分裂症样障碍：1–6个月；精神分裂症：≥6个月——三者均需具备相同的活跃期症状标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 "at least 1 of 3" rule<br />
DSM-5"至少1项来自前3项"规则</td>
<td>Of the ≥2 required symptoms, at least 1 MUST be delusions, hallucinations, OR disorganized speech — you cannot diagnose schizophrenia on negative symptoms + disorganized behavior alone<br />
在≥2项必要症状中，至少1项必须为妄想、幻觉或言语紊乱——仅凭阴性症状+行为紊乱不能诊断精神分裂症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Typical vs. atypical antipsychotics<br />
典型与非典型抗精神病药</td>
<td>Typical (1st-gen): haloperidol, chlorpromazine, fluphenazine — D2 blockade only; high EPS and tardive dyskinesia risk; Atypical (2nd-gen): risperidone, olanzapine, quetiapine, aripiprazole — D2 + 5-HT2A blockade; lower EPS but metabolic syndrome risk (weight gain, dyslipidemia, glucose intolerance)<br />
典型（第一代）：氟哌啶醇、氯丙嗪、氟奋乃静——仅D2阻断；EPS和迟发性运动障碍风险高；非典型（第二代）：利培酮、奥氮平、喹硫平、阿立哌唑——D2+5-HT2A阻断；EPS较少但代谢综合征风险（体重增加、血脂异常、糖耐量受损）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clozapine: indications and monitoring<br />
氯氮平：适应证和监测</td>
<td>Reserved for treatment-resistant schizophrenia (failed ≥2 adequate antipsychotic trials); also reduces suicidality; risk: agranulocytosis (1–2%) requires mandatory ANC monitoring — weekly ×6 months, then every 2 weeks<br />
保留用于难治性精神分裂症（≥2种抗精神病药充分治疗无效）；亦可降低自杀风险；风险：粒细胞缺乏症（1–2%），需强制性ANC监测——前6个月每周，之后每两周一次</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Four dopamine pathways and side effects<br />
四条多巴胺通路及副作用</td>
<td>Mesolimbic ↑DA → positive symptoms; Mesocortical ↓DA → negative/cognitive symptoms; Nigrostriatal ↓DA (from antipsychotic) → EPS (akathisia, parkinsonism, acute dystonia, tardive dyskinesia); Tuberoinfundibular ↓DA (from antipsychotic) → hyperprolactinemia (galactorrhea, amenorrhea, sexual dysfunction)<br />
中脑边缘↑DA→阳性症状；中脑皮质↓DA→阴性/认知症状；黑质纹状体↓DA（抗精神病药所致）→EPS（静坐不能、帕金森样症状、急性肌张力障碍、迟发性运动障碍）；结节漏斗↓DA（抗精神病药所致）→高泌乳素血症（溢乳、闭经、性功能障碍）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Suicide risk in schizophrenia<br />
精神分裂症的自杀风险</td>
<td>Lifetime suicide rate ~5–10%; highest-risk profile: young male, early illness course, good insight (painfully aware of deficits), depressive symptoms, command hallucinations, recent hospitalization discharge<br />
终身自杀率约5–10%；高风险特征：年轻男性、病程早期、自知力良好（痛苦地意识到自身缺陷）、抑郁症状、命令性幻觉、近期出院</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Schizophrenia vs. schizoaffective disorder<br />
精神分裂症与分裂情感性障碍</td>
<td>Schizoaffective: psychotic symptoms present for ≥2 weeks WITHOUT concurrent mood episodes PLUS major mood episodes (MDD or bipolar) occupy the majority of total illness duration; in schizophrenia, mood episodes are absent or brief relative to psychotic duration<br />
分裂情感性障碍：精神病症状在无同期心境发作情况下持续≥2周，加上重大心境发作（MDD或双相）占总病程大部分时间；精神分裂症中心境发作缺失或相对于精神病病程极短暂</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Prodrome recognition:** Schizophrenia typically has a prodromal phase (months to years) of attenuated, subthreshold symptoms — social withdrawal, odd beliefs, declining academic/work performance — before frank psychosis; this patient's 1-year religious preoccupation almost certainly represents his prodrome\
  **前驱期识别:** 精神分裂症通常在明显精神病发作前有数月至数年的前驱期，表现为减弱的亚阈值症状——社交退缩、奇异信念、学业/工作表现下降；本患者1年的宗教先占观念几乎可以确定代表其前驱期

- **New-onset psychosis differential:** Always rule out: substance-induced psychosis (stimulants, cannabis, PCP/ketamine), anti-NMDAR encephalitis (check CSF + serum antibodies — associated with young women, ovarian teratoma, movement abnormalities), temporal lobe epilepsy (automatisms, aura), and Wilson's disease (copper studies, Kayser-Fleischer rings)\
  **新发精神病鉴别诊断:** 必须排除：物质诱导性精神病（兴奋剂、大麻、PCP/氯胺酮）、抗NMDAR脑炎（检查脑脊液+血清抗体——与年轻女性、卵巢畸胎瘤、运动异常相关）、颞叶癫痫（自动症、先兆）、威尔逊病（铜相关检查、Kayser-Fleischer环）

- **Negative symptoms vs. depression overlap:** Both schizophrenia's negative symptoms and MDD cause anhedonia, social withdrawal, and psychomotor slowing; this patient's "depressed mood" may reflect negative symptoms or true comorbid depression — antipsychotics preferentially treat negative symptoms; adding an antidepressant is considered if depressive features persist after psychosis stabilizes\
  **阴性症状与抑郁重叠:** 精神分裂症阴性症状与MDD均可引起快感缺失、社交退缩和精神运动迟缓；本患者的"抑郁情绪"可能反映阴性症状或真性共病抑郁——抗精神病药优先治疗阴性症状；若抑郁特征在精神病稳定后持续存在，则考虑加用抗抑郁药

- **Sex differences in onset and prognosis:** Males: onset late teens–mid 20s, more severe negative symptoms, worse long-term outcome; Females: onset late 20s–early 30s, more affective symptoms, better prognosis — estrogen is thought to exert a partial dopamine-modulating protective effect, explaining the later and milder female presentation\
  **发病和预后的性别差异:** 男性：发病于青少年晚期至25岁，阴性症状更严重，长期预后较差；女性：发病于20岁末至30岁初，情感症状更多，预后较好——雌激素被认为发挥部分多巴胺调节性保护作用，解释了女性发病较晚且较轻的现象

# Question 105 — Preterm Premature Rupture of Membranes (PPROM) / 胎膜早破（早产型）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>26-year-old primigravid woman</strong> has <strong>spontaneous rupture of the membranes</strong> at <strong>30 weeks' gestation</strong>. She is <strong>afebrile</strong> and has <strong>no contractions</strong>. A sterile speculum examination shows a <strong>closed cervix</strong> and a <strong>pool of clear fluid</strong> in the vagina. Which of the following is the most likely complication?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely complication?</strong></p>
<p>A) Amniotic band syndrome<br />
B) Fetal deformation<br />
C) Fetal hypoplastic lungs<br />
D) Preterm delivery<br />
E) Umbilical cord occlusion</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>26-year-old primigravid, 30 weeks<br />
26岁初产妇，妊娠30周</td>
<td>Preterm (&lt;37 weeks) + first pregnancy — meets PPROM definition; lung maturity not yet achieved<br />
早产（&lt;37周）+ 初次妊娠——符合PPROM定义；肺成熟尚未完成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spontaneous rupture of membranes<br />
自发性胎膜破裂</td>
<td>Before labor onset = PPROM; primary driver of preterm labor initiation<br />
在产程启动前破膜 = PPROM；是触发早产的主要机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Afebrile<br />
无发热</td>
<td>Excludes active chorioamnionitis at this moment; but infection risk remains elevated<br />
目前排除活动性绒毛膜羊膜炎；但感染风险仍高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No contractions<br />
无宫缩</td>
<td>Not yet in active labor, but PPROM almost invariably leads to labor onset<br />
尚未进入活跃产程，但PPROM几乎必然导致产程启动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pool of clear fluid, closed cervix<br />
阴道积液清澈，宫颈闭合</td>
<td>Classic sterile speculum finding confirming ROM; closed cervix confirms not yet in labor<br />
消毒窥阴器检查的典型发现，确认胎膜破裂；宫颈闭合确认尚未临产</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Preterm premature rupture of membranes (PPROM)** disrupts the **amniotic barrier**, triggering an inflammatory cascade that stimulates **prostaglandin release** and initiates labor:

**胎膜早破（PPROM）**破坏了**羊膜屏障**，触发炎症级联反应，刺激**前列腺素释放**并启动产程：

- Rupture exposes the amniotic cavity to vaginal flora → ascending infection risk → chorioamnionitis → uterine contractions\
  破膜使羊膜腔暴露于阴道菌群 → 上行感染风险 → 绒毛膜羊膜炎 → 子宫收缩

- Loss of amniotic fluid → oligohydramnios → decreased cushioning of umbilical cord and reduced fetal breathing movements\
  羊水流失 → 羊水过少 → 脐带缓冲减少，胎儿呼吸运动减弱

- Prostaglandins (PGE2, PGF2α) released from membranes and decidua directly stimulate cervical ripening and myometrial contractions\
  胎膜和蜕膜释放前列腺素（PGE2、PGF2α）直接刺激宫颈成熟和子宫肌层收缩

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The earlier PPROM occurs, the greater the risk of pulmonary hypoplasia — but in this patient at 30 weeks, preterm delivery is by far the most immediate and likely outcome.

**解剖小窍门:** PPROM发生越早，肺发育不全风险越高——但在这位30周的患者，早产是目前最直接、最可能的结局。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Preterm Delivery / 正确答案 (D) — 早产

**Preterm delivery** is the dominant complication of PPROM because rupture of membranes almost invariably triggers labor onset before term:

**早产**是PPROM的主要并发症，因为胎膜破裂几乎必然在足月前触发产程启动：

- PPROM accounts for approximately one-third of all preterm births\
  PPROM约占所有早产的三分之一

- ~50% of PPROM patients deliver within 1 week of membrane rupture\
  约50%的PPROM患者在胎膜破裂后1周内分娩

- Betamethasone (2 doses IM 24h apart) is given to accelerate fetal lung maturity in patients \<34 weeks\
  对\<34周患者给予倍他米松（肌注2剂，间隔24小时）以加速胎肺成熟

- Antibiotics (ampicillin + erythromycin) are given prophylactically to reduce chorioamnionitis risk and prolong latency\
  预防性使用抗生素（氨苄西林+红霉素）以降低绒毛膜羊膜炎风险并延长潜伏期

**Diagnosis:** PPROM diagnosed by sterile speculum exam showing pooling + Nitrazine test (pH 7.0–7.3) + ferning on microscopy; ultrasound confirms oligohydramnios.

**诊断:** PPROM通过消毒窥阴器检查见积液 + Nitrazine试验（pH 7.0–7.3）+ 显微镜下羊齿状结晶确诊；超声确认羊水过少。

**Treatment:** Expectant management with fetal monitoring, betamethasone (\<34 weeks), prophylactic antibiotics, and GBS prophylaxis; delivery triggered by chorioamnionitis, non-reassuring fetal status, or labor.

**治疗:** 期待治疗并监测胎儿，给予倍他米松（\<34周）、预防性抗生素及GBS预防；出现绒毛膜羊膜炎、胎儿状态不良或临产时终止妊娠。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Amniotic band syndrome<br />
A — 羊膜带综合征</td>
<td>PPROM is not a risk factor; amniotic bands arise from early amnion disruption independent of PPROM<br />
PPROM不是危险因素；羊膜带来源于与PPROM无关的早期羊膜破坏</td>
<td>Amniotic band syndrome causes limb/craniofacial defects detected on prenatal US; no association with PPROM<br />
羊膜带综合征导致肢体/颅面缺陷，产前超声可见；与PPROM无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Fetal deformation<br />
B — 胎儿畸形</td>
<td>Fetal defects do not cause PPROM; PPROM does not cause structural fetal deformities<br />
胎儿缺陷不引起PPROM；PPROM也不导致结构性胎儿畸形</td>
<td>Deformation implies mechanical force; severe oligohydramnios can cause positional deformation but this is not the most likely complication<br />
畸形意味着机械力；严重羊水过少可导致体位性变形，但这不是最可能的并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Fetal hypoplastic lungs<br />
C — 胎肺发育不全</td>
<td>Can occur with PPROM but requires prolonged oligohydramnios (weeks) at very early gestational ages (&lt;24 weeks); at 30 weeks it is not the most likely complication<br />
可发生于PPROM，但需要极早孕龄（&lt;24周）且长期羊水过少（数周）；在30周并非最可能的并发症</td>
<td>Pulmonary hypoplasia requires severe sustained oligohydramnios early in the canalicular phase; this patient will likely deliver before that occurs<br />
肺发育不全需要在细支气管期严重持续的羊水过少；该患者可能在发生之前已经分娩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Preterm delivery ✓<br />
D — 早产 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — PPROM almost invariably initiates labor before 37 weeks; it is the single most common and immediate complication<br />
正确——PPROM几乎必然在37周前启动产程；是最常见且最直接的并发症</td>
<td>Membrane rupture → prostaglandin release → uterine contractions → delivery<br />
胎膜破裂 → 前列腺素释放 → 子宫收缩 → 分娩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Umbilical cord occlusion<br />
E — 脐带受压</td>
<td>Oligohydramnios can reduce cord cushioning, but cord compression is a less common complication than preterm delivery and requires severe/prolonged fluid loss<br />
羊水过少可减少脐带缓冲，但脐带压迫比早产少见，且需要严重/持续的羊水丢失</td>
<td>Cord prolapse is the acute emergency with ROM + presenting part not engaged; cord occlusion from oligohydramnios is chronic and less likely here<br />
脐带脱垂是胎膜破裂+先露未衔接时的急性急症；羊水过少引起的脐带压迫是慢性的，此处不太可能</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (C) fetal hypoplastic lungs — test-takers often recall the PPROM–oligohydramnios–pulmonary hypoplasia connection, but forget that this complication requires very early gestational age (\<24 weeks) and weeks of sustained oligohydramnios, neither of which applies here.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是（C）胎肺发育不全——考生常记得PPROM→羊水过少→肺发育不全的联系，却忘记这一并发症需要极早孕龄（\<24周）及持续数周的羊水过少，两者在本题均不成立。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**PPROM (rupture of membranes before labor and before 37 weeks) almost invariably leads to preterm delivery, managed with betamethasone for lung maturity and prophylactic antibiotics.**

**胎膜早破（PPROM）（37周前、产程前胎膜破裂）几乎必然导致早产，处理核心为倍他米松促肺成熟+预防性抗生素。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PPROM Management "BAL" / 记忆钩 — PPROM管理 "BAL":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>etamethasone — 2 doses IM to accelerate fetal lung maturity (&lt;34 weeks) / 倍他米松——2次肌注促胎肺成熟（&lt;34周）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ntibiotics — ampicillin + erythromycin to reduce chorioamnionitis and prolong latency / 抗生素——氨苄西林+红霉素，降低绒毛膜羊膜炎风险、延长潜伏期<br />
• <strong>L</strong>atency monitoring — watch for labor, infection, fetal distress; deliver if any develop / 潜伏期监测——监测产程、感染、胎儿窘迫；出现任一情况立即终止妊娠</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — PPROM: Diagnosis, Risks, and Management / 高频知识表 — PPROM：诊断、风险与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of PPROM<br />
PPROM定义</td>
<td>Rupture of membranes before onset of labor AND before 37 weeks' gestation<br />
在产程启动前且妊娠37周前发生胎膜破裂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis triad<br />
诊断三联征</td>
<td>(1) Pooling on speculum exam; (2) Nitrazine+ (pH 7.0–7.3); (3) Ferning on microscopy; US confirms oligohydramnios<br />
（1）窥阴器检查见积液；（2）Nitrazine阳性（pH 7.0–7.3）；（3）显微镜下羊齿结晶；超声确认羊水过少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Prior PPROM, vaginal/cervical infection, cigarette smoking, cervical incompetence, multiple gestation<br />
既往PPROM、阴道/宫颈感染、吸烟、宫颈机能不全、多胎妊娠</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Betamethasone indication<br />
倍他米松适应证</td>
<td>Given at 24–34 weeks to accelerate surfactant production; reduces RDS, IVH, NEC<br />
24–34周给予，促进表面活性物质合成；降低RDS、IVH、NEC发生率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antibiotic regimen<br />
抗生素方案</td>
<td>Ampicillin IV + erythromycin PO for 48 hours, then amoxicillin + erythromycin for 5 days (avoid amoxicillin-clavulanate — increases NEC risk)<br />
氨苄西林静注+红霉素口服48小时，继以阿莫西林+红霉素5天（避免阿莫西林-克拉维酸——增加NEC风险）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Delivery timing<br />
终止妊娠时机</td>
<td>At 34 weeks if stable; earlier if chorioamnionitis, abruption, non-reassuring fetal status, or labor onset<br />
稳定者34周终止；出现绒毛膜羊膜炎、胎盘早剥、胎儿窘迫或临产则提前</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differentiating ROM vs. urinary incontinence:** Nitrazine turns blue (alkaline) with amniotic fluid (pH 7.0–7.3); urine is acidic (pH \<6) — false positive with blood or BV\
  **区分胎膜破裂与尿失禁:** 羊水（pH 7.0–7.3）使Nitrazine变蓝（碱性）；尿液为酸性（pH\<6）——血液或细菌性阴道病可致假阳性

- **Chorioamnionitis signs:** Maternal fever \>38°C, uterine tenderness, maternal/fetal tachycardia, purulent fluid — indicates immediate delivery regardless of GA\
  **绒毛膜羊膜炎体征:** 母体发热\>38°C、子宫压痛、母胎心动过速、脓性羊水——无论孕龄立即终止妊娠

- **Key complication at extreme prematurity (\<24 wks):** Pulmonary hypoplasia due to prolonged oligohydramnios preventing the mechanical stretch needed for alveolar development\
  **极早产（\<24周）的关键并发症:** 长期羊水过少阻碍肺泡发育所需的机械牵张，导致肺发育不全

- **Variant — term PROM (≥37 weeks):** ROM before labor at term; manage with oxytocin induction if no labor within 12–24 hours to reduce chorioamnionitis risk (betamethasone not needed at term)\
  **变式——足月胎膜早破（≥37周）:** 足月后产程前破膜；若12–24小时内未临产则予缩宫素引产以降低绒毛膜羊膜炎风险（足月无需倍他米松）

# Question 106 — Acute Chest Syndrome in Sickle Cell Disease / 镰状细胞病急性胸部综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>An 8-year-old African American girl</strong> with <strong>sickle cell disease</strong> is brought to the physician by her mother because of a <strong>12-hour history of cough and difficulty breathing</strong>. Her medications are penicillin and folic acid. Her <strong>temperature is 39°C (102.2°F)</strong>, pulse is 130/min, <strong>respirations are 40/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 105/60 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an <strong>oxygen saturation of 94%</strong>. On pulmonary examination, <strong>crackles are heard in the upper lobes</strong>. <strong>Breath sounds are decreased at the lung bases bilaterally</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. An x-ray of the chest is shown. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Anti-Mycoplasma pneumoniae IgG titer<br />
B) Rapid antigen detection test for respiratory syncytial virus<br />
C) Blood culture<br />
D) Spiral CT scan of the chest<br />
E) Thoracentesis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>8-year-old with sickle cell disease<br />
患有镰状细胞病的 8 岁女孩</td>
<td>SCD causes autosplenectomy → hyposplenia → inability to clear encapsulated bacteria → dramatically increased infection risk<br />
SCD 导致自体脾脏切除 → 脾功能下降 → 无法清除有荚膜细菌 → 感染风险急剧增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever 39°C + cough + dyspnea<br />
发热 39°C + 咳嗽 + 呼吸困难</td>
<td>Fever + new respiratory symptom in SCD = acute chest syndrome until proven otherwise<br />
SCD 患者发热 + 新出现呼吸道症状 = 需首先排除急性胸部综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RR 40/min + HR 130/min<br />
呼吸频率 40 次/分 + 心率 130 次/分</td>
<td>Tachypnea and tachycardia indicate significant respiratory compromise and physiologic stress<br />
呼吸过速和心动过速提示明显呼吸功能受损和生理应激</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SpO2 94% on room air<br />
室内空气下血氧饱和度 94%</td>
<td>Hypoxemia confirms impaired gas exchange; ACS is defined partly by new hypoxemia in SCD<br />
低氧血症确认气体交换障碍；新发低氧血症是 ACS 诊断标准之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Crackles upper lobes + decreased BS at bases bilaterally<br />
上叶爆裂音 + 双肺底呼吸音减低</td>
<td>Suggests upper lobe consolidation + bilateral pleural effusions — classic chest x-ray findings in ACS<br />
提示上叶实变 + 双侧胸腔积液——ACS 典型胸部影像学表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Already on prophylactic penicillin<br />
已在服用预防性青霉素</td>
<td>SCD patients receive penicillin prophylaxis; this doesn't eliminate bacterial infection risk, especially for resistant organisms<br />
SCD 患者常规服用青霉素预防；但这不能消除细菌感染风险，尤其对耐药菌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Sickle cell disease** causes **vaso-occlusion** within the pulmonary microvasculature, leading to ischemia, inflammation, and alveolar-capillary leak. Simultaneously, **functional asplenia** (autosplenectomy from repeated splenic infarctions) results in profound **immunodeficiency** — particularly against encapsulated organisms — making bacteremia an immediate life threat:

**镰状细胞病**导致肺微血管**血管阻塞**，引起缺血、炎症和肺泡-毛细血管渗漏。与此同时，**功能性无脾**（反复脾梗死导致的自体脾脏切除）造成严重**免疫缺陷**——尤其是针对有荚膜细菌——使菌血症成为即时致命威胁：

- Sickle-shaped RBCs adhere to vascular endothelium → pulmonary microvascular occlusion → infarction + inflammation\
  镰刀形红细胞黏附血管内皮 → 肺微血管阻塞 → 梗死 + 炎症

- Repeated splenic infarctions → functional asplenia → loss of opsonization → Streptococcus pneumoniae, H. influenzae, Salmonella bacteremia risk\
  反复脾梗死 → 功能性无脾 → 调理作用丧失 → 肺炎链球菌、流感嗜血杆菌、沙门菌菌血症风险

- ACS and bacterial pneumonia are clinically and radiographically indistinguishable → must assume bacterial superinfection is present until blood cultures prove otherwise\
  ACS 与细菌性肺炎在临床和影像学上无法区分 → 必须假设存在细菌重叠感染，直到血培养结果排除

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** ACS preferentially involves the lower lobes (unlike typical CAP), but any lobe can be affected; bilateral lower lobe involvement + pleural effusions on CXR is a red flag in SCD.

**解剖小窍门:** ACS 好发于下叶（与典型社区获得性肺炎不同），但任何肺叶均可受累；胸片显示双侧下叶受累 + 胸腔积液在 SCD 患者中是危险信号。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Blood Culture / 正确答案 (C) — 血培养

**Blood culture** is the critical first diagnostic step because it identifies bacteremia before empiric antibiotics are started, guiding definitive therapy without delaying treatment:

**血培养**是关键的第一诊断步骤，因为它能在启动经验性抗生素治疗之前识别菌血症，在不延误治疗的情况下指导最终方案：

- SCD patients are functionally asplenic → cannot clear bacteremia → sepsis progresses with frightening speed\
  SCD 患者功能性无脾 → 无法清除菌血症 → 败血症进展极为迅速

- ACS is clinically indistinguishable from bacterial pneumonia → empiric antibiotics are mandatory, but culture first\
  ACS 临床上与细菌性肺炎无法区分 → 必须使用经验性抗生素，但应先采血培养

- After drawing blood cultures, empiric broad-spectrum antibiotics must be started immediately without waiting for results\
  抽取血培养后，必须立即开始经验性广谱抗生素治疗，无需等待结果

**Diagnosis:** Blood culture is drawn → followed immediately by empiric antibiotics (covering typical + atypical organisms), supplemental O2, analgesia, incentive spirometry, and judicious IV fluids.

**诊断:** 采集血培养 → 立即启动经验性抗生素（覆盖典型 + 非典型病原体）、吸氧、镇痛、激励式肺活量计训练及谨慎补液。

**Treatment:** Empiric antibiotics (β-lactam + macrolide or fluoroquinolone), supplemental oxygen to maintain normoxia, simple or exchange transfusion for severe ACS.

**治疗:** 经验性抗生素（β-内酰胺类 + 大环内酯类或氟喹诺酮类）、吸氧维持正常血氧、重度 ACS 需简单或置换输血。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Anti-Mycoplasma pneumoniae IgG titer<br />
A — 抗肺炎支原体 IgG 滴度</td>
<td>Measures prior exposure, not acute infection; IgG rises weeks after infection; empiric macrolide already covers Mycoplasma<br />
仅反映既往暴露，非急性感染；IgG 在感染数周后才升高；经验性大环内酯类已覆盖支原体</td>
<td>IgG titer timing: takes weeks to rise, useless for acute management<br />
IgG 滴度时间：需数周才升高，对急性处理无用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Rapid antigen detection test for RSV<br />
B — RSV 快速抗原检测</td>
<td>Useful for bronchiolitis workup; however, viral etiology does not preclude concurrent bacteremia — blood culture is more immediately life-saving<br />
适用于细支气管炎诊断；但病毒病因不排除同时存在菌血症——血培养在挽救生命方面更优先</td>
<td>Viral vs. bacterial: both can occur simultaneously in SCD; bacteremia kills faster<br />
病毒 vs 细菌：在 SCD 中可同时存在；菌血症致死更快</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Blood culture ✓<br />
C — 血培养 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — identifies bacteremia before empiric antibiotics, guiding therapy in an immunocompromised patient where sepsis is an immediate threat<br />
正确——在经验性抗生素前识别菌血症，指导免疫受损患者的治疗，因为败血症是即时威胁</td>
<td>Must be done before antibiotics; does not delay empiric treatment<br />
必须在抗生素前采集；不会延误经验性治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Spiral CT scan of the chest<br />
D — 胸部螺旋 CT</td>
<td>Used to evaluate pulmonary embolism; PE risk is elevated in adult SCD but uncommon in children; cannot be prioritized over blood culture<br />
用于评估肺栓塞；成人 SCD 中 PE 风险增加，但儿童不常见；不能优先于血培养</td>
<td>Age matters: PE complicating ACS more common in adults than children<br />
年龄重要：PE 并发 ACS 在成人比儿童更常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Thoracentesis<br />
E — 胸腔穿刺</td>
<td>Useful for diagnosis/drainage of significant pleural effusion; this patient's bilateral effusions are small (decreased breath sounds) — blood culture addresses the life-threatening risk first<br />
用于诊断/引流显著胸腔积液；此患者双侧积液量少——血培养首先处理致命风险</td>
<td>Size of effusion: small effusions are common in ACS and do not require immediate thoracentesis<br />
积液量：少量积液在 ACS 中常见，无需立即穿刺</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) RSV testing — it's reasonable for a febrile child with respiratory symptoms, but in SCD the immediate threat is bacteremia from functional asplenia, making blood culture the undisputed priority.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 (B) RSV 检测——对于发热伴呼吸道症状的儿童看似合理，但 SCD 患者因功能性无脾面临菌血症的即时威胁，血培养毫无疑问是优先选择。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Acute Chest Syndrome vs Bacterial Pneumonia in SCD / 镰状细胞病患者急性胸部综合征与细菌性肺炎对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Acute Chest Syndrome</strong><br />
<strong>急性胸部综合征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bacterial Pneumonia (non-SCD)</strong><br />
<strong>细菌性肺炎（非 SCD）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pathogenesis<br />
发病机制</td>
<td>Vaso-occlusion + ischemia + possible infection trigger<br />
血管阻塞 + 缺血 + 可能的感染诱因</td>
<td>Direct microbial invasion of lung parenchyma<br />
微生物直接侵入肺实质</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria<br />
诊断标准</td>
<td>New infiltrate on CXR + fever OR respiratory symptoms in SCD patient<br />
SCD 患者胸片新发浸润影 + 发热或呼吸道症状</td>
<td>Infiltrate + clinical symptoms + microbiologic confirmation<br />
浸润影 + 临床症状 + 微生物确认</td>

肺叶好发部位</td>

下叶最常见；可累及任何肺叶</td>

任何肺叶；非典型病原体（结核、克雷伯菌）偏好上叶</td>

<tr>
<td>CXR findings<br />
胸片表现</td>
<td>Segmental/subsegmental consolidation; pleural effusions common<br />
节段性/亚节段性实变；胸腔积液常见</td>
<td>Lobar consolidation; air bronchograms<br />
大叶性实变；空气支气管征</td>

<tr>
