## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Anaphylaxis is an IgE-mediated, multi-system hypersensitivity reaction requiring immediate IM epinephrine as the only first-line treatment because it simultaneously reverses vasodilation (α₁), bronchoconstriction (β₂), and distributive shock (β₁) — delays in administration directly increase mortality.**

**过敏反应是 IgE 介导的多系统超敏反应，需要立即肌注肾上腺素作为唯一一线治疗，因为它能同时逆转血管扩张（α₁）、支气管痉挛（β₂）和分布性休克（β₁）——延迟用药直接增加死亡率。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "EPI FIRST" for Anaphylaxis Management / 记忆钩 — 过敏反应处理"EPI FIRST"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>E</strong>pinephrine — ALWAYS the first drug; no contraindications exist in true anaphylaxis / 肾上腺素——永远第一个用；真正过敏反应中无任何禁忌证<br />
• <strong>P</strong>rogression — anaphylaxis can kill within minutes; every delay worsens outcome / 进展——过敏反应可在数分钟内致死；每一次延迟都使预后恶化<br />
• <strong>I</strong>gE-mediated — prior sensitization required; first exposure silent, second exposure = reaction / IgE 介导——需要既往致敏；初次接触无反应，再次接触发病<br />
• <strong>F</strong>luids IV — distributive shock needs volume after epinephrine is given / 静脉补液——给予肾上腺素后需补液纠正分布性休克<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nhibit relapse — corticosteroids + antihistamines added to prevent biphasic reaction (8–72h) / 抑制复发——加用糖皮质激素 + 抗组胺药预防双相反应（8–72小时）<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ash + wheeze + BP drop — the triad confirming anaphylaxis over isolated asthma or urticaria / 皮疹 + 哮鸣 + 血压下降——区别于单纯哮喘或荨麻疹确认过敏反应的三联征<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ubQ/IM thigh — preferred injection site; IM lateral thigh gives fastest absorption / 大腿肌注——首选注射部位；大腿外侧肌注吸收最快<br />
• <strong>T</strong>wo-system rule — ≥2 organ systems involved = anaphylaxis by definition / 双系统法则——≥2个器官系统受累 = 过敏反应的定义标准</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Anaphylaxis: Pathophysiology, Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 过敏反应：病理生理、诊断与治疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria for anaphylaxis<br />
过敏反应诊断标准</td>
<td>≥2 organ systems involved after allergen exposure; OR hypotension alone after a known allergen; skin/mucosal findings present in 80–90% of cases but NOT required<br />
接触过敏原后≥2个器官系统受累；或已知过敏原接触后单纯低血压；80–90% 有皮肤/黏膜表现但不是必须条件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common triggers (food)<br />
常见食物诱因</td>
<td>Peanuts, tree nuts, shellfish, fish, milk, eggs (the "Big 8"); hidden traces in processed foods are a major risk<br />
花生、坚果、贝类、鱼、牛奶、鸡蛋（"大八类"）；加工食品中的隐性成分是主要风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epinephrine dosing &amp; route<br />
肾上腺素剂量和给药途径</td>
<td>0.3–0.5 mg of 1:1,000 solution IM into anterolateral thigh; may repeat every 5–15 min; reserve IV (1:10,000) for cardiac arrest or refractory shock only<br />
1:1,000 溶液 0.3–0.5 mg 肌注大腿前外侧；每 5–15 分钟可重复；仅心搏骤停或难治性休克时静注（1:10,000）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biphasic anaphylaxis<br />
双相过敏反应</td>
<td>Second wave of symptoms 8–72 h after apparent recovery without re-exposure; incidence ~5–20%; IV corticosteroids reduce but do not eliminate risk; observe all anaphylaxis patients ≥4–8 h<br />
初次明显恢复后 8–72 小时内无再次接触情况下的第二波症状；发生率约 5–20%；静脉糖皮质激素降低但不能消除风险；所有过敏反应患者观察≥4–8小时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epinephrine vs albuterol distinction<br />
肾上腺素 vs 沙丁胺醇的本质区别</td>
<td>Both cause β₂ bronchodilation, but only epinephrine adds α₁ vasoconstriction (reverses hypotension + mucosal edema) and β₁ inotropy; albuterol is adjunct only, never first-line in anaphylaxis<br />
两者均有 β₂ 支气管扩张，但只有肾上腺素额外提供 α₁ 血管收缩（逆转低血压 + 黏膜水肿）和 β₁ 正性肌力；沙丁胺醇仅为辅助，在过敏反应中从不作为一线</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anaphylactoid reactions<br />
类过敏反应</td>
<td>Clinically identical to anaphylaxis but not IgE-mediated; caused by direct mast cell activation (IV contrast, opioids, aspirin/NSAIDs); treatment is identical — epinephrine first<br />
临床表现与过敏反应相同但非 IgE 介导；由直接肥大细胞激活引起（静脉造影剂、阿片类、阿司匹林/NSAIDs）；治疗相同——肾上腺素优先</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum tryptase<br />
血清类胰蛋白酶</td>
<td>Marker of mast cell degranulation; peaks 1–2 h after onset, returns to baseline within 24 h; useful for retrospective confirmation when diagnosis is uncertain; not needed for acute management decisions<br />
肥大细胞脱颗粒标志物；发作后 1–2 小时达峰，24 小时内恢复基线；诊断不确定时用于回顾性确认；急性期处理决策无需等待结果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Discharge requirements<br />
出院要求</td>
<td>Prescribe epinephrine auto-injector (EpiPen) for all patients; educate on self-injection technique; refer to allergist for skin testing; advise medical alert bracelet and avoidance of known trigger<br />
所有患者开具肾上腺素自动注射器（EpiPen）；教导自我注射技术；转介过敏科进行皮试；建议佩戴医疗警报手环并避免已知诱因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Hidden allergen distractors:** This question deliberately lists oral contraceptives, smoking, alcohol, and unfamiliar laundry detergents as red herrings — the exam tests whether you connect peanut allergy history + food ingestion + multi-system onset rather than chasing irrelevant exposures\
  **隐性过敏原干扰项：** 本题故意列出口服避孕药、吸烟、饮酒和陌生洗涤剂作为干扰——考试考察你能否将花生过敏史 + 食物摄入 + 多系统发作联系起来，而非追踪无关接触史

- **Differential of multi-system acute presentations:** Anaphylaxis (food/drug/sting trigger + urticaria + wheezing + hypotension), vasovagal syncope (bradycardia + no urticaria + resolves with supine position), panic attack (no objective BP/skin/SpO₂ changes), carcinoid crisis (chronic flushing + diarrhea without urticaria, metastatic history)\
  **多系统急性表现鉴别：** 过敏反应（食物/药物/蜂刺诱因 + 荨麻疹 + 哮鸣 + 低血压），血管迷走性晕厥（心动过缓 + 无荨麻疹 + 仰卧后缓解），惊恐发作（无客观血压/皮肤/血氧变化），类癌危象（慢性潮红 + 腹泻无荨麻疹，有转移性肿瘤病史）

- **Key complication if epinephrine delayed:** Upper airway obstruction from progressive laryngeal edema (stridor → apnea) or cardiovascular arrest from refractory distributive shock — both are rapidly fatal; early epinephrine prevents both pathways\
  **延迟使用肾上腺素的关键并发症：** 进行性喉头水肿导致的上气道梗阻（喘鸣 → 窒息）或难治性分布性休克导致的心搏骤停——两者均可迅速致死；早期肾上腺素可同时预防两条通路

- **Variant — exercise-induced anaphylaxis:** Occurs with physical exertion, sometimes only when combined with a specific food (food-dependent exercise-induced anaphylaxis); no IgE detected on standard testing; management is the same — epinephrine first-line\
  **题目变式——运动诱发过敏反应：** 发生于体力活动时，有时仅在特定食物与运动联合时触发（食物依赖运动诱发过敏反应）；标准检测可能检测不到 IgE；处理相同——肾上腺素一线

# Question 110 — Bladder Transitional Cell Carcinoma / 膀胱移行细胞癌

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because he has noticed <strong>blood in his urine for the past 2 weeks</strong>. He has <strong>no prior history of blood in his urine</strong>. He has <strong>not had pain</strong> or any other symptoms. He has hypertension controlled with a diuretic and hypercholesterolemia controlled with a lipid-lowering agent. His blood pressure is 120/76 mm Hg. Examination shows <strong>no abnormalities</strong>. Urinalysis shows <strong>RBCs that are too numerous to count</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Renal scintigraphy<br />
B) Retrograde urethrography<br />
C) MRI of the pelvis<br />
D) Cystoscopy<br />
E) Renal biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>67-year-old man<br />
67岁男性</td>
<td>Bladder cancer peaks in older men; male sex is an independent risk factor<br />
膀胱癌高发于老年男性；男性是独立危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood in urine for 2 weeks<br />
血尿持续2周</td>
<td>New gross hematuria lasting &gt;1 week in adults mandates urgent urologic evaluation for malignancy<br />
成人新发肉眼血尿持续&gt;1周，需紧急泌尿外科评估排除恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No prior history of hematuria<br />
无既往血尿史</td>
<td>New-onset hematuria in an older male raises strong suspicion for urothelial carcinoma<br />
老年男性新发血尿高度提示尿路上皮癌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Not had pain<br />
无疼痛</td>
<td>Painless hematuria is the hallmark of bladder cancer; painful hematuria suggests stones or infection<br />
无痛血尿是膀胱癌的标志；有痛血尿提示结石或感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Examination shows no abnormalities<br />
体检无异常</td>
<td>Absence of flank mass or tenderness argues against renal cell carcinoma or pyelonephritis<br />
无侧腹包块或压痛，不支持肾细胞癌或肾盂肾炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RBCs too numerous to count<br />
RBC计数不可计数</td>
<td>Massive hematuria without casts or significant proteinuria points to a urothelial (non-glomerular) source<br />
大量血尿但无管型或蛋白尿，提示尿路上皮（非肾小球）来源</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Transitional cell carcinoma (TCC)** of the bladder arises from the **urothelium** lining the bladder wall and produces hematuria by **disrupting the mucosal vasculature** of growing tumors:

**膀胱移行细胞癌（TCC）**起源于膀胱壁的**尿路上皮**，通过破坏生长肿瘤的**黏膜血管**产生血尿：

- Carcinogen exposure (aniline dyes, smoking metabolites, cyclophosphamide) → DNA damage to urothelial stem cells → dysplastic proliferation\
  致癌物暴露（苯胺染料、吸烟代谢物、环磷酰胺）→ 尿路上皮干细胞DNA损伤 → 发育不良性增殖

- Superficial papillary tumors and CIS bleed intermittently → gross, painless hematuria (no nerve irritation until muscle invasion)\
  表浅乳头状瘤和CIS间歇性出血 → 肉眼无痛血尿（肌层浸润前无神经刺激）

- Hematuria is often intermittent — patients may falsely reassure themselves when bleeding stops, delaying diagnosis\
  血尿常为间歇性——患者可能在出血停止时错误地自我安慰，延误诊断

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The urothelium lines the entire urinary tract from renal pelvis to urethra — TCC can arise anywhere, but the bladder accounts for ~90% of all urothelial cancers.

**解剖小窍门:** 尿路上皮从肾盂到尿道衬覆整个泌尿道——TCC可在任何部位发生，但膀胱约占所有尿路上皮癌的90%。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Cystoscopy / 正确答案 (D) — 膀胱镜检查

**Cystoscopy** is the gold-standard first step for evaluating painless gross hematuria in adults ≥40, allowing direct visualization and biopsy of any urothelial lesion:

**膀胱镜检查**是评估≥40岁成人无痛肉眼血尿的金标准首选步骤，可直接观察和活检任何尿路上皮病变：

- Provides direct visualization of the bladder mucosa — identifies papillary tumors, flat CIS, and vascular lesions invisible to imaging\
  直接观察膀胱黏膜——识别影像学不可见的乳头状瘤、扁平原位癌和血管病变

- Allows simultaneous biopsy for histologic confirmation of TCC grade and stage\
  同时允许活检进行TCC分级和分期的组织学确认

- Most sensitive modality for detecting small mucosal tumors missed by CT or MRI\
  对CT或MRI漏诊的小黏膜肿瘤是最灵敏的检查方式

- Superficial tumors can be resected at the same session via TURBT (transurethral resection of bladder tumor)\
  表浅肿瘤可在同一操作中通过TURBT（经尿道膀胱肿瘤切除术）一并切除

**Diagnosis:** In any adult ≥40 with painless gross hematuria, cystoscopy is the mandatory first diagnostic step before cross-sectional imaging or biopsy of other organs.

**诊断:** 对于任何≥40岁无痛肉眼血尿的成人，膀胱镜检查是横断面影像或其他器官活检前必须的首选诊断步骤。

**Treatment:** Non-muscle-invasive TCC → TURBT ± intravesical BCG; muscle-invasive TCC (≥T2) → radical cystectomy ± neoadjuvant cisplatin-based chemotherapy.

**治疗:** 非肌层浸润性TCC → TURBT ± 膀胱内灌注BCG；肌层浸润性TCC（≥T2）→ 根治性膀胱切除术 ± 新辅助铂类化疗。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Renal scintigraphy<br />
A — 肾脏显像</td>
<td>Wrong — evaluates renal blood flow and function (perfusion defects), not urothelial lesions; has no role in hematuria workup<br />
错误——评估肾血流和功能（灌注缺陷），不评估尿路上皮病变；在血尿检查中无作用</td>
<td>Renal scintigraphy diagnoses renal artery stenosis or quantifies split renal function — not mucosal tumors<br />
肾脏显像诊断肾动脉狭窄或量化分肾功能——不用于黏膜肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Retrograde urethrography<br />
B — 逆行尿道造影</td>
<td>Wrong — used exclusively to detect urethral discontinuity after trauma (straddle injuries, pelvic fractures); entirely irrelevant here<br />
错误——专门用于检测外伤后尿道不连续（骑跨伤、骨盆骨折）；此处完全不相关</td>
<td>No trauma history; this patient has a medical, not traumatic, cause of hematuria<br />
无外伤史；此患者血尿为内科原因，非外伤性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — MRI of the pelvis<br />
C — 盆腔MRI</td>
<td>Wrong — useful for staging known bladder cancer (extravesical extension, lymph nodes), but cannot biopsy lesions; diagnosis must precede staging<br />
错误——对已知膀胱癌的分期有用（膀胱外扩展、淋巴结），但无法活检病变；诊断必须先于分期</td>
<td>Staging imaging comes after cystoscopic diagnosis, not before<br />
分期影像在膀胱镜诊断之后，而非之前</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Cystoscopy ✓<br />
D — 膀胱镜检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — direct visualization + biopsy is the gold-standard first step for painless gross hematuria in an older adult<br />
正确——直接观察+活检是老年人无痛肉眼血尿的金标准首选步骤</td>
<td>Only modality that simultaneously diagnoses and can treat superficial TCC in one session<br />
唯一可在一次操作中同时诊断并治疗表浅TCC的检查方式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Renal biopsy<br />
E — 肾活检</td>
<td>Wrong — indicated for glomerular disease (nephrotic/nephritic syndrome, lupus nephritis, interstitial nephritis); no RBC casts or proteinuria here<br />
错误——适用于肾小球疾病（肾病/肾炎综合征、狼疮性肾炎、间质性肾炎）；此处无RBC管型或蛋白尿</td>
<td>Hematuria without proteinuria or RBC casts = non-glomerular source; renal biopsy is not indicated<br />
无蛋白尿或RBC管型的血尿 = 非肾小球来源；肾活检不适用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Retrograde urethrography (B) is the most out-of-place distractor — it is exclusively for urethral trauma workup (straddle injuries, pelvic fractures) and has absolutely no role in any hematuria evaluation without trauma history.*

逆行尿道造影（B）是最离题的干扰项——它专门用于尿道外伤检查（骑跨伤、骨盆骨折），在无外伤史的血尿评估中完全没有作用。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Bladder Cancer vs. Renal Cell Carcinoma vs. Glomerulonephritis / 膀胱癌 vs 肾细胞癌 vs 肾小球肾炎（血尿原因三向对比）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bladder Cancer (TCC)</strong><br />
<strong>膀胱癌（TCC）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Renal Cell Carcinoma</strong><br />
<strong>肾细胞癌</strong></th>
<th><strong>Glomerulonephritis</strong><br />
<strong>肾小球肾炎</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Hematuria character<br />
血尿性质</td>
<td>Painless, gross, intermittent<br />
无痛、肉眼、间歇性</td>
<td>Gross (classic triad: hematuria + flank pain + palpable mass)<br />
肉眼（经典三联征：血尿+侧腹痛+可触及包块）</td>
<td>Microscopic; tea/cola-colored urine (IgA nephropathy)<br />
镜下；茶色/可乐色尿（IgA肾病）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urinalysis<br />
尿液分析</td>
<td>Many RBCs; no casts; no significant proteinuria<br />
大量RBC；无管型；无显著蛋白尿</td>
<td>RBCs; no casts<br />
RBC；无管型</td>
<td>RBC casts + proteinuria (hallmark of glomerular disease)<br />
RBC管型+蛋白尿（肾小球疾病标志）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First diagnostic step<br />
首选诊断步骤</td>
<td>Cystoscopy + biopsy<br />
膀胱镜+活检</td>
<td>Contrast-enhanced CT abdomen/pelvis → biopsy<br />
腹/盆腔增强CT → 活检</td>
<td>Renal biopsy<br />
肾活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Smoking, aniline dyes, cyclophosphamide, schistosomiasis<br />
吸烟、苯胺染料、环磷酰胺、血吸虫病</td>
<td>von Hippel-Lindau syndrome, smoking, obesity, dialysis<br />
VHL综合征、吸烟、肥胖、透析</td>
<td>Post-streptococcal, IgA nephropathy, lupus, ANCA vasculitis<br />
链球菌感染后、IgA肾病、狼疮、ANCA血管炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>TURBT ± intravesical BCG; radical cystectomy if ≥T2<br />
TURBT ± 膀胱内BCG；≥T2则根治性膀胱切除</td>
<td>Radical/partial nephrectomy; sunitinib/immunotherapy for metastatic disease<br />
根治性/部分肾切除；转移性疾病用舒尼替尼/免疫治疗</td>
<td>Steroids, ACE inhibitors, treat underlying cause<br />
激素、ACEI、治疗基础病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surveillance<br />
随访监测</td>
<td>Cystoscopy every 3–6 months (50–70% recurrence rate)<br />
每3-6个月膀胱镜（复发率50-70%）</td>
<td>CT chest/abdomen every 6–12 months<br />
每6-12个月胸/腹CT</td>
<td>Renal function, proteinuria, blood pressure monitoring<br />
肾功能、蛋白尿、血压监测</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In an older adult with new-onset painless gross hematuria, bladder cancer (TCC) is the leading diagnosis and cystoscopy with biopsy is the mandatory first diagnostic step.**

**老年患者出现新发无痛肉眼血尿，膀胱癌（TCC）是首要诊断，膀胱镜加活检是必须的首选诊断步骤。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CATS Cause Bladder Cancer / 记忆钩 — "CATS"记忆膀胱癌危险因素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>yclophosphamide — alkylating agent; acrolein metabolite damages urothelium → hemorrhagic cystitis → TCC / 环磷酰胺——烷化剂；丙烯醛代谢物损伤尿路上皮 → 出血性膀胱炎 → TCC<br />
• <strong>A</strong>niline dyes — occupational exposure (textile, rubber, dye workers); aromatic amines are the culprit / 苯胺染料——职业暴露（纺织、橡胶、染料工人）；芳香胺是罪魁祸首<br />
• <strong>T</strong>obacco (smoking) — single largest modifiable risk factor; doubles TCC risk / 烟草（吸烟）——最大的可改变危险因素；TCC风险加倍<br />
• <strong>S</strong>chistosomiasis (S. haematobium) — causes squamous cell carcinoma of bladder, NOT TCC; endemic in Africa/Middle East / 血吸虫病（埃及血吸虫）——导致膀胱鳞状细胞癌，非TCC；流行于非洲/中东</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Bladder Cancer Diagnosis & Staging / 高频知识表 — 膀胱癌诊断与分期

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation<br />
经典表现</td>
<td>Painless gross hematuria in adults &gt;50; intermittent bleeding without dysuria or fever<br />
&gt;50岁成人无痛肉眼血尿；无尿痛或发热的间歇性出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common histology<br />
最常见组织学类型</td>
<td>Transitional cell (urothelial) carcinoma — 90% of bladder cancers; squamous cell (associated with schistosomiasis/chronic irritation) is #2<br />
移行细胞（尿路上皮）癌——占膀胱癌90%；鳞状细胞癌（与血吸虫病/慢性刺激相关）排第2</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Carcinoma in situ (CIS)<br />
原位癌（CIS）</td>
<td>Flat, high-grade urothelial lesion confined to epithelium; aggressive despite not invading submucosa; treated with intravesical BCG after TURBT<br />
扁平、高级别尿路上皮病变，局限于上皮层；尽管未侵犯黏膜下层但侵袭性强；TURBT后用膀胱内BCG治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>T-staging overview<br />
T分期概述</td>
<td>Ta = papillary, confined to mucosa; T1 = invades lamina propria; T2 = invades muscularis propria; T3 = perivesical fat; T4 = adjacent organs<br />
Ta=乳头状，局限于黏膜；T1=侵犯固有层；T2=侵犯固有肌层；T3=膀胱周围脂肪；T4=邻近器官</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment by stage<br />
按分期治疗</td>
<td>Non-muscle-invasive (Ta/T1/CIS) → TURBT ± BCG; muscle-invasive (T2+) → radical cystectomy ± neoadjuvant cisplatin<br />
非肌层浸润（Ta/T1/CIS）→ TURBT ± BCG；肌层浸润（T2+）→ 根治性膀胱切除 ± 新辅助顺铂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>High recurrence rate<br />
高复发率</td>
<td>50–70% recurrence after TURBT; requires cystoscopic surveillance every 3–6 months<br />
TURBT后50-70%复发；需每3-6个月膀胱镜随访</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Protective agents against cyclophosphamide cystitis<br />
预防环磷酰胺膀胱炎</td>
<td>Mesna (binds acrolein in urine) + aggressive IV hydration; prevents hemorrhagic cystitis<br />
美司那（与尿中丙烯醛结合）+ 积极静脉补液；预防出血性膀胱炎</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of painless gross hematuria:** Bladder cancer (most common in adults \>50), renal cell carcinoma (add flank pain + mass), upper tract TCC (renal pelvis/ureter), AV malformation, BPH (in older men)\
  **无痛肉眼血尿鉴别:** 膀胱癌（\>50岁成人最常见）、肾细胞癌（伴侧腹痛+包块）、上尿路TCC（肾盂/输尿管）、动静脉畸形、BPH（老年男性）

- **Variant — upper tract TCC:** TCC arising in renal pelvis or ureter; diagnosed with CT urogram + ureteroscopy; treated with nephroureterectomy (remove entire ureter to prevent field cancerization)\
  **题目变式——上尿路TCC:** 发生于肾盂或输尿管的TCC；通过CT尿路造影+输尿管镜诊断；行肾输尿管切除术（切除整个输尿管以防止区域癌变）

- **Key distinction — microscopic vs. gross hematuria workup:** Both require cystoscopy in adults \>35; gross hematuria has higher yield for malignancy and requires more urgent evaluation\
  **关键区别——镜下与肉眼血尿检查:** \>35岁成人均需膀胱镜；肉眼血尿恶性肿瘤检出率更高，需更紧急评估

- **Mnemonic for bladder cancer presentation:** "Painless, Persistent, and Profuse" — the 3 P's that should trigger immediate cystoscopy regardless of other findings\
  **膀胱癌表现记忆法:** "无痛（Painless）、持续（Persistent）、大量（Profuse）"——这3个P应立即触发膀胱镜检查，无论其他检查结果如何

# Question 111 — Hypertensive Retinopathy / 高血压性视网膜病变

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>3-week history of headaches</strong> that have been <strong>increasing in severity and frequency</strong>. He also has a <strong>2-week history of progressive blurred vision in both eyes</strong>. He has not had pain in the eyes. His last visit to a physician was 10 years ago because of pain in his fingers; at that visit, he was told he had <strong>high blood pressure</strong>. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 90/min, respirations are 12/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 200/110 mm Hg</strong>. Repeat blood pressure measurements are <strong>210/112 mm Hg</strong> and <strong>214/114 mm Hg</strong>. Findings on funduscopic examination are shown. Examination shows <strong>ulnar deviation of both hands</strong> and <strong>several swollen interphalangeal joints</strong>. His <strong>fasting serum glucose concentration is 160 mg/dL</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely underlying cause of this patient's symptoms?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely underlying cause of this patient's symptoms?</strong></p>
<p>A) Diabetes mellitus<br />
B) Glioblastoma multiforme<br />
C) Hypertension<br />
D) Idiopathic intracranial hypertension<br />
E) Rheumatoid arthritis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Blood pressure 200/110, 210/112, 214/114 mm Hg on repeated measurements<br />
多次测量血压 200/110、210/112、214/114 mmHg</td>
<td>Confirmed hypertensive crisis (BP &gt;180/120); repeated readings rule out artifact and establish true severity<br />
确诊高血压危象（BP&gt;180/120）；多次测量排除误差，确认真实严重程度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-week worsening headaches<br />
3周进行性加重头痛</td>
<td>CNS end-organ damage from hypertensive emergency; signals hypertensive encephalopathy<br />
高血压急症引起的中枢神经系统靶器官损害；提示高血压脑病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2-week progressive bilateral blurred vision, no eye pain<br />
2周双眼渐进性视物模糊，无眼痛</td>
<td>Bilateral painless vision loss → retinal/optic nerve pathology; absence of pain excludes acute angle-closure glaucoma<br />
双眼无痛性视力下降→视网膜/视神经病变；无眼痛排除急性闭角型青光眼</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>High blood pressure diagnosed 10 years ago, no follow-up since<br />
10年前确诊高血压，此后未就医</td>
<td>Decades of untreated hypertension → cumulative arteriolar damage now presenting as hypertensive emergency<br />
数十年未治疗高血压→累积性小动脉损害，现进入高血压急症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Funduscopic findings shown (implied: linear hemorrhages, macular star, disc edema)<br />
眼底镜所见（暗示：线状出血、黄斑星芒、视盘水肿）</td>
<td>Characteristic pattern of hypertensive retinopathy; linear hemorrhages distinguish this from diabetic retinopathy (round)<br />
高血压视网膜病变特征性表现；线状出血区别于糖尿病视网膜病变（圆形出血）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ulnar deviation + swollen interphalangeal joints<br />
尺偏+指间关节肿胀</td>
<td>Suggests rheumatoid arthritis — classic distractor; RA causes anterior segment eye disease, not hypertensive retinopathy<br />
提示类风湿关节炎——经典干扰项；RA累及眼前节，不引起高血压视网膜病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fasting glucose 160 mg/dL<br />
空腹血糖 160 mg/dL</td>
<td>Mildly elevated — possible DM, but diabetic retinopathy shows round/blot hemorrhages without macular star or disc edema<br />
轻度升高——可能有糖尿病，但糖尿病视网膜病变表现为圆形/斑点状出血，无黄斑星芒或视盘水肿</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Chronic uncontrolled hypertension** inflicts progressive **pressure-induced microvasculopathy** on retinal arterioles, producing a cascade of **ischemia**, **hemorrhage**, and **exudate** deposition:

**长期未控制的高血压**通过持续的**压力性微血管病变**损害视网膜小动脉，引发**缺血**、**出血**和**渗出**沉积的级联反应：

- Sustained elevated BP → arteriolar wall hyalinization → lumen narrowing → retinal ischemia and cotton-wool spots (NFL infarcts)\
  持续高血压→小动脉壁玻璃样变→管腔狭窄→视网膜缺血和棉絮斑（神经纤维层梗死）

- Arteriolar rupture within the **nerve fiber layer (inner retina)** → hemorrhages adopt the linear/flame shape of axonal architecture\
  **神经纤维层（内层视网膜）**内小动脉破裂→出血沿轴突走向呈线状/火焰形

- Plasma protein and lipid leakage → **hard exudates** radially deposited along Henle's fiber layer around the fovea → **macular star** sign\
  血浆蛋白和脂质渗漏→**硬性渗出**沿中心凹周围的Henle纤维层放射状沉积→**黄斑星芒**征

- Severe hypertension → axonal swelling of the optic nerve → **bilateral optic disc edema** that can mimic papilledema from raised ICP\
  严重高血压→视神经轴突水肿→**双侧视盘水肿**，可模拟颅内压升高引起的视乳头水肿

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Hemorrhages in the inner retina (NFL) take the linear/flame shape of nerve fiber axons; hemorrhages in the outer retina (diabetic pericyte loss) are round/blot — the anatomical layer determines the shape.

**解剖小窍门:** 内层视网膜（神经纤维层）出血沿神经纤维轴突走向呈线状/火焰形；外层视网膜出血（糖尿病周细胞丧失）呈圆形/斑点状——所在解剖层次决定出血形态。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Hypertension / 正确答案 (C) — 高血压

**Hypertensive retinopathy** is the definitive ocular manifestation of end-organ damage from a hypertensive crisis, producing a constellation of funduscopic findings:

**高血压视网膜病变**是高血压危象引起靶器官损害的确切眼部表现，产生一系列特征性眼底改变：

- Linear (flame-shaped) retinal hemorrhages in the nerve fiber layer (inner retina)\
  神经纤维层（内层视网膜）线状（火焰形）视网膜出血

- Hard exudates distributed in a macular star configuration around the fovea\
  硬性渗出围绕中心凹呈黄斑星芒状分布

- Cotton-wool spots (retinal nerve fiber layer infarctions)\
  棉絮斑（视网膜神经纤维层梗死）

- Bilateral optic disc edema mimicking papilledema\
  双侧视盘水肿，模拟视乳头水肿

- Arteriolar narrowing and arteriovenous (AV) nicking\
  小动脉狭窄及动静脉交叉征

**Diagnosis:** This patient has hypertensive emergency — BP consistently \>200/110 mm Hg on repeated measurements with confirmed end-organ damage (CNS: headaches; eye: retinopathy). The funduscopic triad of linear hemorrhages, macular star exudates, and disc edema is pathognomonic of Grade IV (malignant) hypertensive retinopathy.

**诊断:** 该患者符合高血压急症——多次测量BP持续\>200/110 mmHg，并有确认的靶器官损害（中枢神经系统：头痛；眼：视网膜病变）。线状出血、黄斑星芒渗出和视盘水肿三联征是IV级（恶性）高血压视网膜病变的特征性表现。

**Treatment:** Emergent IV antihypertensive therapy (IV labetalol, nicardipine, or clevidipine); target ≤25% reduction in mean arterial pressure within the first hour, then gradual reduction to 160/100 mm Hg over 2–6 hours to prevent cerebral ischemia from rapid normalization.

**治疗:** 急诊静脉降压治疗（IV拉贝洛尔、尼卡地平或克利维地平）；目标为第1小时内平均动脉压降幅≤25%，2–6小时内再逐渐降至160/100 mmHg，避免快速正常化引起脑缺血。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Diabetes mellitus<br />
A — 糖尿病</td>
<td>Diabetic retinopathy causes round/blot hemorrhages (outer retina) and scattered hard exudates — not linear flame-shaped hemorrhages or macular star; glucose 160 alone does not explain this funduscopic picture<br />
糖尿病视网膜病变引起圆形/斑点状出血（外层视网膜）和散在硬性渗出——不引起线状火焰形出血或黄斑星芒；仅血糖160无法解释此眼底图像</td>
<td>Round vs. linear hemorrhages; macular star and disc edema absent in diabetic retinopathy<br />
圆形vs.线状出血；糖尿病视网膜病变无黄斑星芒和视盘水肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Glioblastoma multiforme<br />
B — 胶质母细胞瘤</td>
<td>GBM causes papilledema from raised ICP but does NOT produce retinal hemorrhages, hard exudates, or macular star; GBM presents with focal neuro deficits and/or seizures, which this patient lacks<br />
GBM引起颅内压升高性视乳头水肿，但不产生视网膜出血、硬性渗出或黄斑星芒；GBM表现为局灶性神经缺损和/或癫痫，该患者无此表现</td>
<td>Retinal hemorrhages + hard exudates + macular star are absent in GBM-related papilledema<br />
GBM相关视乳头水肿无视网膜出血+硬性渗出+黄斑星芒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hypertension ✓<br />
C — 高血压 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Severely elevated BP (200–214/110–114 mm Hg) with linear retinal hemorrhages, macular star hard exudates, and bilateral optic disc edema equals classic Grade IV hypertensive retinopathy<br />
正确——严重血压升高（200–214/110–114 mmHg）伴线状视网膜出血、黄斑星芒硬性渗出及双侧视盘水肿=经典IV级高血压视网膜病变</td>
<td>Triad of linear hemorrhages + macular star + disc edema in the setting of hypertensive crisis<br />
高血压危象背景下线状出血+黄斑星芒+视盘水肿三联征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Idiopathic intracranial hypertension<br />
D — 特发性颅内高压</td>
<td>IIH produces papilledema only — no retinal hemorrhages, hard exudates, or macular star; IIH classically affects obese women of childbearing age with normal BP, not a 57-year-old man with BP &gt;200<br />
IIH仅产生视乳头水肿——无视网膜出血、硬性渗出或黄斑星芒；IIH典型发生于血压正常的育龄期肥胖女性，而非BP&gt;200的57岁男性</td>
<td>IIH lacks retinal hemorrhages and hard exudates; demographics do not fit<br />
IIH无视网膜出血和硬性渗出；人口学特征不符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Rheumatoid arthritis<br />
E — 类风湿关节炎</td>
<td>RA causes anterior segment eye disease (dry eye, episcleritis, scleritis, sterile corneal ulceration) — it does not affect the retina; ulnar deviation and swollen joints here are a deliberate distractor<br />
RA引起眼前节病变（干眼、巩膜外层炎、巩膜炎、无菌性角膜溃疡）——不累及视网膜；此处尺偏和关节肿胀为刻意设置的干扰项</td>
<td>RA = anterior segment; retinal findings are never an RA manifestation<br />
RA=眼前节；视网膜改变绝不是RA的表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice A (Diabetes mellitus) because the mildly elevated fasting glucose of 160 mg/dL implies possible DM — the critical differentiator is hemorrhage morphology: linear/flame-shaped in hypertensive retinopathy (inner retina) versus round/blot in diabetic retinopathy (outer retina), plus the pathognomonic macular star pattern.*

最危险的干扰项是选项A（糖尿病）——空腹血糖160 mg/dL轻度升高暗示可能存在DM。关键鉴别点在于出血形态：高血压视网膜病变为线状/火焰形（内层视网膜），糖尿病视网膜病变为圆形/斑点状（外层视网膜），加之高血压特有的黄斑星芒图案。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Hypertensive vs. Diabetic Retinopathy / 高血压性 vs. 糖尿病性视网膜病变

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Hypertensive Retinopathy</strong><br />
<strong>高血压视网膜病变</strong></th>
<th><strong>Diabetic Retinopathy</strong><br />
<strong>糖尿病视网膜病变</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Hemorrhage morphology<br />
出血形态</td>
<td>Linear / flame-shaped (nerve fiber layer, inner retina)<br />
线状/火焰形（神经纤维层，内层视网膜）</td>
<td>Round / blot-shaped (outer retinal layers)<br />
圆形/斑点状（外层视网膜）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hard exudate pattern<br />
硬性渗出形态</td>
<td>Macular star (radial around fovea along Henle's layer)<br />
黄斑星芒（沿Henle纤维层围绕中心凹放射状）</td>
<td>Scattered, no star pattern<br />
散在分布，无星芒状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Optic disc<br />
视盘改变</td>
<td>Disc edema (Grade IV = malignant HTN); mimics papilledema<br />
视盘水肿（IV级=恶性高血压）；模拟视乳头水肿</td>
<td>Neovascularization on disc (NVD) in proliferative stage<br />
增殖期视盘新生血管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Microaneurysms<br />
微动脉瘤</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Present (hallmark of early diabetic retinopathy)<br />
有（早期糖尿病视网膜病变标志）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Arteriolar changes<br />
小动脉改变</td>
<td>Narrowing, copper/silver wiring, AV nicking<br />
狭窄、铜丝/银丝征、动静脉交叉征</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key pathophysiology<br />
关键病理生理</td>
<td>Pressure-induced arteriolar rupture and ischemia<br />
压力性小动脉破裂和缺血</td>
<td>Hyperglycemia → pericyte loss → VEGF↑ → neovascularization<br />
高血糖→周细胞丧失→VEGF↑→新生血管</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with severely elevated blood pressure presenting with bilateral painless vision loss and the funduscopic triad of linear hemorrhages, macular star exudates, and optic disc edema has hypertensive retinopathy requiring emergent intravenous blood pressure reduction.**

**严重血压升高患者出现双眼无痛性视力下降，眼底镜见线状出血、黄斑星芒渗出和视盘水肿三联征，诊断为高血压视网膜病变，需急诊静脉降压治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — FLAMES of Malignant Hypertension / 记忆钩 — "FLAMES" 恶性高血压眼底六征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>F</strong>lame-shaped hemorrhages — linear, in the nerve fiber layer (inner retina) / 火焰形出血——线状，位于神经纤维层（内层视网膜）<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ipid hard exudates forming a macular star around the fovea / 脂质硬性渗出围绕中心凹形成黄斑星芒<br />
• <strong>A</strong>rteriolar narrowing with AV nicking / 小动脉狭窄伴动静脉交叉征<br />
• <strong>M</strong>imics papilledema — optic disc edema from axonal swelling / 模拟视乳头水肿——轴突水肿致视盘水肿<br />
• <strong>E</strong>mergent BP reduction required (≤25% MAP drop in first hour) / 需急诊降压（第1小时MAP降幅≤25%）<br />
• <strong>S</strong>evere headache + vision loss = hypertensive emergency with end-organ damage / 严重头痛+视力丧失=高血压急症伴靶器官损害</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hypertensive Emergency & Retinopathy / 高频知识表 — 高血压急症与视网膜病变

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Hypertensive emergency vs. urgency<br />
高血压急症 vs. 亚急症</td>
<td>Emergency: BP &gt;180/120 WITH end-organ damage → emergent IV therapy; Urgency: BP &gt;180/120 WITHOUT end-organ damage → oral therapy, close follow-up<br />
急症：BP&gt;180/120伴靶器官损害→急诊静脉治疗；亚急症：BP&gt;180/120无靶器官损害→口服药物，密切随访</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>End-organ damage targets<br />
靶器官损害部位</td>
<td>Brain (hypertensive encephalopathy, ischemic/hemorrhagic stroke), heart (ACS, acute HF with pulmonary edema), kidneys (acute hypertensive nephropathy), eyes (hypertensive retinopathy), aorta (dissection)<br />
脑（高血压脑病、缺血性/出血性卒中）、心（ACS、急性心衰伴肺水肿）、肾（急性高血压肾病）、眼（高血压视网膜病变）、主动脉（夹层）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Keith-Wagener-Barker grading<br />
Keith-Wagener-Barker分级</td>
<td>Grade I: arteriolar narrowing only; Grade II: AV nicking; Grade III: hemorrhages + hard exudates + cotton-wool spots; Grade IV: Grade III + optic disc edema (= malignant hypertension)<br />
Ⅰ级：仅小动脉狭窄；Ⅱ级：动静脉交叉征；Ⅲ级：出血+硬性渗出+棉絮斑；Ⅳ级：Ⅲ级+视盘水肿（=恶性高血压）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment BP reduction targets<br />
降压治疗目标</td>
<td>First hour: reduce MAP by ≤25%; next 2–6 hours: 160/100 mm Hg; next 24–48 hours: gradual normalization; avoid rapid drop to prevent watershed ischemia<br />
第1小时：MAP降幅≤25%；2–6小时：160/100 mmHg；24–48小时：逐步正常化；避免快速下降防止分水岭区缺血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred IV agents by scenario<br />
不同场景首选静脉药物</td>
<td>Most hypertensive emergencies: IV labetalol or nicardipine; Aortic dissection: IV esmolol + nitroprusside (HR + BP control); Avoid nitroprusside long-term (cyanide toxicity)<br />
多数高血压急症：IV拉贝洛尔或尼卡地平；主动脉夹层：IV艾司洛尔+硝普钠（控制心率+血压）；避免长期使用硝普钠（氰化物毒性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Macular star mechanism<br />
黄斑星芒形成机制</td>
<td>Hard exudates (lipid-laden macrophages) deposit along Henle's fiber layer — nerve fibers radiating from the fovea — producing the star appearance visible on funduscopy<br />
硬性渗出（含脂质巨噬细胞）沿Henle纤维层——从中心凹向外放射的神经纤维——沉积，形成眼底镜可见的星芒外观</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>IIH vs. hypertensive disc edema differentiation<br />
特发性颅内高压 vs. 高血压性视盘水肿的鉴别</td>
<td>IIH: obese young women, normal BP, no retinal hemorrhages or hard exudates, visual field defect (enlarged blind spot); Hypertensive: elderly, high BP, retinal hemorrhages + hard exudates + macular star<br />
IIH：肥胖年轻女性，血压正常，无视网膜出血或硬性渗出，视野缺损（生理盲点扩大）；高血压性：老年患者，血压高，视网膜出血+硬性渗出+黄斑星芒</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of bilateral disc edema:** Hypertensive retinopathy (linear hemorrhages + high BP), IIH (obese young woman + normal BP), GBM/space-occupying lesion (focal neuro deficits + mass on MRI), malignant HTN — always check BP first\
  **双侧视盘水肿鉴别:** 高血压视网膜病变（线状出血+高血压）、IIH（肥胖年轻女性+血压正常）、GBM/占位性病变（局灶神经缺损+MRI占位）、恶性高血压——始终先测血压

- **NSAIDs + RA + hypertension interaction:** NSAIDs (used chronically for RA) promote sodium retention and blunt antihypertensive efficacy — a likely contributor to this patient's uncontrolled hypertension\
  **NSAIDs+RA+高血压相互作用:** NSAIDs（RA长期用药）促进钠潴留并削弱降压药疗效——可能是该患者高血压失控的促成因素

- **Coexisting DM + HTN retinopathy:** When both conditions are present, the funduscopic picture is mixed; the severity of BP elevation and presence of macular star + disc edema point predominantly to hypertensive etiology over diabetic\
  **DM+HTN视网膜病变并存:** 两种情况同时存在时眼底图像为混合表现；血压升高的严重程度及黄斑星芒+视盘水肿的存在更指向高血压病因为主

- **Prognosis of malignant hypertension:** Without treatment, 1-year mortality approaches 90%; with emergent BP control, prognosis dramatically improves — highlighting why this is a true medical emergency\
  **恶性高血压预后:** 不治疗1年死亡率接近90%；急诊降压后预后显著改善——这正是其被视为真正内科急症的原因

# Question 112 — Differential Recall Bias in Case-Control Study / 病例对照研究中的差异性回忆偏倚

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>case-control study</strong> is conducted to assess the effect of <strong>dietary fat intake</strong> on the occurrence of <strong>sudden cardiac death</strong>. <strong>One hundred fifty cases and controls</strong> are matched by age, sex assigned at birth, race, and history of hypertension, hypercholesterolemia, and cigarette smoking. <strong>Dietary intake history of the cases is obtained from the next of kin.</strong> Results show an <strong>odds ratio of 1.6</strong> with a <strong>95% confidence interval of 1.2 to 1.9</strong>. The authors conclude that there is a relationship between dietary fat intake and sudden cardiac death. Which of the following raises the most concern about the authors' conclusion?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following raises the most concern about the authors' conclusion?</strong></p>
<p>A) Differential bias in assessing dietary fat<br />
B) Inadequate sample size<br />
C) Lack of blinding<br />
D) Misclassification of cases and controls<br />
E) Weak statistical association</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Case-control study design<br />
病例对照研究设计</td>
<td>Retrospective by nature; exposure assessed after outcome is known — creates structural risk for recall bias<br />
天然回顾性；结局已知后才评估暴露史——产生回忆偏倚的结构性风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dietary history obtained from next of kin (cases only)<br />
病例的饮食史来自家属（仅病例组）</td>
<td>Proxy informants report on behalf of deceased cases; controls have no equivalent emotional motivation, creating asymmetric reporting<br />
代理报告者代替已故病例回答；对照组无相同情绪动机，造成不对称报告</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Matched controls<br />
匹配对照组</td>
<td>Confounders (age, sex, hypertension, smoking) are controlled; residual concern is information bias, not confounding<br />
混杂因素已控制；剩余问题是信息偏倚，而非混杂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OR = 1.6, 95% CI = 1.2 to 1.9<br />
OR = 1.6，95% CI 1.2 到 1.9</td>
<td>CI does not cross 1.0 → statistically significant; but inflation by differential bias may render this spurious<br />
CI 不含 1.0 → 具统计学意义；但差异性偏倚可能使其成为虚假关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>150 matched case-control pairs<br />
150 对匹配病例-对照</td>
<td>Adequate sample size for detecting a moderate association; inadequate sample size is not the concern here<br />
足以检测中等强度关联；样本量不足并非本题核心问题</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Differential recall bias** arises when the **direction or magnitude of exposure misclassification** differs systematically between cases and controls:

**差异性回忆偏倚**产生于病例组与对照组之间，暴露**错分的方向或程度**存在系统性差异：

- Next of kin of sudden cardiac death cases may unconsciously over-report high-fat dietary habits, seeking a causal explanation for the tragic death\
  猝死病例的家属可能无意识地高估高脂饮食习惯，试图为死亡寻找因果解释

- Controls' next of kin (or controls themselves) have no comparable emotional motivation to over-report fat intake\
  对照组家属（或对照本人）没有同等的情绪动机去高报脂肪摄入

- This asymmetric misclassification inflates the apparent OR away from the null\
  这种不对称错分使表观 OR 偏离零假设（即虚高）

- The result: a reported OR of 1.6 may overestimate the true association or even represent a spurious one\
  结果：报告的 OR 1.6 可能高估真实关联，甚至可能是完全虚假的关联

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In any case-control study using proxy reporters for cases but not controls, assume differential recall bias is operating until proven otherwise.

**流行病学小窍门:** 在病例对照研究中，若仅病例组使用代理报告者而对照组不用，默认存在差异性回忆偏倚，除非另有证明。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Differential Recall Bias / 正确答案 (A) — 差异性回忆偏倚

**Differential bias** occurs when exposure misclassification is unequal between cases and controls, systematically distorting the OR:

**差异性偏倚**指暴露错分在病例与对照之间不均等，系统性地扭曲 OR：

- Cases' dietary history is recalled by next of kin who have strong motivation (grief, guilt, need for explanation) to associate fat intake with death\
  病例饮食史由家属回忆，家属有强烈动机（悲痛、内疚、寻求解释）将高脂饮食与死亡关联

- Controls' exposure history is not subject to the same emotional reporting pressure\
  对照组暴露史不受同等的情绪性报告压力影响

- This directional imbalance can inflate the OR substantially beyond the true value\
  这种方向性不平衡可使 OR 大幅高于真实值

**Diagnosis:** The key finding is asymmetric information collection — cases via emotionally invested proxy (next of kin), controls via self-report or neutral proxy — creating a fertile ground for differential recall bias that can render the OR unreliable.

**诊断:** 核心发现是信息收集的不对称——病例通过情绪投入的代理（家属），对照通过自报或中性代理——形成差异性回忆偏倚的温床，可能使 OR 不可靠。

**Treatment:** To minimize: apply identical proxy informant strategy to both cases and controls; blind interviewers to case/control status; use standardized, structured questionnaires.

**治疗/对策:** 最小化方法：对病例和对照采用完全相同的代理报告策略；对访谈者盲化病例/对照身份；使用标准化、结构化问卷。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Differential bias in assessing dietary fat ✓<br />
A — 评估饮食脂肪的差异性偏倚 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — next of kin of cases are emotionally motivated to over-report fat intake, while controls' reporters lack this motivation, creating directional misclassification that inflates OR<br />
正确——病例家属有情绪动机高报脂肪摄入，而对照报告者缺乏此动机，造成方向性错分使 OR 虚高</td>
<td>Asymmetric proxy reporting between cases (deceased, next of kin) vs. controls<br />
病例（已故，家属代报）与对照之间不对称的代理报告方式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Inadequate sample size<br />
B — 样本量不足</td>
<td>The 95% CI (1.2–1.9) does not cross 1.0, indicating statistical significance; 150 matched pairs is adequate for detecting this effect size<br />
95% CI（1.2–1.9）不含 1.0，表明统计学显著；150 对匹配足以检测该效应量</td>
<td>CI entirely above 1.0 → adequate power demonstrated; sample size is not the limiting problem<br />
CI 完全高于 1.0 → 统计效能充足；样本量不是核心问题</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Lack of blinding<br />
C — 缺乏盲法</td>
<td>Blinding of interviewers is a valid general concern, but the stem does not specify whether blinding was absent; the more concrete and directly evidenced concern is differential recall from emotionally motivated proxy reporters<br />
访谈者盲法是合理的普遍顾虑，但题干未说明是否缺乏盲法；更具体且有直接证据支持的是情绪动机代理报告者的差异性回忆</td>
<td>Lack of blinding is a possibility but not directly implied; differential bias is explicitly set up by the study design as described<br />
缺乏盲法是可能性而非直接说明；差异性偏倚由题目描述的研究设计直接导出</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Misclassification of cases and controls<br />
D — 病例与对照的错分</td>
<td>Sudden cardiac death is an unambiguous, objectively verifiable outcome; outcome misclassification is not a meaningful concern here<br />
猝死是明确的、可客观核实的结局；结局错分在此不构成实质性顾虑</td>
<td>Case status (sudden cardiac death) is clear-cut; this option confuses outcome misclassification with exposure misclassification<br />
病例状态（猝死）明确；本选项混淆了结局错分与暴露错分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Weak statistical association<br />
E — 统计关联性弱</td>
<td>OR = 1.6 with 95% CI 1.2–1.9 is a moderate-to-strong, statistically significant association; the CI does not cross 1.0<br />
OR = 1.6，95% CI 1.2–1.9 是中等偏强、具统计学意义的关联；CI 不含 1.0</td>
<td>The concern is that the OR may be <em>artificially inflated</em> by bias, not that it is too weak; the problem is validity, not significance<br />
顾虑是 OR 可能被偏倚人为虚高，而非太弱；问题是效度，不是显著性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is C (lack of blinding), but the stem's explicit detail that cases' dietary history is obtained from next of kin directly and specifically implicates differential recall bias — a more targeted and consequential flaw than unspecified blinding concerns.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 C（缺乏盲法），但题干明确说明病例饮食史来自家属这一细节，直接且具体地指向差异性回忆偏倚——比未特指的盲法顾虑更有针对性、后果更严重。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Differential vs. Non-differential Bias / 差异性偏倚与非差异性偏倚对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Differential Bias</strong><br />
<strong>差异性偏倚</strong></th>
<th><strong>Non-differential Bias</strong><br />
<strong>非差异性偏倚</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition<br />
定义</td>
<td>Exposure misclassification differs in direction or magnitude between cases and controls<br />
暴露错分在病例与对照之间方向或程度不同</td>
<td>Exposure misclassification is equal in both groups<br />
两组暴露错分程度相同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Effect on OR<br />
对 OR 的影响</td>
<td>Can inflate or deflate OR away from null (either direction possible)<br />
可使 OR 向任一方向偏离零假设（虚高或虚低均可）</td>
<td>Biases OR toward the null — underestimates the true association<br />
使 OR 向零假设偏移——低估真实关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic example<br />
经典例子</td>
<td>Recall bias: bereaved families over-report fat intake for deceased cases<br />
回忆偏倚：丧亲家属对已故病例高报脂肪摄入</td>
<td>Random questionnaire error affecting both groups equally<br />
随机问卷误差对两组均等影响</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Danger to validity<br />
对效度的危害</td>
<td>More dangerous — can fabricate or reverse a true association<br />
更危险——可能伪造或逆转真实关联</td>
<td>Less dangerous — attenuates but does not fabricate association<br />
较少危险——削弱但不伪造关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common study setting<br />
常见研究场景</td>
<td>Retrospective case-control with proxy informants used only for cases<br />
仅病例组使用代理报告者的回顾性病例对照研究</td>
<td>Any study with random or symmetric exposure misclassification<br />
任何存在随机或对称暴露错分的研究</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In this case-control study, obtaining dietary history from emotionally invested next of kin only for cases (not controls) introduces differential recall bias, which can artificially inflate the OR and invalidate the authors' conclusion.**

**在本病例对照研究中，仅对病例组（而非对照组）使用情绪投入的家属提供饮食史，引入差异性回忆偏倚，可能人为虚高 OR 并使作者结论失效。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CASE Bias / 记忆钩 — CASE 偏倚记忆法:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ases' families — emotionally motivated to OVER-report fat intake / 病例家属——有情绪动机高报脂肪摄入<br />
• <strong>A</strong>symmetric — misclassification flows in one direction only (cases over-reported) / 不对称——错分仅朝一个方向（病例组高报）<br />
• <strong>S</strong>kews the OR — away from the null, inflating it beyond the true value / 扭曲 OR——偏离零假设，使其超出真实值<br />
• <strong>E</strong>rosion of validity — the entire conclusion may be spurious / 效度侵蚀——整个结论可能是虚假的</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Bias in Case-Control Studies / 高频知识表 — 病例对照研究中的偏倚

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Recall bias (information bias subtype)<br />
回忆偏倚（信息偏倚的亚型）</td>
<td>Cases more likely than controls to remember and report past exposures, especially when the exposure is culturally linked to the disease outcome<br />
病例比对照更可能记住并报告过去的暴露，尤其是文化上与疾病结局相关的暴露</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Differential vs. non-differential misclassification<br />
差异性与非差异性错分</td>
<td>Differential → OR can go either direction (dangerous). Non-differential → OR biased toward null (attenuates association, less dangerous)<br />
差异性→OR 可向任何方向偏移（危险）。非差异性→OR 偏向零假设（削弱关联，较少危险）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Proxy informant bias<br />
代理报告者偏倚</td>
<td>Using next of kin for cases but not controls is a textbook trigger for differential recall bias on USMLE; the asymmetry in reporter motivation is the mechanistic key<br />
仅为病例使用家属代报而对照不用，是 USMLE 上差异性回忆偏倚的经典触发条件；报告者动机的不对称是机制关键</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OR and CI interpretation<br />
OR 与 CI 的解读</td>
<td>OR = 1.6, CI 1.2–1.9: statistically significant (CI excludes 1.0); the concern is not whether it is significant but whether it reflects a true vs. biased association<br />
OR = 1.6，CI 1.2–1.9：统计显著（CI 不含 1.0）；关注点不在于是否显著，而在于是否反映真实而非偏倚的关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Matching and confounding control<br />
匹配与混杂控制</td>
<td>Matching eliminates confounding from matched variables but provides no protection against information bias (recall bias)<br />
匹配消除已匹配变量的混杂，但对信息偏倚（回忆偏倚）无保护作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blinding in case-control studies<br />
病例对照研究的盲法</td>
<td>Blinding interviewers to case/control status reduces interviewer bias; however, it cannot fully eliminate differential recall bias when proxy reporters themselves are emotionally motivated<br />
对访谈者盲化可减少访谈者偏倚；但当代理报告者本人有情绪动机时，无法完全消除差异性回忆偏倚</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Interviewer bias:** Even with standardized questionnaires, interviewers aware of a subject's case status may unconsciously probe more deeply for fat exposure in cases, compounding the differential bias already introduced by proxy reporters\
  **访谈者偏倚:** 即使使用标准化问卷，知晓受试者为病例的访谈者可能无意识地更深入探查脂肪暴露，加剧代理报告者已引入的差异性偏倚

- **Rumination effect:** Bereaved family members of sudden cardiac death cases often spend time analyzing the deceased's lifestyle seeking explanation, systematically enhancing recall of dietary details — a direct biological mechanism of differential bias\
  **反刍效应:** 猝死病例的丧亲家属常花时间分析逝者生活方式寻求解释，系统性地增强对饮食细节的记忆——差异性偏倚的直接机制

- **Design fix — symmetric proxy reporting:** Using deceased hospital controls (e.g., deaths from unrelated causes) whose next of kin are interviewed in the same manner as cases' next of kin would equalize reporting context and reduce differential bias\
  **研究设计修正——对称代理报告:** 使用死于无关原因的住院对照，其家属以与病例家属完全相同的方式接受访谈，可均衡报告情境并减少差异性偏倚

- **Protopathic bias distinction:** A related but different concept — early disease symptoms cause changes in exposure *before* diagnosis (e.g., someone reduces fat intake after prodromal cardiac symptoms), making cases appear to have lower exposure; distinct from recall bias and biases OR toward null\
  **原发病偏倚的区别:** 相关但不同的概念——早期疾病症状在诊断*前*导致暴露改变（如前驱心脏症状后减少脂肪摄入），使病例暴露看似更低；与回忆偏倚不同，且使 OR 偏向零假设

# Question 113 — Suspected Laryngeal Carcinoma / 疑似喉癌

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-month history of hoarseness</strong>. She has not had any other symptoms. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. She has <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 45 years</strong>. Examination, including <strong>examination of the oropharynx, shows no abnormalities</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Follow-up examination in 6 weeks<br />
B) X-rays of the maxillary sinuses<br />
C) CT scan of the chest<br />
D) Bronchodilator therapy<br />
E) Indirect laryngoscopy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Laryngeal carcinoma** most commonly arises as **squamous cell carcinoma** at the glottic level (vocal cords), where even a small tumor disrupts **vocal cord vibration** and produces early hoarseness:

**喉癌**最常见的病理类型是**鳞状细胞癌**，好发于声门区（声带），即便是很小的肿瘤也会干扰**声带振动**，从而在早期就引起声音嘶哑：

- Glottic tumor → vocal cord mass effect or infiltration → asymmetric vibration → hoarseness\
  声门肿瘤 → 声带占位效应或浸润 → 不对称振动 → 声音嘶哑

- Supraglottic tumors → silent early; later dysphagia and referred otalgia predominate\
  声门上肿瘤 → 早期无症状；后期以吞咽困难和放射性耳痛为主

- Subglottic tumors → present late with stridor or airway obstruction\
  声门下肿瘤 → 出现较晚，以喘鸣或气道阻塞为主

- Chronic tobacco smoke → mucosal carcinogen exposure → squamous dysplasia → carcinoma sequence\
  长期烟草烟雾 → 黏膜致癌物暴露 → 鳞状上皮异型增生 → 癌变序列

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Glottic = hoarseness early; Supraglottic = dysphagia early; Subglottic = airway obstruction late.

**解剖小窍门:** 声门区 = 早期声嘶；声门上区 = 早期吞咽困难；声门下区 = 晚期气道梗阻。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Indirect Laryngoscopy / 正确答案 (E) — 间接喉镜检查

**Indirect laryngoscopy** is the first-line diagnostic procedure for evaluating hoarseness in a high-risk patient because it allows direct visualization of the vocal cords and laryngeal structures:

**间接喉镜检查**是高危患者声音嘶哑评估的一线诊断步骤，因为它能够直接观察声带和喉部结构：

- Uses a mirror or flexible fiberoptic nasopharyngoscope to visualize the larynx in the office setting\
  在门诊使用喉镜或软式纤维鼻咽喉镜进行喉部可视化检查

- Identifies vocal cord lesions, masses, mucosal irregularity, and cord mobility\
  可识别声带病变、肿块、黏膜不规则及声带活动性

- Direct visualization establishes the diagnosis before imaging or staging workup\
  直视下确诊先于影像学或分期检查——这是诊断的第一步

**Diagnosis:** Primary tumor must be visualized first; biopsy under direct or endoscopic guidance confirms squamous cell carcinoma. CT chest and PET are used for staging after tissue diagnosis.

**诊断:** 必须首先对原发肿瘤进行可视化检查；在直视或内镜引导下活检确认鳞状细胞癌。组织学确诊后再行 CT 胸部和 PET 分期。

**Treatment:** Stage-dependent — early glottic carcinoma: radiation therapy or endoscopic laser resection with curative intent; advanced disease: laryngectomy ± chemoradiation.

**治疗:** 依分期而定——早期声门癌：放射治疗或内镜激光切除，目标治愈；晚期病变：喉切除术 ± 化放疗。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Follow-up examination in 6 weeks<br />
A — 6 周后随访复诊</td>
<td>Dangerous delay — hoarseness &gt; 2 weeks in a 45 pack-year smoker demands immediate laryngeal evaluation, not watchful waiting<br />
危险的延误——45包年吸烟史患者声嘶超过2周需立即进行喉部评估，而非观察等待</td>
<td>Duration &gt; 2–3 weeks + smoking history = urgent visualization, not reassurance<br />
持续时间 &gt; 2–3 周 + 吸烟史 = 紧急可视化检查，而非安慰观察</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — X-rays of the maxillary sinuses<br />
B — 上颌窦 X 线检查</td>
<td>Maxillary sinus imaging evaluates sinusitis; this patient lacks sinus symptoms (headache, facial pain, postnasal drip, halitosis)<br />
上颌窦影像用于评估鼻窦炎；该患者无鼻窦炎症状（头痛、面痛、鼻后滴漏、口臭）</td>
<td>Hoarseness ≠ sinusitis; site of pathology is the larynx, not sinuses<br />
声音嘶哑 ≠ 鼻窦炎；病变部位是喉部而非鼻窦</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — CT scan of the chest<br />
C — 胸部 CT 扫描</td>
<td>CT chest is a staging tool used after the primary tumor is identified; performing it before laryngoscopy skips the diagnostic sequence<br />
胸部CT是原发肿瘤确认后的分期工具；在喉镜检查之前进行跳过了诊断步骤顺序</td>
<td>Identify primary tumor first → stage later; imaging before tissue ID inverts the workup<br />
先识别原发肿瘤 → 再分期；在组织确认前进行影像学检查颠倒了诊断流程</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Bronchodilator therapy<br />
D — 支气管扩张剂治疗</td>
<td>Bronchodilators treat obstructive airway disease (COPD/asthma), which presents with wheezing and dyspnea — not hoarseness<br />
支气管扩张剂治疗阻塞性气道疾病（COPD/哮喘），其表现为喘鸣和呼吸困难——而非声音嘶哑</td>
<td>Hoarseness = laryngeal pathology, not lower airway disease; empiric bronchodilators without diagnosis is incorrect<br />
声嘶 = 喉部病变，而非下气道疾病；未诊断就经验性使用支气管扩张剂是错误的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Indirect laryngoscopy ✓<br />
E — 间接喉镜检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — provides direct visualization of the larynx and vocal cords; mandatory first step in evaluating hoarseness in a high-risk smoker<br />
正确——提供喉部和声带的直视下可视化；高危吸烟者声嘶评估的必要第一步</td>
<td>Visualize before stage; this is the only option that addresses the actual anatomical site of suspected pathology<br />
先可视化再分期；这是唯一针对疑似病变实际解剖部位的选项</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (CT chest) — it seems logical given the smoking history, but CT is a staging tool that comes after, not before, laryngoscopic identification of the primary tumor.*

CT 胸部扫描（C 选项）是最易混淆的干扰项——考虑到吸烟史似乎合理，但 CT 是分期工具，应在喉镜识别原发肿瘤之后而非之前进行。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a smoker with hoarseness lasting more than 2–3 weeks, indirect laryngoscopy is the mandatory first step to visualize the larynx and rule out glottic carcinoma before any imaging or empiric therapy.**

**在吸烟者中声音嘶哑超过 2–3 周时，间接喉镜是必须的第一步，在任何影像学检查或经验性治疗之前先对喉部进行可视化检查以排除声门癌。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — HOARSE Rule for Smoker's Hoarseness / 记忆钩 — 吸烟者声嘶的 HOARSE 法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>oarseness &gt; 2 weeks → must scope — Cancer until proven otherwise / 声嘶 &gt; 2 周→必须喉镜——排除癌前提下方可考虑良性<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ropharynx normal? → go lower with laryngoscopy — the lesion hides below / 口咽正常？→ 用喉镜往下看——病变藏在更深处<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ge + smoking = high pretest probability for squamous cell carcinoma / 年龄 + 吸烟 = 鳞状细胞癌高验前概率<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ule: Visualize first, Stage second — CT chest comes after tissue ID / 规则：先可视化，再分期——胸部CT在组织确认之后<br />
• <strong>S</strong>upraglottic = dysphagia early; Glottic = hoarseness early (this case!) / 声门上 = 早期吞咽困难；声门区 = 早期声嘶（本题！）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Laryngeal Carcinoma Workup and Management / 高频知识表 — 喉癌诊疗流程

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Tobacco smoking (#1), alcohol (synergistic with tobacco), HPV (especially supraglottic), chronic GERD<br />
吸烟（第一位）、酒精（与烟草协同）、HPV（尤其声门上型）、慢性胃食管反流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic sequence<br />
诊断步骤顺序</td>
<td>Step 1: Indirect/flexible laryngoscopy → visualize primary tumor; Step 2: Biopsy → histologic confirmation; Step 3: CT/PET → staging<br />
第1步：间接/软式喉镜→可视化原发肿瘤；第2步：活检→组织学确认；第3步：CT/PET→分期</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Histology<br />
组织学</td>
<td>&gt; 95% squamous cell carcinoma; glottic most common site; well-differentiated tumors more common at glottis<br />
&gt; 95% 鳞状细胞癌；声门区最常见；声门区肿瘤分化程度较高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Staging key points<br />
分期要点</td>
<td>T1/T2 (limited to larynx, mobile cords) → good prognosis; T3 (cord fixation) / T4 (extralaryngeal spread) → poor prognosis; N+ = nodal metastasis<br />
T1/T2（局限于喉部，声带活动）→预后良好；T3（声带固定）/T4（喉外扩散）→预后差；N+ = 淋巴结转移</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment by stage<br />
分期治疗</td>
<td>Early (T1–T2): Radiation alone or transoral laser microsurgery (organ-preserving); Advanced: Total laryngectomy ± concurrent chemoradiation<br />
早期（T1–T2）：单纯放疗或经口激光显微手术（保留器官）；晚期：全喉切除术 ± 同步化放疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognosis<br />
预后</td>
<td>Glottic T1 5-year survival ~90%; supraglottic with nodal disease ~50%; distant metastasis ~30%<br />
声门T1五年生存率约90%；声门上型伴淋巴结转移约50%；远处转移约30%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why hoarseness is an early sign<br />
声嘶为何是早期症状</td>
<td>Glottic mucosa has sparse lymphatics → early local disease without nodal spread; vocal cord mass causes early vibratory disruption<br />
声门黏膜淋巴管稀少→早期局部病变无淋巴结扩散；声带肿块早期即破坏声带振动</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of chronic hoarseness:** Laryngeal carcinoma, vocal cord polyp/nodule, laryngopharyngeal reflux, recurrent laryngeal nerve palsy (think mediastinal mass, aortic aneurysm, thyroid cancer), functional dysphonia\
  **声嘶鉴别诊断:** 喉癌、声带息肉/结节、喉咽反流、喉返神经麻痹（考虑纵隔肿块、主动脉瘤、甲状腺癌）、功能性发音障碍

- **Recurrent laryngeal nerve palsy:** Unilateral RLN palsy causes hoarseness + breathy voice; always image the entire RLN course (neck + chest) to find the compressive cause before attributing to idiopathic\
  **喉返神经麻痹:** 单侧喉返神经麻痹引起声嘶+气息声；在归因于特发性之前，始终对整个喉返神经走行（颈部+胸部）进行影像学检查以寻找压迫性原因

- **Key complication of laryngectomy:** Total laryngectomy results in permanent tracheostomy and loss of natural voice; patients learn tracheoesophageal speech, esophageal speech, or use electrolarynx\
  **喉切除术的关键并发症:** 全喉切除术导致永久性气管造口术和自然发声丧失；患者学习气管食管语音、食管语音或使用电子喉

- **Variant — Leukoplakia:** White mucosal plaques on vocal cords in smokers represent precancerous lesions (dysplasia); require biopsy and close follow-up; transformation to invasive SCC occurs in ~5–15%\
  **题目变式——白斑症:** 吸烟者声带上的白色黏膜斑块代表癌前病变（异型增生）；需要活检和密切随访；向浸润性鳞癌转化率约5–15%

# Question 114 — Advance Directive with Reversible Acute Respiratory Failure / 预立医嘱与急性可逆性呼吸衰竭

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> is admitted to the hospital because of <strong>fever</strong>, <strong>shortness of breath</strong>, and <strong>cough productive of yellow sputum</strong>. He has prostate cancer metastatic to the bone; his only symptom from the cancer is occasional back pain well controlled with oral acetaminophen and hydrocodone. At his last appointment 6 months ago, his serum prostate-specific antigen assay was stable, and his disease had not progressed. He plays golf several times each week and enjoys traveling with his wife. His advance directive states that he does not want intubation or mechanical ventilation <strong>unless he has an acute illness with a reasonable chance of recovery to a good quality of life</strong>. He is <strong>lethargic and unable to communicate</strong>. His temperature is <strong>38.9°C (102°F)</strong>, pulse is 100/min, respirations are <strong>30/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 148/92 mm Hg. Pulmonary examination shows shallow, rapid breathing. He is <strong>using accessory muscles of respiration</strong>. Inspiratory crackles are heard at the right upper and lower lung fields. Arterial blood gas analysis on 100% oxygen shows: pH 7.36, PCO2 45 mm Hg, <strong>PO2 42 mm Hg</strong>. An x-ray of the chest shows diffuse right-sided infiltrates. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Consult the hospital ethics committee<br />
B) Begin noninvasive positive pressure ventilation by face mask<br />
C) Continue oxygen by face mask and administer intravenous morphine for comfort<br />
D) Intubate and begin mechanical ventilation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>PO2 42 mmHg on 100% O2<br />
100%氧气下PO2 42 mmHg</td>
<td>Severe refractory hypoxemia unresponsive to supplemental oxygen; immediate airway intervention required<br />
严重难治性低氧血症，补充给氧无效，须立即干预气道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RR 30/min + accessory muscles<br />
呼吸频率30次/分 + 辅助呼吸肌参与</td>
<td>Markedly increased work of breathing indicating impending respiratory failure<br />
呼吸做功明显增加，提示即将发生呼吸衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Advance directive: no intubation UNLESS acute illness with reasonable chance of recovery<br />
预立医嘱：除非急性病且有合理恢复可能，否则不插管</td>
<td>Conditional directive, not absolute — explicitly permits intubation when recovery is likely<br />
有条件医嘱，并非绝对——明确允许在有恢复可能时进行插管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prostate cancer stable; plays golf, travels<br />
前列腺癌病情稳定；仍打高尔夫、旅行</td>
<td>Good baseline quality of life → recovery to good QoL is achievable if acute event is treated<br />
基线生活质量良好，提示治疗急性事件后可恢复良好生活质量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lethargic and unable to communicate<br />
嗜睡、无法沟通</td>
<td>Cannot update wishes verbally; physician must act on existing directive<br />
无法口头更新意愿，医生须依据现有预立医嘱做紧急决定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever + yellow sputum + right-sided infiltrates<br />
发热 + 脓性黄痰 + 右侧浸润影</td>
<td>Bacterial pneumonia — an acute, treatable, potentially reversible condition<br />
细菌性肺炎——急性、可治疗、潜在可逆的疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PCO2 45 mmHg (near normal) despite maximal effort<br />
极度费力下PCO2 45 mmHg（接近正常）</td>
<td>Normal CO2 maintained only by exhausting respiratory muscles; impending fatigue and respiratory arrest<br />
仅靠耗尽呼吸肌才维持正常CO2，提示即将因疲劳发生呼吸骤停</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

This patient develops **severe hypoxic respiratory failure** from **bacterial pneumonia** superimposed on a background of stable, well-controlled metastatic prostate cancer — a classic setup for testing advance directive interpretation:

本患者在病情稳定的转移性前列腺癌基础上，因**细菌性肺炎**发生了**严重低氧性呼吸衰竭**——这是考查预立医嘱解读的经典情景：

- Pneumonia → alveolar consolidation → V/Q mismatch → refractory hypoxemia (PO2 42 on 100% O2)\
  肺炎→肺泡实变→通气/血流比例失调→难治性低氧血症（100%氧气下PO2仍为42）

- Increased work of breathing → progressive respiratory muscle fatigue → impending arrest\
  呼吸做功增加→呼吸肌进行性疲劳→即将发生呼吸骤停

- Altered mental status from hypoxia → inability to protect airway → aspiration risk\
  低氧导致意识改变→无法保护气道→误吸风险

- Bacterial pneumonia with antibiotics = highly treatable; his cancer is stable and unrelated to this acute event\
  细菌性肺炎用抗生素可高效治疗；其癌症病情稳定，与此急性事件无关

**Advance directive interpretation rule:** "No intubation UNLESS acute illness with reasonable chance of recovery" is a conditional clause — intubation is not prohibited; it is permitted precisely when conditions are met.

**预立医嘱解读规则:** "除非急性病且有合理恢复可能，否则不插管"是有条件条款——并非禁止插管，而是在满足条件时明确允许插管。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Intubation Indicated Under Advance Directive Exception / 正确答案 (D) — 依据预立医嘱例外条款应行气管插管

**Intubation and mechanical ventilation** is correct because the clinical situation satisfies every element of the patient's own advance directive exception clause:

**气管插管和机械通气**是正确选择，因为临床情况满足患者本人预立医嘱例外条款的每个要素：

- This is an acute illness (bacterial pneumonia), entirely distinct from his underlying cancer\
  这是急性病（细菌性肺炎），与基础癌症完全无关

- The acute illness has a reasonable chance of recovery — bacterial pneumonia responds well to antibiotics\
  该急性病有合理恢复可能——细菌性肺炎对抗生素反应良好

- His baseline quality of life was excellent: independent, active, playing golf, traveling with his wife\
  基线生活质量优秀：独立生活、活跃、打高尔夫、与妻子旅行

- The hypoxic respiratory failure is immediately life-threatening, requiring urgent action without delay\
  低氧性呼吸衰竭即刻危及生命，须立即行动，不能延误

**Diagnosis:** Severe hypoxic respiratory failure secondary to right-sided bacterial pneumonia in a patient with stable metastatic prostate cancer and a conditional DNI advance directive

**诊断:** 病情稳定的转移性前列腺癌患者，继发于右侧细菌性肺炎的严重低氧性呼吸衰竭，伴有条件性DNI预立医嘱

**Treatment:** Immediate endotracheal intubation + mechanical ventilation + IV antibiotics (covering community-acquired vs. healthcare-associated pneumonia based on exposure history)

**治疗:** 立即气管插管+机械通气+静脉抗生素（依据暴露史覆盖社区获得性或医疗保健相关性肺炎）

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Consult the hospital ethics committee<br />
A — 会诊医院伦理委员会</td>
<td>Unnecessary — the advance directive is clear and explicitly addresses this scenario; delay risks cardiac arrest<br />
不必要——预立医嘱清楚明确，已涵盖该情景；延误有心脏骤停风险</td>
<td>Ethics committee is for unresolved conflicts or ambiguous directives, not for executing a clear conditional clause<br />
伦理委员会用于未解决冲突或不明确医嘱，而非执行明确的有条件条款</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Begin noninvasive positive pressure ventilation by face mask<br />
B — 无创正压通气面罩</td>
<td>NIPPV is contraindicated with altered mental status and inability to protect airway; insufficient for this severity<br />
无创通气在意识改变且无法保护气道时禁忌；对该严重程度不足够</td>
<td>NIPPV requires cooperative, awake patient with intact airway reflexes — altered sensorium is an absolute contraindication<br />
无创通气要求患者清醒配合且气道反射完整——感觉改变是绝对禁忌证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Continue O2 by face mask and IV morphine for comfort<br />
C — 继续面罩吸氧 + 静脉吗啡舒适治疗</td>
<td>Misinterpretation of advance directive — treats a reversible, treatable condition as if it were terminal<br />
误解预立医嘱——将可逆可治疗疾病视为终末期疾病对待</td>
<td>Comfort/palliative approach is for terminal irreversible decline, not for bacterial pneumonia in a previously functional patient<br />
舒适/姑息治疗适用于终末期不可逆衰退，不适用于既往功能良好患者的细菌性肺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Intubate and begin mechanical ventilation ✓<br />
D — 气管插管并开始机械通气 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — satisfies the advance directive exception: acute reversible illness with excellent baseline QoL<br />
正确——满足预立医嘱例外条款：急性可逆疾病，基线生活质量优秀</td>
<td>Directive permits intubation for "acute illness with a reasonable chance of recovery to a good quality of life" — all criteria met<br />
预立医嘱允许对"有合理可能恢复良好生活质量的急性病"插管——所有标准均满足</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is C — "comfort care" sounds compassionate given his cancer history, but the advance directive explicitly carves out an exception for exactly this scenario: a reversible acute illness in a patient with excellent baseline QoL.*

选项C是最危险的干扰项——"舒适治疗"在癌症背景下听起来富有人情味，但预立医嘱明确为此情景设立了例外：在基线生活质量优秀的患者中发生可逆急性疾病。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — When to Honor DNI vs. When Intubation Is Indicated / 何时遵守拒绝插管意愿 vs. 何时应行气管插管

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Honor DNI (Do Not Intubate)</strong><br />
<strong>遵守拒绝插管意愿</strong></th>
<th><strong>Proceed with Intubation</strong><br />
<strong>进行气管插管</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Underlying disease trajectory<br />
基础疾病轨迹</td>
<td>Terminal, irreversible, actively dying from the disease<br />
终末期、不可逆、正在因疾病死亡</td>
<td>Stable chronic disease; acute illness is superimposed and unrelated<br />
慢性病稳定；叠加无关的急性疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute event reversibility<br />
急性事件可逆性</td>
<td>No reasonable chance of recovery<br />
无合理恢复可能</td>
<td>Reasonable chance of recovery with treatment (e.g., pneumonia)<br />
治疗后有合理恢复可能（如肺炎）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Directive language<br />
医嘱措辞</td>
<td>Unconditional: "I do not want intubation under any circumstances"<br />
无条件："任何情况下均不插管"</td>
<td>Conditional: "unless acute illness with chance of recovery to good QoL"<br />
有条件："除非急性病且有可能恢复良好生活质量"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Baseline quality of life<br />
基线生活质量</td>
<td>Poor, debilitated, functionally dependent<br />
差、衰弱、功能依赖</td>
<td>Good: independent, active, able to perform valued activities<br />
良好：独立、活跃、能从事有意义的活动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>NIPPV appropriateness<br />
无创通气适用性</td>
<td>N/A (intubation already declined)<br />
不适用（已拒绝插管）</td>
<td>Contraindicated if altered MS, unable to protect airway<br />
意识状态改变、无法保护气道时禁忌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
