伦理委员会作用</td>
<td>When directive is ambiguous or family disputes<br />
医嘱不明确或家属有争议时</td>
<td>Not needed when directive is clear and applicable<br />
医嘱明确且适用时不需要</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A conditional advance directive prohibiting intubation "unless" recovery is possible must be read carefully — intubation IS the correct choice when the exception clause is met, as with treatable bacterial pneumonia in a previously functional patient.**

**有条件预立医嘱中"除非有恢复可能"的条款必须仔细解读——当例外条款满足时，插管才是正确选择，例如既往功能良好患者发生可治疗的细菌性肺炎。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The "UNLESS" Clause Test / 记忆钩 — "除非"条款检验:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>U</strong>nderlying disease: Is it stable or terminal? Stable chronic disease = exception may apply / 基础疾病：稳定还是终末期？慢性病稳定 = 例外可能适用<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ew acute event: Is it reversible? Bacterial pneumonia, PE, DKA = YES; metastatic progression = NO / 新急性事件：可逆吗？细菌性肺炎、PE、DKA = 是；转移进展 = 否<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ife quality at baseline: Was it good? Golf + travel = YES; bedridden + dependent = NO / 基线生活质量：良好吗？打高尔夫+旅行 = 是；卧床+依赖 = 否<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xpress directive language: Read the exact words — "unless" is conditional, not absolute / 预立医嘱明确措辞：仔细阅读原文——"除非"是有条件的，非绝对禁止<br />
• <strong>S</strong>urrogate/Status update: Reassess code status every admission with patient or decision-maker / 代理人/状态更新：每次住院与患者或决策者重新确认代码状态</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Advance Directives and Code Status in Clinical Practice / 高频知识表 — 临床实践中的预立医嘱与代码状态

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Types of advance directives<br />
预立医嘱的类型</td>
<td>Living will (written treatment preferences), durable power of attorney for healthcare (designates surrogate), POLST/MOLST (physician orders for life-sustaining treatment)<br />
生前遗嘱（书面治疗意愿）、医疗持久授权书（指定代理人）、POLST/MOLST（维持生命治疗的医嘱）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Code status reassessment each hospitalization<br />
每次住院重新评估代码状态</td>
<td>Code status must be reviewed at every new hospitalization — prior DNR/DNI from a different clinical context may not apply to the current acute event<br />
每次新住院必须审查代码状态——不同临床背景下的既往DNR/DNI可能不适用于当前急性事件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Conditional vs. unconditional directives<br />
有条件与无条件预立医嘱</td>
<td>Conditional directives contain "unless" clauses requiring clinical judgment; unconditional directives admit no exceptions — the exact wording determines management<br />
有条件医嘱含"除非"条款，须临床判断；无条件医嘱无例外——确切措辞决定管理方案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When ethics committee is appropriate<br />
伦理委员会适用情形</td>
<td>Unresolved conflict between surrogate and medical team; ambiguous or contradictory directive language; disagreement about prognosis or best interest<br />
代理人与医疗团队之间的未解决冲突；模糊或矛盾的医嘱措辞；关于预后或最佳利益的分歧</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>NIPPV contraindications<br />
无创通气禁忌证</td>
<td>Altered mental status, inability to cooperate, inability to protect airway (aspiration risk), facial trauma, hemodynamic instability, copious secretions<br />
意识状态改变、无法配合、无法保护气道（误吸风险）、面部创伤、血流动力学不稳定、大量分泌物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surrogate decision-maker hierarchy<br />
代理决策者层级</td>
<td>1) Designated healthcare proxy/DPOA → 2) Legal guardian → 3) Spouse → 4) Adult children → 5) Parents → 6) Siblings (order varies by jurisdiction)<br />
1)指定医疗代理人/持久授权书持有者→2)法定监护人→3)配偶→4)成年子女→5)父母→6)兄弟姐妹（顺序因司法管辖区而异）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Best interest standard<br />
最佳利益标准</td>
<td>Applied when no surrogate is available and no advance directive exists; physician acts in what a reasonable person in the patient's situation would want<br />
无代理人且无预立医嘱时适用；医生依据患者情境下理性人的意愿行事</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of comfort care indications:** Comfort/palliative-only management is appropriate for actively dying patients with terminal irreversible disease — not for patients with treatable acute illness and good pre-morbid function, regardless of cancer history\
  **舒适治疗适应症鉴别:** 舒适/纯姑息治疗适用于终末期不可逆疾病的临终患者——不适用于有良好病前功能且急性病可治疗的患者，无论有无癌症史

- **Key complication of delayed intubation:** Choosing NIPPV in a patient with altered mental status risks aspiration, worsening hypoxia, and eventual intubation in a more hemodynamically compromised state with higher mortality\
  **延迟插管的关键并发症:** 对意识改变患者选择无创通气，有误吸、低氧加重风险，最终在血流动力学更差的状态下插管，死亡率更高

- **Variant — unconditional DNI:** If the directive had read "I do not want intubation under any circumstances," intubation would be inappropriate even for reversible pneumonia — exact wording is determinative\
  **题目变式——无条件DNI:** 若预立医嘱写明"任何情况下均不插管"，则即使对可逆肺炎插管也不恰当——确切措辞具有决定性意义

- **Risk factor for advance directive misinterpretation:** A cancer diagnosis creates cognitive anchoring — clinicians may default to "terminal" framing; the key skill is separating the acute event from the chronic disease trajectory\
  **预立医嘱误解的危险因素:** 癌症诊断造成认知锚定效应——临床医生可能默认"终末期"框架；关键技能是将急性事件与慢性疾病轨迹区分开来

# Question 115 — Colovesical Fistula from Diverticular Disease / 憩室病性结肠膀胱瘘

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>77-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-day history of passing air and fecal material during urination</strong>. He has a long-standing history of <strong>intermittent constipation</strong>. His last examination was 20 years ago. He has smoked <strong>two packs of cigarettes daily for 55 years</strong>. He is 183 cm (6 ft) tall and weighs 70 kg (155 lb); BMI is 21 kg/m². Vital signs are within normal limits. Abdominal examination shows <strong>mild distention</strong>. Bowel sounds are <strong>decreased</strong>. Rectal examination shows a diffusely enlarged prostate. There is no stool in the rectal vault. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 14 g/dL, Leukocyte count 9600/mm³, Platelet count 444,000/mm³, <strong>Urine WBC &gt;100/hpf, Flora mixed</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's symptoms?</strong></p>
<p>A) Appendiceal abscess<br />
B) Diverticular disease<br />
C) Inflammatory bowel disease<br />
D) Prostate cancer<br />
E) Transitional cell carcinoma of the bladder</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Passing air + fecal material during urination<br />
排尿时排气+粪质</td>
<td>Classic presentation of colovesical fistula — bowel contents cross into the bladder<br />
结肠膀胱瘘的经典表现——肠内容物进入膀胱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-standing intermittent constipation<br />
长期间歇性便秘</td>
<td>Key risk factor for diverticulosis — elevated intraluminal pressure drives mucosal herniation<br />
憩室病的关键危险因素——肠腔内压升高驱动黏膜疝出</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>77-year-old male<br />
77岁男性</td>
<td>Age &gt;60: diverticulosis highly prevalent; male sex = no uterine barrier between sigmoid and bladder<br />
年龄&gt;60岁：憩室病高发；男性无子宫屏障隔开乙状结肠与膀胱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine WBC &gt;100/hpf, Flora mixed<br />
尿WBC &gt;100/hpf，混合菌群</td>
<td>Polymicrobial UTI = hallmark of enteric fistula (coliform organisms contaminating the bladder)<br />
多菌种UTI = 肠道瘘管的标志（结肠菌群污染膀胱）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diffusely enlarged prostate, no stool in rectal vault<br />
弥漫性前列腺增大，直肠空虚</td>
<td>Diffuse enlargement = BPH, not cancer; empty rectal vault argues against active rectal source<br />
弥漫性增大=BPH而非癌；直肠空虚不支持活动性直肠来源</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Heavy smoker (2 packs × 55 years)<br />
重度吸烟者（2包/天×55年）</td>
<td>Classic risk factor for bladder TCC — serves as a deliberate distractor in this question<br />
膀胱TCC的经典危险因素——在本题作为刻意干扰项出现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Diverticular disease** results from **increased intraluminal colonic pressure** forcing the **mucosa and submucosa** to herniate through weaknesses in the **muscularis propria** (at sites of vasa recta penetration):

**憩室病**源于**结肠腔内压增高**，迫使**黏膜和黏膜下层**经**固有肌层**薄弱点（直小血管穿入处）疝出：

- Diverticula most commonly form in the **sigmoid colon**, which has the highest intraluminal pressure\
  憩室最常见于**乙状结肠**，该段肠腔内压最高

- Repeated episodes of **diverticulitis** → pericolic inflammation, abscess, adhesions → fistula tract forms to the adjacent bladder\
  反复**憩室炎**发作→结肠旁炎症、脓肿、粘连→形成通向邻近膀胱的瘘管

- The fistula tract allows **colonic gas (pneumaturia)**, **fecal material (fecaluria)**, and **enteric bacteria** to enter the bladder\
  瘘管使**结肠气体（气尿）**、**粪质（粪尿）**和**肠道细菌**进入膀胱

- Result: **polymicrobial UTI** with mixed flora (E. coli, Bacteroides, Enterococcus, etc.)\
  结果：**多菌种UTI**，混合菌群（大肠杆菌、拟杆菌、肠球菌等）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In men, the uterus is absent — the sigmoid colon lies directly adjacent to the bladder dome, making colovesical fistulas 2–3× more common in men than women.

**解剖小窍门:** 男性无子宫，乙状结肠与膀胱顶直接毗邻——结肠膀胱瘘在男性中发生率是女性的2–3倍。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Colovesical Fistula from Diverticular Disease / 正确答案 (B) — 憩室病性结肠膀胱瘘

**Diverticular disease** is the most common cause (~65%) of colovesical fistulas and presents with a classic triad of symptoms:

**憩室病**是结肠膀胱瘘最常见的原因（约65%），表现为经典三联征：

- Pneumaturia — passage of air bubbles during urination\
  气尿——排尿时排出气泡

- Fecaluria — passage of fecal material in the urine stream\
  粪尿——尿流中带有粪质

- Recurrent polymicrobial UTI with mixed enteric flora\
  反复多菌种泌尿道感染，伴混合肠道菌群

**Diagnosis:** CT scan with oral/IV contrast (best initial test) to identify fistulous tract and sigmoid disease; cystoscopy with biopsy; colonoscopy to evaluate extent of diverticular involvement.

**诊断:** 口服/静脉造影CT（最佳初步检查）以识别瘘管和乙状结肠病变；膀胱镜+活检；结肠镜评估憩室病累及范围。

**Treatment:** Antibiotics for acute polymicrobial UTI + elective one-stage sigmoid resection with primary anastomosis; Hartmann's procedure if patient is unstable or bowel is unprepared.

**治疗:** 急性多菌种UTI抗生素治疗+择期乙状结肠一期切除吻合；患者不稳定或肠道未准备时行Hartmann手术。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<tr>
<td>A — Appendiceal abscess<br />
A — 阑尾脓肿</td>
<td>Wrong — presents with RLQ pain, fever, nausea/vomiting; does NOT cause pneumaturia or fecaluria<br />
错误——表现为右下腹痛、发热、恶心呕吐；不引起气尿或粪尿</td>

D — 前列腺癌</td>
<td>Wrong — diffusely enlarged prostate = BPH; even prostate cancer causes urinary obstruction, NOT pneumaturia or fecaluria without a concurrent fistula<br />
错误——弥漫性增大=BPH；前列腺癌引起尿路梗阻，无并发瘘管不会引起气尿或粪尿</td>
<td>Diffuse enlargement = BPH not cancer; prostate disease has no fistula mechanism to explain pneumaturia<br />

E — 膀胱移行细胞癌</td>
<td>Wrong — smoking IS a risk factor, but TCC presents with painless hematuria and obstruction, NOT fecaluria or polymicrobial bowel-origin UTI<br />
错误——吸烟确是危险因素，但TCC表现为无痛血尿和梗阻，不引起粪尿或多菌种肠道来源UTI</td>
<td>Hematuria (not fecaluria) is TCC hallmark; no bowel-bladder communication<br />
血尿（非粪尿）是TCC标志；无肠-膀胱交通</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The heavy smoking history is a deliberate distractor toward bladder TCC — but pneumaturia + fecaluria + polymicrobial UTI is the unmistakable fingerprint of a colovesical fistula, a combination that TCC simply cannot produce.*

重度吸烟史是指向膀胱TCC的刻意干扰项——但气尿+粪尿+多菌种UTI是结肠膀胱瘘无可辩驳的指纹，这一组合TCC根本无法产生。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An elderly constipated man with pneumaturia, fecaluria, and polymicrobial UTI has a colovesical fistula caused by sigmoid diverticular disease.**

**便秘老年男性出现气尿、粪尿和多菌种泌尿道感染，提示乙状结肠憩室病所致结肠膀胱瘘。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "PFM" Triad of Colovesical Fistula / 记忆钩 — 结肠膀胱瘘"PFM"三联征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>neumaturia — air crosses the fistula from colon into bladder / 气尿——气体经瘘管从结肠进入膀胱<br />
• <strong>F</strong>ecaluria — fecal material crosses the fistula into the urine stream / 粪尿——粪质经瘘管进入尿流<br />
• <strong>M</strong>ixed flora UTI — enteric bacteria contaminate the bladder, producing polymicrobial infection / 混合菌群UTI——肠道细菌污染膀胱，产生多菌种感染</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Diverticular Disease and Colovesical Fistula / 高频知识表 — 憩室病与结肠膀胱瘘

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />

</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Diverticulosis epidemiology<br />
憩室病流行病学</td>
<td>Affects &gt;50% of Americans over age 60; most are asymptomatic; sigmoid colon most commonly involved due to highest intraluminal pressure<br />
影响&gt;50%的60岁以上美国人；大多数无症状；乙状结肠最常受累（肠腔压最高）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathogenesis of diverticula<br />
憩室形成机制</td>
<td>Mucosa/submucosa herniates through muscularis propria at sites of vasa recta penetration; low-fiber diet → ↓ stool bulk → ↑ intraluminal pressure<br />
黏膜/黏膜下层经固有肌层直小血管穿入点疝出；低纤维饮食→↓粪便体积→↑肠腔压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Colovesical fistula etiology<br />
结肠膀胱瘘病因</td>
<td>Diverticular disease ~65% &gt; Colon cancer ~20% &gt; Crohn's disease ~7%; men &gt;&gt; women (uterus protects bladder in women)<br />
憩室病约65%&gt;结肠癌约20%&gt;克罗恩病约7%；男性远多于女性（女性子宫保护膀胱）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis of colovesical fistula<br />
结肠膀胱瘘诊断</td>
<td>CT with oral/IV contrast (best initial test); cystoscopy + biopsy; colonoscopy; poppy seed test (ingested seeds appear in urine)<br />
口服/静脉造影CT（最佳初步检查）；膀胱镜+活检；结肠镜；罂粟籽试验（吞服后种子出现在尿中）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications of diverticular disease<br />
憩室病并发症</td>
<td>(1) Diverticulitis — LLQ pain, fever; (2) Lower GI bleed — painless hematochezia; (3) Abscess; (4) Perforation; (5) Fistula (colovesical &gt; colovaginal &gt; colocutaneous)<br />
(1)憩室炎——左下腹痛、发热；(2)下消化道出血——无痛便血；(3)脓肿；(4)穿孔；(5)瘘管（结肠膀胱&gt;结肠阴道&gt;结肠皮肤）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why male sex predisposes to colovesical fistula<br />
男性易患结肠膀胱瘘的原因</td>
<td>In women, the uterus physically interposes between the sigmoid colon and bladder dome, preventing direct fistula formation<br />
女性子宫在乙状结肠和膀胱穹窿之间形成物理屏障，阻止瘘管直接形成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical management<br />
外科处理</td>
<td>One-stage resection: sigmoid colectomy + primary anastomosis + fistula closure; if unstable/unprepared bowel: Hartmann's procedure (colostomy) with delayed anastomosis<br />
一期手术：乙状结肠切除+一期吻合+瘘管关闭；不稳定/肠道未准备时：Hartmann手术（结肠造口）后延期吻合</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of pneumaturia:** Gas-forming organisms causing emphysematous cystitis (especially in diabetics), recent urinary tract instrumentation, or any enteric fistula (colovesical, rectovesical, enterovesical)\
  **气尿鉴别:** 产气菌引起的气肿性膀胱炎（尤见于糖尿病患者）、近期尿道器械操作、任何肠道瘘管（结肠膀胱、直肠膀胱、小肠膀胱）

- **Colovaginal fistula variant:** In women, diverticular disease more commonly causes colovaginal fistula — presents with passage of gas or fecal material per vagina (sigmoid protected from bladder by uterus)\
  **结肠阴道瘘变式:** 女性中，憩室病更常引起结肠阴道瘘——表现为阴道排气或排粪（乙状结肠受子宫保护，不易与膀胱形成瘘）

- **Poppy seed test:** Patient ingests poppy seeds; appearance in urine within 24–36 hours confirms colovesical fistula — simple, non-invasive, and low-cost confirmatory bedside test\
  **罂粟籽试验:** 患者吞服罂粟籽；24–36小时内尿中出现种子即确认结肠膀胱瘘——简单无创、低成本的床旁确认试验

- **Smoking as distractor:** Smoking is the single greatest risk factor for transitional cell carcinoma (accounts for ~50% of cases), making it a classic NBME distractor — but TCC presents with painless hematuria, not fecaluria\
  **吸烟作为干扰项:** 吸烟是移行细胞癌最大的单一危险因素（占约50%的病例），是经典的NBME干扰项——但TCC表现为无痛血尿，而非粪尿

# Question 116 — Acute Sciatica (Lumbar Disc Herniation) / 急性坐骨神经痛（腰椎椎间盘突出）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>25-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician <strong>2 hours after the sudden onset of sharp right buttock pain that radiates to the back of his knee</strong>. The pain <strong>worsens when he sits for a prolonged period or drives</strong>. He is able to walk. Use of over-the-counter ibuprofen has provided mild relief. He has no history of serious illness and takes no other medications. On examination, <strong>ipsilateral and contralateral straight-leg raise testing is positive</strong>. <strong>Muscle strength is normal throughout</strong>. <strong>Sensation is intact throughout</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Electromyography and nerve conduction studies<br />
B) MRI of the lumbosacral spine<br />
C) Myelography<br />
D) X-ray of the lumbosacral spine<br />
E) No further testing is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sharp right buttock pain radiating to back of knee<br />
右侧臀部锐痛放射至膝后</td>
<td>Classic sciatic nerve (L4–S1) dermatomal distribution; localizes the involved nerve root<br />
坐骨神经（L4–S1）经典皮节分布；定位受累神经根</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worsens with prolonged sitting or driving<br />
久坐或驾车时加重</td>
<td>Sitting increases intradiscal pressure; strongly suggests lumbar disc herniation as the etiology<br />
坐姿增加椎间盘内压；强烈提示腰椎椎间盘突出为病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Positive ipsilateral AND contralateral SLR<br />
同侧和对侧直腿抬高试验均阳性</td>
<td>Contralateral ("crossed") SLR is ~90% specific for disc herniation; bilateral positivity increases diagnostic confidence<br />
对侧（"交叉"）SLR 对椎间盘突出特异度约90%；双侧阳性增加诊断可信度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Muscle strength normal throughout<br />
全身肌力正常</td>
<td>No objective motor deficit → no indication for urgent imaging or EMG<br />
无客观运动缺损 → 无紧急影像或肌电图检查指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sensation intact throughout<br />
感觉完整</td>
<td>No objective sensory deficit → excludes significant nerve root compression requiring escalation<br />
无客观感觉缺损 → 排除需要升级处理的严重神经根压迫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Able to walk; mild relief with ibuprofen<br />
可以行走；布洛芬轻度缓解</td>
<td>Preserved functional mobility and NSAID response → appropriate candidate for conservative management first<br />
功能活动保留且对 NSAID 有反应 → 适合先行保守治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **sciatic nerve** (L4–S1) is the largest peripheral nerve; compression by a **herniated nucleus pulposus** or the **piriformis muscle** produces the characteristic pain syndrome known as sciatica:

**坐骨神经**（L4–S1）是人体最大的外周神经；**突出的髓核**或**梨状肌**压迫可产生称为坐骨神经痛的特征性疼痛综合征：

- Disc herniation: nucleus pulposus extrudes through the annulus fibrosus → compresses the adjacent nerve root → dermatomal pain ± motor/sensory deficits\
  椎间盘突出：髓核穿过纤维环突出 → 压迫邻近神经根 → 皮节性疼痛 ± 运动/感觉缺损

- Piriformis syndrome: piriformis muscle compresses the sciatic nerve at the greater sciatic notch → identical pain distribution but no identifiable spinal pathology\
  梨状肌综合征：梨状肌在坐骨大切迹处压迫坐骨神经 → 疼痛分布相同，但无可识别的脊柱病变

- Straight-leg raise (SLR) test: hip flexion with knee in extension stretches the sciatic nerve → reproduces radicular pain at 30–70° = positive\
  直腿抬高（SLR）试验：膝关节伸直时屈髋牵拉坐骨神经 → 30–70° 时再现放射痛 = 阳性

- Crossed SLR: flexing the contralateral (unaffected) leg reproduces pain in the affected leg — ~25% sensitive but ~90% specific for disc herniation\
  交叉 SLR：屈曲对侧（健侧）腿可再现患侧腿疼痛——灵敏度约25%，但对椎间盘突出特异度约90%

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** L5–S1 is the most commonly herniated disc, compressing the S1 root → pain radiates down the posterior thigh to the heel and lateral foot.

**解剖小窍门:** L5–S1 是最常见的椎间盘突出节段，压迫 S1 神经根 → 疼痛沿大腿后侧放射至足跟及足外侧。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Clinical Diagnosis of Sciatica, No Imaging Required / 正确答案 (E) — 坐骨神经痛的临床诊断，无需立即影像检查

**Sciatica** is a clinical diagnosis established by history and physical examination alone — imaging is not required when objective neurologic deficits are absent:

**坐骨神经痛**是单纯依靠病史和体格检查建立的临床诊断——在无客观神经缺损时不需要影像学检查：

- Clinical diagnosis requires: radicular pain in sciatic distribution + positive SLR + absence of cauda equina signs (bowel/bladder, saddle anesthesia, bilateral weakness)\
  临床诊断要求：坐骨神经分布区放射痛 + SLR 阳性 + 无马尾综合征征象（大小便障碍、鞍区麻木、双侧无力）

- No objective deficits (normal strength, intact sensation) → no urgent imaging, no EMG/NCS\
  无客观缺损（肌力正常、感觉完整）→ 无需紧急影像检查，无需肌电图/神经传导检查

- First-line management: NSAIDs, activity as tolerated, physical therapy; prolonged bed rest should be avoided as it worsens outcomes\
  一线治疗：NSAID、耐受范围内活动、物理治疗；应避免长期卧床，因其会加重预后

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — positive SLR (especially crossed SLR highly specific), posterior leg dermatomal pain, worsening with sitting (raised intradiscal pressure), fully intact neurologic exam.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——SLR 阳性（尤其是高度特异的交叉 SLR）、大腿后侧皮节性疼痛、久坐加重（椎间盘内压升高）、神经系统查体完全正常。

**Treatment:** NSAIDs (first-line), acetaminophen, activity modification, physical therapy; escalate to imaging only if no improvement after 6 weeks or red-flag deficits emerge.

**治疗:** NSAID（一线）、对乙酰氨基酚、活动调整、物理治疗；仅在6周保守治疗无效或出现红旗缺损时才升级至影像检查。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Electromyography and nerve conduction studies<br />
A — 肌电图和神经传导检查</td>
<td>Wrong — EMG/NCS is used to evaluate objective motor weakness and differentiate neuropathic from myopathic causes; this patient has normal strength and sensation<br />
错误——肌电图/神经传导检查用于评估客观运动无力，鉴别神经源性与肌源性病因；本患者肌力和感觉均正常</td>
<td>Indicated only with objective weakness present; pain alone is not an indication<br />
仅在存在客观无力时适用；单纯疼痛不是适应证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — MRI of the lumbosacral spine<br />
B — 腰骶椎 MRI</td>
<td>Wrong — MRI is indicated for cauda equina syndrome (bowel/bladder dysfunction, saddle anesthesia, bilateral leg weakness) or acute neurologic deterioration; none present here<br />
错误——MRI 适用于马尾综合征（大小便障碍、鞍区麻木、双下肢无力）或急性神经功能恶化；本例均不存在</td>
<td>Reserve for red-flag deficits; normal neuro exam = no MRI yet<br />
保留用于红旗神经缺损；神经系统查体正常 = 暂不行 MRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Myelography<br />
C — 脊髓造影</td>
<td>Wrong — myelography has been largely replaced by MRI due to superior image quality, no radiation, and noninvasive technique; not first-line even if imaging were warranted<br />
错误——脊髓造影已基本被 MRI 取代（更优图像质量、无辐射、非侵入性）；即使需要影像检查也不是一线</td>
<td>Obsolete for most indications; always choose MRI over myelography<br />
大多数适应证已过时；MRI 始终优于脊髓造影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — X-ray of the lumbosacral spine<br />
D — 腰骶椎 X 线平片</td>
<td>Wrong — X-ray can detect vertebral fractures or spondylolisthesis but cannot visualize soft-tissue disc herniation; appropriate for elderly patients with osteoporosis, not a 25-year-old without trauma<br />
错误——X 线可显示椎体骨折或脊椎滑脱，但无法显示软组织椎间盘突出；适用于骨质疏松老年患者，不适用于无外伤史的25岁患者</td>
<td>25-year-old, no trauma, no osteoporosis risk → fracture not the concern<br />
25岁、无外伤、无骨质疏松风险 → 骨折不是关注点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No further testing is indicated ✓<br />
E — 无需进一步检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — sciatica is a clinical diagnosis; intact motor strength and sensation mean no red flags; conservative management is the appropriate first step before any imaging<br />
正确——坐骨神经痛是临床诊断；运动肌力和感觉完整意味着无红旗表现；保守治疗是影像检查前的恰当第一步</td>
<td>Clinical diagnosis + no objective neurologic deficits = no testing needed first<br />
临床诊断 + 无客观神经缺损 = 先无需任何检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractor is B (MRI) — students reflexively order lumbar MRI for back pain with radiculopathy, but the critical teaching point is that normal motor strength and intact sensation mean no objective deficit exists, making clinical diagnosis and conservative trial the correct first move.*

最强干扰项是 B（MRI）——学生常对伴放射痛的背痛条件反射地开腰椎 MRI，但关键考点在于：肌力正常、感觉完整意味着无客观缺损，临床诊断加保守治疗试验才是正确的第一步。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Sciatica Without Deficits vs. Cauda Equina Syndrome: When to Image / 无缺损坐骨神经痛 vs. 马尾综合征：何时需要影像检查

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Sciatica with a positive straight-leg raise but normal motor strength and intact sensation is a clinical diagnosis — no imaging is needed until conservative management fails or red-flag neurologic deficits develop.**

**坐骨神经痛伴直腿抬高试验阳性但肌力正常、感觉完整者为临床诊断——在保守治疗失败或出现红旗神经缺损前无需影像学检查。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SCAN: When to Image Sciatica / 记忆钩 — SCAN：何时对坐骨神经痛进行影像检查:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>evere or progressive motor deficit (objective weakness) — new muscle weakness warrants MRI / 严重或进行性运动缺损（客观无力）——新发肌无力需 MRI<br />
• <strong>C</strong>auda equina signs (bowel/bladder dysfunction, saddle anesthesia) — emergent MRI and surgery / 马尾综合征征象（大小便障碍、鞍区麻木）——急诊 MRI 及手术<br />
• <strong>A</strong>cute neurologic deterioration despite conservative therapy — escalate to imaging / 保守治疗期间急性神经功能恶化——升级至影像检查<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eoplasm or infection suspected (fever, weight loss, cancer history, IV drug use) — image immediately / 怀疑肿瘤或感染（发热、体重减轻、肿瘤史、静脉吸毒）——立即影像检查</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Sciatica: Diagnosis and Management / 高频知识表 — 坐骨神经痛：诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common causes<br />
最常见病因</td>
<td>Lumbar disc herniation (L4–L5 or L5–S1); piriformis syndrome; less commonly: spinal stenosis, spondylolisthesis<br />
腰椎椎间盘突出（L4–L5 或 L5–S1）；梨状肌综合征；较少见：椎管狭窄、脊椎滑脱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SLR sensitivity and specificity<br />
SLR 灵敏度与特异度</td>
<td>Ipsilateral SLR: ~80% sensitive, ~40% specific; Crossed SLR: ~25% sensitive, ~90% specific for disc herniation<br />
同侧 SLR：约80%灵敏度、约40%特异度；交叉 SLR：约25%灵敏度、约90%特异度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cauda equina syndrome — emergent imaging<br />
马尾综合征——急诊影像</td>
<td>Bowel/bladder dysfunction + saddle anesthesia + bilateral leg weakness → emergent MRI + neurosurgical decompression; failure to act causes permanent deficits<br />
大小便障碍 + 鞍区麻木 + 双下肢无力 → 急诊 MRI + 神经外科减压；延误处理导致永久性缺损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Indications for non-urgent imaging<br />
非急诊影像适应证</td>
<td>Failure to improve after 6 weeks conservative management; new or worsening objective neurologic deficit; suspicion for malignancy, infection, or fracture<br />
保守治疗6周无效；新发或加重的客观神经缺损；怀疑恶性肿瘤、感染或骨折</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Conservative management<br />
保守治疗</td>
<td>NSAIDs or acetaminophen (first-line analgesia), activity as tolerated, physical therapy, epidural steroid injections for refractory cases; prolonged bed rest worsens outcomes<br />
NSAID 或对乙酰氨基酚（一线镇痛）、耐受范围内活动、物理治疗、顽固性病例可行硬膜外激素注射；长期卧床会加重预后</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognosis<br />
预后</td>
<td>~90% of patients improve spontaneously within 6–12 weeks with conservative management; surgical discectomy reserved for refractory cases with objective deficits<br />
约90%患者在保守治疗6–12周内自发改善；手术椎间盘切除术保留用于有客观缺损的顽固性病例</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Root level localization<br />
神经根水平定位</td>
<td>L4 root: knee extension weakness, medial calf/foot sensation, reduced patellar reflex; L5 root: ankle/great toe dorsiflexion weakness, dorsal foot sensation; S1 root: ankle plantarflexion weakness, lateral foot sensation, absent Achilles reflex<br />
L4 根：膝伸展无力、小腿内侧/足部感觉、膝腱反射减弱；L5 根：踝/拇趾背屈无力、足背感觉；S1 根：踝跖屈无力、足外侧感觉、跟腱反射消失</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Red flags requiring urgent escalation:** bowel or bladder dysfunction, saddle anesthesia, bilateral lower extremity weakness (→ cauda equina), fever with back pain (→ epidural abscess), history of cancer (→ metastatic disease), IV drug use (→ discitis/osteomyelitis)\
  **需要紧急升级处理的红旗症状:** 大小便功能障碍、鞍区麻木、双下肢无力（→马尾综合征）、发热伴背痛（→硬膜外脓肿）、肿瘤病史（→转移性疾病）、静脉吸毒（→椎间盘炎/骨髓炎）

- **Piriformis syndrome vs. disc herniation distinction:** piriformis syndrome is reproduced by palpation of the piriformis muscle at the greater sciatic notch and by the FAIR test (Flexion, Adduction, Internal Rotation of hip); MRI of the spine is normal\
  **梨状肌综合征 vs. 椎间盘突出的鉴别:** 梨状肌综合征可通过按压坐骨大切迹处的梨状肌及 FAIR 试验（髋关节屈曲、内收、内旋）再现；脊椎 MRI 正常

- **Variant presentation — bilateral sciatica:** bilateral symptoms should raise immediate concern for cauda equina syndrome from central disc herniation; urgent MRI is indicated\
  **变式表现——双侧坐骨神经痛:** 双侧症状应立即警惕中央型椎间盘突出引起的马尾综合征；需行急诊 MRI

- **EMG/NCS scope:** useful only when objective motor weakness is present to distinguish radiculopathy (denervation in myotomal distribution) from peripheral neuropathy or myopathy; never indicated for radicular pain without weakness\
  **肌电图/神经传导检查的适用范围:** 仅在存在客观运动无力时有用，用于区分神经根病（肌节分布去神经支配）与周围神经病或肌病；无无力时的放射痛绝对不适用

# Question 117 — Polycystic Ovarian Syndrome (PCOS) / 多囊卵巢综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>16-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician by her mother because of an <strong>8-month history of irregular menstrual periods, acne, and facial hair</strong>. Menarche was at the age of 12 years. Menses occur at <strong>irregular 35- to 42-day intervals</strong>; they last 1 week, and the flow is heavy. Moderate cramps on the first 2 days are relieved with ibuprofen therapy. The patient had recurrent urinary tract infections until the age of 10 years. She has no other history of serious illness and takes no other medications. She is 163 cm (5 ft 4 in) tall and weighs 77 kg (170 lb); <strong>BMI is 29 kg/m²</strong>. Her temperature is 36.9°C (98.4°F), pulse is 78/min, respirations are 20/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 128/84 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows <strong>scattered papules, pustules, and comedones</strong> over the face. There is <strong>sparse, coarse hair over the chin</strong>. The neck is supple; there is no thyromegaly. Breast examination shows no masses. Breast and pubic hair development are sexual maturity rating (SMR) stage 5.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Serum studies are most likely to show an increased concentration of which of the following?</strong></p>
<p>A) Follicle-stimulating hormone<br />
B) 11α-Hydroxyprogesterone<br />
C) 21α-Hydroxyprogesterone<br />
D) Luteinizing hormone<br />
E) Thyroid-stimulating hormone</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Irregular periods, 35–42-day intervals<br />
月经不规则，周期 35-42 天</td>
<td>Oligomenorrhea is one of the Rotterdam diagnostic criteria for PCOS<br />
稀发月经是 PCOS 鹿特丹诊断标准之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acne + coarse facial hair (chin)<br />
痤疮 + 下巴粗毛</td>
<td>Clinical signs of hyperandrogenism — core feature of PCOS<br />
高雄激素血症的临床表现——PCOS 核心特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 29 kg/m², 16-year-old<br />
BMI 29，16 岁青少年</td>
<td>Overweight/obesity + adolescent onset strongly suggests PCOS with insulin resistance<br />
超重/肥胖 + 青春期发病强烈提示 PCOS 伴胰岛素抵抗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 128/84 mmHg<br />
血压 128/84 mmHg</td>
<td>Borderline hypertension — consistent with metabolic syndrome component of PCOS<br />
临界高血压——与 PCOS 代谢综合征成分一致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMR stage 5, no thyromegaly<br />
性成熟评级 5 期，无甲状腺肿大</td>
<td>Rules out delayed puberty and hypothyroidism as cause of irregular menses<br />
排除青春期延迟和甲状腺功能减退作为月经不规则的原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Heavy flow lasting 1 week<br />
经量多，持续 1 周</td>
<td>Menorrhagia from anovulatory cycles — unopposed estrogen builds thick endometrium<br />
无排卵周期导致月经过多——无拮抗的雌激素使子宫内膜增厚</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

In **PCOS**, an abnormal **hypothalamic GnRH pulse frequency** is accelerated, selectively increasing **LH secretion** over FSH. This elevated **LH:FSH ratio** drives excess **androgen production** from theca cells, impairing follicle maturation and causing chronic anovulation:

在 **PCOS** 中，**下丘脑 GnRH 脉冲频率**异常加快，选择性增加 **LH 分泌**而非 FSH。升高的 **LH:FSH 比值**驱动卵泡膜细胞过量产生**雄激素**，损害卵泡成熟并导致慢性无排卵：

- Elevated LH → stimulates theca cells → excess testosterone → peripheral conversion to estrone\
  LH 升高→刺激卵泡膜细胞→睾酮过量→外周转化为雌酮

- Elevated androgens → inhibit follicular development → multiple small arrested follicles (polycystic appearance)\
  雄激素升高→抑制卵泡发育→多个小卵泡停滞（多囊样外观）

- Insulin resistance → hyperinsulinemia → further amplifies LH-driven androgen production\
  胰岛素抵抗→高胰岛素血症→进一步放大 LH 驱动的雄激素产生

- Chronic anovulation → no progesterone → unopposed estrogen → oligomenorrhea / menorrhagia\
  慢性无排卵→无孕激素→无拮抗雌激素→稀发月经/月经过多

**Hormonal rule of thumb:** In PCOS, LH is elevated but FSH is normal-to-low; the LH:FSH ratio is classically \>2:1 or even \>3:1.

**激素小窍门:** PCOS 中 LH 升高而 FSH 正常偏低；LH:FSH 比值经典地 \>2:1 甚至 \>3:1。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Elevated Luteinizing Hormone / 正确答案 (D) — 黄体生成素升高

**Luteinizing hormone (LH)** is characteristically elevated in PCOS due to abnormally rapid hypothalamic GnRH pulsing that preferentially stimulates LH release:

**黄体生成素（LH）**在 PCOS 中因下丘脑 GnRH 脉冲异常加速而特征性升高，优先刺激 LH 释放：

- Increased LH pulse amplitude and frequency drive tonic LH elevation\
  LH 脉冲幅度和频率增加驱动 LH 持续升高

- High LH → excess theca cell androgen (testosterone, androstenedione) production\
  LH 高→卵泡膜细胞雄激素（睾酮、雄烯二酮）过量产生

- LH:FSH ratio \>2–3:1 is a classic (though not required) biochemical finding in PCOS\
  LH:FSH 比值 \>2-3:1 是 PCOS 的经典（但非必需）生化表现

**Diagnosis:** Rotterdam criteria require 2 of 3: oligo/anovulation, clinical/biochemical hyperandrogenism, polycystic ovaries on ultrasound. This patient has both anovulation and hyperandrogenism.

**诊断:** 鹿特丹标准要求以下 3 项中满足 2 项：稀发/无排卵、临床/生化高雄激素血症、超声示多囊卵巢。该患者同时具有无排卵和高雄激素血症。

**Treatment:** Weight loss (first-line); combined oral contraceptives for cycle regulation and androgen suppression; spironolactone or ketoconazole for hirsutism/acne; metformin for insulin resistance.

**治疗:** 减重（一线）；联合口服避孕药调节周期并抑制雄激素；螺内酯或酮康唑治疗多毛/痤疮；二甲双胍改善胰岛素抵抗。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Follicle-stimulating hormone<br />
A — 促卵泡激素</td>
<td>FSH is normal or low in PCOS (LH:FSH ratio inverted); FSH elevation suggests menopause or ovarian failure<br />
PCOS 中 FSH 正常或偏低（LH:FSH 比值倒置）；FSH 升高提示绝经或卵巢衰竭</td>
<td>PCOS = high LH, normal/low FSH; Primary ovarian insufficiency = both FSH and LH elevated<br />
PCOS = LH 高，FSH 正常/低；原发性卵巢功能不全 = FSH 和 LH 均升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — 11α-Hydroxyprogesterone<br />
B — 11α-羟孕酮</td>
<td>Precursor in mineralocorticoid pathway; elevated in rare 11β-hydroxylase deficiency CAH, not PCOS<br />
矿皮质激素通路前体；在罕见的 11β-羟化酶缺乏症 CAH 中升高，与 PCOS 无关</td>
<td>CAH (11β-hydroxylase) = hypertension + virilization + no polycystic ovaries<br />
CAH（11β-羟化酶）= 高血压 + 男性化 + 无多囊卵巢</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — 21α-Hydroxyprogesterone<br />
C — 21α-羟孕酮</td>
<td>Mineralocorticoid precursor; elevated in 21-hydroxylase deficiency CAH — but that causes salt-wasting or hypertension with virilization, not isolated PCOS picture<br />
矿皮质激素前体；21-羟化酶缺乏症 CAH 中升高——但表现为失盐危象或高血压合并男性化，而非单纯 PCOS</td>
<td>17-hydroxyprogesterone (not 21α-OHP) is the marker for 21-hydroxylase deficiency CAH<br />
17-羟孕酮（而非 21α-OHP）才是 21-羟化酶缺乏症 CAH 的标志物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Luteinizing hormone ✓<br />
D — 黄体生成素 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — elevated LH from aberrant GnRH pulsing drives theca cell androgen excess and anovulation in PCOS<br />
正确——GnRH 脉冲异常导致 LH 升高，驱动卵泡膜细胞雄激素过量和无排卵</td>
<td>LH:FSH &gt;2:1 + hyperandrogenism + oligomenorrhea = classic PCOS biochemistry<br />
LH:FSH &gt;2:1 + 高雄激素血症 + 稀发月经 = PCOS 经典生化表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Thyroid-stimulating hormone<br />
E — 促甲状腺激素</td>
<td>TSH elevated in primary hypothyroidism, which can cause weight gain and irregular menses but does NOT cause hyperandrogenism (no acne, no hirsutism)<br />
TSH 在原发性甲状腺功能减退中升高，可引起体重增加和月经不规则，但不导致高雄激素血症（无痤疮、无多毛）</td>
<td>Key discriminator: hypothyroidism lacks acne and hirsutism; SMR 5 and no thyromegaly argue against it here<br />
鉴别要点：甲减无痤疮和多毛；SMR 5 期且无甲状腺肿大在此处排除该诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (TSH/hypothyroidism), because weight gain and oligomenorrhea overlap — but hypothyroidism cannot explain the hyperandrogenism (acne + chin hair), making PCOS the only unifying diagnosis.*

TSH/甲减是最有迷惑性的干扰项，因为体重增加和稀发月经与 PCOS 重叠——但甲减无法解释高雄激素血症（痤疮 + 下巴毛），使 PCOS 成为唯一能统一所有表现的诊断。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**PCOS causes elevated LH (from rapid GnRH pulsing) that drives theca cell hyperandrogenism, leading to the triad of oligomenorrhea, acne/hirsutism, and obesity in reproductive-age women.**

**PCOS 因 GnRH 脉冲加速导致 LH 升高，驱动卵泡膜细胞高雄激素血症，在育龄女性中形成稀发月经、痤疮/多毛和肥胖三联征。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PCOS "HAIR" Mnemonic / 记忆钩 — PCOS "HAIR" 助记法:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>yperandrogenism — acne, hirsutism, elevated testosterone / 高雄激素血症——痤疮、多毛、睾酮升高<br />
• <strong>A</strong>novulation — oligomenorrhea, LH:FSH ratio &gt;2:1, infertility / 无排卵——稀发月经、LH:FSH &gt;2:1、不孕<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nsulin resistance — obesity, acanthosis nigricans, hyperglycemia / 胰岛素抵抗——肥胖、黑棘皮症、高血糖<br />
• <strong>R</strong>aised LH — the key serum finding; drives theca androgen overproduction / LH 升高——关键血清表现；驱动卵泡膜雄激素过度产生</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — PCOS Pathophysiology & Management / 高频知识表 — PCOS 病理生理与管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Rotterdam Diagnostic Criteria<br />
鹿特丹诊断标准</td>
<td>2 of 3 required: (1) oligo/anovulation, (2) clinical or biochemical hyperandrogenism, (3) polycystic ovaries on ultrasound; must exclude other etiologies<br />
3 项中满足 2 项：（1）稀发/无排卵，（2）临床或生化高雄激素血症，（3）超声示多囊卵巢；需排除其他病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LH:FSH Ratio in PCOS<br />
PCOS 中 LH:FSH 比值</td>
<td>Classically &gt;2:1 or &gt;3:1; caused by accelerated hypothalamic GnRH pulse frequency; NOT required for diagnosis but highly supportive<br />
经典值 &gt;2:1 或 &gt;3:1；由下丘脑 GnRH 脉冲频率加速引起；非诊断必需，但高度支持</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Insulin Resistance in PCOS<br />
PCOS 中的胰岛素抵抗</td>
<td>Hyperinsulinemia amplifies LH-driven androgen production; look for acanthosis nigricans, impaired fasting glucose; metformin used as adjunct<br />
高胰岛素血症放大 LH 驱动的雄激素产生；注意黑棘皮症、空腹血糖受损；二甲双胍作为辅助治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-term Risks of PCOS<br />
PCOS 长期风险</td>
<td>Type 2 diabetes, metabolic syndrome, endometrial hyperplasia/carcinoma (from unopposed estrogen), cardiovascular disease<br />
2 型糖尿病、代谢综合征、子宫内膜增生/癌（无拮抗雌激素所致）、心血管疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment Hierarchy<br />
治疗层次</td>
<td>(1) Weight loss — improves all parameters; (2) Combined OCP — regulates cycle, suppresses androgens; (3) Spironolactone — antiandrogen for hirsutism/acne; (4) Clomiphene/letrozole — for ovulation induction when fertility desired<br />
（1）减重——改善所有指标；（2）联合口服避孕药——调节周期、抑制雄激素；（3）螺内酯——抗雄激素治疗多毛/痤疮；（4）氯米芬/来曲唑——有生育需求时促排卵</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PCOS vs. CAH Distinction<br />
PCOS 与 CAH 鉴别</td>
<td>Both cause hyperandrogenism; key test: early morning 17-hydroxyprogesterone (elevated in 21-hydroxylase deficiency CAH); PCOS has no 17-OHP elevation<br />
两者均可引起高雄激素血症；关键检查：清晨 17-羟孕酮（21-羟化酶缺乏症 CAH 中升高）；PCOS 无 17-OHP 升高</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of secondary amenorrhea/oligomenorrhea:** Hypothyroidism (TSH↑, no androgens), hyperprolactinemia (galactorrhea, PRL↑), premature ovarian insufficiency (FSH↑, LH↑), CAH (17-OHP↑), PCOS (LH↑, androgens↑)\
  **继发性闭经/稀发月经鉴别:** 甲减（TSH↑，无雄激素），高泌乳素血症（泌乳、PRL↑），卵巢早衰（FSH↑、LH↑），CAH（17-OHP↑），PCOS（LH↑、雄激素↑）

- **Key complication — endometrial cancer risk:** Chronic anovulation → no progesterone → prolonged unopposed estrogen → endometrial hyperplasia → cancer; OCP use reduces this risk significantly\
  **关键并发症——子宫内膜癌风险:** 慢性无排卵→无孕激素→长期无拮抗雌激素→子宫内膜增生→癌变；口服避孕药可显著降低此风险

- **Variant — lean PCOS:** Not all PCOS patients are obese; ~20–30% are normal weight; hormonal and ovulatory abnormalities identical but metabolic features less pronounced\
  **题目变式——瘦型 PCOS:** 并非所有 PCOS 患者均肥胖；约 20-30% 体重正常；激素和排卵异常相同，但代谢特征不那么突出

- **Spironolactone mechanism in PCOS:** Acts as androgen receptor antagonist AND inhibits 5α-reductase → reduces hirsutism and acne; teratogenic (must use contraception concurrently)\
  **螺内酯在 PCOS 中的作用机制:** 作为雄激素受体拮抗剂并抑制 5α-还原酶→减少多毛和痤疮；有致畸性（必须同时使用避孕措施）

# Question 118 — Preoperative Cervical Spine Evaluation in Rheumatoid Arthritis / 类风湿关节炎术前颈椎评估（寰枢关节不稳）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>49-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician for preoperative examination before she undergoes <strong>cholecystectomy</strong>. During the past <strong>3 years</strong>, she has had recurrent cholecystitis and multiple gallstones. She has not had shortness of breath, difficulty swallowing, or hoarseness. She has <strong>rheumatoid arthritis</strong> with <strong>morning stiffness</strong> and <strong>widespread joint swelling</strong>. Her medications are methotrexate, folic acid, and <strong>prednisone</strong>. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows <strong>nodules over the extensor aspect</strong> of the upper extremities. There is swelling of the wrists, metacarpophalangeal joints of the hands, and knees; there are <strong>swan neck deformities</strong> of the fingers. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management to decrease this patient's risk for operative complications?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management to decrease operative complications?</strong></p>
<p>A) Discontinuation of methotrexate<br />
B) Discontinuation of prednisone<br />
C) Indirect laryngoscopy<br />
D) Pulmonary function testing<br />
E) X-rays of the cervical spine</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Rheumatoid arthritis × 3 years<br />
类风湿关节炎 × 3 年病史</td>
<td>Chronic RA frequently involves the cervical spine, especially the atlantoaxial joint (C1-C2)<br />
慢性 RA 常累及颈椎，尤其是寰枢关节（C1-C2）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Swan neck deformities + extensor nodules<br />
天鹅颈畸形 + 伸侧皮下结节</td>
<td>Markers of severe, systemic RA — indicates high likelihood of atlantoaxial involvement<br />
提示病情严重且系统性受累，颈椎受累风险高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Undergoing general anesthesia for cholecystectomy<br />
即将在全身麻醉下行胆囊切除术</td>
<td>Intubation requires direct laryngoscopy with neck extension — dangerous if C1-C2 is unstable<br />
气管插管需颈椎后伸，寰枢不稳时可致灾难性脊髓损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Morning stiffness + widespread joint swelling<br />
晨僵 + 广泛关节肿胀</td>
<td>Classic features confirming active RA with ongoing systemic inflammation<br />
典型 RA 活动期表现，印证系统性炎症持续存在</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic prednisone use<br />
长期使用泼尼松</td>
<td>Long-term glucocorticoids suppress the HPA axis — abrupt discontinuation risks adrenal crisis<br />
长期使用糖皮质激素抑制 HPA 轴，突然停药有肾上腺危象风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No respiratory symptoms (no dyspnea, no hoarseness)<br />
无呼吸系统症状（无呼吸困难、无声音嘶哑）</td>
<td>Makes pulmonary function testing low-yield; redirects focus to cervical spine evaluation<br />
排除了需要肺功能检查的依据，重点应放在颈椎评估上</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Rheumatoid arthritis** causes **synovial inflammation** that progressively destroys cartilage and bone across multiple joints, including the **atlantoaxial joint (C1-C2)**:

**类风湿关节炎**引起**滑膜炎症**，进行性破坏软骨和骨，包括**寰枢关节（C1-C2）**：

- Synovitis erodes the **transverse ligament** of the atlas and the **dens of C2**, leading to **atlantoaxial instability**\
  滑膜炎侵蚀寰椎**横韧带**和 C2 的**齿突**，导致**寰枢关节不稳定**

- During **direct laryngoscopy**, the anesthesiologist extends the neck to visualize the glottis — this can sublux an unstable C1-C2 joint\
  **直接喉镜检查**时，麻醉医师通过颈部后伸来显露声门——这可能使不稳定的 C1-C2 发生半脱位

- Subluxation compresses the **spinal cord** or **vertebral arteries**, causing catastrophic **quadriplegia or death**\
  半脱位压迫**脊髓**或**椎动脉**，可引起灾难性的**四肢瘫痪甚至死亡**

- **Flexion-extension cervical spine x-rays** quantify the degree of atlantoaxial instability and guide intubation strategy (e.g., awake fiberoptic intubation)\
  颈椎**屈伸位 X 线片**可量化寰枢关节不稳程度，指导插管策略（如清醒纤支镜插管）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The atlantodental interval (ADI) on lateral flexion x-ray — \>3 mm in adults suggests atlantoaxial instability; \>9 mm indicates high risk of spinal cord injury.

**解剖小窍门:** 侧位屈曲 X 线片上的寰齿间距（ADI）——成人 \>3 mm 提示寰枢关节不稳；\>9 mm 提示脊髓损伤高风险。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Preoperative Cervical Spine X-rays / 正确答案 (E) — 术前颈椎 X 线检查

**Atlantoaxial instability** is a well-recognized complication of chronic RA caused by synovitis-mediated destruction of the C1-C2 stabilizing structures:

**寰枢关节不稳**是慢性 RA 的已知并发症，由滑膜炎介导的 C1-C2 稳定结构破坏所致：

- The standard screening study is **lateral cervical spine x-ray in flexion and extension** to measure the atlantodental interval\
  标准筛查方法是**颈椎侧位屈伸位 X 线片**，测量寰齿间距

- If instability is identified, **awake fiberoptic intubation** with in-line stabilization (rather than direct laryngoscopy) prevents catastrophic neurologic injury\
  若发现不稳定，采用**清醒纤支镜插管**并保持颈椎轴向固定（而非直接喉镜），防止灾难性神经损伤

- Performing this evaluation **before any elective surgery requiring general anesthesia** is mandatory in patients with chronic RA\
  在慢性 RA 患者行**任何需全身麻醉的择期手术前**，此评估是必须的

**Diagnosis:** Atlantoaxial instability is clinically silent until the neck is stressed by manipulation; preoperative screening is the only way to identify at-risk patients.

**诊断:** 寰枢关节不稳在颈部受力前往往无临床症状，术前筛查是识别高危患者的唯一途径。

**Treatment:** If significant instability is found: awake fiberoptic intubation with manual in-line stabilization; if severe, neurosurgical consultation before proceeding with elective surgery.

**治疗:** 若发现显著不稳定：采用清醒纤支镜插管并保持颈椎轴向固定；若极为严重，择期手术前需神经外科会诊。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Discontinuation of methotrexate<br />
A — 停用甲氨蝶呤</td>
<td>Not indicated — methotrexate's anti-inflammatory benefit in controlling RA outweighs perioperative infection risk; stopping it does not address the operative complication in question<br />
不需要——甲氨蝶呤的抗炎益处超过围手术期感染风险；停药并不能降低本题所指的手术并发症风险</td>
<td>Methotrexate does not affect intubation risk; the operative complication here is neurologic, not infectious<br />
甲氨蝶呤不影响插管风险；本题的手术并发症是神经系统性，而非感染性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Discontinuation of prednisone<br />
B — 停用泼尼松</td>
<td>Dangerous — chronic prednisone suppresses the HPA axis; abrupt discontinuation can precipitate life-threatening adrenal insufficiency perioperatively<br />
危险——长期使用泼尼松抑制 HPA 轴；突然停药可在围手术期诱发危及生命的肾上腺功能不全</td>
<td>Stopping prednisone increases risk rather than decreasing it; stress-dose steroids should be considered instead<br />
停用泼尼松会增加而非降低风险；应考虑围手术期应激剂量糖皮质激素替代</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Indirect laryngoscopy<br />
C — 间接喉镜检查</td>
<td>Less useful than cervical spine x-ray — also requires neck movement and does not quantify instability or guide intubation strategy<br />
不如颈椎 X 线片有用——同样需要颈部活动，且不能量化不稳定程度或指导插管策略</td>
<td>Must first know cervical stability before deciding on any laryngoscopic approach; cervical x-ray is the prerequisite<br />
必须先了解颈椎稳定性才能决定喉镜检查方案；颈椎 X 线片是前提</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Pulmonary function testing<br />
D — 肺功能检查</td>
<td>Not indicated — this patient has no respiratory symptoms; while RA can cause interstitial lung disease, there is no clinical evidence of it here<br />
不适应——此患者无呼吸道症状；虽然 RA 可致间质性肺病，但目前无临床依据</td>
<td>Absence of dyspnea/cough makes RA-ILD unlikely; PFTs are ordered only when respiratory symptoms suggest functional compromise<br />
无呼吸困难/咳嗽提示 RA-ILD 可能性低；PFTs 仅在呼吸症状提示功能受损时才有指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — X-rays of the cervical spine ✓<br />
E — 颈椎 X 线片 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — flexion-extension cervical spine x-rays detect atlantoaxial instability; if present, intubation technique must be modified to prevent spinal cord injury<br />
正确——颈椎屈伸位 X 线片检测寰枢关节不稳；若存在，必须改变插管方式以防脊髓损伤</td>
<td>Only intervention that directly addresses the primary operative complication risk (neurologic injury from laryngoscopy)<br />
唯一直接针对主要手术并发症风险（喉镜检查导致神经损伤）的干预措施</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is C (indirect laryngoscopy) — it seems relevant because intubation is the concern, but it cannot substitute for cervical spine stability assessment; the x-ray must come first to determine whether any laryngoscopy is safe.*

间接喉镜检查（C）是最大的干扰项——表面上与气管插管问题相关，但无法替代颈椎稳定性评估；X 线片是前提，必须先行以判断任何喉镜操作是否安全。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Preoperative Considerations in Chronic Rheumatoid Arthritis / 慢性类风湿关节炎患者术前注意事项对比

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In patients with chronic rheumatoid arthritis undergoing general anesthesia, cervical spine flexion-extension x-rays are mandatory before intubation to screen for atlantoaxial instability.**

**慢性类风湿关节炎患者接受全身麻醉前，必须行颈椎屈伸位 X 线片筛查寰枢关节不稳，以避免插管相关灾难性脊髓损伤。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — RA Before the OR: "SPINE" / 记忆钩 — RA 术前五要素："SPINE":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ynovitis destroys C1-C2 stabilizers — the root mechanism of atlantoaxial instability / 滑膜炎破坏 C1-C2 稳定结构——寰枢不稳的根本机制<br />
• <strong>P</strong>reoperative flexion-extension x-ray is the mandatory screen before GA / 术前屈伸位 X 线片是全身麻醉前的必查项目<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ntubation technique changes: fiberoptic if ADI &gt;3 mm, avoid neck extension / 插管方式改变：ADI&gt;3 mm 用纤支镜，避免颈部后伸<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eck extension during laryngoscopy = danger zone for any chronic RA patient / 喉镜操作时颈部后伸对慢性 RA 患者是危险区<br />
• <strong>E</strong>valuate before every elective surgery under general anesthesia — never skip it / 每次择期全麻手术前均需评估，不可省略</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Rheumatoid Arthritis Cervical Spine and Perioperative Management / 高频知识表 — 类风湿关节炎颈椎受累与围手术期管理

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />

<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>

</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Atlantoaxial instability prevalence in RA<br />
RA 中寰枢关节不稳的发生率</td>
<td>Occurs in up to 40–86% of patients with severe or long-standing RA; often asymptomatic until neck is mechanically stressed<br />
严重或长期 RA 患者中发生率高达 40–86%；通常无症状，直到颈椎受到机械性应力才表现出来</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Atlantodental interval (ADI) interpretation<br />
寰齿间距（ADI）解读</td>
<td>Normal ≤3 mm in adults; 3–9 mm = instability; &gt;9 mm = high risk of spinal cord compression<br />
成人正常≤3 mm；3–9 mm 提示不稳定；&gt;9 mm 提示脊髓受压高风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intubation approach when instability confirmed<br />
证实不稳定时的插管方法</td>
<td>Awake fiberoptic nasotracheal or orotracheal intubation with manual in-line stabilization; avoids all neck extension<br />
清醒纤支镜经鼻或经口插管并保持颈椎轴向固定，完全避免颈椎后伸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic prednisone and perioperative stress-dose steroids<br />
长期泼尼松与围手术期应激剂量糖皮质激素</td>
<td>Patients on prednisone &gt;5 mg/day for &gt;3 weeks likely have HPA suppression; give hydrocortisone 50–100 mg IV at induction to prevent intraoperative adrenal crisis<br />
每日泼尼松&gt;5 mg 且持续&gt;3 周的患者可能存在 HPA 抑制；麻醉诱导时给予氢化可的松 50–100 mg 静注以防术中肾上腺危象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Methotrexate perioperative management<br />
甲氨蝶呤围手术期管理</td>
<td>Generally continued perioperatively for RA disease control; folic acid co-prescription prevents mucositis and megaloblastic anemia<br />
通常术中继续使用以控制 RA；同时补充叶酸以预防口腔炎和巨幼细胞性贫血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RA extra-articular manifestations to know<br />
需掌握的 RA 关节外表现</td>
<td>Subcutaneous nodules (extensor surfaces), interstitial lung disease, pleuritis, pericarditis, vasculitis, anemia of chronic disease, Felty syndrome (RA + splenomegaly + neutropenia)<br />
皮下结节（伸肌面）、间质性肺病、胸膜炎、心包炎、血管炎、慢性病贫血、Felty 综合征（RA+脾大+中性粒细胞减少）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Distinguishing RA from OA on boards<br />
考试中 RA 与 OA 的鉴别</td>
<td>RA: symmetric small joints (MCPs, PIPs, wrists), morning stiffness &gt;1 hour, positive RF/anti-CCP; OA: asymmetric, weight-bearing joints, Heberden/Bouchard nodes, morning stiffness &lt;30 minutes<br />
RA：对称性小关节（MCP、PIP、腕），晨僵&gt;1 小时，RF/抗 CCP 阳性；OA：非对称，负重关节，Heberden/Bouchard 结节，晨僵&lt;30 分钟</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Variant — subaxial cervical subluxation in RA:** Besides C1-C2, RA can cause subluxation at lower cervical levels (C2-C7), also detectable on flexion-extension x-rays and requiring the same intubation precautions\
  **变式——RA 下颈椎半脱位:** 除 C1-C2 外，RA 还可引起下颈椎节段半脱位（C2-C7），同样可通过屈伸位 X 线检测，需采取相同插管预防措施

- **Key complication — missed atlantoaxial instability:** Published case reports document quadriplegia following routine intubation in unscreened RA patients; this is why preoperative cervical x-ray is standard of care, not optional\
  **关键并发症——漏诊寰枢关节不稳:** 文献报道有未经筛查的 RA 患者在常规插管后发生四肢瘫痪；这也是术前颈椎 X 线片是诊疗标准而非可选项的原因

- **Risk factors for cervical involvement in RA:** Long disease duration, high disease activity (elevated ESR/CRP), positive RF/anti-CCP antibodies, and radiographic erosive disease all predict higher likelihood of atlantoaxial involvement\
  **RA 颈椎受累的危险因素:** 病程长、疾病活动度高（ESR/CRP 升高）、RF/抗 CCP 抗体阳性、X 线侵蚀性病变均预示寰枢关节受累可能性更高

- **Differential of preoperative anemia in RA patients:** Anemia of chronic disease (normocytic, low reticulocyte count) from RA itself vs. methotrexate-induced megaloblastic anemia (macrocytic) — folic acid co-prescription specifically prevents the latter\
  **RA 患者术前贫血鉴别:** RA 本身所致慢性病贫血（正细胞性，网织红细胞低）vs 甲氨蝶呤所致巨幼细胞性贫血（大细胞性）——补充叶酸正是为了预防后者

# Question 119 — Hyperprolactinemia Secondary to Hypothyroidism / 继发于甲状腺功能减退的高泌乳素血症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, comes to the physician because of <strong>spontaneous discharge from her nipples</strong> during the <strong>past 3 months</strong>. She <strong>discontinued breast-feeding her child 1 year ago</strong>. She takes <strong>no medications</strong>. Menses occur at <strong>regular 28-day intervals</strong>. On physical examination, a <strong>milky white discharge</strong> can be expressed from both nipples. Examination shows no other abnormalities. Her <strong>fasting serum prolactin concentration is 40 ng/mL</strong>. The most appropriate next step in diagnosis is measurement of which of the following serum concentrations?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis — measure which serum concentration?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cortisol<br />
B) Dopamine<br />
C) Estrogen<br />
D) Gonadotropin-releasing hormone<br />
E) Thyroid-stimulating hormone</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Spontaneous bilateral milky nipple discharge<br />
自发性双侧乳白色乳头溢液</td>
<td>Galactorrhea = pathologic prolactin excess; bilateral presentation rules out local ductal lesion<br />
溢乳症 = 病理性泌乳素过多；双侧表现排除局部导管病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Stopped breastfeeding 1 year ago<br />
停止哺乳已1年</td>
<td>Physiologic lactation resolves within weeks of weaning; persistence at 1 year is pathologic<br />
生理性泌乳在断奶后数周内消退；1年后仍持续属于病理性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No medications<br />
无用药史</td>
<td>Dopamine antagonists (antipsychotics, metoclopramide) are a leading drug cause; absence narrows the differential<br />
多巴胺拮抗剂（抗精神病药、甲氧氯普胺）是主要药物原因；无用药史缩小鉴别范围</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Regular 28-day menses<br />
月经规律，28天周期</td>
<td>Intact hypothalamic-pituitary-ovarian axis; severe hyperprolactinemia typically causes amenorrhea; milder elevation can preserve cycles<br />
下丘脑-垂体-卵巢轴完整；严重高泌乳素血症通常致闭经；轻度升高可保留月经</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fasting prolactin 40 ng/mL<br />
空腹泌乳素40 ng/mL</td>
<td>&gt;30 ng/mL in premenopausal women = hyperprolactinemia; fasting eliminates physiologic post-meal rise<br />
育龄女性&gt;30 ng/mL = 高泌乳素血症；空腹排除餐后生理性升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No other examination abnormalities<br />
体检无其他异常</td>
<td>No signs of pituitary mass effect (visual field defects, headache); suggests microadenoma or systemic cause<br />
无垂体占位效应体征（视野缺损、头痛）；提示微腺瘤或系统性病因可能性大</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Prolactin** secretion is tonically suppressed by **dopamine** from the hypothalamus; any disruption of this inhibitory tone causes prolactin to rise. A second, less-appreciated driver is **TRH (thyrotropin-releasing hormone)**: in primary hypothyroidism, the hypothalamus upregulates TRH to stimulate TSH, but TRH simultaneously acts as a **prolactin-releasing factor** at the anterior pituitary lactotrophs:

**泌乳素**分泌受下丘脑**多巴胺**的持续抑制调控；任何打破这种抑制性调节的因素都会导致泌乳素升高。另一个常被忽视的驱动因素是**TRH（促甲状腺激素释放激素）**：在原发性甲状腺功能减退时，下丘脑上调TRH以刺激TSH分泌，但TRH同时作为**泌乳素释放因子**作用于垂体前叶的泌乳素细胞：

- Hypothyroidism → ↓T3/T4 → ↑TRH (compensatory) → TRH binds pituitary lactotrophs → ↑prolactin → galactorrhea\
  甲状腺功能减退 → T3/T4↓ → TRH代偿性↑ → TRH结合垂体泌乳素细胞 → 泌乳素↑ → 溢乳症

- Dopamine-blocking drugs (haloperidol, metoclopramide) remove tonic inhibition → ↑prolactin\
  多巴胺阻断药（氟哌啶醇、甲氧氯普胺）解除持续性抑制 → 泌乳素↑

- Prolactinoma: autonomous lactotroph secretion independent of regulatory signals\
  泌乳素瘤：泌乳素细胞自主分泌，不受调节信号影响

**Workup rule of thumb:** Check TSH and review medications first; if both are unremarkable, obtain pituitary MRI to evaluate for prolactinoma.

**诊断小窍门:** 先查TSH并排查用药；若两者均正常，再行垂体MRI评估泌乳素瘤。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Thyroid-Stimulating Hormone Measurement / 正确答案 (E) — 测量促甲状腺激素

**TSH measurement** is the essential first step because hypothyroidism is a readily treatable, common cause of hyperprolactinemia that must be excluded before assuming a pituitary adenoma:

**TSH测量**是关键的第一步，因为甲状腺功能减退是高泌乳素血症常见且可治疗的原因，在考虑垂体腺瘤之前必须先排除：

- Elevated TSH with low free T4 confirms primary hypothyroidism → TRH-driven prolactin elevation\
  TSH升高伴游离T4降低证实原发性甲状腺功能减退 → TRH驱动的泌乳素升高

- Treating hypothyroidism with levothyroxine normalizes TRH → prolactin falls → galactorrhea resolves without pituitary-directed therapy\
  左甲状腺素治疗后TRH恢复正常 → 泌乳素下降 → 无需针对垂体治疗，溢乳症自行消失

- If TSH is normal and no offending medications exist, next step is pituitary MRI to evaluate for prolactinoma\
  若TSH正常且无致病药物，下一步为垂体MRI评估泌乳素瘤

**Diagnosis:** Hyperprolactinemia (prolactin \>30 ng/mL in premenopausal women) with galactorrhea 1 year post-lactation; hypothyroidism must be ruled out as the etiology before imaging.

**诊断:** 高泌乳素血症（育龄女性泌乳素\>30 ng/mL），停止哺乳1年后出现溢乳症；影像检查前必须排除甲状腺功能减退作为病因。

**Treatment:** If hypothyroidism confirmed → levothyroxine replacement resolves galactorrhea; if prolactinoma confirmed → cabergoline or bromocriptine (dopamine agonists).

**治疗:** 确认甲状腺功能减退 → 左甲状腺素替代治疗，溢乳症消失；确认泌乳素瘤 → 卡麦角林或溴隐亭（多巴胺激动剂）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cortisol<br />
A — 皮质醇</td>
<td>Cortisol workup is for adrenal disorders or panhypopituitarism; panhypopituitarism causes prolactin deficiency (inability to lactate), not galactorrhea<br />
皮质醇检查适用于肾上腺疾病或全垂体功能减退；全垂体功能减退导致泌乳素缺乏（无法哺乳），而非溢乳症</td>
<td>Galactorrhea with elevated prolactin points to prolactin excess, not HPA axis dysfunction<br />
高泌乳素血症伴溢乳症指向泌乳素过多，而非HPA轴功能障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Dopamine<br />
B — 多巴胺</td>
<td>Serum dopamine levels do not reflect the hypothalamic portal dopamine that regulates prolactin; peripheral serum measurement has no clinical utility here<br />
血清多巴胺水平不能反映调节泌乳素的下丘脑门脉多巴胺；外周血测定在此无临床价值</td>
<td>Dopamine's role is assessed indirectly by reviewing dopamine-blocking medications, not serum level<br />
多巴胺的作用通过审查多巴胺阻断药物间接评估，而非血清水平</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Estrogen<br />
C — 雌激素</td>
<td>Estrogen is not a first-line test in galactorrhea workup; while high-dose estrogen can mildly raise prolactin, it does not explain the elevation seen here<br />
雌激素不是溢乳症检查的一线项目；高剂量雌激素可轻度升高泌乳素，但无法解释此处的升高</td>
<td>FSH/LH are more relevant if pituitary gonadotropin deficiency is suspected; regular menses here make gonadotropin deficiency unlikely<br />
若怀疑垂体促性腺激素缺乏，FSH/LH更相关；月经规律使促性腺激素缺乏可能性低</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Gonadotropin-releasing hormone<br />
D — 促性腺激素释放激素</td>
<td>GnRH is not routinely measurable as a serum test and is not part of the standard hyperprolactinemia workup<br />
GnRH通常无法作为常规血清检测项目，也不是高泌乳素血症的标准检查流程</td>
<td>Regular menses confirm intact GnRH-LH/FSH axis; GnRH measurement adds no diagnostic value here<br />
月经规律证实GnRH-LH/FSH轴完整；GnRH测量在此无诊断价值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Thyroid-stimulating hormone ✓<br />
E — 促甲状腺激素 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Hypothyroidism causes compensatory TRH rise, which directly stimulates lactotrophs; TSH is the essential first diagnostic step<br />
正确——甲状腺功能减退导致代偿性TRH升高，直接刺激泌乳素细胞；TSH是关键的第一诊断步骤</td>
<td>Only option targeting a common, treatable systemic cause of hyperprolactinemia; treating hypothyroidism alone resolves the galactorrhea<br />
唯一针对高泌乳素血症常见且可治疗的系统性病因的选项；仅治疗甲状腺功能减退即可消除溢乳症</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The classic distractor is choice A (cortisol): candidates incorrectly reason that any pituitary-adjacent problem should prompt an HPA axis evaluation, but isolated hyperprolactinemia with galactorrhea does not implicate the corticotroph axis — cortisol deficiency in panhypopituitarism actually abolishes lactation, not causes it.*

经典干扰项是选项A（皮质醇）：考生错误地认为任何涉及垂体的问题都应评估HPA轴，但单纯高泌乳素血症伴溢乳症不涉及促肾上腺皮质激素细胞轴——全垂体功能减退中的皮质醇缺乏实际上是抑制泌乳，而非引起溢乳。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Hypothyroidism vs. Prolactinoma vs. Drug-Induced Hyperprolactinemia / 甲状腺功能减退 vs. 泌乳素瘤 vs. 药物性高泌乳素血症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Hypothyroidism</strong><br />
<strong>甲状腺功能减退</strong></th>
<th><strong>Prolactinoma</strong><br />
<strong>泌乳素瘤</strong></th>
<th><strong>Drug-Induced</strong><br />
<strong>药物性</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Prolactin level<br />
泌乳素水平</td>
<td>Mildly elevated (30–100 ng/mL)<br />
轻度升高（30–100 ng/mL）</td>
<td>Often markedly elevated (&gt;200 ng/mL in macroadenoma)<br />
通常显著升高（大腺瘤&gt;200 ng/mL）</td>
<td>Variable, usually mild–moderate<br />
不定，通常轻–中度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key additional symptoms<br />
其他关键症状</td>
<td>Fatigue, cold intolerance, weight gain, constipation, dry skin<br />
疲劳、畏寒、体重增加、便秘、皮肤干燥</td>
<td>Headache, bitemporal hemianopsia (macroadenoma)<br />
头痛、双颞侧偏盲（大腺瘤）</td>
<td>Symptoms of primary condition (e.g., psychosis, nausea)<br />
原发病症状（如精神病、恶心）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Menses<br />
月经</td>
<td>May be irregular but often present<br />
可不规律但通常存在</td>
<td>Amenorrhea (with higher prolactin levels)<br />
闭经（泌乳素较高时）</td>
<td>Variable<br />
不定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First diagnostic test<br />
首要诊断检查</td>
<td>TSH + free T4<br />
TSH + 游离T4</td>
<td>Pituitary MRI (after excluding systemic causes)<br />
垂体MRI（排除系统性原因后）</td>
<td>Medication history review<br />
用药史回顾</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Levothyroxine — resolves galactorrhea<br />
左甲状腺素——溢乳症消失</td>
<td>Cabergoline / bromocriptine; surgery if refractory<br />
卡麦角林/溴隐亭；难治性者手术</td>
<td>Discontinue or switch the offending drug<br />
停用或更换致病药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Workup priority<br />
检查优先级</td>
<td>Always rule out first — cheap and treatable<br />
始终首先排除——廉价且可治疗</td>
<td>Step 2 after TSH/meds are negative<br />
TSH/用药阴性后的第2步</td>
<td>Step 1 alongside TSH<br />
与TSH同为第1步</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a woman with galactorrhea and elevated prolactin who stopped breastfeeding over 6 months ago and takes no medications, measure TSH first — hypothyroidism drives compensatory TRH rise that directly stimulates pituitary lactotrophs.**

**对于停止哺乳\>6个月、无用药史、出现溢乳症伴泌乳素升高的女性，首先测量TSH——甲状腺功能减退驱动代偿性TRH升高，直接刺激垂体泌乳素细胞。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — STAMP Causes of Hyperprolactinemia / 记忆钩 — STAMP 助记高泌乳素血症病因:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ystemic (hypothyroidism): TRH↑ → lactotroph stimulation — check TSH first / 系统性（甲状腺功能减退）：TRH↑ → 泌乳素细胞受刺激 — 先查TSH<br />
• <strong>T</strong>umor (prolactinoma): autonomous adenoma — MRI after TSH is normal / 肿瘤（泌乳素瘤）：自主性腺瘤 — TSH正常后查MRI<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ntipsychotics (D2 blockers): remove dopamine inhibition / 抗精神病药（D2阻断剂）：解除多巴胺抑制<br />
• <strong>M</strong>etoclopramide / domperidone (GI prokinetics): same D2-blockade mechanism / 甲氧氯普胺/多潘立酮（胃肠道促动力药）：同一D2阻断机制<br />
• <strong>P</strong>regnancy / lactation: physiologic — resolves within weeks of weaning / 妊娠/哺乳：生理性 — 断奶后数周消退</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hyperprolactinemia Workup & Physiology / 高频知识表 — 高泌乳素血症的检查流程与生理学

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Hyperprolactinemia definition<br />
高泌乳素血症定义</td>
<td>&gt;30 ng/mL in premenopausal women; &gt;20 ng/mL in men and postmenopausal women<br />
育龄女性&gt;30 ng/mL；男性和绝经后女性&gt;20 ng/mL</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TRH–prolactin connection<br />
TRH–泌乳素联系</td>
<td>TRH stimulates both TSH and prolactin from anterior pituitary; hypothyroidism → ↑TRH → hyperprolactinemia<br />
TRH刺激垂体前叶同时分泌TSH和泌乳素；甲状腺功能减退→TRH↑→高泌乳素血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dopamine regulation<br />
多巴胺调节</td>
<td>Dopamine is the primary tonic inhibitor of prolactin via D2 receptors on lactotrophs; D2 blockade or dopamine deficiency raises prolactin<br />
多巴胺通过泌乳素细胞上的D2受体持续抑制泌乳素；D2阻断或多巴胺缺乏导致泌乳素升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic workup sequence<br />
诊断检查顺序</td>
<td>Step 1: TSH + medication review → Step 2: Pituitary MRI → Step 3: Full pituitary hormone panel if mass found<br />
第1步：TSH+用药回顾 → 第2步：垂体MRI → 第3步：发现占位后查全套垂体激素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prolactinoma size classification<br />
泌乳素瘤大小分类</td>
<td>Microadenoma &lt;10 mm (prolactin 30–200); macroadenoma ≥10 mm (prolactin often &gt;200, can cause bitemporal hemianopsia)<br />
微腺瘤&lt;10 mm（泌乳素30–200）；大腺瘤≥10 mm（泌乳素通常&gt;200，可致双颞侧偏盲）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment of prolactinoma<br />
泌乳素瘤一线治疗</td>
<td>Dopamine agonists (cabergoline preferred over bromocriptine): normalize prolactin and reduce tumor size in &gt;80% of cases<br />
多巴胺激动剂（卡麦角林优于溴隐亭）：&gt;80%病例可使泌乳素正常化并缩小肿瘤体积</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physiologic galactorrhea timeline<br />
生理性溢乳的时间线</td>
<td>Prolactin returns to pre-pregnancy baseline within weeks of weaning; persistence beyond 6 months warrants formal workup<br />
断奶后数周内泌乳素恢复妊娠前基线；超过6个月仍持续者需进行正式检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Renal failure as a cause:** Kidneys clear prolactin; chronic kidney disease can cause hyperprolactinemia even without pituitary pathology — check serum creatinine if TSH and medications are unremarkable\
  **肾衰竭作为病因:** 肾脏负责清除泌乳素；慢性肾病即使无垂体病变也可致高泌乳素血症——若TSH和用药排查无异常，需查血肌酐

- **Macroprolactinemia (big-big prolactin):** IgG-bound prolactin is biologically inactive; serum prolactin appears elevated but patient is asymptomatic; confirmed by polyethylene glycol precipitation — avoids unnecessary MRI\
  **巨泌乳素血症（大-大泌乳素）:** IgG结合的泌乳素无生物活性；血清泌乳素看似升高但患者无症状；聚乙二醇沉淀法确认——避免不必要的MRI检查

- **Cabergoline vs. bromocriptine in pregnancy planning:** Cabergoline is preferred for efficacy and tolerability generally, but bromocriptine is favored in women actively trying to conceive due to its longer safety data during early pregnancy\
  **备孕时卡麦角林 vs. 溴隐亭的选择:** 卡麦角林在疗效和耐受性方面通常更优，但对于积极备孕的女性，溴隐亭因其妊娠早期安全数据更充分而更受青睐

- **Variant — nipple discharge without elevated prolactin:** If discharge is unilateral, bloody, or serous (not milky), think intraductal papilloma or malignancy — prolactin level will be normal and workup pivots to mammography/ductography\
  **题目变式——泌乳素正常的乳头溢液:** 若溢液为单侧、血性或浆液性（非乳白色），考虑导管内乳头状瘤或恶性肿瘤——泌乳素水平正常，检查转向乳腺钼靶/乳腺导管造影

# Question 120 — Uncontrolled Hypertension in Post-MI Patient with Diabetes / 心肌梗死后合并糖尿病的高血压未达标

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician for a follow-up examination. One year ago, he sustained a <strong>myocardial infarction</strong>. He has coronary artery disease, hypertension, and <strong>type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong>. His medications are atorvastatin, lisinopril, metformin, metoprolol, and aspirin. He has smoked one-half pack of cigarettes daily for 25 years. He is 178 cm (5 ft 10 in) tall and weighs 97 kg (213 lb); BMI is <strong>31 kg/m²</strong>. He feels well. His pulse is 62/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 145/78 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows no other abnormalities. Laboratory studies show a <strong>hemoglobin A1c of 6.5%</strong> and serum <strong>LDL-cholesterol concentration of 110 mg/dL</strong>. Serum electrolyte, urea nitrogen, glucose, and creatinine concentrations are within the reference ranges. The physician recommends smoking cessation. Addition of which of the following is the most appropriate next step in pharmacotherapy?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Addition of which of the following is the most appropriate next step in pharmacotherapy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Clonidine<br />
B) Exenatide<br />
C) Hydrochlorothiazide<br />
D) Rosiglitazone<br />
E) Sitagliptin<br />
F) Spironolactone</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Prior myocardial infarction (1 year ago)<br />
1年前心肌梗死史</td>
<td>Establishes very high cardiovascular risk; mandates secondary prevention targets<br />
确立极高心血管风险；要求达到二级预防目标</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Type 2 diabetes mellitus<br />
2型糖尿病</td>
<td>Lowers BP target to &lt;130/80 mmHg (vs. &lt;140/90 for general adults)<br />
将血压目标降至&lt;130/80 mmHg（普通成人为&lt;140/90）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood pressure 145/78 mmHg<br />
血压145/78 mmHg</td>
<td>Above goal for DM + CVD patient; the single uncontrolled parameter in this scenario<br />
超过DM合并CVD患者的目标值；本题中唯一未达标的参数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Already on lisinopril<br />
已在使用赖诺普利</td>
<td>First-line ACE inhibitor in place; BP still uncontrolled → need to add a second agent<br />
已使用一线ACE抑制剂；血压仍未达标→需要加用第二种药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HbA1c 6.5%<br />
糖化血红蛋白6.5%</td>
<td>At acceptable goal for known CVD patient; tighter control risks hypoglycemia without benefit<br />
对已知CVD患者而言已达可接受目标；过度控制增加低血糖风险而无获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Electrolytes and creatinine normal<br />
电解质和肌酐正常</td>
<td>No contraindication to thiazide diuretic; safe to add HCTZ<br />
无噻嗪类利尿剂禁忌；可安全加用HCTZ</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Antihypertensive combination therapy** in patients with **diabetes mellitus** and **established cardiovascular disease** targets a BP goal of \<130/80 mmHg to minimize end-organ damage and recurrent events:

在**糖尿病**合并**已确立心血管疾病**的患者中，**联合降压治疗**的目标是血压\<130/80 mmHg，以最大限度减少器官损害和复发事件：

- ACE inhibitors (lisinopril) block the renin-angiotensin-aldosterone system, providing both antihypertensive and renoprotective effects; they are first-line in DM+HTN\
  ACE抑制剂（赖诺普利）阻断肾素-血管紧张素-醛固酮系统，既降压又保护肾脏；是DM合并高血压的一线用药

- **Thiazide diuretics** (hydrochlorothiazide) inhibit the Na-Cl cotransporter in the distal convoluted tubule → reduced sodium retention → lower blood volume → lower BP\
  **噻嗪类利尿剂**（氢氯噻嗪）抑制远曲小管Na-Cl共转运体→减少钠潴留→降低血容量→降低血压

- The combination of ACE inhibitor + thiazide is synergistic: ACE inhibition prevents the compensatory RAAS activation that would blunt the diuretic's effect\
  ACE抑制剂+噻嗪类利尿剂联用具有协同效应：ACE抑制防止代偿性RAAS激活从而避免抵消利尿剂的效果

**Pharmacotherapy rule of thumb:** When BP exceeds goal in a diabetic post-MI patient already on an ACE inhibitor, add a thiazide diuretic — not a glycemic agent, even if the patient has diabetes.

**药物治疗小窍门:** 已用ACE抑制剂的糖尿病心梗后患者血压仍超标时，应加噻嗪类利尿剂——而不是降糖药，即使患者有糖尿病。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Hydrochlorothiazide for Uncontrolled Hypertension / 正确答案 (C) — 加用氢氯噻嗪控制未达标高血压

**Hydrochlorothiazide** is the appropriate second antihypertensive agent to add when BP remains above the \<130/80 mmHg target despite ACE inhibitor therapy:

**氢氯噻嗪**是在ACE抑制剂治疗后血压仍未达到\<130/80 mmHg目标时应加用的第二种降压药：

- Current BP 145/78 mmHg exceeds the \<130/80 mmHg goal mandated by DM + prior MI; the systolic gap is ~15 mmHg\
  目前血压145/78 mmHg超过DM合并既往心梗要求的\<130/80 mmHg目标；收缩压差距约15 mmHg

- Thiazide diuretics are guideline-recommended as complementary agents to ACE inhibitors/ARBs, with proven CV outcome benefit\
  噻嗪类利尿剂是指南推荐的与ACE抑制剂/ARB互补的药物，具有明确的心血管结局获益

- Normal electrolytes and creatinine confirm no contraindication; monitor for hypokalemia and mild hyperglycemia after initiation\
  电解质和肌酐正常确认无禁忌；启动后监测低钾血症和轻度高血糖

**Diagnosis:** Uncontrolled hypertension above the \<130/80 mmHg goal in a patient with DM and established CAD post-MI; HbA1c 6.5% and LDL 110 are noted but hypertension is the most pressing uncontrolled risk factor

**诊断:** DM合并CAD心梗后患者高血压未达\<130/80 mmHg目标；HbA1c 6.5%和LDL 110已记录，但高血压是最迫切的未控制危险因素

**Treatment:** Add hydrochlorothiazide; continue lisinopril, metoprolol, atorvastatin, metformin, aspirin; reinforce smoking cessation; reassess BP and electrolytes at follow-up

**治疗:** 加用氢氯噻嗪；继续赖诺普利、美托洛尔、阿托伐他汀、二甲双胍、阿司匹林；强调戒烟；随访时复查血压和电解质

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Clonidine<br />
A — 可乐定</td>
<td>Not first- or second-line antihypertensive; alpha-2 agonist with rebound hypertension risk, sedation, dry mouth; reserved for special situations<br />
非一线或二线降压药；α-2激动剂，有反弹性高血压风险、镇静、口干；用于特殊情况</td>
<td>Thiazides have better safety profile and proven CV outcome data vs. clonidine for routine HTN add-on<br />
噻嗪类比可乐定有更好的安全性和明确的心血管结局数据，用于常规联合降压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Exenatide<br />
B — 艾塞那肽</td>
<td>GLP-1 receptor agonist for glycemic control; HbA1c 6.5% is already at goal for this CVD patient — intensifying glycemia is unnecessary<br />
GLP-1受体激动剂用于降糖；此CVD患者HbA1c 6.5%已达标——强化降糖不必要</td>
<td>Identify the uncontrolled parameter first: BP is out of range, glycemia is not<br />
先识别未达标参数：血压超标，血糖未超标</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hydrochlorothiazide ✓<br />
C — 氢氯噻嗪 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — BP 145/78 exceeds the &lt;130/80 goal for DM+CAD; HCTZ is guideline-preferred second agent after ACE-I<br />
正确——血压145/78超过DM+CAD目标&lt;130/80；HCTZ是ACE抑制剂后指南首选第二药</td>
<td>Correctly identifies hypertension as the uncontrolled risk factor and selects appropriate combination therapy<br />
正确识别高血压为未控制危险因素并选择合适联合治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Rosiglitazone<br />
D — 罗格列酮</td>
<td>Thiazolidinedione class; FDA black box warning for increased risk of myocardial infarction and heart failure; explicitly contraindicated in CAD<br />
噻唑烷二酮类；FDA黑框警告增加心梗和心衰风险；CAD中明确禁忌</td>
<td>Known CAD is a direct contraindication to rosiglitazone; never use in post-MI patients<br />
已知CAD是罗格列酮的直接禁忌；心梗后患者中绝不使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Sitagliptin<br />
E — 西格列汀</td>
<td>DPP-4 inhibitor for glycemic control; same issue as exenatide — HbA1c at goal, no indication to add glycemic agent<br />
DPP-4抑制剂用于降糖；同艾塞那肽——HbA1c已达标，无需加降糖药</td>
<td>Distractor exploiting the "diabetes" framing; always check whether glycemia is actually uncontrolled<br />
利用"糖尿病"背景设置的干扰项；始终检查血糖是否真正未达标</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Spironolactone<br />
F — 螺内酯</td>
<td>Aldosterone antagonist/potassium-sparing diuretic; indicated for HFrEF, hyperaldosteronism, or resistant HTN; not routine second-line<br />
醛固酮拮抗剂/保钾利尿剂；适用于HFrEF、醛固酮增多症或顽固性高血压；非常规二线</td>
<td>No signs of volume overload, reduced EF, or hyperaldosteronism; normal electrolytes; no indication<br />
无容量超负荷、EF降低或醛固酮增多症表现；电解质正常；无适应证</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Exenatide or Sitagliptin — the "diabetic patient" framing invites candidates to automatically intensify glycemic therapy, overlooking that HbA1c 6.5% is already at goal while BP 145/78 is the actual problem.*

最危险的干扰项是艾塞那肽或西格列汀——"糖尿病患者"的背景容易让考生自动强化降糖，却忽略了HbA1c 6.5%已达标而血压145/78才是真正的问题所在。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — BP Goals and Antihypertensive Selection by Risk Category / 高频知识表 — 不同风险类别的血压目标与降压药选择

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />

<th><strong>General Adult HTN</strong><br />

<td>Thiazide or CCB<br />

</tr>

</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In this post-MI diabetic patient, blood pressure 145/78 is the only uncontrolled parameter — HbA1c is at goal — so the correct next step is adding hydrochlorothiazide to reach the \<130/80 mmHg target, not intensifying glycemic therapy.**

**在这位心梗后糖尿病患者中，血压145/78是唯一未达标参数——HbA1c已达标——因此正确的下一步是加用氢氯噻嗪以达到\<130/80 mmHg目标，而非强化降糖治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "Spot the Outlier" / 记忆钩 — "找出未达标项":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>P 145/78 → ABOVE goal (&lt;130/80 for DM+CVD) → add antihypertensive / <strong>血</strong>压145/78→超目标值（DM+CVD要求&lt;130/80）→加降压药<br />
• <strong>H</strong>bA1c 6.5% → AT goal for CVD patient → do NOT intensify / <strong>糖</strong>化血红蛋白6.5%→CVD患者已达标→不强化降糖<br />
• <strong>R</strong>osiglitazone → BANNED in CAD (black box: MI + HF risk) / <strong>罗</strong>格列酮→CAD禁用（黑框：心梗+心衰风险）<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hiazide pairs with ACE-I synergistically → step 2 in BP ladder / <strong>噻</strong>嗪类与ACE抑制剂协同→血压阶梯第二步</p></th>
</tr>
