## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Secondary Prevention and BP Management After ACS / 高频知识表 — ACS后二级预防与血压管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>BP goal: DM or CKD<br />
血压目标：DM或CKD</td>
<td>&lt;130/80 mmHg per AHA/ACC guidelines; stricter than general population threshold of &lt;140/90<br />
AHA/ACC指南要求&lt;130/80 mmHg；比普通人群&lt;140/90更严格</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mandatory post-ACS drug quartet<br />
ACS后必须使用的四联方案</td>
<td>Aspirin + high-intensity statin + ACE-I (or ARB) + beta-blocker; all 4 independently reduce mortality<br />
阿司匹林+高强度他汀+ACE抑制剂（或ARB）+β受体阻滞剂；四药各自独立降低死亡率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HbA1c target in established CVD<br />
已确立CVD患者的HbA1c目标</td>
<td>7.0–7.5% is acceptable; aggressive control (&lt;6.5%) increases hypoglycemia with no CV benefit; individualize<br />
7.0-7.5%可接受；激进控制（&lt;6.5%）增加低血糖且无心血管获益；个体化决策</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rosiglitazone CV risk<br />
罗格列酮心血管风险</td>
<td>FDA black box: increased MI and heart failure; entire TZD class avoided in CAD; pioglitazone also causes fluid retention<br />
FDA黑框：增加心梗和心衰；CAD中避免整个TZD类；吡格列酮也引起液体潴留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thiazide diuretic metabolic effects<br />
噻嗪类利尿剂代谢影响</td>
<td>Hypokalemia, mild hyperglycemia, hyperuricemia, hyponatremia (SIADH-like); monitor electrolytes; low doses minimize risk<br />
低钾血症、轻度高血糖、高尿酸血症、低钠血症（类SIADH）；监测电解质；低剂量可降低风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spironolactone indications vs. HTN<br />
螺内酯适应证与高血压</td>
<td>Indicated: HFrEF (EF&lt;35%), primary hyperaldosteronism, resistant HTN (4+ agents); NOT routine step 2 for uncomplicated HTN<br />
适应证：HFrEF（EF&lt;35%）、原发性醛固酮增多症、顽固性高血压（4种以上药物）；不是未并发症高血压的常规第二步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LDL target post-ACS<br />
ACS后LDL目标</td>
<td>&lt;70 mg/dL for very high-risk; this patient at 110 mg/dL suggests statin intensification or adding ezetimibe is a separate future consideration<br />
极高危患者&lt;70 mg/dL；此患者110 mg/dL提示强化他汀或加依折麦布是独立的未来考量</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Dual RAAS blockade warning:** Combining an ACE inhibitor + ARB (dual blockade) is not recommended — increases hyperkalemia, hypotension, and acute kidney injury without additional CV benefit\
  **双重RAAS阻断警告:** ACE抑制剂+ARB联合（双重阻断）不推荐——在无额外心血管获益的情况下增加高钾血症、低血压和急性肾损伤风险

- **Smoking cessation pharmacotherapy:** First-line agents are varenicline (most effective), bupropion, and NRT patches/gum; clonidine is a second-line cessation aid — its antihypertensive use is reserved for specific situations\
  **戒烟药物治疗:** 一线药物是伐尼克兰（最有效）、安非他酮和NRT贴片/口香糖；可乐定是二线戒烟辅助药——其降压用途仅限于特定情况

- **GLP-1 agonist CV benefit exception:** Newer GLP-1 agonists (semaglutide, liraglutide) have proven CV benefit in high-risk DM patients — unlike exenatide, which lacks this outcome data; if glycemia were uncontrolled, semaglutide would be preferred\
  **GLP-1激动剂心血管获益例外:** 新型GLP-1激动剂（司美格鲁肽、利拉鲁肽）在高风险DM患者中有明确心血管获益——不同于缺乏此数据的艾塞那肽；若血糖未达标，司美格鲁肽将是优选

- **LDL intensification strategy:** At 110 mg/dL post-ACS, consider switching to high-intensity statin (rosuvastatin 20–40 mg or atorvastatin 40–80 mg) or adding ezetimibe; PCSK9 inhibitors for statin-intolerant patients\
  **LDL强化策略:** ACS后LDL 110 mg/dL时，考虑换用高强度他汀（瑞舒伐他汀20-40 mg或阿托伐他汀40-80 mg）或加用依折麦布；不耐受他汀的患者考虑PCSK9抑制剂

# Question 121 — Institutional Case Series Study Design / 机构病例系列研究设计

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>60-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>osteoarthritis of the right knee</strong> comes to the office to discuss treatment options, including <strong>total knee replacement</strong>. Medications are naproxen and 81-mg aspirin. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows <strong>edema of the right knee</strong>; range of motion of the right knee is decreased. Results of laboratory studies are within the reference ranges. The patient asks the physician about the <strong>success and complication rates</strong> associated with total knee replacement at the <strong>local university hospital</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following types of studies is most appropriate for the physician to reference to answer this patient's question?</strong></p>
<p>A) Case-control study<br />
B) Cross-sectional study<br />
C) Institutional case series<br />
D) Randomized controlled trial</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Success and complication rates<br />
成功率与并发症发生率</td>
<td>Patient is asking for descriptive outcomes data, not a causal comparison between treatments<br />
患者询问的是描述性结局数据，而非治疗之间的因果比较</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>At the local university hospital<br />
在当地大学医院</td>
<td>"Local/institutional" restricts the data source to a single institution — the defining feature of an institutional case series<br />
"当地/机构"将数据来源限定在单一机构——这正是机构病例系列的定义特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Total knee replacement<br />
全膝关节置换术</td>
<td>A specific procedure whose outcomes are trackable within a single hospital's patient cohort<br />
特定外科手术，其结局可在单一医院患者群体中追踪</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Asks the physician about outcomes<br />
向医生询问结局</td>
<td>Implies need for descriptive (not analytic) institutional data, not a generalizable efficacy trial<br />
意味着需要描述性（非分析性）机构数据，而非可推广的疗效试验数据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>60-year-old woman with osteoarthritis<br />
60岁女性，骨关节炎</td>
<td>Establishes clinical context; not directly relevant to study design selection here<br />
建立临床背景；与此处研究设计的选择不直接相关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The question tests ability to match a **clinical question type** to the correct **study design**, specifically recognizing when a patient's question requires institution-specific descriptive data rather than generalizable analytic evidence:

该题考查将**临床问题类型**与正确**研究设计**匹配的能力，尤其是识别患者的问题何时需要机构特定的描述性数据，而非可推广的分析性证据：

- An **institutional case series** is a descriptive observational study that tracks outcomes (success rates, complication rates) in patients sharing a diagnosis or procedure at one institution\
  **机构病例系列**是描述性观察研究，追踪单一机构中具有相同诊断或手术患者的结局（成功率、并发症率）

- It does **not** require a control group, randomization, or hypothesis testing — it simply describes "what happened to our patients"\
  它**不**需要对照组、随机化或假说检验——仅描述"我们的患者发生了什么"

- The word "**local** university hospital" is the critical qualifier: the patient wants to know how *this specific institution* performs, which only an institutional case series from that center can answer\
  "**当地**大学医院"是关键限定词：患者想知道*这家特定机构*的表现如何，只有来自该机构的病例系列才能回答

**Clinical rule of thumb:** When a patient asks "how does THIS hospital do with THIS procedure?" → think **institutional case series**, not RCT

**临床小窍门:** 当患者问"这家医院做这个手术效果如何？" → 想到**机构病例系列**，而非RCT

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Institutional Case Series / 正确答案 (C) — 机构病例系列

**Institutional case series** is a descriptive study design that reports outcomes for a group of patients at a single institution who shared a diagnosis or underwent the same procedure:

**机构病例系列**是描述性研究设计，报告单一机构中具有相同诊断或接受相同手术的一组患者的结局：

- Captures success rates, complication rates, and natural history without requiring a comparison group\
  无需比较组即可捕捉成功率、并发症发生率和自然病史

- Does **not** establish causation or test a hypothesis — purely descriptive\
  **不**建立因果关系或检验假说——纯粹是描述性的

- Provides **institution-specific** data that generalizable multi-center trials (like RCTs) cannot offer\
  提供**机构特定**数据，这是可推广的多中心试验（如RCT）无法提供的

- Especially useful for rare conditions or procedures where large randomized trials are not feasible\
  对于无法开展大型随机试验的罕见疾病或手术尤其有用

- Represents the lowest tier in the evidence hierarchy but is exactly what is needed for this clinical question\
  代表证据层次中的最低层级，但恰好是回答这个临床问题所需要的

**Diagnosis:** Patient needs local hospital-specific outcome data → no comparison group required → institutional case series is the only option that fits

**诊断:** 患者需要当地医院特定的结局数据 → 无需比较组 → 机构病例系列是唯一符合的选项

**Treatment:** N/A — this is a study design question, not a clinical management question

**治疗:** 不适用——这是研究设计题，而非临床管理题

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Case-control study<br />
A — 病例对照研究</td>
<td>Groups patients by outcome status (disease vs. no disease), looks backward for exposure, and reports odds ratios — cannot describe procedure success/complication rates at one institution<br />
按结局状态（患病 vs. 未患病）分组，回顾性分析暴露因素，报告比值比——无法描述一个机构的手术成功率/并发症率</td>
<td>Case-control asks "what caused the outcome?" not "what are the outcomes at our center?"<br />
病例对照研究问"什么导致了结局？"而非"我们中心的结局是什么？"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Cross-sectional study<br />
B — 横断面研究</td>
<td>Captures a snapshot of disease prevalence and risk factors at a single point in time; does not follow patients through a procedure to track longitudinal outcomes<br />
捕捉某一时间点的疾病流行率和危险因素快照；不纵向追踪患者经历手术后的结局</td>
<td>Cross-sectional measures prevalence at one moment, not procedure outcomes over time<br />
横断面测量某一时刻的患病率，而非随时间变化的手术结局</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Institutional case series ✓<br />
C — 机构病例系列 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Describes success and complication rates of a specific procedure at a specific institution; exactly what the patient is requesting<br />
正确——描述特定机构特定手术的成功率和并发症发生率；正是患者所要求的</td>
<td>"Local hospital" + "outcome rates" → institutional case series is the only fit<br />
"当地医院" + "结局率" → 机构病例系列是唯一合适的选项</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Randomized controlled trial<br />
D — 随机对照试验</td>
<td>Gold standard for treatment efficacy; conducted across multiple centers; provides generalizable data — but cannot tell you how one specific local hospital performs<br />
治疗疗效金标准；在多个中心开展；提供可推广数据——但无法告诉你某一特定当地医院的表现如何</td>
<td>RCT answers "is this treatment better than another?" — not "how does our hospital do?"<br />
RCT回答"这种治疗比另一种更好吗？"——而非"我们医院效果如何？"</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is (D) RCT — students conflate "highest-quality evidence" with "best study to answer this patient's specific institutional question"; RCTs are multi-center and cannot provide institution-specific outcome data.*

最诱人的干扰项是（D）RCT——学生容易混淆"最高质量证据"与"回答患者特定机构问题的最佳研究"；RCT是多中心研究，无法提供特定机构的结局数据。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Institutional Case Series vs. Analytic Study Designs / 机构病例系列与分析性研究设计对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Institutional Case Series</strong><br />
<strong>机构病例系列</strong></th>
<th><strong>Analytic Studies (Case-Control / RCT)</strong><br />
<strong>分析性研究（病例对照 / RCT）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Design type<br />
设计类型</td>
<td>Descriptive only<br />
仅描述性</td>
<td>Analytic — tests a hypothesis<br />
分析性——检验假说</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Control group required<br />
是否需要对照组</td>
<td>No<br />
否</td>
<td>Yes<br />
是</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Randomization<br />
随机化</td>
<td>No<br />
否</td>
<td>RCT: Yes; Case-control: No<br />
RCT：是；病例对照：否</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary outcome measure<br />
主要结局指标</td>
<td>Success rate, complication rate<br />
成功率、并发症率</td>
<td>OR (case-control) / RR or ARR (RCT)<br />
比值比（病例对照）/ 相对危险度或绝对危险度降低（RCT）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Establishes causation<br />
能否建立因果关系</td>
<td>No<br />
否</td>
<td>Partially (case-control) / Yes (RCT)<br />
部分（病例对照）/ 是（RCT）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Evidence hierarchy<br />
证据层次</td>
<td>Lowest (descriptive)<br />
最低（描述性）</td>
<td>Higher — RCT is gold standard<br />
更高——RCT是金标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Best answers the question<br />
最适合回答的问题</td>
<td>"How does our hospital do with this procedure?"<br />
"我们医院做这个手术效果如何？"</td>
<td>"Is this treatment better than the alternative?"<br />
"这种治疗比替代方案更好吗？"</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a patient asks about outcomes at a specific institution, the physician references an institutional case series — the only study design that captures procedure-specific results at a single center without requiring a control group or hypothesis testing.**

**当患者询问特定机构的结局时，医生应参考机构病例系列——这是唯一一种在无需对照组或假说检验的情况下，捕捉单一中心特定手术结果的研究设计。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "LOCAL = Case Series" / 记忆钩 — "LOCAL = 病例系列":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>L</strong>ocal hospital question → <strong>L</strong>ook for a case series / 当地医院问题 → 寻找病例系列<br />
• <strong>O</strong>utcomes described, not compared / 描述结局，而非比较结局<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ontrol group absent — no randomization needed / 无对照组——无需随机化<br />
• <strong>A</strong>nalytic studies (CC, RCT) answer "why/better?" not "how does our center do?" / 分析性研究（病例对照、RCT）回答"为什么/更好？"而非"我们中心如何？"<br />
• <strong>L</strong>owest on the evidence hierarchy but perfect for institutional reporting / 证据层次最低，但非常适合机构报告</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Study Design Selection in Clinical Questions / 高频知识表 — 临床问题中的研究设计选择

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Case series definition<br />
病例系列定义</td>
<td>Descriptive study reporting outcomes of patients sharing a diagnosis/procedure; no control group, no randomization, no hypothesis testing; lowest in evidence hierarchy<br />
描述性研究，报告具有相同诊断/手术患者的结局；无对照组、无随机化、无假说检验；证据层次最低</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to choose case series<br />
何时选择病例系列</td>
<td>(1) Patient asks about outcomes at a specific institution; (2) rare diseases where RCTs are infeasible; (3) hypothesis generation for future studies<br />
（1）患者询问特定机构的结局；（2）RCT不可行的罕见病；（3）为未来研究生成假说</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Case-control study<br />
病例对照研究</td>
<td>Retrospective; groups by disease outcome status; measures odds ratio (OR); best for rare outcomes and identifying multiple risk factors<br />
回顾性；按疾病结局状态分组；测量比值比（OR）；最适合罕见结局和识别多种危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cross-sectional study<br />
横断面研究</td>
<td>Single time-point "snapshot"; measures prevalence; analyzes exposure and disease simultaneously; cannot establish temporal sequence<br />
单一时间点"快照"；测量患病率；同时分析暴露和疾病；无法建立时间先后顺序</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RCT key features<br />
RCT关键特征</td>
<td>Prospective; randomized; minimizes confounding; gold standard for efficacy; typically multi-center; measures relative risk (RR) and absolute risk reduction (ARR)<br />
前瞻性；随机化；最小化混杂因素；疗效评价金标准；通常多中心；测量相对危险度（RR）和绝对危险度降低（ARR）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Evidence hierarchy<br />
证据层次</td>
<td>Meta-analysis &gt; Systematic review &gt; RCT &gt; Cohort &gt; Case-control &gt; Cross-sectional &gt; Case series &gt; Expert opinion<br />
荟萃分析 &gt; 系统综述 &gt; RCT &gt; 队列研究 &gt; 病例对照 &gt; 横断面 &gt; 病例系列 &gt; 专家意见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic USMLE trap<br />
经典USMLE陷阱</td>
<td>"Best evidence" ≠ "Best study to answer this question" — RCT is highest quality but wrong when the patient asks about a single local institution's outcomes<br />
"最佳证据"≠"回答该问题的最佳研究"——RCT质量最高，但当患者询问单一当地机构的结局时，RCT并不合适</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Limitations of case series:** Subject to selection bias (only patients at one center), lacks generalizability, cannot determine if outcomes differ from national averages without an external comparison\
  **病例系列的局限性:** 存在选择偏倚（仅限一个中心的患者），缺乏普遍性，若无外部比较则无法确定结局是否与全国平均水平不同

- **Hypothesis generation role:** Case series findings often seed future analytic studies — an unusual complication pattern in a case series can motivate a case-control study to identify its risk factors\
  **假说生成作用:** 病例系列结果通常为未来分析性研究奠定基础——病例系列中异常并发症模式可促使开展病例对照研究以识别其危险因素

- **Rare disease applicability:** For uncommon conditions (e.g., rare surgical complications), sample sizes are too small for adequately powered RCTs or cohort studies; case series remain the primary evidence source\
  **罕见病的适用性:** 对于罕见疾病（如不常见手术并发症），样本量太小无法开展效力足够的RCT或队列研究；病例系列仍是主要证据来源

- **Step 2 CK test strategy:** Any question stem that specifies "at this hospital," "at our institution," or "local center" almost invariably points to institutional case series, regardless of the clinical context surrounding the question\
  **Step 2 CK考试策略:** 任何题干特别指出"在这家医院""在我们机构"或"当地中心"的情况，无论题目的临床背景如何，几乎总是指向机构病例系列

# Question 122 — Seborrheic Keratosis / 脂溢性角化病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>72-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office with her son because of a <strong>"strange mole" on her back</strong> that she first noticed 6 months ago. The patient's son says he thinks it has <strong>enlarged during the past month</strong>. The patient says the mole is <strong>mildly itchy</strong> but <strong>not painful</strong>, and she has <strong>not had bleeding</strong> from the area. She has not had any weight loss or changes in appetite. Medical history is unremarkable, and she takes no medications. The patient has <strong>spent a lot of time outside by her son's new swimming pool</strong> during the past summer months. Vital signs are within normal limits. A photograph of the lesion is shown. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate diagnostic study at this time?</strong></p>
<p>A) Culture of the lesion<br />
B) Full-thickness biopsy of the lesion<br />
C) KOH testing of a scraping of the lesion<br />
D) Shave biopsy of the lesion<br />
E) No diagnostic study is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>72-year-old woman<br />
72 岁女性</td>
<td>Increasing age is the primary risk factor for seborrheic keratosis; lesions are common in middle-aged and older adults<br />
年龄增长是脂溢性角化病的主要危险因素；中老年人群中常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mole enlarged during the past month<br />
近一个月皮损增大</td>
<td>Growth raises concern for malignancy (e.g., melanoma), but in context of classic SK features, gradual benign expansion is consistent<br />
皮损增大可引发恶性肿瘤警觉（如黑色素瘤），但结合典型脂溢性角化病特征，符合良性缓慢生长</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mildly itchy, not painful, no bleeding<br />
轻度瘙痒、无疼痛、无出血</td>
<td>Pruritus is common with SK; absence of bleeding and pain argues against melanoma or ulcerated BCC<br />
瘙痒是脂溢性角化病常见症状；无出血和疼痛有助于排除黑色素瘤或溃疡型基底细胞癌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Significant sun exposure (poolside)<br />
大量日光暴露（泳池旁）</td>
<td>UV exposure is a risk for melanoma/actinic keratosis; SK is primarily age-driven — this clue is intentional distractor<br />
紫外线暴露是黑色素瘤/光化性角化病危险因素；脂溢性角化病主要由年龄驱动——此线索为意图性干扰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No weight loss, no appetite changes<br />
无体重下降、无食欲改变</td>
<td>Absence of systemic B-symptoms argues against paraneoplastic Leser-Trélat context<br />
无全身症状有助于排除副肿瘤性 Leser-Trélat 征的背景</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Photograph of lesion shown (clinical appearance)<br />
图示皮损（临床外观）</td>
<td>SK is diagnosed purely on clinical appearance; the photograph IS the diagnostic tool — no additional study needed<br />
脂溢性角化病纯靠临床外观诊断；照片即为诊断工具——无需额外检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Seborrheic keratosis** is a **benign epidermal proliferation** arising from **keratinocytes** of the epidermis. Unlike malignant neoplasms, SK lesions demonstrate **no cellular atypia** and remain confined above the basement membrane:

**脂溢性角化病**是起源于表皮**角质形成细胞**的**良性表皮增殖**。与恶性肿瘤不同，SK 皮损**无细胞异型性**，局限于基底膜以上：

- Epidermal acanthosis (thickening) without dermal invasion → macroscopic "stuck-on" or waxy appearance\
  表皮棘层增厚（无真皮浸润）→ 宏观呈现"贴附"或蜡质外观

- Keratin-filled horn cysts (pseudocysts) scattered throughout — pathognomonic feature on histology\
  角蛋白填充的角囊肿（假囊）散在分布——组织学上具有特征性

- No dysplasia, no mitotic figures, no lymphocytic infiltrate → entirely benign biological behavior\
  无异型增生、无核分裂象、无淋巴细胞浸润→ 完全良性生物学行为

- Melanin deposition within keratinocytes (not melanocytes) → characteristic brown/tan color\
  黑色素沉积于角质形成细胞（非黑色素细胞）内→ 典型棕色/棕褐色外观

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** SK originates above the basement membrane — it is a purely surface proliferation, never invasive, which is why clinical diagnosis alone is sufficient.

**解剖小窍门:** 脂溢性角化病起源于基底膜以上——属纯粹表面增殖，绝无侵袭性，因此临床诊断已完全足够。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Clinical Diagnosis of Seborrheic Keratosis / 正确答案 (E) — 脂溢性角化病的临床诊断

**Seborrheic keratosis** is diagnosed entirely on clinical appearance — no biopsy, culture, or laboratory test is required when the lesion displays classic features:

**脂溢性角化病**完全依赖临床外观诊断——当皮损呈现典型特征时，无需活检、培养或实验室检查：

- Round, well-demarcated, raised plaque with a "stuck-on" or waxy texture; surface may be verrucous or granular\
  圆形、边界清晰、隆起斑块，呈"贴附"或蜡质质感；表面可呈疣状或颗粒状

- Color ranges from tan to dark brown; multiple lesions common in the elderly\
  颜色从棕褐色到深棕色不等；老年患者常见多发皮损

- Lesions may be pruritic but are not painful; no ulceration or bleeding in uncomplicated cases\
  皮损可伴瘙痒但无疼痛；无并发症时无溃疡或出血

**Diagnosis:** Clinical appearance alone is sufficient; when the photograph shows a classic stuck-on waxy brown plaque in a 72-year-old, no further workup is warranted.

**诊断:** 单凭临床外观即可确诊；当照片显示 72 岁患者典型蜡质棕色贴附性斑块时，无需进一步检查。

**Treatment:** Not required for benign SK; cosmetically bothersome or irritated lesions may be removed by cryotherapy, curettage, or simple excision.

**治疗:** 良性脂溢性角化病无需治疗；影响美观或反复刺激者可行冷冻、刮除或简单切除。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Culture of the lesion<br />
A — 皮损培养</td>
<td>Wrong — SK is a benign keratinocyte proliferation, not an infectious process; cultures are appropriate for bacterial abscess or fungal cellulitis, not SK<br />
错误——脂溢性角化病是良性角质形成细胞增殖，非感染性病变；培养适用于细菌脓肿或真菌感染，不适用于本病</td>
<td>SK has no infectious etiology<br />
脂溢性角化病无感染性病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Full-thickness biopsy of the lesion<br />
B — 全层活检</td>
<td>Wrong — Full-thickness (excisional/punch) biopsy is reserved for lesions where Breslow thickness determination is necessary (e.g., suspected melanoma); SK diagnosed clinically needs no biopsy<br />
错误——全层活检用于需测定 Breslow 厚度的皮损（如疑似黑色素瘤）；临床诊断脂溢性角化病无需活检</td>
<td>Biopsy depth matters for melanoma staging, not SK<br />
活检深度对黑色素瘤分期重要，对脂溢性角化病无意义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — KOH testing of a scraping of the lesion<br />
C — 皮损刮屑 KOH 检测</td>
<td>Wrong — KOH preparation detects fungal hyphae/spores; used for tinea corporis and tinea versicolor; SK has no fungal etiology<br />
错误——KOH 制备用于检测真菌菌丝/孢子，适用于体癣和花斑癣；脂溢性角化病无真菌病因</td>
<td>No scaling satellite lesions; no fungal involvement<br />
无鳞屑卫星皮损；无真菌参与</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Shave biopsy of the lesion<br />
D — 刮除活检</td>
<td>Wrong — Shave biopsy is acceptable for superficial BCC but would transect a melanoma and prevent accurate Breslow staging; SK requires no biopsy at all<br />
错误——刮除活检适用于浅表基底细胞癌，但会切断黑色素瘤并妨碍 Breslow 分期；脂溢性角化病根本无需活检</td>
<td>Appropriate for BCC; not for SK or suspected melanoma<br />
适用于基底细胞癌；不适用于脂溢性角化病或疑似黑色素瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No diagnostic study is indicated ✓<br />
E — 无需诊断性检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Classic clinical presentation of SK (stuck-on waxy brown plaque, elderly patient, pruritic, no bleeding) is sufficient for clinical diagnosis without additional workup<br />
正确——脂溢性角化病典型临床表现（蜡质棕色贴附性斑块、老年患者、瘙痒、无出血）足以临床诊断，无需额外检查</td>
<td>Diagnosis by clinical appearance alone<br />
单凭临床外观即可诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is D (shave biopsy) — test-takers may feel compelled to biopsy any enlarging pigmented lesion; recognizing the classic "stuck-on" waxy morphology of SK as sufficient for clinical diagnosis is the key discriminating skill.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 D（刮除活检）——考生见到生长中的色素性皮损往往倾向活检；识别脂溢性角化病典型"贴附"蜡质形态即可临床诊断，是本题核心鉴别技能。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Seborrheic Keratosis vs. Melanoma vs. Actinic Keratosis / 脂溢性角化病 vs. 黑色素瘤 vs. 光化性角化病

<colgroup>

<th><strong>Melanoma</strong><br />

<td>None required; cryotherapy if bothersome<br />
无需治疗；影响美观可行冷冻</td>
<td>Excision with margins; ± sentinel node biopsy<br />
手术切除（安全切缘）± 前哨淋巴结活检</td>
<td>Topical 5-FU, imiquimod, cryotherapy<br />
外用 5-氟尿嘧啶、咪喹莫特、冷冻疗法</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Seborrheic keratosis is a benign, age-related epidermal keratinocyte proliferation with a classic waxy "stuck-on" appearance that is diagnosed purely by clinical inspection — no biopsy, culture, or lab work is indicated.**

**脂溢性角化病是良性、年龄相关性表皮角质形成细胞增殖，具有经典蜡质"贴附"外观，纯靠临床视诊诊断——无需活检、培养或实验室检查。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — STUCK Mnemonic for SK / 记忆钩 — SK 的"STUCK"助记法:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>tuck-on waxy appearance — looks pasted onto skin, not growing from within / 贴附蜡质外观——像粘贴在皮肤上，非来自皮肤深部<br />
• <strong>T</strong>an-to-brown color — melanin deposited in keratinocytes, NOT melanocytes / 棕褐至棕色——黑色素沉积于角质细胞，而非黑色素细胞<br />
• <strong>U</strong>V not the main driver — age is; sun exposure in stem is a distractor / 紫外线非主要驱动因素——年龄才是；题干中的日晒是干扰项<br />
• <strong>C</strong>linical diagnosis only — no biopsy, no KOH, no culture needed / 仅凭临床诊断——无需活检、KOH 检测或培养<br />
• <strong>K</strong>eratinocyte acanthosis + horn cysts — hallmark histology / 角质形成细胞棘层增厚伴角囊肿——组织学标志性特征</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Seborrheic Keratosis & Pigmented Skin Lesions / 高频知识表 — 脂溢性角化病与色素性皮损

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic histology of SK<br />
脂溢性角化病典型组织学</td>
<td>Acanthotic epidermis, hyperkeratosis, horn cysts (keratin pseudocysts), no atypia, no dermal invasion<br />
表皮棘层增厚、角化过度、角囊肿（角蛋白假囊），无异型性，无真皮浸润</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leser-Trélat sign<br />
Leser-Trélat 征</td>
<td>Sudden eruption of numerous SK lesions → paraneoplastic marker for GI malignancy (especially gastric adenocarcinoma); also associated with lymphoma<br />
脂溢性角化病皮损骤然大量出现→副肿瘤综合征标志，提示消化道恶性肿瘤（尤其胃腺癌）；也与淋巴瘤相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SK vs. melanoma key differentiator<br />
脂溢性角化病与黑色素瘤的关键鉴别</td>
<td>SK: uniform stuck-on texture, no bleeding, pruritic not painful; Melanoma: ABCDE criteria (Asymmetry, Border irregularity, Color variation, Diameter &gt;6 mm, Evolution)<br />
脂溢性角化病：均匀贴附质感、无出血、瘙痒非疼痛；黑色素瘤：ABCDE 标准（不对称、边缘不规则、颜色多变、直径&gt;6mm、演变）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to biopsy a pigmented lesion<br />
色素性皮损何时需要活检</td>
<td>Biopsy indicated if: irregular border, color heterogeneity, diameter &gt;6 mm, bleeding, rapid unexplained growth, or clinical uncertainty; classic SK → no biopsy<br />
以下情况需活检：边缘不规则、颜色不均、直径&gt;6mm、出血、快速不明原因增大或临床不确定；典型脂溢性角化病→无需活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biopsy type by suspected diagnosis<br />
不同疑似诊断对应的活检类型</td>
<td>Melanoma: excisional/punch biopsy (Breslow thickness); BCC: shave biopsy acceptable; SCC: punch biopsy preferred; SK: none required<br />
黑色素瘤：切除/钻孔活检（测 Breslow 厚度）；基底细胞癌：刮除活检可接受；鳞状细胞癌：优选钻孔活检；脂溢性角化病：无需活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>KOH preparation — indications<br />
KOH 制备——适应证</td>
<td>KOH dissolves keratin to visualize fungal hyphae/spores; used for tinea corporis (dermatophytes), tinea versicolor (Malassezia furfur), cutaneous candidiasis; NOT appropriate for SK<br />
KOH 溶解角质以显示真菌菌丝/孢子；适用于体癣（皮肤癣菌）、花斑癣（糠秕马拉色菌）、皮肤念珠菌病；不适用于脂溢性角化病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment options for SK<br />
脂溢性角化病的治疗选择</td>
<td>No treatment required for asymptomatic SK; symptomatic/cosmetically bothersome lesions: cryotherapy (first-line), curettage, electrodessication, laser ablation, or topical 40% hydrogen peroxide (FDA-approved)<br />
无症状脂溢性角化病无需治疗；有症状或影响美观者：冷冻疗法（一线）、刮除、电干燥、激光消融或 40% 过氧化氢外用（FDA 批准）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of pruritic pigmented skin lesions:** Seborrheic keratosis (stuck-on waxy, benign, clinical diagnosis), melanoma (ABCDE positive, urgent excisional biopsy), dysplastic nevus (irregular pigmentation, family history), dermatofibroma (dimple sign positive, fibrous texture)\
  **色素性瘙痒皮损的鉴别诊断:** 脂溢性角化病（蜡质贴附，良性，临床诊断）、黑色素瘤（ABCDE 阳性，急需切除活检）、异型痣（色素不规则，家族史）、皮肤纤维瘤（酒窝征阳性，纤维质感）

- **Leser-Trélat sign workup:** Sudden eruption of multiple SK lesions should prompt GI malignancy evaluation (colonoscopy, upper endoscopy, CT abdomen/pelvis) — the skin finding may precede the tumor diagnosis by months\
  **Leser-Trélat 征的处理:** 多发脂溢性角化病皮损骤然出现应提示消化道恶性肿瘤评估（结肠镜、上消化道内镜、腹盆 CT）——皮肤表现可早于肿瘤诊断数月出现

- **Exam trap — sun exposure as distractor:** NBME frequently includes UV/poolside history with SK questions to prompt consideration of actinic keratosis or melanoma; SK is age-driven, not UV-driven — resist the urge to order KOH or biopsy\
  **考试陷阱——日晒作为干扰因素:** NBME 常在脂溢性角化病题目中加入泳池旁日晒史，诱导考虑光化性角化病或黑色素瘤；脂溢性角化病由年龄驱动而非紫外线——克制进行 KOH 检测或活检的冲动

- **Key complication to know:** Irritated SK (from repeated friction/trauma) can become inflamed and mimic more aggressive lesions; even then, clinical recognition and reassurance — not biopsy — remain appropriate in classic presentations\
  **需掌握的关键并发症:** 受刺激的脂溢性角化病（反复摩擦/外伤所致）可发生炎症，外观类似更具侵袭性的皮损；即便如此，典型表现下仍以临床识别和观察随访为主，而非活检

# Question 123 — Septic Shock with Adrenal Crisis / 脓毒性休克合并肾上腺危象

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>27-year-old woman</strong> is brought to the emergency department because of a <strong>2-day history of fever, pain with urination, and progressive generalized weakness</strong>. She has <strong>systemic lupus erythematosus</strong> complicated by nephritis. Current medications include <strong>prednisone and cyclophosphamide</strong>. Her <strong>temperature is 39.4°C (103°F), pulse is 122/min, respirations are 24/min, and blood pressure is 88/62 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows warm, flushed skin. There is moderate suprapubic and right flank tenderness. Her <strong>leukocyte count is 18,000/mm³ (80% segmented neutrophils, 5% bands</strong>, 1% basophils, 10% lymphocytes, and 3% monocytes). Urinalysis shows <strong>100 WBC/hpf</strong>. A Gram stain shows numerous <strong>gram-negative rods</strong>. Intravenous administration of piperacillin and tazobactam and 2 liters of 0.9% saline is started. Thirty minutes later, her <strong>pulse is 124/min, and blood pressure is 92/68 mm Hg</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Administration of ciprofloxacin<br />
B) Administration of gentamicin<br />
C) Administration of hydrocortisone<br />
D) Administration of metoprolol<br />
E) Cardioversion</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Chronic prednisone use<br />
长期使用泼尼松</td>
<td>Exogenous steroids suppress the HPA axis → adrenal glands atrophy and cannot mount a cortisol stress response<br />
外源性激素抑制下丘脑-垂体-肾上腺轴 → 肾上腺萎缩，无法产生应激所需皮质醇</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 88/62 → 92/68 after 2L NS + antibiotics<br />
补液2L加抗生素后血压仅从88/62升至92/68</td>
<td>Hypotension refractory to initial resuscitation signals a cause beyond sepsis alone — adrenal crisis must be considered<br />
初始液体复苏后血压无明显改善，提示存在脓毒症以外的病因——必须考虑肾上腺危象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever + dysuria + right flank tenderness + gram-negative rods<br />
发热 + 排尿疼痛 + 右腰部压痛 + 革兰阴性杆菌</td>
<td>Confirms pyelonephritis/urosepsis as the acute infectious stressor that precipitated adrenal crisis<br />
确认肾盂肾炎/尿路脓毒症为诱发肾上腺危象的急性感染应激源</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia 122/min, warm flushed skin, RR 24<br />
心率122次/分、皮肤温暖潮红、呼吸24次/分</td>
<td>Signs of distributive (septic) shock — vasodilation with inadequate vascular tone<br />
分布性（脓毒性）休克表现——血管扩张、血管张力不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Progressive generalized weakness<br />
进行性全身无力</td>
<td>Non-specific early symptom of adrenal insufficiency; often overlooked amid the sepsis picture<br />
肾上腺功能不全的非特异性早期表现，在脓毒症背景下容易被忽视</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SLE on cyclophosphamide + prednisone<br />
SLE使用环磷酰胺+泼尼松</td>
<td>Dual significance: immunosuppression increases infection risk AND confirms HPA axis suppression<br />
双重意义：免疫抑制增加感染风险，同时确认HPA轴被外源性激素抑制</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Secondary adrenal insufficiency** from chronic exogenous steroid use causes **HPA axis suppression**, leaving the adrenal glands atrophied and unable to upregulate **cortisol** during physiologic stress:

长期外源性激素所致的**继发性肾上腺功能不全**造成**HPA轴抑制**，肾上腺萎缩，在应激时无法上调**皮质醇**分泌：

- Normally: severe infection → ↑CRH → ↑ACTH → ↑cortisol → maintains vascular adrenergic tone + gluconeogenesis\
  正常情况：严重感染 → CRH升高 → ACTH升高 → 皮质醇升高 → 维持血管肾上腺素能张力+糖异生

- With HPA suppression: cortisol cannot rise → vascular smooth muscle loses catecholamine sensitivity → refractory hypotension\
  HPA轴受抑时：皮质醇无法升高 → 血管平滑肌对儿茶酚胺敏感性下降 → 难治性低血压

- Cortisol also has intrinsic mineralocorticoid-like effects; its absence impairs sodium/water retention even when aldosterone is preserved\
  皮质醇本身具有类盐皮质激素效应；即使醛固酮保留，皮质醇缺乏仍会损害钠水潴留

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The adrenal glands sit atop the kidneys — in this case the very same organ system under infectious attack, making the anatomic proximity a memory anchor.

**解剖小窍门:** 肾上腺位于肾脏顶部——本题中感染攻击的正是同一器官系统（肾脏），形成"病灶在哪，危机在哪"的记忆锚点。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Hydrocortisone for Adrenal Crisis / 正确答案 (C) — 氢化可的松治疗肾上腺危象

**Hydrocortisone** replaces the endogenous cortisol that the suppressed adrenal glands cannot produce, rapidly restoring vascular adrenergic tone and hemodynamic stability:

**氢化可的松**补充受抑制肾上腺无法产生的内源性皮质醇，迅速恢复血管肾上腺素能张力和血流动力学稳定性：

- Dose: 100 mg IV bolus immediately, then 50–100 mg IV q6–8h (or continuous infusion 200 mg/24h)\
  剂量：立即100 mg静脉推注，然后50-100 mg静脉注射每6-8小时（或200 mg/24h持续输注）

- Mechanism: upregulates vascular adrenergic receptors → restores pressor response to catecholamines and vasopressors\
  机制：上调血管肾上腺素受体 → 恢复对儿茶酚胺及升压药的反应性

- Do NOT wait for serum cortisol results in acute crisis — empiric treatment saves lives; draw the level before giving if feasible\
  急性危象时不要等血清皮质醇结果——经验性治疗挽救生命；如可行则在给药前抽血

**Diagnosis:** Adrenal crisis precipitated by urosepsis in a patient with HPA axis suppression from chronic prednisone; the pivotal diagnostic clue is fluid-refractory hypotension in a steroid-dependent patient.

**诊断:** 长期泼尼松导致HPA轴抑制的患者由尿路脓毒症诱发肾上腺危象；关键诊断线索是激素依赖患者的液体复苏无效低血压。

**Treatment:** Immediate IV hydrocortisone + continued fluid resuscitation + appropriate antibiotics (pip-tazo already appropriate); adrenal crisis must be treated concurrently with sepsis management.

**治疗:** 立即静脉氢化可的松 + 继续液体复苏 + 合适抗生素（哌拉西林-他唑巴坦已合适）；肾上腺危象须与脓毒症治疗同步进行。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Administration of ciprofloxacin<br />
A — 给予环丙沙星</td>
<td>Fluoroquinolones face widespread resistance among common uropathogens; pip-tazo already provides appropriate broad-spectrum gram-negative coverage including Pseudomonas<br />
氟喹诺酮类面临尿路病原体广泛耐药；哌拉西林-他唑巴坦已提供含假单胞菌的广谱覆盖</td>
<td>Escalating antibiotics does not address the hemodynamic instability — the core problem is adrenal crisis, not antibiotic coverage gap<br />
升级抗生素不能解决血流动力学不稳定——核心问题是肾上腺危象，而非抗生素覆盖不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Administration of gentamicin<br />
B — 给予庆大霉素</td>
<td>Aminoglycosides are nephrotoxic; this patient already has lupus nephritis — the risk of further renal injury far outweighs any marginal benefit<br />
氨基糖苷类有肾毒性；患者已有狼疮性肾炎——进一步肾损伤的风险远超边际收益</td>
<td>Pip-tazo already covers gram-negatives adequately; adding gentamicin adds toxicity without addressing the refractory shock<br />
哌拉西林-他唑巴坦已充分覆盖革兰阴性菌；加用庆大霉素只增加毒性，不能解决难治性休克</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Administration of hydrocortisone ✓<br />
C — 给予氢化可的松 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — stress-dose hydrocortisone directly addresses the adrenal crisis precipitated by infection in a chronic steroid user with fluid-refractory hypotension<br />
正确——应激剂量氢化可的松直接解决长期激素使用者因感染诱发的肾上腺危象和液体无效低血压</td>
<td>Chronic steroids + acute infectious stressor + refractory hypotension = adrenal crisis until proven otherwise<br />
长期激素 + 急性感染应激 + 难治性低血压 = 除外其他之前先按肾上腺危象处理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Administration of metoprolol<br />
D — 给予美托洛尔</td>
<td>Beta-blockers are absolutely contraindicated in shock; they blunt the compensatory tachycardia that maintains cardiac output and mean arterial pressure<br />
β受体阻滞剂在休克中绝对禁忌；会抑制维持心输出量和平均动脉压的代偿性心动过速</td>
<td>Tachycardia here is sinus tachycardia — a physiologic compensation for shock, NOT an arrhythmia requiring rate control<br />
此处心动过速为窦性心动过速——是对休克的生理代偿反应，而非需要控制心率的心律失常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Cardioversion<br />
E — 心脏复律</td>
<td>Cardioversion is indicated for unstable tachyarrhythmias (VT, SVT, AF with RVR); this patient has compensatory sinus tachycardia<br />
心脏复律用于不稳定性快速性心律失常（室速、SVT、快室率房颤）；本患者为代偿性窦性心动过速</td>
<td>Sinus tachycardia cannot be cardioverted technically and must be permitted to continue as a compensatory mechanism in shock<br />
窦性心动过速技术上无法复律，且在休克中必须保留作为代偿机制</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (A) ciprofloxacin — it mimics clinical urgency to "do something" about the infection, but the pivot is recognizing refractory hypotension as adrenal crisis rather than antibiotic failure.*

最容易犯错的干扰项是(A)环丙沙星——它迎合了"升级抗感染治疗"的直觉，但关键转折在于识别难治性低血压是肾上腺危象而非抗生素失败。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Primary vs. Secondary Adrenal Insufficiency / 原发性 vs. 继发性肾上腺功能不全

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Primary (Addison's Disease)</strong><br />
<strong>原发性（Addison病）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Secondary (Exogenous Steroids / Pituitary)</strong><br />
<strong>继发性（外源性激素/垂体病变）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Cause<br />
病因</td>
<td>Adrenal gland destruction: autoimmune (most common), TB, hemorrhage, metastasis<br />
肾上腺腺体破坏：自身免疫（最常见）、结核、出血、转移</td>
<td>Chronic exogenous steroid use, pituitary tumor, Sheehan syndrome<br />
长期外源性激素使用、垂体肿瘤、Sheehan综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ACTH level<br />
ACTH水平</td>
<td>↑↑ elevated (no cortisol feedback inhibition)<br />
↑↑升高（无皮质醇负反馈抑制）</td>
<td>↓ low (pituitary suppressed by exogenous steroids)<br />
↓降低（垂体被外源性激素抑制）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Aldosterone<br />
醛固酮</td>
<td>↓ deficient (zona glomerulosa destroyed)<br />
↓缺乏（球状带被破坏）</td>
<td>Normal (zona glomerulosa responds to angiotensin II, not ACTH)<br />
正常（球状带对血管紧张素II反应，不依赖ACTH）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hyperkalemia<br />
高钾血症</td>
<td>Present (aldosterone deficiency → ↓K⁺ excretion)<br />
存在（醛固酮缺乏 → 排钾减少）</td>
<td>Absent or mild<br />
不存在或轻微</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hyperpigmentation<br />
皮肤色素沉着</td>
<td>Present (↑ACTH → ↑MSH via POMC cleavage)<br />
存在（ACTH升高 → POMC裂解产生MSH增多）</td>
<td>Absent<br />
不存在</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Crisis trigger<br />
危象诱因</td>
<td>Any physiologic stress, missed fludrocortisone/hydrocortisone dose<br />
任何生理应激、漏服氟氢可的松/氢化可的松</td>
<td>Acute stress during chronic steroid use or after taper<br />
慢性激素使用期间或减量后的急性应激</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recovery after stressor<br />
应激后恢复</td>
<td>Cannot recover without lifelong replacement<br />
无法在没有终身替代治疗的情况下恢复</td>
<td>Adrenal function may recover months after steroid discontinuation<br />
停用激素后数月肾上腺功能可能恢复</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a patient on chronic steroids develops refractory hypotension during acute illness, immediately give IV hydrocortisone for adrenal crisis — the adrenal glands cannot meet the sudden cortisol demand.**

**长期使用激素的患者在急性病期间出现难治性低血压时，立即静脉给予氢化可的松治疗肾上腺危象——肾上腺无法满足突然增加的皮质醇需求。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CRASH" for Adrenal Crisis Recognition / 记忆钩 — "CRASH"识别肾上腺危象:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>hronic steroids → HPA suppressed / <strong>C</strong>hronic激素 → HPA轴受抑<br />
• <strong>R</strong>efractory hypotension → fluids not enough / <strong>R</strong>efractory低血压 → 补液不够<br />
• <strong>A</strong>cute stressor (infection, surgery) → cortisol demand spikes / <strong>A</strong>cute应激（感染、手术）→ 皮质醇需求骤增<br />
• <strong>S</strong>tress-dose hydrocortisone → give immediately / <strong>S</strong>tress剂量氢化可的松 → 立即给药<br />
• <strong>H</strong>PA axis recovery takes months after stopping steroids / <strong>H</strong>PA轴恢复需停药后数月</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Adrenal Crisis / 高频知识表 — 肾上腺危象

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Stress-dose steroid indication<br />
应激剂量激素适应证</td>
<td>Patients on ≥5 mg/day prednisone (or equivalent) for ≥3 weeks undergoing major physiologic stress (surgery, serious infection, trauma, MI)<br />
接受≥5 mg/天泼尼松（或等效量）≥3周且遭受重大生理应激（手术、严重感染、创伤、心梗）的患者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hydrocortisone dosing<br />
氢化可的松剂量</td>
<td>Crisis: 100 mg IV bolus → 50–100 mg q6–8h; taper over 1–3 days as hemodynamics improve; switch to oral maintenance when stable<br />
危象：100 mg静脉推注→50-100 mg每6-8小时；随血流动力学改善在1-3天内减量；稳定后改口服维持</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Empiric treatment timing<br />
经验性治疗时机</td>
<td>Treat empirically when adrenal crisis is suspected; draw cortisol and ACTH before administration if possible but DO NOT delay treatment for results<br />
疑诊肾上腺危象时经验性治疗；尽可能在给药前抽皮质醇和ACTH，但不得因等待结果而延误治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why vasopressors fail<br />
升压药为何失效</td>
<td>Cortisol upregulates alpha-adrenergic receptors on vasculature; without cortisol, norepinephrine and vasopressors lose efficacy<br />
皮质醇上调血管壁α-肾上腺素受体；缺乏皮质醇时去甲肾上腺素及升压药效果减弱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary AI and aldosterone<br />
继发性肾上腺功能不全与醛固酮</td>
<td>Aldosterone is usually preserved (zona glomerulosa intact, regulated by RAAS not ACTH); severe hyperkalemia and salt-wasting are less prominent than in primary AI<br />
醛固酮通常保留（球状带完整，由RAAS而非ACTH调节）；高钾血症和失盐症状不如原发性肾上腺功能不全突出</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HPA recovery timeline<br />
HPA轴恢复时间线</td>
<td>After stopping chronic steroids, full HPA axis recovery can take 6–12 months; patients remain at risk for adrenal crisis throughout this period<br />
停用慢性激素后，完整HPA轴恢复可能需要6-12个月；此期间患者持续存在肾上腺危象风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Relative adrenal insufficiency:** Even without classic HPA suppression, critically ill patients (especially septic shock on vasopressors) may have cortisol deficiency relative to the physiologic demand; empiric hydrocortisone is considered in vasopressor-dependent septic shock\
  **相对性肾上腺功能不全:** 即使没有经典HPA抑制，危重患者（尤其是使用升压药的脓毒性休克）也可能存在相对于生理需求的皮质醇缺乏；对升压药依赖性脓毒性休克可考虑经验性氢化可的松

- **Steroid taper trap:** Patients tapering steroids for SLE, IBD, or asthma remain at adrenal crisis risk for up to 12 months post-discontinuation — the adrenal glands need time to recover from HPA suppression\
  **激素减量陷阱:** 因SLE、炎症性肠病或哮喘而减量激素的患者停药后长达12个月内仍有肾上腺危象风险——肾上腺需要时间从HPA抑制中恢复

- **Metoprolol contraindication in shock:** Any beta-blocker in distributive, cardiogenic, or hypovolemic shock removes the compensatory sympathetic response; tachycardia in shock is protective, not harmful\
  **美托洛尔在休克中的禁忌:** 任何β受体阻滞剂在分布性、心源性或低血容量性休克中都会消除代偿性交感反应；休克中的心动过速是保护性的，而非有害的

- **Fluoroquinolone resistance:** Empiric fluoroquinolones for UTI/pyelonephritis in hospitalized patients are no longer recommended in most guidelines due to rising E. coli resistance rates (\>20% in many regions); pip-tazo or ceftriaxone preferred for sick patients\
  **氟喹诺酮耐药:** 由于大肠杆菌耐药率上升（许多地区\>20%），大多数指南不再推荐对住院患者UTI/肾盂肾炎进行氟喹诺酮经验性治疗；重症患者首选哌拉西林-他唑巴坦或头孢曲松

# Question 124 — Cor Pulmonale (COPD-Induced Right Heart Failure) / 肺源性心脏病（COPD所致右心衰竭）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>72-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-month history of progressive shortness of breath</strong>, <strong>nonproductive cough</strong>, and fatigue. During this period, he has had early satiety resulting in a 2.3-kg (5-lb) weight loss. He has no known sick contacts. He has a <strong>20-year history of chronic obstructive pulmonary disease</strong> and a 10-year history of hypertension. Current medications are an inhaled bronchodilator and an oral thiazide diuretic. He has <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 50 years</strong>. He is in mild respiratory distress. He is 165 cm (5 ft 5 in) tall and weighs 52 kg (115 lb); BMI is 19 kg/m². His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 103/min, respirations are 20/min, and blood pressure is 130/90 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an <strong>oxygen saturation of 87%</strong>. Examination shows no scleral icterus. There is <strong>jugular venous distention</strong>. Breath sounds are distant. There is a <strong>right ventricular heave</strong> and a <strong>loud S2</strong>. A grade 2/6 systolic murmur is heard best over the left sternal border. The liver is <strong>tender, smooth, and pulsatile</strong>. There is no peripheral edema. His <strong>hematocrit is 50%</strong>, leukocyte count is 4500/mm³, and platelet count is 200,000/mm³. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Digoxin therapy<br />
B) Furosemide therapy<br />
C) Incentive spirometry<br />
D) Continuous positive airway pressure<br />
E) Home oxygen therapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Oxygen saturation 87% on room air<br />
室内空气氧饱和度87%</td>
<td>Meets home O2 therapy threshold (SpO2 ≤88%); confirms severe chronic hypoxemia<br />
达到家庭氧疗指征（SpO2≤88%）；确认严重慢性低氧血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Right ventricular heave + loud S2<br />
右室搏动感 + 第二心音亢进</td>
<td>Classic signs of pulmonary hypertension and RV pressure overload; hallmark of cor pulmonale<br />
肺动脉高压及右室压力超负荷的经典体征；肺源性心脏病的标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Jugular venous distention<br />
颈静脉怒张</td>
<td>Elevated right-sided filling pressures from RV failure causing venous congestion<br />
右心衰竭所致右侧充盈压升高，引起静脉系统淤血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pulsatile liver<br />
搏动性肝脏</td>
<td>Pathognomonic of tricuspid regurgitation from RV dilation; confirms backward failure into venous circulation<br />
右室扩张致三尖瓣反流的特征性表现；确认右心衰向静脉循环的逆向衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>50 pack-year smoking + 20-year COPD<br />
50包年吸烟 + COPD 20年</td>
<td>Chronic alveolar hypoxia from COPD drives pulmonary vasoconstriction → pulmonary HTN → cor pulmonale<br />
COPD所致慢性肺泡低氧驱动肺血管收缩→肺动脉高压→肺源性心脏病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hematocrit 50%<br />
血细胞比容50%</td>
<td>Secondary polycythemia from chronic hypoxia; EPO-driven compensatory increase in O2-carrying capacity<br />
慢性低氧所致继发性红细胞增多症；EPO驱动的代偿性携氧能力提升</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

Chronic **COPD** causes sustained **alveolar hypoxia**, which triggers **hypoxic pulmonary vasoconstriction (HPV)**. Over years, this remodels pulmonary vasculature, producing **pulmonary arterial hypertension**. The right ventricle must chronically pump against elevated resistance, eventually developing **cor pulmonale** — a sequence of RV hypertrophy, dilation, and failure:

慢性 **COPD** 导致持续性 **肺泡低氧**，触发 **低氧性肺血管收缩（HPV）**。经年累月，肺血管发生重塑，形成 **肺动脉高压**。右室持续对抗升高的阻力，最终发展为 **肺源性心脏病**——经历右室肥厚、扩张、衰竭的序贯过程：

- Alveolar hypoxia → HPV → pulmonary vascular remodeling → ↑ pulmonary vascular resistance (PVR)\
  肺泡低氧 → 低氧性肺血管收缩 → 肺血管重塑 → 肺血管阻力（PVR）升高

- ↑ PVR → RV pressure overload → RV hypertrophy → RV dilation and failure\
  PVR升高 → 右室压力超负荷 → 右室肥厚 → 右室扩张和衰竭

- RV failure → ↑ right-sided filling pressures → JVD, hepatic congestion, pulsatile liver\
  右心衰竭 → 右侧充盈压升高 → 颈静脉怒张、肝淤血、搏动性肝脏

- Supplemental O2 reverses HPV → ↓ PVR → reduced RV afterload → improved survival\
  补充氧气逆转低氧性肺血管收缩 → PVR降低 → 右室后负荷减轻 → 生存率改善

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The loud P2 (pulmonic component of S2) and RV heave are both consequences of increased pulmonary artery pressure — the higher the pressure, the harder the RV contracts and the louder the pulmonic valve slams shut.

**解剖小窍门:** 响亮的P2（S2肺动脉瓣成分）和右室搏动感均源于肺动脉压升高——压力越高，右室收缩越有力，肺动脉瓣关闭时"撞击"声越响。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Home Oxygen Therapy / 正确答案 (E) — 家庭氧疗

**Home oxygen therapy** is one of only two interventions proven to improve long-term survival in severe hypoxemic COPD (the other being smoking cessation):

**家庭氧疗** 是仅有的两种被证实改善严重低氧血症COPD患者长期生存率的干预措施之一（另一种为戒烟）：

- Indicated when resting SpO2 ≤88% or PaO2 ≤55 mmHg on room air — this patient qualifies at SpO2 87%\
  指征：室内空气静息SpO2≤88%或PaO2≤55 mmHg——该患者SpO2 87%符合指征

- Reverses hypoxic pulmonary vasoconstriction → reduces pulmonary HTN → decreases RV afterload\
  逆转低氧性肺血管收缩 → 降低肺动脉高压 → 减轻右室后负荷

- MRC (1981) and NOTT (1980) trials demonstrated 20–30% mortality reduction with ≥15 hours/day O2\
  MRC（1981年）和NOTT（1980年）研究证实每日≥15小时氧疗可降低20–30%死亡率

**Diagnosis:** Cor pulmonale — COPD-driven pulmonary HTN causing RV hypertrophy and failure, evidenced by SpO2 87%, JVD, RV heave, loud S2, pulsatile liver, and secondary polycythemia (Hct 50%).

**诊断:** 肺源性心脏病——COPD驱动肺动脉高压导致右室肥厚和衰竭，表现为SpO2 87%、颈静脉怒张、右室搏动感、S2亢进、搏动性肝脏及继发性红细胞增多症（血细胞比容50%）。

**Treatment:** Home O2 ≥15 hrs/day; smoking cessation (primary); continue inhaled bronchodilator; consider pulmonary rehabilitation; loop diuretics if congestion persists after O2 optimization.

**治疗:** 家庭氧疗每日≥15小时；戒烟（首要措施）；继续吸入支气管扩张剂；考虑肺康复训练；若氧疗优化后仍有淤血，可加用袢利尿剂。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Digoxin therapy<br />
A — 地高辛治疗</td>
<td>Improves HF symptoms but confers no long-term survival benefit; not first-line for cor pulmonale<br />
可改善心衰症状但无长期生存获益；非肺源性心脏病一线治疗</td>
<td>Only O2 therapy and smoking cessation improve survival in COPD; digoxin does not<br />
仅氧疗和戒烟改善COPD生存率；地高辛无此效果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Furosemide therapy<br />
B — 呋塞米治疗</td>
<td>May relieve venous congestion symptoms, but does not treat root cause (hypoxia-driven vasoconstriction); home O2 must come first<br />
可缓解静脉淤血症状，但不治疗根本原因（低氧性血管收缩）；应先启动家庭氧疗</td>
<td>Treat the mechanism (hypoxia → HPV → PVR) before the downstream symptom (fluid congestion)<br />
先处理机制（低氧→肺血管收缩→肺血管阻力升高），再处理下游症状（液体淤积）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Incentive spirometry<br />
C — 激励性肺量计</td>
<td>Prevents postoperative atelectasis; no role in routine outpatient COPD management<br />
用于预防术后肺不张；在常规门诊COPD管理中无地位</td>
<td>Incentive spirometry is a postoperative tool, not a COPD intervention<br />
激励性肺量计是术后工具，不是COPD治疗措施</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Continuous positive airway pressure<br />
D — 持续气道正压通气</td>
<td>Indicated for COPD acute exacerbation with hypercapnic respiratory failure; this patient has stable chronic disease, not an acute exacerbation<br />
用于COPD急性加重伴高碳酸血症性呼吸衰竭；该患者为慢性稳定期，非急性加重</td>
<td>No acute exacerbation here; CPAP/BiPAP is reserved for acute hypoventilatory crisis<br />
本例无急性加重；CPAP/BiPAP留用于急性通气不足危象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Home oxygen therapy ✓<br />
E — 家庭氧疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — SpO2 87% meets criteria; reverses HPV, reduces PVR, decreases RV afterload, and improves mortality<br />
正确——SpO2 87%符合指征；逆转低氧性肺血管收缩，降低肺血管阻力，减轻右室后负荷，改善死亡率</td>
<td>Only intervention that directly targets the pathophysiologic driver of cor pulmonale<br />
唯一直接针对肺源性心脏病病理生理驱动因素的干预措施</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is furosemide (Choice B) — the patient has JVD and a pulsatile liver, which scream "diuretics." But diuretics treat the downstream congestion without addressing the upstream driver; home O2 must be initiated first to reverse hypoxic vasoconstriction.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是呋塞米（选项B）——颈静脉怒张和搏动性肝脏强烈提示"给利尿剂"。但利尿剂只处理下游淤血，而非上游根因；必须先启动家庭氧疗来逆转低氧性血管收缩。

---

SpO2&gt;90%且无并发症——无适应症</td>

对肺源性心脏病作用</td>

氧疗→低氧性肺血管收缩减轻→肺动脉高压降低→右室重塑减少</td>
<td>Diuretics reduce preload; digoxin ↑ contractility — neither reverses mechanism<br />
利尿剂降低前负荷；地高辛增强收缩力——均不逆转发病机制</td>
</tr>

关键临床试验</td>

MRC研究1981年，NOTT研究1980年</td>
<td>No landmark RCT evidence for survival with bronchodilators alone<br />
单用支气管扩张剂无里程碑RCT生存获益证据</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In COPD with cor pulmonale and SpO2 ≤88%, home oxygen therapy is the most appropriate next step because it directly reverses hypoxic pulmonary vasoconstriction, reduces right ventricular afterload, and — alongside smoking cessation — is one of only two interventions proven to improve survival.**

**在COPD合并肺源性心脏病且SpO2≤88%的患者中，家庭氧疗是最合适的下一步，因为它能直接逆转低氧性肺血管收缩、降低右室后负荷，并与戒烟共同构成仅有的两种被证实改善生存率的干预措施。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "O2 SAVES" for Cor Pulmonale / 记忆钩 — "O2 SAVES" 肺源性心脏病管理:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>O</strong>xygen therapy — the #1 next step when SpO2 ≤88%; reverses HPV / 氧疗——SpO2≤88%时的首选下一步；逆转低氧性肺血管收缩<br />
• <strong>S</strong>moking cessation — only other proven survival intervention / 戒烟——唯一另一种经证实改善生存率的措施<br />
• <strong>A</strong>void diuretics as first step — treat upstream hypoxia before downstream congestion / 避免首先使用利尿剂——先治上游低氧，再治下游淤血<br />
• <strong>V</strong>ascular remodeling reversed by O2 — ↓ PVR → ↓ RV afterload / 氧气逆转血管重塑——降低PVR→减轻右室后负荷<br />
• <strong>E</strong>levated Hct (polycythemia) — clue for chronic hypoxia, not primary treatment target / 血细胞比容升高（红细胞增多）——慢性低氧线索，非主要治疗靶点<br />
• <strong>S</strong>2 loud + RV heave — signs of pulmonary HTN; disappear with successful O2 treatment / S2亢进 + 右室搏动感——肺动脉高压体征；氧疗成功后可消退</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

</tbody>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cor Pulmonale and Home Oxygen in COPD / 高频知识表 — COPD中的肺源性心脏病与家庭氧疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of cor pulmonale<br />
肺源性心脏病定义</td>
<td>RV hypertrophy and/or failure caused by pulmonary hypertension from a primary pulmonary disorder (most commonly COPD)<br />
原发肺部疾病（最常见COPD）所致肺动脉高压引起的右室肥厚和/或衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology sequence<br />
病理生理序列</td>
<td>COPD → alveolar hypoxia → HPV → vascular remodeling → ↑ PVR → RV pressure overload → RV hypertrophy → failure<br />
COPD→肺泡低氧→低氧性肺血管收缩→血管重塑→PVR升高→右室压力超负荷→右室肥厚→衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic physical exam findings<br />
经典体格检查发现</td>
<td>JVD, RV heave (parasternal), loud P2, pansystolic murmur (TR) at left sternal border, pulsatile liver, peripheral edema (late sign)<br />
颈静脉怒张、右室搏动感（胸骨旁）、P2亢进、胸骨左缘全收缩期杂音（三尖瓣反流）、搏动性肝脏、外周水肿（晚期表现）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Home O2 therapy criteria<br />
家庭氧疗指征</td>
<td>SpO2 ≤88% (or PaO2 ≤55 mmHg) at rest; SpO2 89–90% qualifies if pulmonary HTN, cor pulmonale, or polycythemia present<br />
静息SpO2≤88%（或PaO2≤55 mmHg）；若合并肺动脉高压、肺源性心脏病或红细胞增多症，SpO2 89–90%也符合指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Two survival-improving interventions<br />
两种改善生存率的干预措施</td>
<td>(1) Smoking cessation — slows FEV1 decline rate; (2) Home O2 ≥15 hrs/day — reduces HPV and mortality (MRC, NOTT trials)<br />
①戒烟——减缓FEV1下降速率；②家庭氧疗≥15小时/天——降低低氧性肺血管收缩和死亡率（MRC、NOTT研究）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary polycythemia in COPD<br />
COPD中继发性红细胞增多症</td>
<td>Chronic hypoxia → ↑ EPO → ↑ RBC production → ↑ Hct; distinguishable from polycythemia vera by normal WBC/platelets and ↑ EPO<br />
慢性低氧→EPO升高→红细胞生成增多→血细胞比容升高；与真性红细胞增多症的区别：白细胞/血小板正常且EPO升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CPAP/BiPAP indications in COPD<br />
CPAP/BiPAP在COPD中的适应症</td>
<td>Acute exacerbation with hypercapnic respiratory failure (pH &lt;7.35, PaCO2 &gt;45); BiPAP preferred over CPAP; NOT indicated for stable chronic hypoxemia<br />
急性加重伴高碳酸血症性呼吸衰竭（pH&lt;7.35，PaCO2&gt;45）；首选BiPAP而非CPAP；稳定性慢性低氧血症不适用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Furosemide role in cor pulmonale<br />
呋塞米在肺源性心脏病中的作用</td>
<td>Adjunct therapy after O2 initiated; reduces preload/venous congestion symptoms; does not reverse pulmonary HTN mechanism<br />
氧疗启动后的辅助治疗；降低前负荷/缓解静脉淤血症状；不能逆转肺动脉高压的发病机制</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of pulsatile liver:** Tricuspid regurgitation from RV dilation (as here), severe RV failure alone, constrictive pericarditis — distinguished by JVP waveform (CV wave in TR) and echocardiography\
  **搏动性肝脏鉴别:** 右室扩张致三尖瓣反流（如本例）、单纯严重右心衰竭、缩窄性心包炎——通过颈静脉压波形（三尖瓣反流可见CV波）和超声心动图鉴别

- **Variant — exercise-induced desaturation:** If resting SpO2 is 89–90% but drops during exertion, ambulatory O2 during activity may be indicated; assess with 6-minute walk test\
  **题目变式——运动性去饱和:** 若静息SpO2为89–90%但活动时下降，可能需要活动时便携式氧疗；通过6分钟步行试验评估

- **Key complication — O2 in hypercapnic COPD:** High-flow O2 can suppress hypoxic respiratory drive in chronic CO2 retainers; titrate to SpO2 88–92%, not to 100%\
  **关键并发症——高碳酸血症COPD患者的氧疗:** 高流量氧气可抑制慢性CO2潴留患者的低氧性呼吸驱动；应将SpO2调至88–92%，而非100%

- **Risk factor — thiazide diuretic in COPD:** Thiazides cause hypokalemia and metabolic alkalosis, which can suppress respiratory drive and worsen CO2 retention — monitor electrolytes closely\
  **危险因素——COPD患者使用噻嗪类利尿剂:** 噻嗪类利尿剂导致低钾血症和代谢性碱中毒，可抑制呼吸驱动并加重CO2潴留——需密切监测电解质

# Question 125 — Cardiogenic Shock Post-Myocardial Infarction / 心肌梗死后心源性休克

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Four days after admission</strong> to the hospital for treatment of a <strong>myocardial infarction</strong>, a <strong>72-year-old woman</strong> has the sudden onset of <strong>shortness of breath and confusion</strong>. She has atrial fibrillation, type 2 diabetes mellitus, essential hypertension, and hypercholesterolemia. Her medications are diltiazem, quinapril, metformin, and simvastatin. She has smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 50 years and has drunk one glass of wine daily for 52 years. She is anxious and oriented to person but not to place or time. Her temperature is <strong>35°C (95°F)</strong>, pulse is <strong>116/min and irregularly irregular</strong>, respirations are <strong>30/min</strong>, and blood pressure is <strong>92/58 mm Hg</strong>. Pulse oximetry on 100% oxygen by face mask shows an oxygen saturation of <strong>91%</strong>. The skin is <strong>cool to the touch</strong>. Examination shows <strong>jugular venous distention</strong>. Decreased breath sounds are heard in the lung bases bilaterally. Scattered expiratory wheezes and crackles are heard bilaterally. A rub is heard in the lower lobe of the left lung. There is 2+ pretibial and pedal edema bilaterally. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 11.6 g/dL, Leukocyte count 11,000/mm³ (Segmented neutrophils 65%, Bands 3%, Lymphocytes 30%, Monocytes 2%), Serum Na⁺ 136 mEq/L, K⁺ 3.7 mEq/L, Cl⁻ 105 mEq/L, <strong>HCO₃⁻ 14 mEq/L</strong>, Glucose 86 mg/dL, Creatine kinase 68 U/L, <strong>Lactic acid 3.6 mEq/L</strong> (N=0.5–2). Arterial blood gas analysis shows: <strong>pH 7.29</strong>, PCO₂ 30 mm Hg, PO₂ 64 mm Hg. An ECG is shown. A chest x-ray shows <strong>cardiomegaly and pulmonary infiltrates, and pleural effusions bilaterally</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cardiac catheterization<br />
B) CT angiography<br />
C) Echocardiography<br />
D) Measurement of serum brain natriuretic peptide concentration<br />
E) Radionuclide myocardial scan</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>

<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>

<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>4 days post-MI, sudden deterioration<br />
心梗后第 4 天急剧恶化</td>
<td>Classic time window for post-MI mechanical complications (papillary muscle rupture, free wall rupture, VSD)<br />
心梗后机械性并发症（乳头肌断裂、游离壁破裂、室间隔缺损）的经典时间窗</td>
</tr>
<tr>

心源性休克的血流动力学不稳定三联征</td>

<tr>
<td>Cool skin + JVD + pulmonary crackles<br />
皮肤湿冷 + 颈静脉怒张 + 肺湿啰音</td>

经典"冷湿型"心源性休克表现</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>CXR: cardiomegaly + pulmonary infiltrates + bilateral pleural effusions<br />
胸片：心脏扩大 + 肺浸润影 + 双侧胸腔积液</td>
<td>Radiographic hallmarks of acute decompensated heart failure<br />
急性失代偿性心力衰竭的影像学标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temp 35°C (hypothermia)<br />
体温 35°C（低体温）</td>
<td>Peripheral vasoconstriction + reduced cardiac output → impaired thermogenesis<br />
外周血管收缩 + 心输出量减少 → 产热障碍</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Cardiogenic shock** arises when **myocardial pump failure** reduces cardiac output below the threshold needed to maintain end-organ perfusion. In the post-MI setting, **mechanical complications** superimposed on ischemic myocardium amplify pump failure dramatically:

心源性休克发生于**心肌泵功能衰竭**导致心输出量降至无法维持终末器官灌注的水平。心梗后**机械性并发症**叠加在缺血心肌之上，可急剧加重泵衰竭：

- Ischemic myocardial necrosis → reduced contractility → ↓ stroke volume → ↓ cardiac output\
  缺血性心肌坏死 → 收缩力下降 → ↓ 每搏量 → ↓ 心输出量

- Low output → compensatory vasoconstriction → cool, clammy skin + peripheral hypoperfusion\
  低心输出量 → 代偿性血管收缩 → 皮肤湿冷 + 外周低灌注

- Backpressure → pulmonary venous hypertension → alveolar flooding → crackles + hypoxemia\
  反向压力 → 肺静脉高压 → 肺泡水肿 → 湿啰音 + 低氧血症

- Lactic acidosis develops when aerobic metabolism fails and tissues switch to anaerobic glycolysis\
  当有氧代谢衰竭、组织转为无氧糖酵解时出现乳酸酸中毒

- Compensatory respiratory alkalosis (↓ PCO₂ to 30) partially offsets metabolic acidosis but is insufficient\
  代偿性呼吸性碱中毒（↓ PCO₂ 至 30）部分抵消代谢性酸中毒但仍不足

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The 3–7 day post-MI window is when fibrinous necrosis peaks — highest risk for papillary muscle rupture (→ acute MR), free wall rupture (→ tamponade), and ventricular septal rupture.

**解剖小窍门:** 心梗后第 3-7 天是纤维素性坏死高峰期——乳头肌断裂（→ 急性二尖瓣反流）、游离壁破裂（→ 心脏压塞）及室间隔穿孔的风险最高。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Bedside Echocardiography / 正确答案 (C) — 床旁超声心动图

**Echocardiography** is the first-line, rapid bedside diagnostic tool that simultaneously assesses cardiac structure, wall motion, valvular function, and pericardium — covering all causes of post-MI cardiogenic shock — without patient transport:

**超声心动图**是一线快速床旁诊断工具，能同时评估心脏结构、室壁运动、瓣膜功能及心包——涵盖心梗后心源性休克的所有病因——无需转运患者：

- Identifies regional wall motion abnormalities confirming ischemic etiology\
  识别节段性室壁运动异常，确认缺血性病因

- Detects acute mitral regurgitation from papillary muscle rupture (flail leaflet + regurgitant jet)\
  检测乳头肌断裂所致急性二尖瓣反流（连枷瓣叶 + 反流束）

- Diagnoses ventricular septal defect (left-to-right shunt) or free wall rupture with hemopericardium\
  诊断室间隔缺损（左向右分流）或伴血心包的游离壁破裂

- Evaluates pericardial effusion causing tamponade (post-MI pericarditis or Dressler syndrome)\
  评估导致心脏压塞的心包积液（心梗后心包炎或 Dressler 综合征）

- Guides immediate management: vasopressors, IABP, emergent surgery vs. medical optimization\
  指导即时处置：血管活性药、主动脉内球囊反搏、急诊手术 vs. 药物优化

**Diagnosis:** Post-MI cardiogenic shock — rapid echo-based identification of etiology determines whether mechanical complication (surgical emergency) vs. ischemic LV dysfunction (medical/catheter management) is present.

**诊断:** 心梗后心源性休克——通过超声快速明确病因，判断是机械性并发症（外科急症）还是缺血性左室功能障碍（药物/导管处置）。

**Treatment:** Stabilize hemodynamics (norepinephrine first-line, IABP if needed) → echo-directed: papillary muscle rupture/VSD → urgent surgery; ischemic LV failure → vasopressors + diuretics + possible percutaneous revascularization.

**治疗:** 稳定血流动力学（去甲肾上腺素首选，必要时主动脉内球囊反搏）→ 超声引导：乳头肌断裂/室间隔缺损 → 急诊手术；缺血性左室衰竭 → 血管活性药 + 利尿剂 + 可能的经皮血运重建。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cardiac catheterization<br />
A — 心导管检查</td>
<td>Invasive; reserved for after echo identifies stent thrombosis or ACS requiring intervention; not the first step in undifferentiated shock<br />
有创；仅在超声提示支架血栓或需介入 ACS 后使用；不是不明原因休克的第一步</td>
<td>Echo defines the cause first; cath is a downstream therapeutic step<br />
超声先明确病因；心导管是后续治疗步骤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — CT angiography<br />
B — CT 血管造影</td>
<td>Time-consuming; requires contrast + patient transport; provides no actionable bedside information in acute hemodynamic collapse<br />
耗时；需造影剂 + 转运；急性血流动力学崩溃时无法提供可操作的床旁信息</td>
<td>Cardiogenic shock demands immediate bedside diagnosis, not time-intensive imaging<br />
心源性休克需即时床旁诊断，而非耗时影像学检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Echocardiography ✓<br />
C — 超声心动图 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Bedside echo rapidly identifies the cause of cardiogenic shock (wall motion, valvular competence, pericardium) and directly guides management<br />
正确——床旁超声快速识别心源性休克病因（室壁运动、瓣膜功能、心包）并直接指导处置</td>
<td>Immediate, non-invasive, bedside-capable; covers all post-MI mechanical complications<br />
即时、无创、床旁可行；覆盖所有心梗后机械性并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Serum BNP measurement<br />
D — 血清 BNP 测定</td>
<td>BNP is expected to be elevated in any setting of heart failure; does not identify the specific cause or guide urgent intervention<br />
任何心衰情境下 BNP 均升高；不能明确具体病因或指导紧急干预</td>
<td>Clinical exam + CXR already confirm heart failure; BNP adds no actionable information beyond what is known<br />
临床检查 + 胸片已确认心衰；BNP 无法提供超出已知信息的可操作依据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Radionuclide myocardial scan<br />
E — 放射性核素心肌扫描</td>
<td>Outpatient test comparing perfusion at rest vs. stress; wholly inappropriate for acute hemodynamic emergencies<br />
门诊检查，比较静息与运动灌注；完全不适用于急性血流动力学紧急状态</td>
<td>Indicated for stable angina workup or post-MI viability assessment — not acute shock<br />
用于稳定型心绞痛检查或心梗后存活心肌评估——不用于急性休克</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most common distractor is Choice A (cardiac catheterization) — while it may be needed if echo reveals stent thrombosis, echo must precede cath to differentiate mechanical complications (papillary rupture, VSD, tamponade) from pure ischemic LV dysfunction, as management differs fundamentally.*

最常见干扰项是 Choice A（心导管检查）——虽然超声发现支架血栓后最终可能需要心导管，但超声必须先行，以区分机械性并发症（乳头肌断裂、室间隔缺损、心脏压塞）与单纯缺血性左室功能障碍，因两者的处置方案根本不同。
