疼痛特征</td>
<td>Diffuse soreness from trauma; may have tearing chest/back pain<br />
创伤引起的弥漫性酸痛；可有撕裂样胸背痛</td>
<td>Sudden tearing/ripping chest pain radiating to back (Type B: interscapular)<br />
突发撕裂样胸痛放射至背部（B 型：肩胛间区）</td>
<td>Severe chest pain + odynophagia; Mackler's triad<br />
剧烈胸痛 + 吞咽痛；Mackler 三联征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key CXR finding<br />
关键胸片表现</td>
<td>Widened mediastinum, loss of aortic knob, left hemothorax<br />
纵隔增宽、主动脉弓消失、左侧血胸</td>
<td>Widened mediastinum, aortic contour enlargement<br />
纵隔增宽、主动脉轮廓增大</td>
<td>Mediastinal air, left pleural effusion, subcutaneous emphysema<br />
纵隔积气、左侧胸腔积液、皮下气肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard diagnosis<br />
金标准诊断</td>
<td>CT angiography<br />
CT 血管造影</td>
<td>CT angiography<br />
CT 血管造影</td>
<td>Water-soluble contrast esophagography (Gastrografin)<br />
水溶性造影剂食管造影（泛影葡胺）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>TEVAR or open surgical repair<br />
TEVAR 或开放手术修复</td>
<td>Type A: emergent surgery; Type B: BP control ± TEVAR<br />
A 型：急诊手术；B 型：血压控制 ± TEVAR</td>
<td>Primary surgical repair + broad-spectrum antibiotics for mediastinitis<br />
一期手术修复 + 广谱抗生素治疗纵隔炎</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In any deceleration trauma patient with tachycardia and a widened mediastinum on chest x-ray, traumatic aortic disruption at the isthmus must be presumed until CT angiography rules it out.**

**任何减速创伤患者出现心动过速和胸片纵隔增宽时，必须在 CT 血管造影排除之前假定存在主动脉峡部创伤性损伤。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — AORTA for Traumatic Aortic Disruption / 记忆钩 — AORTA 助记符记忆创伤性主动脉损伤:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>cceleration-deceleration mechanism (head-on MVC, high-speed fall) / 加速-减速机制（正面碰撞、高速坠落）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>utcome: ~80% die at scene; isthmus is the #1 site (90%) / 结局：约 80% 现场死亡；峡部是第一好发部位（90%）<br />
• <strong>R</strong>adiograph — widened mediastinum (&gt;8 cm), loss of aortic knob / 胸片——纵隔增宽（&gt;8 cm）、主动脉弓消失<br />
• <strong>T</strong>EVAR is first-line repair (endovascular); open surgery if anatomy unfavorable / TEVAR 是一线修复方案（腔内）；解剖条件不佳则开放手术<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ngio-CT chest is gold standard for diagnosis and injury grading / 胸部 CT 血管造影是诊断和损伤分级的金标准</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Traumatic Aortic Injury / 高频知识表 — 创伤性主动脉损伤

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common injury site<br />
最常见损伤部位</td>
<td>Aortic isthmus (~90%): just distal to left subclavian artery origin at the ligamentum arteriosum; the transition between the mobile arch and the fixed descending aorta; second most common is the ascending aorta near the aortic root<br />
主动脉峡部（约 90%）：左锁骨下动脉起源远端、动脉韧带处；活动弓部与固定降主动脉的过渡点；第二常见为升主动脉近主动脉根部</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic CXR findings<br />
经典胸片表现</td>
<td>Widened mediastinum (&gt;8 cm at aortic knob level), loss of aortic knob contour, rightward tracheal deviation, left apical pleural cap (extrapleural blood), left hemothorax, depression of left mainstem bronchus<br />
纵隔增宽（主动脉弓水平 &gt;8 cm）、主动脉弓轮廓消失、气管右偏、左肺尖胸膜帽（胸膜外血液）、左侧血胸、左主支气管受压下移</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard diagnosis<br />
金标准诊断</td>
<td>CT angiography of the chest; differentiates AAST grades I–IV (intimal tear → pseudoaneurysm → rupture); echocardiography and formal aortography used historically but now rarely needed<br />
胸部 CT 血管造影；区分 AAST I–IV 级（内膜撕裂→假性动脉瘤→破裂）；超声心动图和正规主动脉造影历史上使用，现已少需要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Survival epidemiology<br />
存活流行病学</td>
<td>~80% die at scene (complete transection); ~10–15% arrive at ED with a contained tear; of those who arrive, risk of free rupture is high — even "stable" patients can decompensate without warning<br />
约 80% 现场死亡（完全横断）；约 10–15% 以包裹性撕裂到达急诊；到达急诊者仍有高度游离破裂风险——即使"稳定"患者也可无预警恶化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AAST injury grading<br />
AAST 损伤分级</td>
<td>Grade I (intimal tear only): medical management with BP control; Grade II (intramural hematoma) and Grade III (pseudoaneurysm): TEVAR; Grade IV (rupture with free hemorrhage): emergent open or endovascular repair<br />
I 级（仅内膜撕裂）：血压控制药物治疗；II 级（壁内血肿）和 III 级（假性动脉瘤）：TEVAR；IV 级（游离出血性破裂）：急诊开放或腔内修复</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hemodynamic management before repair<br />
修复前血流动力学管理</td>
<td>Permissive hypotension (target SBP 80–90 mm Hg) to reduce aortic wall tension and prevent extension; avoid aggressive fluid resuscitation that raises BP and increases shear stress on the contained hematoma<br />
允许性低血压（目标收缩压 80–90 mmHg）以降低主动脉壁张力并防止扩展；避免积极补液升压，以免增加包裹性血肿的剪切应力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associated injuries in blunt chest trauma<br />
钝性胸外伤伴随损伤</td>
<td>Rib fractures, pulmonary contusion, hemopneumothorax, sternal fracture, cardiac contusion, solid organ lacerations (spleen, liver, kidney); aortic injury evaluation must occur within the context of full trauma survey<br />
肋骨骨折、肺挫伤、血气胸、胸骨骨折、心肌挫伤、实质脏器撕裂伤（脾、肝、肾）；主动脉损伤评估必须在全面创伤评估框架内进行</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of widened mediastinum:** Traumatic aortic injury, spontaneous aortic dissection, esophageal perforation with mediastinitis, anterior mediastinal mass (lymphoma, thymoma), pericardial effusion, and superior vena cava syndrome — mechanism and clinical context are the key discriminators\
  **纵隔增宽鉴别诊断:** 创伤性主动脉损伤、自发性主动脉夹层、食管穿孔伴纵隔炎、前纵隔肿块（淋巴瘤、胸腺瘤）、心包积液和上腔静脉综合征——机制和临床背景是关键鉴别要素

- **Variant — other deceleration mechanisms:** High-speed falls from height (\>3 meters), aircraft ejection, and pedestrian-versus-vehicle collisions carry identical aortic shear risk; the mechanism (deceleration), not the vehicle type, is the critical trigger for suspicion\
  **变式——其他减速机制:** 高处坠落（\>3 米）、飞机弹射和行人与车辆碰撞具有相同主动脉剪切风险；关键触发因素是机制（减速），而非交通工具类型

- **Key complication — delayed traumatic pseudoaneurysm:** A missed contained partial tear can organize into a chronic traumatic pseudoaneurysm presenting years later as an incidental mediastinal mass; always obtain CT angiography in blunt chest trauma patients with any mediastinal abnormality on CXR\
  **重要并发症——迟发性创伤性假性动脉瘤:** 漏诊的包裹性部分撕裂可机化形成慢性创伤性假性动脉瘤，数年后以偶发纵隔肿块就诊；所有胸片纵隔异常的钝性胸外伤患者均应行 CT 血管造影

- **TEVAR vs. open repair considerations:** TEVAR has lower perioperative mortality and avoids thoracotomy; however, it requires adequate proximal landing zone (≥15 mm from left subclavian artery) and may not be suitable for all anatomy; long-term endograft surveillance is mandatory\
  **TEVAR vs. 开放手术考量:** TEVAR 具有更低的围手术期死亡率且避免开胸手术；但需要足够的近端锚定区（距左锁骨下动脉 ≥15 mm），不适合所有解剖结构；术后必须进行长期腔内移植物随访

# Question 131 — Cancer Pain: Opioid Dose Titration / 癌症疼痛：阿片类药物剂量滴定

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>77-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-week history of increasing back pain</strong>. <strong>Eight years ago, he was diagnosed with prostate cancer.</strong> Gonadotropin inhibitor therapy was begun, and he was asymptomatic until 2 months ago; <strong>metastatic lesions at L3 and T8</strong> were confirmed at that time. Ibuprofen therapy sufficiently controlled the pain for 1 month, after which <strong>oxycodone (5 mg every 4 hours)</strong> and laxatives were added to the medication regimen. At his last visit 1 month ago, he reported his pain as between <strong>0 and 2 on a 10-point scale</strong>. He now describes his pain as <strong>4 to 5 on a 10-point scale.</strong> Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Massage therapy and reevaluation in 1 week<br />
B) Add oral acetaminophen therapy to the regimen<br />
C) Begin intravenous morphine therapy<br />
D) Begin oral propoxyphene therapy<br />
E) Increase the oxycodone dosage by 25% to 50%<br />
F) Switch from codeine to meperidine therapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>77-year-old man with prostate cancer diagnosed 8 years ago<br />
77岁男性，8年前确诊前列腺癌</td>
<td>Metastatic prostate cancer is a classic cause of chronic severe cancer pain requiring long-term opioid management<br />
转移性前列腺癌是需要长期阿片类药物管理的慢性重度癌症疼痛的经典病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Metastatic lesions at L3 and T8<br />
L3和T8处转移性病灶</td>
<td>Bone metastases cause opioid-responsive pain; also raises concern for spinal cord compression if new neurologic signs develop<br />
骨转移引起阿片类药物反应性疼痛；若出现新发神经系统体征还需警惕脊髓压迫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Oxycodone 5 mg every 4 hours (already on scheduled opioid)<br />
羟考酮5mg每4小时一次（已在使用定时阿片类药物）</td>
<td>This is the agent to titrate for progressive pain — scheduled oral opioids are the backbone of cancer pain management<br />
这是针对进展性疼痛需要滴定的药物——定时口服阿片类药物是癌症疼痛管理的基础</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain 0–2/10 last month, now 4–5/10<br />
上月疼痛0–2/10，现为4–5/10</td>
<td>Demonstrates progressive/breakthrough pain — current dose is insufficient, but oxycodone was previously effective<br />
表明疼痛进展/突破——当前剂量不足，但羟考酮既往有效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Laxatives already co-prescribed<br />
已同时处方泻药</td>
<td>Confirms appropriate management of opioid-induced constipation — the prescriber understands opioid side effects<br />
证实已妥善处理阿片类药物所致便秘——处方者了解阿片类药物副作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Previously well-controlled pain (0–2/10)<br />
既往疼痛控制良好（0–2/10）</td>
<td>Confirms oxycodone is an effective agent for this patient; the problem is underdosing, not drug failure<br />
证实羟考酮对该患者有效；问题是剂量不足，而非药物失效</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Opioid analgesics** exert their effects primarily through **mu (μ) opioid receptor agonism** in the central and peripheral nervous systems, modulating **pain transmission** at multiple levels:

**阿片类镇痛药**主要通过在中枢和外周神经系统激动 **μ阿片受体** 发挥作用，在多个层面调节**疼痛传导**：

- Inhibit presynaptic release of substance P and glutamate → reduces ascending pain signal transmission\
  抑制突触前P物质和谷氨酸的释放 → 减少上行疼痛信号传导

- Hyperpolarize postsynaptic neurons via increased K⁺ conductance and decreased Ca²⁺ influx → raises pain threshold\
  通过增加K⁺电导和减少Ca²⁺内流使突触后神经元超极化 → 提高疼痛阈值

- Activate descending inhibitory pathways from the periaqueductal gray to the dorsal horn\
  激活从导水管周围灰质到脊髓背角的下行抑制通路

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Oral opioids on a scheduled (fixed-interval) dosing schedule provide basal analgesia. When pain "breaks through" or progressively worsens, dose titration of the existing agent is the correct first move — increase scheduled dose by 25–50%, not switch to IV or add weak adjuvants.

**解剖小窍门:** 定时给药的口服阿片类药物提供基础镇痛。当疼痛"突破"或进行性加重时，正确的第一步是对现有药物进行剂量滴定——在定时剂量基础上增加25–50%，而非换用静脉给药或添加弱辅助药物。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Opioid Dose Titration for Progressive Cancer Pain / 正确答案 (E) — 进展性癌症疼痛的阿片类药物剂量滴定

**Opioid dose titration** is the standard first step when a patient on scheduled oral opioids develops worsening pain that was previously controlled:

**阿片类药物剂量滴定**是定时口服阿片类药物的患者发生既往已控制的疼痛加重时的标准首选步骤：

- Current dose: oxycodone 5 mg q4h = 30 mg/day total; a 25–50% increase yields ~6.5–7.5 mg q4h (≈37.5–45 mg/day)\
  当前剂量：羟考酮5mg/4h = 30mg/天；增加25–50%后约为6.5–7.5mg/4h（≈37.5–45mg/天）

- Titrating the existing agent avoids premature escalation to IV opioids and unnecessary drug switching\
  滴定现有药物可避免过早升级为静脉阿片类药物和不必要的换药

- The 25–50% increment balances adequate analgesia against overdose risk; severe pain may warrant up to 100% increase\
  增加25–50%在充分镇痛与过量风险之间取得平衡；严重疼痛可增加至100%

**Diagnosis:** Progressive cancer pain on current opioid dose — pain increased from 0–2/10 to 4–5/10 despite scheduled oxycodone, confirming underdosing rather than drug failure.

**诊断:** 当前阿片类药物剂量下的进展性癌症疼痛——尽管按时服用羟考酮，疼痛从0–2/10升至4–5/10，证实为剂量不足而非药物失效。

**Treatment:** Increase scheduled oxycodone by 25–50%; reassess within days; reserve transdermal patches or IV opioids for pain refractory to adequate oral doses.

**治疗:** 将定时羟考酮剂量增加25–50%；数天内重新评估；将经皮贴片或静脉阿片类药物保留用于足量口服后仍难治的疼痛。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Massage therapy and reevaluation in 1 week<br />
A — 按摩治疗并1周后复诊</td>
<td>Wrong — bone metastases do not respond to massage; nonpharmacologic therapy alone is wholly inadequate for metastatic cancer pain<br />
错误——骨转移对按摩无效；单纯非药物治疗对转移性癌症疼痛完全不足</td>
<td>Bone metastasis pain requires pharmacologic management; massage cannot address the pathophysiologic cause<br />
骨转移疼痛需要药物治疗；按摩无法解决病理生理原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Add oral acetaminophen therapy to the regimen<br />
B — 加用口服对乙酰氨基酚</td>
<td>Wrong — acetaminophen provides far less analgesia than opioids and is inadequate for this pain level; also carries hepatotoxicity risk at high doses<br />
错误——对乙酰氨基酚镇痛力远弱于阿片类药物，对此疼痛程度不足；高剂量还有肝毒性风险</td>
<td>Pain level and etiology (bone mets on opioids) require opioid titration, not addition of a non-opioid adjuvant<br />
疼痛程度和病因（已用阿片类药物的骨转移）需要阿片类药物滴定，而非添加非阿片类辅助药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Begin intravenous morphine therapy<br />
C — 开始静脉吗啡治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — IV opioids are appropriate for truly refractory pain uncontrolled on high oral doses; this patient is on a low dose and has not been adequately titrated yet<br />
错误——静脉阿片类药物适用于高剂量口服无效的真正难治性疼痛；此患者剂量低且尚未充分滴定</td>
<td>IV opioids are premature; oral titration must be attempted first before parenteral escalation<br />
静脉阿片类药物为时过早；在升级为肠外给药前必须先尝试口服滴定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Begin oral propoxyphene therapy<br />
D — 开始口服右丙氧芬治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — propoxyphene (Darvon) was withdrawn from the US market in 2010 due to fatal QT prolongation and cardiac arrhythmias; no longer available<br />
错误——右丙氧芬（Darvon）因致命性QT间期延长和心律失常于2010年从美国市场撤出，不再可用</td>
<td>Propoxyphene is a withdrawn drug — automatically never the correct answer on USMLE<br />
右丙氧芬是已撤市药物——在USMLE中永远自动排除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Increase the oxycodone dosage by 25% to 50% ✓<br />
E — 将羟考酮剂量增加25%至50% ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — guideline-concordant first step for breakthrough or progressive pain in a patient on scheduled oral opioids<br />
正确——定时口服阿片类药物患者出现突破性或进展性疼痛时的指南一致性首选步骤</td>
<td>25–50% dose titration is the established evidence-based protocol for inadequate opioid analgesia<br />
增加25–50%是阿片类药物镇痛不足的成熟循证方案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Switch from codeine to meperidine therapy<br />
F — 从可待因换为哌替啶治疗</td>
<td>Wrong on two counts: patient is on oxycodone, not codeine; and meperidine is contraindicated for cancer pain because normeperidine (toxic metabolite) accumulates causing seizures and delirium<br />
双重错误：患者服用的是羟考酮而非可待因；且哌替啶因毒性代谢物去甲哌替啶蓄积导致癫痫和谵妄，禁用于癌症疼痛</td>
<td>Meperidine is specifically contraindicated for chronic/cancer pain — neurotoxic metabolite accumulation with repeated dosing<br />
哌替啶特别禁用于慢性/癌症疼痛——反复给药导致神经毒性代谢物蓄积</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (IV morphine) — it is technically appropriate for refractory cancer pain but premature here; this question specifically tests whether you know to titrate the existing oral opioid before escalating to parenteral therapy.*

最诱人的干扰项是选项C（静脉吗啡）——它在技术上适用于难治性癌症疼痛，但在此处操之过急；本题专门考查在升级为肠外给药前是否知道先滴定现有口服阿片类药物。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Opioid Escalation Strategy: Titration vs. Route Change vs. Rotation / 阿片类药物升级策略：剂量滴定 vs. 给药途径改变 vs. 阿片类药物轮换

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Oral Dose Titration</strong><br />
<strong>口服剂量滴定</strong></th>
<th><strong>IV/Parenteral Switch</strong><br />
<strong>改为静脉/肠外给药</strong></th>
<th><strong>Opioid Rotation</strong><br />
<strong>阿片类药物轮换</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>When to use<br />
使用时机</td>
<td>First-line for breakthrough or progressive pain on current scheduled oral opioid<br />
当前定时口服阿片类药物下突破性或进展性疼痛的一线方案</td>
<td>Pain refractory to adequate oral doses; unable to swallow; crisis pain<br />
足量口服无效的难治性疼痛；无法吞咽；疼痛危象</td>
<td>Intolerable side effects at effective dose; suspected incomplete cross-tolerance<br />
有效剂量下不可耐受的副作用；疑似不完全交叉耐受</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dose adjustment<br />
剂量调整</td>
<td>Increase current scheduled dose by 25–50% (up to 100% for severe pain)<br />
将当前定时剂量增加25–50%（严重疼痛可至100%）</td>
<td>Convert oral dose via equianalgesic table; reduce 25–50% for safety<br />
通过等效镇痛换算表换算口服剂量；安全起见减少25–50%</td>
<td>Reduce new agent by 25–50% to account for incomplete cross-tolerance<br />
新药减少25–50%以弥补不完全交叉耐受</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reassessment timing<br />
重新评估时机</td>
<td>Within days; titrate until pain ≤3/10<br />
数天内；滴定至疼痛≤3/10</td>
<td>Hours (controlled setting); rapid titration possible<br />
数小时（受控环境）；可快速滴定</td>
<td>Within 24–48 hours of switching<br />
换药后24–48小时内</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Example agents<br />
示例药物</td>
<td>Oxycodone IR/ER, morphine IR/SR, hydromorphone<br />
羟考酮速释/缓释、吗啡速释/缓释、氢吗啡酮</td>
<td>Morphine IV, hydromorphone IV, fentanyl IV/PCA<br />
静脉吗啡、静脉氢吗啡酮、静脉/PCA芬太尼</td>
<td>Oxycodone → fentanyl patch; morphine → hydromorphone<br />
羟考酮→芬太尼贴片；吗啡→氢吗啡酮</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Laxative requirement<br />
泻药要求</td>
<td>Always — constipation does not develop tolerance with opioids<br />
始终——阿片类药物所致便秘不产生耐受</td>
<td>Always<br />
始终</td>
<td>Always; restart prophylaxis with new agent<br />
始终；换药后重新开始预防</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For a cancer patient on scheduled oral opioids with progressive pain, increase the current dose by 25–50% before escalating to IV opioids or switching agents.**

**对于按时口服阿片类药物后疼痛进展的癌症患者，应在升级为静脉阿片类药物或换药之前将当前剂量增加25–50%。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — TITRATE Before You Escalate / 记忆钩 — 升级前先滴定 "TITRATE":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>T</strong>itrate current oral opioid by 25–50% first — always the first move for breakthrough pain / 先将当前口服阿片类药物滴定25–50%——突破性疼痛的第一步<br />
• <strong>I</strong>V opioids only for pain refractory to adequate oral doses or for NPO patients / 静脉阿片类药物仅用于足量口服无效或无法口服的患者<br />
• <strong>T</strong>oxic/Terminated drugs never win: propoxyphene (cardiac death) and meperidine (seizures) are always wrong / 毒性/撤市药物永远不对：右丙氧芬（心源性死亡）和哌替啶（癫痫）始终是错误答案<br />
• <strong>R</strong>eassess frequently — target pain ≤3/10; adjust until goal achieved / 频繁重新评估——目标疼痛≤3/10；调整至达标<br />
• <strong>A</strong>lways co-prescribe laxatives — opioid constipation never tolerates (unlike nausea and sedation) / 始终同时处方泻药——阿片类药物便秘不产生耐受（不同于恶心和镇静）<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ransdermal or rotation next — after oral titration fails at adequate doses / 之后考虑经皮或轮换——在足量口服滴定失败后<br />
• <strong>E</strong>scalate stepwise — WHO ladder guides: non-opioid → mild opioid → strong opioid / 逐步升级——WHO阶梯指导：非阿片类→弱阿片类→强阿片类</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cancer Pain Management & Opioid Pharmacology / 高频知识表 — 癌症疼痛管理与阿片类药物药理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>WHO Analgesic Ladder<br />
WHO镇痛阶梯</td>
<td>Step 1: NSAIDs/acetaminophen → Step 2: mild opioids (codeine, tramadol) → Step 3: strong opioids (morphine, oxycodone, hydromorphone, fentanyl); adjuvants (steroids, antidepressants, anticonvulsants) may be added at any step<br />
第1步：NSAIDs/对乙酰氨基酚→第2步：弱阿片类（可待因、曲马多）→第3步：强阿片类（吗啡、羟考酮、氢吗啡酮、芬太尼）；任何步骤均可加辅助药（糖皮质激素、抗抑郁药、抗惊厥药）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opioid dose titration protocol<br />
阿片类药物剂量滴定方案</td>
<td>Increase scheduled oral dose by 25–50% for breakthrough/progressive pain; up to 100% for severe or crisis pain; reassess within days<br />
突破/进展性疼痛将定时口服剂量增加25–50%；严重或危象性疼痛可增加至100%；数天内重新评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opioid side effects and tolerance<br />
阿片类药物副作用与耐受性</td>
<td>Constipation — NO tolerance develops (always prescribe laxatives); nausea, sedation, respiratory depression — tolerance develops with time; pruritus most common with intrathecal use<br />
便秘——不产生耐受（始终处方泻药）；恶心、镇静、呼吸抑制——随时间产生耐受；瘙痒最常见于鞘内用药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Propoxyphene (Darvon)<br />
右丙氧芬（达尔丰）</td>
<td>Withdrawn from US market in 2010 due to fatal QT prolongation and ventricular arrhythmias (FDA withdrawal); never correct on USMLE<br />
因致命性QT间期延长和室性心律失常于2010年从美国市场撤出（FDA撤市）；在USMLE中永远不是正确答案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Meperidine contraindication in cancer pain<br />
哌替啶在癌症疼痛中的禁忌</td>
<td>Normeperidine (active metabolite) accumulates with repeated dosing → lowers seizure threshold, causes myoclonus and delirium; short half-life requires q3–4h dosing, accelerating accumulation; avoid in renal impairment and elderly<br />
反复给药导致去甲哌替啶（活性代谢物）蓄积→降低癫痫阈值、引起肌阵挛和谵妄；半衰期短需q3–4h给药，加速蓄积；肾损害和老年患者禁用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Equianalgesic opioid conversion<br />
等效镇痛阿片类药物换算</td>
<td>Oral morphine 30 mg ≈ oral oxycodone 20 mg ≈ oral hydromorphone 7.5 mg ≈ fentanyl patch 12.5 mcg/h; when rotating, reduce new dose 25–50% for incomplete cross-tolerance<br />
口服吗啡30mg≈口服羟考酮20mg≈口服氢吗啡酮7.5mg≈芬太尼贴片12.5mcg/h；轮换时因不完全交叉耐受将新剂量减少25–50%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Spinal cord compression in bone mets<br />
骨转移脊髓压迫</td>
<td>New/worsening back pain + neurologic symptoms in cancer patient → urgent MRI; treat with high-dose dexamethasone + radiation ± surgery; irreversible paralysis if delayed<br />
癌症患者新发/加重的背痛+神经系统症状→急诊MRI；予大剂量地塞米松+放疗±手术；延误可导致不可逆性瘫痪</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Prostate Cancer Bone Metastases Pattern:** Osteoblastic (sclerotic) lesions — "ivory vertebra" on X-ray; elevated alkaline phosphatase; PSA used for disease monitoring; zoledronic acid or denosumab reduces skeletal-related events\
  **前列腺癌骨转移模式:** 成骨性（硬化性）病灶——X线上"象牙椎体"；碱性磷酸酶升高；PSA用于疾病监测；唑来膦酸或地舒单抗减少骨骼相关事件

- **Adjuvant Analgesics for Neuropathic Component:** Gabapentin/pregabalin for neuropathic pain from nerve root compression at L3/T8; NSAIDs/steroids for inflammatory bone pain; radiation therapy for localized painful bone metastases\
  **神经病理性成分的辅助镇痛药:** 加巴喷丁/普瑞巴林用于L3/T8神经根压迫的神经病理性疼痛；NSAIDs/糖皮质激素用于炎症性骨痛；局部放疗用于局限性疼痛性骨转移

- **Principle of Double Effect:** Providing adequate opioids for cancer pain is ethically justified even if respiratory depression secondarily hastens death — palliative intent (relieve suffering) distinguishes this from euthanasia\
  **双重效应原则:** 为癌症疼痛提供足量阿片类药物在伦理上是合理的，即使呼吸抑制可能间接加速死亡——姑息意图（缓解痛苦）将其与安乐死区分开来

- **Opioid Use Disorder vs. Cancer Pain:** Patients with cancer pain on appropriate opioids demonstrate tolerance and physical dependence (expected) — do not confuse with addiction (compulsive use despite harm); pseudoaddiction describes drug-seeking due to undertreated pain\
  **阿片类药物使用障碍与癌症疼痛:** 接受适当阿片类药物治疗的癌症疼痛患者会出现耐受性和躯体依赖（预期现象）——不要与成瘾（尽管有害仍强迫使用）混淆；假性成瘾描述因疼痛治疗不足导致的觅药行为

# Question 132 — Allergic Asthma: Dust Mite Allergen Avoidance / 过敏性哮喘：尘螨变应原规避

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>18-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician for a follow-up examination. She has a <strong>5-year history of asthma</strong> treated with <strong>inhaled albuterol as needed</strong> and <strong>inhaled beclomethasone daily</strong>. She has never required treatment in the hospital for an acute episode. She says that her asthma is <strong>worse after she spends prolonged periods of time indoors</strong> and after she <strong>visits homes of friends who own cats</strong>. Her house has hardwood floors, which she and her family clean every week. She sleeps with her windows closed and changes her bedding regularly. She does not smoke or drink alcohol. Examination shows no abnormalities. The lungs are clear to auscultation. <strong>Skin testing shows allergies to dust mites and cat dander.</strong> The physician advises the patient to avoid direct contact with cats. Which of the following environmental changes is likely to be most helpful in preventing exacerbations of this patient's asthma?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following environmental changes is likely to be most helpful in preventing exacerbations of this patient's asthma?</strong></p>
<p>A) Humidifier use<br />
B) Placement of carpet in her bedroom<br />
C) Sleeping with the windows open<br />
D) Use of allergen-impermeable mattress and pillow covers<br />
E) Vacuuming the floors of her house daily</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>5-year history of asthma on daily ICS + PRN SABA<br />
5年哮喘史，使用每日ICS + 按需SABA</td>
<td>Persistent asthma on controller therapy — optimization requires allergen avoidance, not just medication adjustment<br />
持续性哮喘已用控制治疗——优化需要变应原规避，而不仅仅是调整药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worse with prolonged time indoors<br />
长时间在室内症状加重</td>
<td>Points to indoor allergen trigger rather than outdoor (pollen, pollution, cold air)<br />
指向室内变应原诱因，而非户外（花粉、污染物、冷空气）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worse in homes of friends who own cats<br />
在养猫朋友家症状加重</td>
<td>Identifies cat dander as a specific exacerbating allergen<br />
确认猫毛皮屑为特异性加重变应原</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>House has hardwood floors, cleaned weekly<br />
家中硬木地板，每周清洁</td>
<td>Already a protective factor; absence of carpets reduces allergen reservoir<br />
已有防护因素；无地毯减少变应原储库</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin testing positive for dust mites AND cat dander<br />
皮肤点刺试验：尘螨和猫毛皮屑均阳性</td>
<td>Confirms IgE-mediated sensitization to two specific indoor allergens; guides targeted avoidance<br />
证实对两种室内变应原存在IgE介导致敏；指导针对性规避</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sleeps with windows closed, changes bedding regularly<br />
关窗睡觉，定期更换床上用品</td>
<td>Some protective measures already in place; the missing step is encasing the mattress and pillow<br />
已采取部分防护措施；缺失的步骤是套住床垫和枕头</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Dust mites** (*Dermatophagoides pteronyssinus* and *farinae*) are the most prevalent indoor allergen worldwide. They thrive in **warm, humid environments** and colonize **mattresses, pillows, carpets, and upholstered furniture** — areas where humans shed skin scales (their primary food source):

**尘螨**（屋尘螨和粉尘螨）是全球最常见的室内变应原。它们在**温暖潮湿的环境**中大量繁殖，聚集于**床垫、枕头、地毯和布艺家具**——人类脱落皮屑（其主要食物来源）最多的区域：

- Sensitized individuals produce **IgE antibodies** against dust mite fecal proteins (Der p 1, Der f 1); re-exposure triggers mast cell degranulation → **early-phase bronchoconstriction** and **late-phase eosinophilic airway inflammation**\
  致敏个体产生针对尘螨粪便蛋白（Der p 1、Der f 1）的**IgE抗体**；再次接触触发肥大细胞脱颗粒→**早期支气管痉挛**和**迟发相嗜酸性粒细胞气道炎症**

- A person spends approximately 8 hours per night in bed, making the **mattress and pillow** the single highest-exposure reservoir for dust mite allergen in any home\
  人每晚在床上约8小时，使**床垫和枕头**成为任何家庭中尘螨变应原暴露量最高的单一储库

- **Allergen-impermeable encasements** (fabric with pore size \<10 μm) create a durable physical barrier between the person and the mite colony, reducing airborne allergen levels by over 50%\
  **防变应原密封套**（孔径\<10μm的织物）在人与尘螨群落之间形成持久物理屏障，使空气中变应原水平降低50%以上

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Dust mites live where humans sleep — encase the mattress and pillow first, then address the rest of the room.

**解剖小窍门:** 尘螨生活在人类睡觉的地方——先封住床垫和枕头，再处理房间其他区域。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Allergen-Impermeable Mattress and Pillow Covers / 正确答案 (D) — 防变应原床垫与枕头密封套

**Allergen-impermeable encasements** are the most evidence-based, single intervention for reducing dust mite exposure in sensitized asthmatic patients:

**防变应原密封套**是减少致敏哮喘患者尘螨暴露中循证证据最强的单一干预措施：

- Mattresses and pillows harbor millions of dust mites and cannot be routinely laundered; encasements permanently seal this allergen reservoir\
  床垫和枕头藏匿数百万尘螨且无法定期水洗；密封套能永久封闭这一变应原储库

- Randomized trials show encasements reduce peak expiratory flow variability, nighttime symptoms, and rescue inhaler use in dust-mite-sensitive asthmatics\
  随机试验显示密封套可降低尘螨敏感哮喘患者的峰流速变异性、夜间症状和急救吸入剂使用频率

- This patient already has hardwood floors, closed windows at night, and regular bedding changes — encasements are the logical next missing step\
  该患者已有硬木地板、夜间关窗和定期换洗床品——密封套是合乎逻辑的缺失下一步

**Diagnosis:** Allergic (extrinsic) asthma with documented IgE sensitization to dust mites and cat dander; nightly mattress allergen exposure is the primary unaddressed modifiable trigger.

**诊断:** 过敏性（外源性）哮喘，证实存在针对尘螨和猫毛皮屑的IgE致敏；夜间床垫变应原暴露是首要未解决的可干预诱因。

**Treatment:** Allergen-impermeable encasements + continued cat avoidance combined with current pharmacotherapy (daily ICS + PRN SABA); consider allergen immunotherapy or step-up therapy if symptoms remain uncontrolled.

**治疗:** 防变应原密封套+继续避免接触猫，联合现有药物治疗（每日ICS + 按需SABA）；若症状仍不受控，考虑变应原免疫治疗或升级药物治疗。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Humidifier use<br />
A — 使用加湿器</td>
<td>Dust mites thrive at relative humidity &gt;50%; humidifiers increase indoor humidity and directly promote mite proliferation<br />
尘螨在相对湿度&gt;50%时繁殖旺盛；加湿器增加室内湿度，直接促进尘螨增殖</td>
<td>Humidity ↑ = dust mite burden ↑; this is the opposite of what a dust-mite-sensitized patient needs<br />
湿度↑=尘螨负荷↑；这与尘螨致敏患者的需求完全相反</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Placement of carpet in her bedroom<br />
B — 在卧室铺地毯</td>
<td>Carpets are a major reservoir for dust mites, pet dander, and mold; foot traffic disperses allergens into the breathing zone<br />
地毯是尘螨、宠物皮屑和霉菌的主要储库；踩踏使变应原扬入呼吸区</td>
<td>Patient already has protective hardwood floors; adding carpet would significantly worsen allergen exposure<br />
患者已有保护性硬木地板；铺地毯会显著加重变应原暴露</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Sleeping with the windows open<br />
C — 开窗睡觉</td>
<td>Increases exposure to outdoor allergens (pollen, mold spores, air pollution) without reducing established indoor allergen burden<br />
增加户外变应原（花粉、霉菌孢子、空气污染物）暴露，但不能减少已有的室内变应原负荷</td>
<td>Confirmed triggers are indoor (dust mites, cat dander); open windows do not address the primary problem and introduce additional triggers<br />
已证实诱因为室内（尘螨、猫毛皮屑）；开窗无法解决主要问题且引入额外诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Use of allergen-impermeable mattress and pillow covers ✓<br />
D — 使用防变应原床垫与枕头密封套 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — directly seals the highest-exposure dust mite reservoir where this patient spends 8 hours nightly<br />
正确——直接封闭该患者每晚暴露8小时的最高尘螨变应原储库</td>
<td>Addresses the primary uncontrolled modifiable trigger with the strongest clinical evidence<br />
以最强临床证据针对首要未控制的可干预诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Vacuuming the floors of her house daily<br />
E — 每天吸尘</td>
<td>Vacuuming aerosolizes fine allergen particles even while removing surface dust; daily frequency adds little additional benefit over weekly cleaning<br />
吸尘在清除表面灰尘的同时使细微变应原颗粒扬入空气；每日吸尘相比每周清洁几乎没有额外获益</td>
<td>Patient already has hardwood floors (low-allergen surface); daily vacuuming does not target the mattress, which is the primary mite reservoir<br />
患者已有硬木地板（低变应原表面）；每天吸尘无法针对床垫这一主要尘螨储库</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E — daily vacuuming seems proactive and hygienic, but it paradoxically aerosolizes fine allergen particles and does not address the mattress, which is the patient's primary dust mite exposure source.*

最易迷惑人的干扰项是选项E——每天吸尘看似积极且卫生，但实际上会将细微变应原颗粒扬入空气，且无法针对床垫这一该患者的主要尘螨暴露来源。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Helpful vs. Harmful Environmental Interventions for Dust-Mite-Sensitive Asthma / 尘螨敏感哮喘有益与有害环境干预对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Recommended (Reduces Exposure)</strong><br />
<strong>推荐（降低暴露）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Contraindicated (Increases Exposure)</strong><br />
<strong>禁忌（增加暴露）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Bedding strategy<br />
床上用品策略</td>
<td>Allergen-impermeable mattress + pillow encasements; hot water wash (&gt;55°C) weekly<br />
防变应原床垫+枕头密封套；每周热水（&gt;55°C）洗涤</td>
<td>No encasements; infrequent washing; feather-filled pillows<br />
不用密封套；洗涤不频繁；羽绒枕头</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Flooring<br />
地板</td>
<td>Hardwood, tile, or linoleum floors<br />
硬木地板、瓷砖或油毡地板</td>
<td>Carpeting, especially in the bedroom<br />
地毯，尤其是卧室地毯</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Humidity control<br />
湿度控制</td>
<td>Dehumidifier; maintain RH &lt;50%<br />
除湿机；维持相对湿度&lt;50%</td>
<td>Humidifier; RH &gt;50% promotes mite growth<br />
加湿器；RH&gt;50%促进尘螨生长</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vacuuming<br />
吸尘</td>
<td>HEPA-filtered vacuum; patient absent during vacuuming<br />
HEPA过滤吸尘器；吸尘时患者不在场</td>
<td>Standard (non-HEPA) vacuum; patient present; daily frequency provides minimal extra benefit<br />
普通（非HEPA）吸尘器；患者在场；每日吸尘几乎无额外获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Window management<br />
窗户管理</td>
<td>Keep windows closed during high-pollen seasons<br />
高花粉季节保持关窗</td>
<td>Sleeping with windows open; increases outdoor allergen infiltration<br />
开窗睡觉；增加室外变应原渗入</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Air filtration<br />
空气过滤</td>
<td>HEPA air purifier in bedroom (primarily for cat dander/mold)<br />
卧室HEPA空气净化器（主要针对猫毛皮屑/霉菌）</td>
<td>No air filtration in high-allergen environments<br />
高变应原环境中不使用空气过滤</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For a dust-mite-sensitized asthmatic who spends 8 hours nightly in the highest-allergen spot in the home, allergen-impermeable mattress and pillow encasements are the most evidence-based single environmental intervention.**

**对于每晚在家中最高变应原区域——床上——度过8小时的尘螨致敏哮喘患者，防变应原床垫与枕头密封套是循证证据最强的单一环境干预措施。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The D-A-M-P Rule for Dust Mite Control / 记忆钩 — 尘螨控制 "D-A-M-P" 法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>ust-mite encasements first — allergen-impermeable mattress and pillow covers are the #1 proven intervention / 尘螨密封套优先——防变应原床垫和枕头套是第一位循证干预<br />
• <strong>A</strong>void carpets — hard floors harbor far fewer mites than carpet fibers / 避免地毯——硬地板藏匿的尘螨远少于地毯纤维<br />
• <strong>M</strong>aintain low humidity — target RH &lt;50%; humidifiers are contraindicated in dust-mite allergy / 维持低湿度——目标RH&lt;50%；加湿器在尘螨过敏中是禁忌<br />
• <strong>P</strong>illow encasements too — don't forget pillows; encase both mattress AND pillow / 枕头也要套——别忘了枕头；床垫和枕头都要套上</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Indoor Allergen Management in Allergic Asthma / 高频知识表 — 过敏性哮喘室内变应原管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Dust mite biology<br />
尘螨生物学</td>
<td><em>Dermatophagoides</em> spp.; thrive at &gt;50% RH and &gt;20°C; feed on human skin scales; major allergens are fecal proteins Der p 1 and Der f 1<br />
尘螨属；在RH&gt;50%和&gt;20°C中繁殖；以人类皮屑为食；主要变应原为粪便蛋白Der p 1和Der f 1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Allergen-impermeable encasements<br />
防变应原密封套</td>
<td>Woven fabric with pore size &lt;10 μm; must cover mattress, box spring, and pillows; reduces airborne allergen by &gt;50%; evidence supports improved asthma outcomes<br />
孔径&lt;10μm编织面料；必须覆盖床垫、床箱和枕头；使空气中变应原降低&gt;50%；有证据支持改善哮喘结局</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hot water laundering<br />
热水洗涤</td>
<td>Washing bedding at ≥55°C (130°F) kills dust mites; cold water washing physically removes mites but does not kill them<br />
在≥55°C（130°F）洗涤床上用品可杀死尘螨；冷水洗涤只能物理去除尘螨而不能杀灭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Humidifier contraindication<br />
加湿器禁忌</td>
<td>Indoor humidity &gt;50% RH promotes dust mite proliferation and mold growth; humidifiers are contraindicated for dust-mite-sensitive patients<br />
室内湿度&gt;50%RH促进尘螨繁殖和霉菌生长；对尘螨敏感患者，加湿器是禁忌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vacuuming paradox<br />
吸尘悖论</td>
<td>Standard vacuuming aerosolizes fine allergen particles; HEPA-filtered vacuums are preferred; patient should not be present during vacuuming; once-weekly is sufficient for hardwood floors<br />
普通吸尘使细微变应原颗粒扬起；首选HEPA过滤吸尘器；吸尘时患者不应在场；硬木地板每周一次即可</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cat allergen (Fel d 1) characteristics<br />
猫变应原（Fel d 1）特性</td>
<td>Secreted from cat skin glands and saliva; highly airborne and adherent to surfaces; persists in homes for months after cat removal; HEPA filtration + cat exclusion from bedroom are primary strategies<br />
由猫皮脂腺和唾液分泌；高度空气传播且黏附表面；猫移走后在家中持续数月；HEPA过滤+猫不进卧室是主要策略</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin prick test clinical correlation<br />
皮肤点刺试验临床相关性</td>
<td>Positive test confirms IgE sensitization but must correlate with clinical history (asthma worsens with exposure); guides allergen-specific avoidance and immunotherapy candidacy<br />
阳性结果证实IgE致敏，但必须与临床病史相关联（接触时哮喘加重）；指导特异性变应原规避和免疫治疗候选资格</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Allergen immunotherapy (AIT):** If environmental controls and pharmacotherapy remain insufficient, subcutaneous or sublingual immunotherapy with dust mite extracts can desensitize the patient and reduce long-term asthma severity and medication burden\
  **变应原免疫治疗（AIT）:** 若环境控制和药物治疗仍不足，皮下或舌下尘螨提取物免疫治疗可使患者脱敏，减轻长期哮喘严重程度和用药负担

- **GINA step-up consideration:** This patient is on Step 2 (low-dose ICS + PRN SABA); if allergen avoidance fails to reduce exacerbations, Step 3 therapy (medium-dose ICS or low-dose ICS/LABA combination) should be considered per GINA guidelines\
  **GINA升级治疗考虑:** 该患者处于第2阶梯（低剂量ICS + 按需SABA）；若变应原规避未能减少急性发作，应按GINA指南考虑第3阶梯治疗（中剂量ICS或低剂量ICS/LABA联合）

- **Mold as co-indoor allergen:** *Alternaria* and *Cladosporium* mold species are common indoor allergens that co-exist with dust mites; management includes fixing plumbing leaks, using bathroom exhaust fans, and maintaining humidity below 50%\
  **霉菌作为共同室内变应原:** 交链孢霉和枝孢霉是常见室内变应原，与尘螨共存；管理包括修复管道漏水、使用浴室排气扇、维持湿度低于50%

- **Differential of indoor vs. outdoor asthma triggers:** Indoor triggers (dust mites, pet dander, mold, cockroach) worsen with time spent inside; outdoor triggers (pollen, air pollution, cold air) worsen during outdoor activity or seasonally — history and skin testing distinguish them\
  **室内与室外哮喘诱因鉴别:** 室内诱因（尘螨、宠物皮屑、霉菌、蟑螂）在室内停留时间长时加重；室外诱因（花粉、空气污染、冷空气）在户外活动或季节性时加重——病史和皮肤试验可区分两者

# Question 133 — Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder / 强迫症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>44-year-old man</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>6-month history of intermittent moderate headache</strong>. He has had <strong>one to two headaches weekly</strong> since residents of the neighboring apartment got a dog that barks a lot. He says he has had <strong>recurrent thoughts about killing the dog</strong> during the past 6 months, but he has no intent or plan to harm the animal. He worries that his headaches are punishment for these thoughts about killing; he says <strong>he realizes this does not make sense</strong> but remains concerned. He <strong>vacuums 2 hours daily</strong> because he is worried that dog hair is coming into his apartment. He has no history of serious illness. His only medication is acetaminophen, which resolves his headaches. He drinks two to three 12-oz beers on weekends. His pulse is 72/min, respirations are 16/min, and blood pressure is 150/105 mm Hg. Physical examination shows no other abnormalities. Mental status examination shows an <strong>anxious affect</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Delusional disorder<br />
B) Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
C) Obsessive-compulsive disorder<br />
D) Paranoid personality disorder<br />
E) Somatic symptom disorder</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Recurrent thoughts about killing the dog — unwanted, intrusive<br />
反复出现想杀狗的念头——非自愿、侵入性</td>
<td>Classic obsession: ego-dystonic intrusive thought causing anxiety<br />
经典强迫思维：自我不协调的侵入性想法，引起焦虑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Realizes it does not make sense, but remains concerned<br />
意识到不合理，但仍无法控释</td>
<td>Preserved insight is hallmark of OCD; distinguishes from delusion<br />
保留自知力是强迫症标志，与妄想障碍的关键区别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vacuums 2 hours daily for dog hair<br />
每天吸尘2小时以防狗毛进入</td>
<td>Classic compulsion: repetitive behavior aimed at neutralizing obsessional anxiety<br />
经典强迫行为：重复行为以中和强迫焦虑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worries headaches are punishment for bad thoughts<br />
担心头痛是恶念的惩罚</td>
<td>Magical thinking pattern linked to obsessional guilt — still retains insight<br />
强迫性内疚的魔幻思维模式，但保留自知力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No intent or plan to harm the animal<br />
无伤害动物的意图或计划</td>
<td>Rules out actual violent ideation; the thought is ego-dystonic, not acted upon<br />
排除真实暴力意图；思维是自我不协调的，未付诸行动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anxious affect on mental status exam<br />
精神状态检查显示焦虑情感</td>
<td>Confirms anxiety as the driving emotional state underlying OCD<br />
证实焦虑是强迫症背后的驱动情感状态</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Obsessive-compulsive disorder** is driven by a cycle of **ego-dystonic intrusive thoughts** (obsessions) that generate **anxiety**, followed by **compulsive behaviors** that temporarily relieve that anxiety, thereby reinforcing the cycle through negative reinforcement:

**强迫症**由**自我不协调的侵入性思维**（强迫思维）驱动，产生**焦虑**，随后**强迫行为**暂时缓解焦虑，通过负强化进一步巩固这一循环：

- Obsessions are unwanted, repetitive thoughts that the patient recognizes as irrational yet cannot suppress\
  强迫思维是患者认为不合理却无法压制的非自愿、重复性思维

- Compulsions are repetitive behaviors or mental acts performed to reduce obsessional distress — relief is temporary\
  强迫行为是为减轻强迫痛苦而进行的重复行为或心理活动——缓解是暂时的

- Preserved insight (ego-dystonia) is key: the patient knows the thoughts and behaviors are excessive but cannot stop\
  保留自知力（自我不协调）是关键：患者知道思维和行为过度但无法停止

- Serotonergic dysregulation in cortico-striato-thalamo-cortical (CSTC) circuits underlies the pathophysiology\
  皮质-纹状体-丘脑-皮质（CSTC）环路的5-羟色胺失调是病理生理基础

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The CSTC loop, when hyperactive, creates a stuck "stuck record" of thought — SSRIs dampen this loop by restoring serotonin balance in the striatum.

**解剖小窍门:** CSTC环路过度活跃时，产生"卡碟"式的重复思维——SSRIs通过恢复纹状体5-羟色胺平衡来抑制这一环路。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder / 正确答案 (C) — 强迫症

**Obsessive-compulsive disorder (OCD)** is characterized by obsessions (intrusive, ego-dystonic thoughts/urges causing anxiety) and/or compulsions (repetitive behaviors aimed at neutralizing that anxiety), with preserved insight:

**强迫症（OCD）** 以强迫思维（侵入性、自我不协调的思想/冲动引起焦虑）和/或强迫行为（旨在中和焦虑的重复行为）为特征，保留自知力：

- Obsessions: recurrent thoughts of killing the dog + magical thinking that headaches are punishment\
  强迫思维：反复出现杀狗念头 + 头痛是惩罚的魔幻思维

- Compulsions: 2 hours of daily vacuuming to prevent dog hair contamination\
  强迫行为：每天吸尘2小时以防狗毛污染

- Insight intact: patient explicitly states "he realizes this does not make sense"\
  自知力完整：患者明确表示"意识到这没有道理"

- Duration ≥ 6 months with significant time consumption (\>1 hour/day) confirms clinical significance\
  持续≥6个月且消耗大量时间（\>1小时/天）确认临床意义

**Diagnosis:** OCD requires obsessions and/or compulsions that are time-consuming (\>1 hr/day) or cause clinically significant distress/impairment, with ego-dystonic recognition of irrationality.

**诊断:** 强迫症要求强迫思维和/或行为耗时（\>1小时/天）或造成显著痛苦/损害，且具有自我不协调的不合理性认识。

**Treatment:** First-line: SSRIs (fluoxetine, fluvoxamine, sertraline) + cognitive behavioral therapy (CBT) with Exposure and Response Prevention (ERP). Second-line: clomipramine (TCA) or venlafaxine (SNRI).

**治疗:** 一线治疗：SSRIs（氟西汀、氟伏沙明、舍曲林）+ 认知行为治疗（CBT），重点是暴露与反应阻止（ERP）。二线：氯米帕明（TCA）或文拉法辛（SNRI）。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Delusional disorder<br />
A — 妄想障碍</td>
<td>Delusions are fixed false beliefs held with certainty — patient here retains insight and knows thoughts are irrational<br />
妄想是坚定持有的固定错误信念——本患者保留自知力，知道想法不合理</td>
<td>Preserved insight (ego-dystonia) rules out delusion; delusions are ego-syntonic<br />
保留自知力（自我不协调）排除妄想；妄想是自我协调的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
B — 广泛性焦虑障碍</td>
<td>GAD features excessive worry about multiple life domains (health, finances, family), not specific intrusive thoughts paired with ritualistic behaviors<br />
GAD以多个生活领域的过度担忧为特征，而非与仪式行为配对的特定侵入性思维</td>
<td>Specific obsession-compulsion pairing (dog thoughts → vacuuming) distinguishes OCD from GAD's diffuse worry<br />
特定的强迫思维-行为配对（狗的想法→吸尘）将OCD与GAD的弥漫性担忧区分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Obsessive-compulsive disorder ✓<br />
C — 强迫症 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Ego-dystonic intrusive obsessions (killing dog, magical headache punishment) + time-consuming compulsion (2 hrs vacuuming) + intact insight<br />
正确——自我不协调的侵入性强迫思维（杀狗、魔幻惩罚）+ 耗时的强迫行为（吸尘2小时）+ 完整自知力</td>
<td>Classic obsession + compulsion dyad with preserved insight<br />
经典的强迫思维+行为二联征，保留自知力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Paranoid personality disorder<br />
D — 偏执型人格障碍</td>
<td>PPD features pervasive mistrust and suspicion of others' motives; no intrusive thoughts or compulsive rituals<br />
偏执型人格障碍以对他人动机的普遍不信任和怀疑为特征；无侵入性思维或强迫仪式</td>
<td>PPD = "others are out to get me" (external threat); OCD = "my own mind is betraying me" (internal)<br />
偏执型人格障碍="别人要害我"（外部威胁）；OCD="我自己的思维在背叛我"（内部）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Somatic symptom disorder<br />
E — 躯体症状障碍</td>
<td>SSD requires preoccupation with somatic symptoms causing disproportionate distress; headaches here resolve with acetaminophen and are not the focus of the psychiatric illness<br />
躯体症状障碍需要对躯体症状的过度关注造成不成比例的痛苦；头痛用对乙酰氨基酚即缓解，不是精神疾病的核心</td>
<td>Primary issue is intrusive thoughts + ritualistic behavior, not bodily symptom preoccupation<br />
主要问题是侵入性思维+仪式行为，而非躯体症状的过度关注</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is (B) GAD — both involve anxiety and repetitive worry. The key is the stereotyped obsession-compulsion pairing: a specific intrusive thought (dog/hair) driving a specific ritual (vacuuming) is OCD, not the diffuse, free-floating worry of GAD.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是(B)GAD——两者都涉及焦虑和反复担忧。关键在于固定的强迫思维-行为配对：特定侵入性思维（狗/狗毛）驱动特定仪式（吸尘）是OCD，而非GAD的弥漫性、游离性担忧。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — OCD vs. GAD vs. Delusional Disorder / OCD vs. GAD vs. 妄想障碍鉴别

<table>
<colgroup>

<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />

<th><strong>OCD</strong><br />
<strong>强迫症</strong></th>

<strong>妄想障碍</strong></th>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Core pathology<br />

自我不协调强迫思维+行为</td>
<td>Excessive, uncontrollable worry (multiple domains)<br />

固定、错误、不可动摇的信念</td>

<tr>
<td>Insight<br />
自知力</td>
<td>Intact — recognizes irrationality<br />
完整——认识到不合理</td>
<td>Intact — knows worry is excessive<br />

仪式行为</td>

思维内容</td>
<td>Specific intrusive themes (contamination, harm, symmetry)<br />
特定侵入性主题（污染、伤害、对称）</td>
<td>Diffuse real-life worries (health, job, family)<br />
弥漫性现实担忧（健康、工作、家庭）</td>
<td>Usually persecutory, grandiose, or somatic<br />
通常为被迫害、夸大或躯体性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>SSRI + CBT/ERP<br />
SSRIs + CBT/暴露反应阻止</td>
<td>SSRI/SNRI + CBT<br />
SSRIs/SNRIs + CBT</td>
<td>Antipsychotics (low-dose)<br />
抗精神病药（低剂量）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Duration criterion<br />
病程标准</td>
<td>≥1 hr/day; causes distress or impairment<br />
≥1小时/天；导致痛苦或损害</td>
<td>≥6 months of worry more days than not<br />
≥6个月多数时间担忧</td>
<td>≥1 month of delusion(s)<br />
≥1个月的妄想</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**OCD presents with ego-dystonic obsessions (intrusive, irrational thoughts the patient recognizes as their own but cannot stop) paired with compulsions (rituals that temporarily relieve anxiety), treated with SSRIs and CBT/ERP.**

**强迫症以自我不协调的强迫思维（患者认识到是自己的想法但无法停止的侵入性、非理性思维）配合强迫行为（暂时缓解焦虑的仪式）为特征，用SSRIs和CBT/ERP治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — OCD "3 O's" Rule / 记忆钩 — 强迫症"3个O"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>O</strong>bsessions — unwanted intrusive thoughts (ego-DYStonic = patient knows they're irrational) / 强迫思维——非自愿侵入性思维（自我不协调 = 患者知道不合理）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>verride attempt — compulsions are the failed attempt to "override" the anxiety (vacuuming, handwashing, counting) / 强迫行为——强迫行为是"覆盖"焦虑的失败尝试（吸尘、洗手、计数）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>nly relief is temporary — compulsions provide momentary relief, reinforcing the cycle via negative reinforcement / 缓解只是暂时的——强迫行为提供短暂缓解，通过负强化强化循环</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — OCD Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 强迫症诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 Diagnostic Criteria for OCD<br />
DSM-5强迫症诊断标准</td>
<td>Presence of obsessions, compulsions, or both; time-consuming (&gt;1 hr/day) or causing significant distress/impairment; not attributable to substances or another medical condition<br />
存在强迫思维、强迫行为或两者兼有；耗时（&gt;1小时/天）或造成显著痛苦/损害；不归因于物质或其他躯体疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Insight Specifier<br />
自知力标注</td>
<td>Good/fair insight (recognizes OCD beliefs are probably not true); poor insight; absent insight/delusional beliefs — determines treatment approach and prognosis<br />
良好/一般自知力（认识到OCD信念可能不真实）；自知力差；无自知力/妄想性信念——决定治疗方法和预后</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-Line Pharmacotherapy<br />
一线药物治疗</td>
<td>SSRIs (fluoxetine, fluvoxamine, sertraline, paroxetine); require higher doses and longer duration (8-12 weeks) than for depression<br />
SSRIs（氟西汀、氟伏沙明、舍曲林、帕罗西汀）；需要比抑郁症更高剂量和更长疗程（8-12周）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Second-Line Agents<br />
二线药物</td>
<td>Clomipramine (TCA — most serotonergic of TCAs, effective but more side effects); venlafaxine (SNRI); augmentation with low-dose antipsychotics for refractory cases<br />
氯米帕明（TCA——TCAs中5-羟色胺能最强，有效但副作用更多）；文拉法辛（SNRI）；难治性病例用低剂量抗精神病药增效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CBT with ERP<br />
暴露反应阻止CBT</td>
<td>Gold-standard psychotherapy: deliberately expose patient to feared stimulus (dog hair), then prevent the compulsive response (vacuuming) — extinguishes anxiety over time<br />
金标准心理治疗：故意将患者暴露于恐惧刺激（狗毛），然后阻止强迫反应（吸尘）——随时间消除焦虑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common OCD Subtypes<br />
常见OCD亚型</td>
<td>Contamination/cleaning; harm obsessions (as here); symmetry/ordering; forbidden thoughts (sexual, religious, aggressive); hoarding disorder (separate DSM-5 diagnosis)<br />
污染/清洁；伤害强迫（如本题）；对称/整理；禁忌思想（性、宗教、攻击性）；囤积障碍（单独的DSM-5诊断）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OCD vs. OCPD<br />
OCD vs. 强迫型人格障碍</td>
<td>OCD = ego-dystonic obsessions + compulsions (distressing, recognized as irrational); OCPD = ego-syntonic pervasive pattern of orderliness, perfectionism, control (feels "right" to patient)<br />
OCD = 自我不协调强迫思维+行为（痛苦，认识到不合理）；OCPD = 自我协调的普遍整洁、完美主义、控制模式（患者感觉"正确"）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Magical thinking in OCD:** Belief that one's thoughts can directly cause harm (thinking about killing → headache as punishment) is a classic OCD cognitive distortion, not a delusion — insight is preserved\
  **OCD中的魔幻思维:** 相信自己的想法能直接造成伤害（想到杀戮→头痛作为惩罚）是经典OCD认知扭曲，不是妄想——自知力保留

- **Blood pressure finding:** BP 150/105 in this 44-year-old is incidental hypertension requiring follow-up — a common NBME "red herring" to distract from the psychiatric diagnosis\
  **血压发现:** 这位44岁患者BP 150/105是偶然发现的高血压需要随访——NBME常见"红鲱鱼"以分散对精神诊断的注意

- **Comorbidity pattern:** OCD frequently co-occurs with major depression (30-40%), other anxiety disorders, and tic disorders (especially in pediatric OCD); always screen for these\
  **共病模式:** OCD频繁与重性抑郁（30-40%）、其他焦虑障碍和抽动障碍共病（尤其在儿科OCD中）；始终筛查这些

- **Harm obsessions distinction:** Ego-dystonic harm obsessions (like this patient) are NOT predictive of actual violence — they are distressing precisely because the patient does NOT want to cause harm; contrast with true homicidal ideation\
  **伤害性强迫思维的区别:** 自我不协调的伤害性强迫思维（如本患者）不预测实际暴力——它们之所以令人痛苦正是因为患者不想造成伤害；与真正的杀人意念相区别

# Question 134 — Bell's Palsy in Pregnancy / 妊娠合并贝尔麻痹

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>27-year-old primigravid woman</strong> at <strong>32 weeks' gestation</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>2-day history of progressive drooping of the right side of her face</strong>, an <strong>inability to close her right eye</strong>, and <strong>right-sided facial pain</strong>. She has <strong>not had loss of hearing or balance</strong>. Her pregnancy had been uncomplicated. She has no personal or family history of serious illness. Her temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 88/min, respirations is 16/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 140/82 mm Hg</strong>. Examination of the face shows <strong>paralysis on the right side and an inability to close the right eye</strong>. The patient moves her head stiffly; there is <strong>no nuchal rigidity</strong>. Heart sounds are normal. A grade 2/6 holosystolic murmur is heard best at the apex. The abdomen is soft. The fundal height is 32 cm. There is mild edema of the lower extremities. Muscle strength is normal. Deep tendon reflexes are 2+. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Carotid ultrasonography<br />
B) CT scan of the head<br />
C) Corticosteroid therapy<br />
D) Angiography of the brain<br />
E) Nerve conduction studies</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Complete unilateral facial paralysis including inability to close eye<br />
完全单侧面瘫且无法闭眼</td>
<td>Upper + lower face both affected = LMN lesion (Bell's palsy); if only lower face → UMN (stroke)<br />
上下面部均受累 = 下运动神经元病变（贝尔麻痹）；若仅下面部 → UMN（卒中）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>32 weeks' gestation, third trimester<br />
妊娠 32 周，第三孕期</td>
<td>Bell's palsy incidence is 3× higher in pregnancy, peaking in third trimester and postpartum<br />
贝尔麻痹在妊娠期发病率高 3 倍，第三孕期及产后期达高峰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No hearing loss, no balance disturbance<br />
无听力丧失，无平衡障碍</td>
<td>Distinguishes Bell's palsy from Ramsay Hunt syndrome (VZV, CN VII + VIII, ear vesicles)<br />
与 Ramsay Hunt 综合征鉴别（VZV，CN VII + VIII，耳廓疱疹）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Right-sided facial pain<br />
右侧面部疼痛</td>
<td>Classic prodrome of Bell's palsy — nerve inflammation within narrow bony facial canal causes pain<br />
贝尔麻痹典型前驱症状——骨性面神经管内神经炎症引起疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No nuchal rigidity, no other focal neurological deficits<br />
无颈项强直，无其他局灶性神经功能缺损</td>
<td>Rules out meningitis, brainstem encephalitis, or ischemic stroke as underlying cause<br />
排除脑膜炎、脑干脑炎或缺血性卒中作为基础病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal muscle strength, DTR 2+<br />
肌力正常，腱反射 2+</td>
<td>No limb weakness = lesion confined to CN VII, not a hemispheric event<br />
无肢体无力 = 病变局限于 CN VII，非半球性事件</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Bell's palsy** results from **inflammation and edema** of the **facial nerve (CN VII)** within the narrow **bony facial canal (stylomastoid foramen)**. The swollen nerve becomes compressed against the bony walls, producing **complete ipsilateral LMN palsy** of all facial muscles.

**贝尔麻痹**由**面神经（CN VII）**在狭窄**骨性面神经管（茎乳孔）**内发生**炎症和水肿**引起，水肿的神经被压迫在骨壁之间，导致同侧所有面部肌肉的**完全性下运动神经元麻痹**：

- LMN lesion (Bell's palsy): forehead AND lower face affected ipsilaterally — cannot wrinkle brow, close eye, or smile on affected side\
  LMN 病变（贝尔麻痹）：同侧额部和下面部均受累——无法皱眉、闭眼或微笑

- UMN lesion (stroke): forehead spared — bilateral cortical representation of forehead muscles means only the contralateral lower face is weakened\
  UMN 病变（卒中）：额部保留——额肌受双侧皮质支配，故仅对侧下面部无力

- Pregnancy association: increased fluid retention causes relative nerve compression; immunologic shift toward Th2 promotes HSV-1 reactivation within the geniculate ganglion\
  妊娠关联：体液潴留增加导致相对神经受压；Th2 免疫偏移促进膝状神经节内 HSV-1 再激活

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The forehead is the decisive clue — forehead weakness = peripheral CN VII (treat with steroids); forehead spared = central UMN (work up for stroke).

**解剖小窍门:** 额部是决定性线索——额部无力 = 周围性 CN VII（糖皮质激素治疗）；额部保留 = 中枢性 UMN（排查卒中）。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Corticosteroid Therapy / 正确答案 (C) — 糖皮质激素治疗

**Oral corticosteroids (prednisolone)** are the mainstay of treatment for Bell's palsy, reducing nerve inflammation and substantially improving complete recovery rates when initiated promptly:

**口服糖皮质激素（泼尼松龙）**是贝尔麻痹的主要治疗手段，及时启动可减轻神经炎症并显著提高完全恢复率：

- Reduce edema and inflammatory mediators compressing CN VII within the bony canal\
  减轻压迫骨管内 CN VII 的水肿和炎症介质

- Best benefit when started within 72 hours of symptom onset; improves complete recovery from ~70% to ~85%\
  发病 72 小时内开始效果最佳；完全恢复率从约 70% 提升至约 85%

- Prednisolone is preferred in pregnancy over dexamethasone — it is extensively metabolized by placental 11β-HSD2, limiting fetal exposure\
  妊娠期优选泼尼松龙而非地塞米松——胎盘 11β-HSD2 广泛代谢泼尼松龙，限制胎儿暴露

- Antivirals (acyclovir/valacyclovir) may be added for severe cases, but evidence for Bell's palsy is weaker than for Ramsay Hunt\
  重症病例可加用抗病毒药（阿昔洛韦/伐昔洛韦），但其在贝尔麻痹中的证据弱于 Ramsay Hunt

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis — complete unilateral LMN facial palsy with forehead involvement, no other neurological deficits, no vesicles, typical history; imaging is not required in classic presentation.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——完全单侧 LMN 面瘫伴额部受累，无其他神经功能缺损，无疱疹，典型病史；典型表现无需影像学检查。

**Treatment:** Oral prednisolone 60 mg/day × 5 days then taper; eye protection (artificial tears during day, lubricating ointment + eye patch at night) to prevent corneal exposure ulceration.

**治疗:** 口服泼尼松龙 60 mg/d × 5 天后逐渐减量；眼部保护（白天人工泪液，夜间润滑眼膏 + 眼罩）防止角膜暴露性溃疡。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Carotid ultrasonography<br />
A — 颈动脉超声</td>
<td>Evaluates carotid stenosis causing TIA/stroke — irrelevant for isolated peripheral CN VII palsy with no hemispheric deficits<br />
评估颈动脉狭窄导致的 TIA/卒中——对孤立性周围性 CN VII 麻痹（无半球性缺损）无意义</td>
<td>Carotid disease causes hemispheric or retinal deficits, not isolated facial nerve palsy<br />
颈动脉病变引起半球或视网膜缺损，而非孤立性面神经麻痹</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — CT scan of the head<br />
B — 头颅 CT</td>
<td>Indicated for thunderclap headache or focal deficits suggesting stroke — forehead involvement here excludes UMN etiology; also exposes fetus to radiation unnecessarily<br />
适用于雷击样头痛或提示卒中的局灶缺损——本例额部受累已排除 UMN 病因；还会使胎儿不必要地暴露于辐射</td>
<td>Classic LMN Bell's palsy pattern in a pregnant patient is a clinical diagnosis; imaging does not change management<br />
妊娠患者典型 LMN 贝尔麻痹为临床诊断；影像学不改变处理方案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Corticosteroid therapy ✓<br />
C — 糖皮质激素治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — First-line treatment for Bell's palsy; oral prednisolone reduces CN VII inflammation and maximizes recovery<br />
正确——贝尔麻痹一线治疗；口服泼尼松龙减轻面神经炎症，最大化恢复率</td>
<td>Complete LMN facial palsy + third-trimester pregnancy = prompt corticosteroids, no imaging needed<br />
完全性 LMN 面瘫 + 第三孕期 = 及时糖皮质激素，无需影像学</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Angiography of the brain<br />
D — 脑血管造影</td>
<td>Invasive evaluation for large vessel occlusion in ischemic stroke — this patient has peripheral CN VII palsy, not a vascular hemispheric event<br />
评估缺血性卒中大血管闭塞的有创检查——患者为周围性面神经麻痹，非血管性半球事件</td>
<td>No hemiplegia, no aphasia, no altered consciousness — no indication for cerebral angiography<br />
无偏瘫、无失语、无意识改变——无脑血管造影指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Nerve conduction studies<br />
E — 神经传导研究</td>
<td>Can quantify axonal damage severity but are NOT needed for diagnosis or to initiate treatment — Bell's palsy is a clinical diagnosis<br />
可量化轴索损伤严重程度，但诊断和开始治疗均不需要——贝尔麻痹为临床诊断</td>
<td>NCS has no role in acute management; performing it would only delay corticosteroid therapy<br />
NCS 在急性处理中无作用；执行只会延误糖皮质激素治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is B — the BP of 140/82 mm Hg might raise concern for hypertensive or hemorrhagic stroke, but the complete LMN pattern (forehead weak), absence of limb deficits, and typical pregnancy-associated history clinch Bell's palsy clinically, making CT unnecessary and radiation-exposing.*

最迷惑的干扰项是 B——血压 140/82 mm Hg 可能引发对高血压性或出血性卒中的担忧，但完全性 LMN 模式（额部无力）、无肢体缺损以及典型妊娠相关病史已临床确诊贝尔麻痹，CT 既无必要又使胎儿暴露于辐射。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Bell's Palsy vs. UMN Facial Palsy vs. Ramsay Hunt Syndrome / 贝尔麻痹 vs. UMN 面瘫 vs. Ramsay Hunt 综合征

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bell's Palsy</strong><br />
<strong>贝尔麻痹</strong></th>
<th><strong>Central (UMN) Facial Palsy</strong><br />
<strong>中枢性（UMN）面瘫</strong></th>
<th><strong>Ramsay Hunt Syndrome</strong><br />
<strong>Ramsay Hunt 综合征</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Lesion location<br />
病变位置</td>
<td>Peripheral CN VII (LMN), facial canal<br />
周围性 CN VII（LMN），面神经管</td>
<td>Contralateral motor cortex or PLIC (UMN)<br />
对侧运动皮质或内囊后肢（UMN）</td>
<td>Geniculate ganglion, CN VII ± VIII<br />
膝状神经节，CN VII ± VIII</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Forehead weakness<br />
额部无力</td>
<td>Yes — both upper and lower face<br />
有——上下面部均受累</td>
<td>No — forehead spared bilaterally<br />
无——双侧皮质支配额部保留</td>
<td>Yes — both upper and lower face<br />
有——上下面部均受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eye closure<br />
眼睑闭合</td>
<td>Impaired — corneal exposure risk<br />
受损——角膜暴露风险</td>

完好（额部保留）</td>
<td>Impaired<br />

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Additional findings<br />
伴随表现</td>
<td>Facial pain, no vesicles, no hearing loss<br />
面部疼痛，无疱疹，无听力丧失</td>
<td>Arm/leg weakness, dysarthria, UMN signs<br />
肢体无力，构音障碍，UMN 体征</td>
<td>Ear vesicles (zoster), sensorineural hearing loss, vertigo<br />
耳廓疱疹，感音神经性听力丧失，眩晕</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cause<br />
病因</td>
<td>HSV-1 reactivation, inflammation<br />
HSV-1 再激活，炎症</td>
<td>Ischemic or hemorrhagic stroke<br />
缺血性或出血性卒中</td>
<td>VZV reactivation<br />
VZV 再激活</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Prednisolone ± acyclovir<br />
泼尼松龙 ± 阿昔洛韦</td>
<td>Thrombolytics (tPA), antihypertensives<br />
溶栓（tPA），降压治疗</td>
<td>Acyclovir + prednisolone (combined)<br />
阿昔洛韦 + 泼尼松龙（联合）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pregnancy link<br />
妊娠关联</td>
<td>3× higher risk, 3rd trimester peak<br />
风险高 3 倍，第三孕期高峰</td>
<td>Risk via pre-eclampsia/eclampsia<br />
子痫前期/子痫风险途径</td>
<td>No specific pregnancy association<br />
无特殊妊娠关联</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A pregnant woman at 32 weeks with complete ipsilateral facial paralysis including the forehead and no other neurological deficits has Bell's palsy, and the first-line management is prompt oral corticosteroids.**

**妊娠 32 周女性出现包括额部在内的完全同侧面瘫且无其他神经功能缺损，诊断为贝尔麻痹，一线处理为及时口服糖皮质激素。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "BELL" for Bell's Palsy Diagnosis &amp; Management / 记忆钩 — "BELL" 记忆贝尔麻痹诊断与处理:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>row (forehead) is weak — LMN pattern; if brow spared, think central stroke instead / 眉部（额部）无力——LMN 模式；若额部保留，考虑中枢性卒中<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ye cannot close — lagophthalmos means corneal ulcer risk; start eye drops and patch immediately / 眼睑无法闭合——兔眼意味着角膜溃疡风险；立即开始眼药水和眼罩<br />
• <strong>L</strong>MN of CN VII — facial canal inflammation/HSV-1; pain is a prodrome / CN VII 下运动神经元病变——面神经管炎症/HSV-1；疼痛是前驱症状<br />
• <strong>L</strong>aunch steroids promptly — prednisolone within 72 h; safe in pregnancy / 及时启动糖皮质激素——72 小时内泼尼松龙；妊娠期安全</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Bell's Palsy and CN VII Palsy / 高频知识表 — 贝尔麻痹与面神经麻痹

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>LMN vs UMN distinction<br />
LMN vs UMN 面瘫鉴别</td>
<td>LMN: forehead + lower face ipsilateral weakness (Bell's palsy, Ramsay Hunt); UMN: forehead spared, contralateral lower face only (stroke)<br />
LMN：同侧额部 + 下面部无力（贝尔麻痹、Ramsay Hunt）；UMN：额部保留，仅对侧下面部（卒中）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bell's palsy in pregnancy<br />
妊娠期贝尔麻痹</td>
<td>Risk is 3× higher; peaks in third trimester and first postpartum week; related to fluid retention and relative immunosuppression promoting HSV-1 reactivation<br />
风险高 3 倍；第三孕期和产后第一周达高峰；与体液潴留和相对免疫抑制促进 HSV-1 再激活有关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Etiology<br />
病因</td>
<td>Bell's palsy: HSV-1 reactivation in geniculate ganglion; Ramsay Hunt: VZV reactivation (same location but also involves CN VIII → hearing loss + vertigo)<br />
贝尔麻痹：膝状神经节 HSV-1 再激活；Ramsay Hunt：VZV 再激活（同部位但累及 CN VIII → 听力丧失 + 眩晕）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Corticosteroid regimen<br />
糖皮质激素方案</td>
<td>Oral prednisolone 60 mg/day × 5 days, then 10 mg/day taper × 5 days; start within 72 hours of onset for maximum benefit<br />
口服泼尼松龙 60 mg/d × 5 天，然后 10 mg/d 减量 × 5 天；发病 72 小时内开始以获最大获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eye protection<br />
眼部保护</td>
<td>Mandatory when eye closure is incomplete — artificial tears q2-4h, lubricating ointment at night, eye patch or moisture chamber goggles; prevents corneal exposure keratitis<br />
眼睑闭合不全时必须进行——人工泪液每 2-4 小时一次，夜间润滑眼膏，眼罩或湿房眼镜；预防角膜暴露性角膜炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognosis<br />
预后</td>
<td>~70% complete recovery without treatment; prednisolone improves this to ~85%; recovery occurs over weeks to months; residual synkinesis (aberrant reinnervation) may occur in incomplete recovery<br />
不治疗约 70% 完全恢复；泼尼松龙提高至约 85%；恢复历时数周至数月；不完全恢复时可能出现残余联带运动（异常神经再支配）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to image<br />
何时需影像学</td>
<td>Atypical features warrant MRI: gradual onset (weeks), no pain, multiple cranial nerve involvement, parotid mass, bilateral facial palsy, or failure to improve after 3 months<br />
不典型特征需 MRI：缓慢起病（数周）、无疼痛、多颅神经受累、腮腺肿块、双侧面瘫或 3 个月后无改善</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of unilateral LMN facial palsy:** Beyond Bell's palsy, consider Lyme disease (bilateral in endemic areas — check serology), parotid gland tumor (slow-onset, painless, no pain prodrome), cholesteatoma (progressive, ear findings), sarcoidosis (Heerfordt syndrome: facial palsy + uveitis + parotid enlargement)\
  **单侧 LMN 面瘫鉴别:** 除贝尔麻痹外，考虑莱姆病（流行区可双侧——查血清学）、腮腺肿瘤（缓慢起病、无痛、无疼痛前驱）、胆脂瘤（进行性、耳部表现）、结节病（Heerfordt 综合征：面瘫 + 葡萄膜炎 + 腮腺肿大）

- **Blood pressure in this case:** BP 140/82 at 32 weeks meets gestational hypertension criteria; however, normal DTRs, no proteinuria, no headache, and no visual changes make pre-eclampsia unlikely — the facial palsy is independent of the BP and should be treated with steroids regardless\
  **本例血压考量:** 32 周 BP 140/82 符合妊娠期高血压标准；但 DTR 正常、无蛋白尿、无头痛、无视觉改变，子痫前期可能性小——面瘫与血压无关，应独立给予糖皮质激素治疗

- **Key complication of incomplete eye closure:** Corneal exposure ulceration can lead to perforation and permanent vision loss — this is the most time-sensitive non-neurological complication; begin eye protection on the same day as diagnosis\
  **眼睑闭合不全的关键并发症:** 角膜暴露性溃疡可导致穿孔和永久性视力丧失——这是最具时间敏感性的非神经系统并发症；诊断当天即开始眼部保护

- **Mnemonic for Bell's vs. stroke:** "If the forehead moves, it's peripheral (Bell's); if the forehead grooves (is preserved), it's central (stroke)" — the forehead wrinkle test at bedside differentiates the two instantly\
  **贝尔麻痹与卒中记忆口诀:** "额部能动是周围性（贝尔麻痹）；额部完好是中枢性（卒中）"——床旁额部皱纹测试可立即鉴别二者

# Question 135 — Alzheimer's Disease Dementia / 阿尔茨海默病痴呆

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>73-year-old woman</strong> is brought to the clinic by her husband because of a <strong>6-month history of progressive memory difficulty</strong>. During this time, she has <strong>misplaced objects more frequently</strong> than usual and has had <strong>trouble following recipes</strong>. Six days ago, she <strong>became lost while walking their dog in their neighborhood</strong>. Today, she <strong>forgot that their daughter had called the previous day</strong>. The patient has type 2 diabetes mellitus and hypertension. Her medications are metformin and lisinopril. She does not smoke cigarettes or drink alcohol. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, she is <strong>oriented to person but not to place or time</strong>. She <strong>recalls zero of three objects after 5 minutes</strong>. She makes <strong>four errors when performing serial sevens</strong>. She can name the US President and Vice President. She can name eight animals in 1 minute. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Results of a complete blood count, her erythrocyte sedimentation rate, and results of liver and thyroid function tests are within the reference ranges. VDRL testing for syphilis is negative. MRIs of the brain are shown. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Deep brain stimulation<br />
B) Placement of a ventriculoperitoneal shunt<br />
C) Transcranial magnetic stimulation<br />
D) Treatment with an acetylcholine precursor<br />
E) Treatment with a cholinesterase inhibitor<br />
F) Treatment with a postsynaptic choline receptor agonist</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>73-year-old woman, 6-month progressive course<br />
73岁女性，6个月进行性病程</td>
<td>Age &gt;65 and insidious onset are hallmarks of Alzheimer's disease; subacute onset rules out delirium<br />
年龄&gt;65岁、隐匿起病是阿尔茨海默病的特征；亚急性起病排除谵妄</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gets lost in familiar neighborhood<br />
在熟悉的街区迷路</td>
<td>Visuospatial disorientation reflects hippocampal and entorhinal cortex involvement in early-to-moderate AD<br />
视空间定向障碍反映海马和内嗅皮质受累，见于早中期AD</td>

<tr>
<td>Forgets daughter's call from the day before<br />
忘记女儿前一天打来的电话</td>
<td>Episodic (anterograde) memory failure = classic early AD signature; declarative memory lost first<br />
情节记忆（顺行性遗忘）= 经典早期AD特征；陈述性记忆最先受损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
