5分钟后回忆0/3个物品</td>
<td>Severe short-term memory deficit; 0/3 is characteristic of AD, not normal aging or mild cognitive impairment<br />
严重短期记忆缺陷；0/3是AD的特征，正常老化或轻度认知障碍不会如此严重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Oriented to person but NOT to place or time<br />
对人定向保留，对地点/时间定向丧失</td>
<td>Disorientation to place/time in a non-delirious patient indicates moderate-stage AD<br />
非谵妄患者中地点/时间定向丧失提示中度AD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal CBC, ESR, LFTs, TFTs; VDRL negative<br />
CBC、ESR、肝功能、甲状腺功能正常；VDRL阴性</td>
<td>Workup excludes reversible causes of dementia (hypothyroidism, B12 deficiency, syphilis, hepatic encephalopathy)<br />
排查排除了可逆性痴呆病因（甲减、B12缺乏、梅毒、肝性脑病）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No gait instability, no urinary incontinence<br />
无步态不稳，无尿失禁</td>
<td>Absence of classic NPH triad helps distinguish AD from normal pressure hydrocephalus<br />
缺乏经典NPH三联征有助于将AD与正常压力脑积水区分</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Alzheimer's disease** results from the progressive loss of **cholinergic neurons** in the **nucleus basalis of Meynert** and basal forebrain, leading to a profound deficit of **acetylcholine (ACh)** in the cortex and hippocampus:

**阿尔茨海默病**源于**Meynert基底核**及基底前脑**胆碱能神经元**的进行性丧失，导致皮质和海马中**乙酰胆碱（ACh）**严重缺乏：

- Amyloid plaques (Aβ 42) and neurofibrillary tangles (hyperphosphorylated tau) accumulate and disrupt synaptic transmission\
  淀粉样斑块（Aβ42）和神经纤维缠结（过度磷酸化tau蛋白）积累，破坏突触传递

- Loss of cholinergic neurons → decreased ACh synthesis and release in cortical circuits\
  胆碱能神经元丧失 → 皮质回路中ACh合成和释放减少

- Acetylcholinesterase (AChE) continues to degrade the residual ACh → available ACh at synapses falls even further\
  乙酰胆碱酯酶（AChE）继续降解残余ACh → 突触处可用ACh进一步减少

- Cholinesterase inhibitors block AChE → preserve what little ACh remains → modest symptomatic improvement\
  胆碱酯酶抑制剂阻断AChE → 保留残余ACh → 症状轻度改善

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The nucleus basalis of Meynert (in the substantia innominata of the basal forebrain) is the primary source of cortical cholinergic innervation — it is the key structure damaged in AD.

**解剖小窍门:** Meynert基底核（位于基底前脑的无名质）是皮质胆碱能支配的主要来源——它是AD中受损的关键结构。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Cholinesterase Inhibitor Therapy / 正确答案 (E) — 胆碱酯酶抑制剂治疗

**Cholinesterase inhibitors** (donepezil, rivastigmine, galantamine) noncompetitively and reversibly inhibit AChE, thereby increasing synaptic ACh availability in the cortex and hippocampus:

**胆碱酯酶抑制剂**（多奈哌齐、卡巴拉汀、加兰他敏）非竞争性、可逆性地抑制AChE，从而增加皮质和海马突触处ACh的可利用性：

- They do not cure AD or halt neurodegeneration — they modestly slow cognitive decline and improve daily functioning\
  它们不能治愈AD或阻止神经退行性变——只能轻度延缓认知衰退，改善日常功能

- Donepezil is first-line for mild-to-moderate AD; rivastigmine patch is preferred for patients with GI intolerance\
  多奈哌齐是轻中度AD的一线药物；卡巴拉汀贴片适用于胃肠道不耐受患者

- Memantine (NMDA antagonist) is added for moderate-to-severe AD (MMSE \<15) and may be combined with a cholinesterase inhibitor\
  美金刚（NMDA拮抗剂）用于中重度AD（MMSE \<15），可与胆碱酯酶抑制剂联用

**Diagnosis:** This patient has classic moderate Alzheimer's dementia — progressive amnestic syndrome, disorientation to place/time, 0/3 recall, normal labs ruling out reversible causes, and MRI showing cortical atrophy with hippocampal volume loss.

**诊断:** 该患者具有典型中度阿尔茨海默病痴呆——进行性遗忘综合征、地点/时间定向丧失、0/3回忆、正常实验室检查排除可逆病因，MRI显示皮质萎缩伴海马体积减小。

**Treatment:** First-line: donepezil (5 mg daily, may increase to 10 mg). For moderate-severe stage, add memantine. Manage comorbidities; caregiver education and support are essential.

**治疗:** 一线：多奈哌齐（5 mg/日，可加量至10 mg）。中重度阶段加用美金刚。管理合并症；照料者教育和支持至关重要。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Deep brain stimulation<br />
A — 深部脑刺激</td>
<td>Effective for motor symptoms of Parkinson's disease (subthalamic nucleus or globus pallidus interna targets); no evidence of benefit in Alzheimer's dementia<br />
有效用于帕金森病运动症状（靶点：丘脑底核或苍白球内侧部）；在阿尔茨海默病痴呆中无获益证据</td>
<td>No motor symptoms (tremor, rigidity, bradykinesia) here; this is a purely amnestic presentation<br />
此处无运动症状（震颤、僵直、运动迟缓）；这是纯遗忘型表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Placement of a ventriculoperitoneal shunt<br />
B — 脑室腹腔分流术</td>
<td>Treats normal pressure hydrocephalus (NPH); this patient lacks the NPH triad (cognitive impairment + gait instability + urinary incontinence)<br />
用于治疗正常压力脑积水（NPH）；该患者缺乏NPH三联征（认知损害+步态不稳+尿失禁）</td>
<td>No gait ataxia, no urinary incontinence; ventriculomegaly alone on MRI is nonspecific and also seen in AD atrophy<br />
无步态共济失调，无尿失禁；MRI上单纯脑室扩大是非特异性发现，AD萎缩亦可见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Transcranial magnetic stimulation<br />
C — 经颅磁刺激</td>
<td>FDA-approved for treatment-resistant unipolar major depressive disorder, not dementia; depression can cause pseudodementia but this patient has 6 months of objective cognitive decline<br />
FDA批准用于难治性单相重性抑郁障碍，非痴呆；抑郁可引起假性痴呆，但该患者有6个月客观认知衰退</td>
<td>No depressive symptoms described; the cognitive profile (0/3 recall, serial sevens errors) exceeds what pseudodementia would produce<br />
无抑郁症状描述；认知特征（0/3回忆、连续7误差）超过假性痴呆的程度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Treatment with an acetylcholine precursor<br />
D — 乙酰胆碱前体治疗</td>
<td>Choline supplementation does not meaningfully raise brain ACh levels or improve AD symptoms despite the known cholinergic deficit<br />
尽管存在已知的胆碱能缺乏，补充胆碱并不能有效提高脑内ACh水平或改善AD症状</td>
<td>The blood-brain barrier limits choline delivery; clinical trials showed no benefit<br />
血脑屏障限制了胆碱的输送；临床试验显示无获益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Treatment with a cholinesterase inhibitor ✓<br />
E — 胆碱酯酶抑制剂治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Inhibiting AChE increases synaptic ACh and provides modest symptomatic improvement in Alzheimer's dementia<br />
正确——抑制AChE增加突触ACh，在阿尔茨海默病痴呆中提供轻度症状改善</td>
<td>Matches the pathophysiology (cholinergic deficit); donepezil is the standard of care<br />
符合病理生理机制（胆碱能缺乏）；多奈哌齐是标准治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Treatment with a postsynaptic choline receptor agonist<br />
F — 突触后胆碱能受体激动剂治疗</td>
<td>Muscarinic agonists were tested in AD but failed clinically; systemic side effects (bradycardia, excess secretions, GI cramping) are prohibitive<br />
毒蕈碱受体激动剂已在AD中测试但临床失败；全身副作用（心动过缓、分泌物增多、胃肠痉挛）难以耐受</td>
<td>Receptor agonists bypass the presynaptic deficit but lack selectivity and efficacy; not standard of care<br />
受体激动剂绕过突触前缺陷但缺乏选择性和疗效；非标准治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice B (VP shunt for NPH) — both NPH and AD cause cognitive impairment and ventriculomegaly on MRI, but NPH requires the full "wet, wobbly, wacky" triad; this patient has only cognitive impairment.*

VP分流术（选项B）是最迷惑性的干扰项——NPH和AD均可出现认知损害及MRI脑室扩大，但NPH需满足完整"尿湿、走路摇、思维乱"三联征；该患者仅有认知损害。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Alzheimer's Dementia vs. Normal Pressure Hydrocephalus / 阿尔茨海默病痴呆 vs. 正常压力脑积水

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Alzheimer's Dementia</strong><br />
<strong>阿尔茨海默病痴呆</strong></th>
<th><strong>Normal Pressure Hydrocephalus</strong><br />
<strong>正常压力脑积水</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation<br />
经典表现</td>
<td>Progressive amnestic syndrome, visuospatial deficits, word-finding difficulty<br />
进行性遗忘综合征、视空间缺陷、找词困难</td>
<td>"Wet, Wobbly, Wacky" triad: urinary incontinence + magnetic gait + cognitive impairment<br />
"尿湿、摇晃、迷糊"三联征：尿失禁+磁性步态+认知损害</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gait<br />
步态</td>
<td>Normal until late stages<br />
直到晚期才异常</td>
<td>Magnetic (wide-based, shuffling, feet appear glued to floor) — appears early<br />
磁性步态（宽基底、拖曳、双脚似粘地）——早期出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urinary symptoms<br />
泌尿系症状</td>
<td>Absent until advanced disease<br />
直至晚期才出现</td>
<td>Urinary incontinence or urgency — often an early symptom<br />
尿失禁或尿急——常为早期症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MRI findings<br />
MRI表现</td>
<td>Hippocampal/medial temporal atrophy; cortical atrophy; ex vacuo ventriculomegaly<br />
海马/内侧颞叶萎缩；皮质萎缩；代偿性脑室扩大</td>
<td>Communicating hydrocephalus (all ventricles enlarged out of proportion to sulci); periventricular edema<br />
交通性脑积水（脑室扩大与脑沟扩大不成比例）；脑室周围水肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CSF pressure<br />
脑脊液压力</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
<td>Normal (by definition, &lt; 25 cmH₂O) but volume increased<br />
正常（定义上&lt;25 cmH₂O）但容量增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Cholinesterase inhibitors (donepezil); memantine for moderate-severe<br />
胆碱酯酶抑制剂（多奈哌齐）；中重度加用美金刚</td>
<td>Ventriculoperitoneal (VP) shunt — can be dramatically effective if diagnosed early<br />
脑室腹腔（VP）分流术——早期诊断可获显著疗效</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In Alzheimer's disease, progressive cholinergic neuron loss causes a synaptic ACh deficit; cholinesterase inhibitors (donepezil) are first-line therapy by blocking ACh degradation to modestly preserve cognitive function.**

**阿尔茨海默病中，进行性胆碱能神经元丧失导致突触ACh缺乏；胆碱酯酶抑制剂（多奈哌齐）是一线治疗，通过阻断ACh降解来轻度保护认知功能。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — D-R-G Rule for AD Pharmacotherapy / 记忆钩 — AD药物治疗"D-R-G"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>onepezil — most commonly prescribed cholinesterase inhibitor; once-daily oral / 最常用胆碱酯酶抑制剂；每日一次口服<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ivastigmine — also inhibits butyrylcholinesterase; available as transdermal patch / 同时抑制丁酰胆碱酯酶；有贴片剂型<br />
• <strong>G</strong>alantamine — additionally modulates nicotinic ACh receptors (allosteric potentiator) / 还调节烟碱型ACh受体（变构增效剂）<br />
• <strong>M</strong>emantine — add for moderate-to-severe AD (NMDA antagonist, reduces excitotoxicity) / 中重度AD加用（NMDA拮抗剂，减少兴奋毒性）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Alzheimer's Disease: Diagnosis and Management / 高频知识表 — 阿尔茨海默病：诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Reversible dementia workup<br />
可逆性痴呆排查</td>
<td>Must rule out: thyroid disease (TSH), B12 deficiency, syphilis (VDRL/RPR), HIV, depression (pseudodementia), normal pressure hydrocephalus, subdural hematoma, and drug toxicity before diagnosing AD<br />
确诊AD前必须排除：甲状腺疾病（TSH）、B12缺乏、梅毒（VDRL/RPR）、HIV、抑郁（假性痴呆）、正常压力脑积水、硬膜下血肿及药物毒性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cholinergic hypothesis<br />
胆碱能假说</td>
<td>Nucleus basalis of Meynert (basal forebrain) → primary source of cortical ACh; its degeneration is a hallmark of AD; CHAT (choline acetyltransferase) activity is markedly reduced<br />
Meynert基底核（基底前脑）→皮质ACh的主要来源；其退变是AD的标志；CHAT（胆碱乙酰转移酶）活性显著降低</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Staging by MMSE<br />
按MMSE分期</td>
<td>Mild AD: MMSE 21–26; Moderate: 10–20 (this patient — disoriented to place/time); Severe: &lt;10 (incontinent, nonverbal, bedridden)<br />
轻度AD：MMSE 21–26；中度：10–20（该患者——对地点/时间失定向）；重度：&lt;10（尿失禁、丧失语言、卧床）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MRI findings in AD<br />
AD的MRI表现</td>
<td>Medial temporal lobe and hippocampal atrophy (earliest finding); widened cortical sulci; ex vacuo ventriculomegaly; spared primary motor/sensory cortex until late<br />
内侧颞叶和海马萎缩（最早表现）；皮质脑沟增宽；代偿性脑室扩大；初级运动/感觉皮质直至晚期才受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cholinesterase inhibitor side effects<br />
胆碱酯酶抑制剂副作用</td>
<td>Cholinergic excess: nausea, vomiting, diarrhea, bradycardia, syncope; take with food; donepezil can worsen peptic ulcer disease (increases gastric acid)<br />
胆碱能过量：恶心、呕吐、腹泻、心动过缓、晕厥；随餐服用；多奈哌齐可加重消化性溃疡（增加胃酸分泌）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Memantine mechanism<br />
美金刚机制</td>
<td>Uncompetitive antagonist of NMDA glutamate receptors; reduces excitotoxic calcium influx in moderate-to-severe AD; used alone or with donepezil<br />
NMDA谷氨酸受体非竞争性拮抗剂；减少中重度AD中兴奋毒性钙内流；可单用或与多奈哌齐联用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Amyloid cascade vs. tau<br />
淀粉样级联 vs. tau</td>
<td>Aβ plaques (extracellular) → trigger inflammation → tau hyperphosphorylation → neurofibrillary tangles (intracellular) → neuronal death; tau tangles correlate better with clinical severity<br />
Aβ斑块（细胞外）→触发炎症→tau蛋白过度磷酸化→神经纤维缠结（细胞内）→神经元死亡；tau缠结与临床严重程度相关性更好</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of progressive dementia:** Lewy body dementia (visual hallucinations, REM sleep behavior disorder, parkinsonism, fluctuating cognition — sensitive to antipsychotics), frontotemporal dementia (personality/behavioral changes first, language \> memory), vascular dementia (stepwise decline, focal neurological signs, cardiovascular risk factors)\
  **进行性痴呆的鉴别:** 路易体痴呆（视幻觉、REM睡眠行为障碍、帕金森症状、波动性认知——对抗精神病药敏感），额颞叶痴呆（人格/行为改变在先，语言\>记忆），血管性痴呆（阶梯样衰退、局灶神经系统体征、心血管危险因素）

- **Key complication — late-stage AD:** Loss of ability to perform ADLs, dysphagia (aspiration pneumonia = most common cause of death), pressure ulcers, contractures, and complete dependence; advance directives should be established early\
  **关键并发症——晚期AD:** 日常生活能力丧失，吞咽困难（吸入性肺炎=最常见死亡原因），压疮，挛缩，完全依赖照护；应早期建立预嘱

- **Risk factor — ApoE4:** ApoE ε4 allele is the strongest genetic risk factor for sporadic AD; homozygous ApoE4 increases lifetime risk ~12-fold; ApoE ε2 is protective; autosomal dominant early-onset AD involves APP, PSEN1, or PSEN2 mutations\
  **危险因素——ApoE4:** ApoE ε4等位基因是散发性AD最强的遗传危险因素；ApoE4纯合子终生风险增加约12倍；ApoE ε2具有保护作用；常染色体显性早发AD涉及APP、PSEN1或PSEN2突变

- **Variant — pseudodementia vs. true dementia:** Elderly patients with depression can present with cognitive complaints and poor concentration mimicking dementia; key distinguishing features: depressed patients complain more about memory loss (subjective), tend to say "I don't know" rather than confabulate, have preserved MMSE, and rapidly improve with antidepressant treatment\
  **题目变式——假性痴呆 vs. 真性痴呆:** 老年抑郁患者可出现认知主诉和注意力差，模拟痴呆；关键鉴别：抑郁患者更多主动抱怨记忆力（主观），倾向回答"我不知道"而非虚构，MMSE保留，抗抑郁治疗后迅速改善

# Question 136 — Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia with Acute Urinary Retention / 良性前列腺增生伴急性尿潴留

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 77-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>6-hour history of increasingly severe, nonradiating lower abdominal pain</strong>. He also has had <strong>urinary urgency</strong> during this time but <strong>has not been able to void for 8 hours</strong>. He has <strong>not had fever, chills</strong>, diarrhea, nausea, or vomiting. Vital signs are within normal limits. On examination, there is <strong>fullness in the midline from the umbilicus to the pubic symphysis</strong>; the area is tender to palpation, but <strong>there are no peritoneal signs</strong>. Rectal examination shows an <strong>enlarged prostate</strong>; sphincter tone is normal, and no masses are palpable. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bacterial prostatitis<br />
B) Benign prostatic hyperplasia<br />
C) Cecal volvulus<br />
D) Prostatic adenocarcinoma<br />
E) Sigmoid volvulus<br />
F) Urinary tract infection</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>77-year-old man<br />
77岁男性</td>
<td>BPH is a disease of elderly men; age &gt;50 is a major risk factor for development<br />
BPH是老年男性疾病，年龄&gt;50岁是发病的主要危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unable to void for 8 hours<br />
8小时无法排尿</td>
<td>Acute urinary retention — the hallmark complication of BPH-related bladder outlet obstruction<br />
急性尿潴留——BPH相关膀胱出口梗阻的标志性并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fullness in midline from umbilicus to pubic symphysis<br />
从脐部到耻骨联合中线饱满感</td>
<td>Distended bladder on exam — classic physical sign of acute urinary retention with large residual volume<br />
查体见膀胱膨胀——急性尿潴留伴大量残余尿的经典体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, chills<br />
无发热、寒战</td>
<td>Rules out bacterial prostatitis and UTI as primary diagnoses; systemic signs of infection are absent<br />
排除细菌性前列腺炎和尿路感染作为主要诊断；无全身感染征象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Enlarged prostate on rectal exam, no masses palpable<br />
直肠指检前列腺增大，未触及肿块</td>
<td>Smooth, enlarged prostate favors BPH; hard irregular nodules would suggest malignancy<br />
前列腺光滑增大倾向BPH；质硬不规则结节则提示恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No peritoneal signs<br />
无腹膜刺激征</td>
<td>Rules out bowel emergencies such as volvulus; confirms the midline fullness is bladder, not distended bowel<br />
排除肠道急症如肠扭转；确认中线区饱满感来自膀胱而非扩张的肠管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urinary urgency preceding retention<br />
尿潴留前出现尿急</td>
<td>Prior LUTS consistent with BPH causing partial obstruction that progressed to complete retention<br />
提示既往下尿路症状与BPH部分梗阻进展为完全性尿潴留相符</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Benign prostatic hyperplasia** results from **dihydrotestosterone (DHT)**-driven proliferation of stromal and epithelial cells in the **transition zone** of the prostate, progressively compressing the urethra:

**良性前列腺增生**源于**双氢睾酮(DHT)**驱动的前列腺**移行带**基质细胞和上皮细胞增殖，逐渐压迫尿道：

- The transition zone surrounds the proximal urethra, so enlargement directly narrows the lumen → **bladder outlet obstruction (BOO)**\
  移行带包绕近端尿道，故前列腺增大直接导致尿道腔狭窄→**膀胱出口梗阻(BOO)**

- The detrusor muscle compensates by hypertrophy (causing urgency and frequency), but eventually decompensates → **acute urinary retention**\
  逼尿肌通过肥厚代偿（引起尿急和尿频），但最终失代偿→**急性尿潴留**

- Bladder distension from retained urine causes suprapubic pain and the palpable midline fullness seen on exam\
  尿液潴留导致膀胱过度膨胀，引起耻骨上疼痛和查体可触及的中线区饱满感

- Unlike prostate cancer, BPH arises in the central transition zone — this location explains why it obstructs the urethra early\
  与前列腺癌不同，BPH起源于中央移行带——该解剖位置解释了为何它早期即可梗阻尿道

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** BPH (transition zone) compresses the urethra from within; prostate cancer (peripheral zone, 70%) does not impinge on the urethra until very late — that is why BPH causes urethral obstruction far more commonly than malignancy.

**解剖小窍门:** BPH（移行带）从内部压迫尿道；前列腺癌（外周带，70%）直到晚期才侵犯尿道——这就是为什么BPH比恶性肿瘤更常引起尿道梗阻。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia / 正确答案 (B) — 良性前列腺增生

**Benign prostatic hyperplasia (BPH)** is the most common cause of lower urinary tract symptoms (LUTS) and bladder outlet obstruction in elderly men, and this case is a textbook presentation:

**良性前列腺增生(BPH)** 是老年男性下尿路症状(LUTS)和膀胱出口梗阻最常见的原因，本病例是教科书式的典型表现：

- Classic LUTS: hesitancy, weak stream, urgency, frequency, nocturia, incomplete bladder emptying\
  经典下尿路症状：尿踌躇、尿流弱、尿急、尿频、夜尿增多、排尿不尽感

- Acute urinary retention: inability to void + suprapubic/lower abdominal pain + palpably distended bladder on exam\
  急性尿潴留：无法排尿+耻骨上/下腹疼痛+查体膀胱触诊膨胀

- DRE findings in BPH: enlarged, smooth, rubbery, non-tender prostate with symmetric enlargement — absence of hard nodules\
  BPH直肠指检：前列腺增大、光滑、橡皮样、无压痛、对称性增大——无质硬结节

**Diagnosis:** Clinical history + DRE + post-void residual (PVR) ultrasound; PSA obtained to screen for concurrent malignancy; urodynamic studies for complex or atypical cases

**诊断:** 病史+直肠指检+排尿后残余尿量超声；检测PSA筛查并存恶性肿瘤；复杂或不典型病例行尿动力学检查

**Treatment:** Immediate urethral catheterization to decompress the bladder in acute retention; long-term LUTS management: α-blockers (tamsulosin), 5α-reductase inhibitors (finasteride), or TURP for medically refractory cases

**治疗:** 急性尿潴留立即行尿道导尿减压膀胱；长期下尿路症状管理：α受体阻滞剂（坦索罗辛）、5α-还原酶抑制剂（非那雄胺），药物治疗无效者行经尿道前列腺电切术(TURP)

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bacterial prostatitis<br />
A — 细菌性前列腺炎</td>
<td>Can cause urinary retention, but requires fever, chills, malaise, dysuria — all absent here<br />
可引起尿潴留，但需有发热、寒战、乏力、排尿困难——本题均无</td>
<td>Systemic infection signs are mandatory; their absence definitively rules this out<br />
全身感染征象是必要条件；无此表现可明确排除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Benign prostatic hyperplasia ✓<br />
B — 良性前列腺增生 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — elderly man, 8-hour urinary retention, distended bladder, enlarged smooth prostate, no fever<br />
正确——老年男性、8小时尿潴留、膀胱膨胀、前列腺光滑增大、无发热</td>
<td>Classic acute urinary retention from BPH with all elements of the clinical triad present<br />
BPH导致急性尿潴留的经典表现，临床三联征齐全</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cecal volvulus<br />
C — 盲肠扭转</td>
<td>Causes large bowel obstruction with distension, obstipation, and colicky pain — does not cause urinary retention<br />
引起大肠梗阻伴腹胀、顽固性便秘和绞痛——不引起尿潴留</td>
<td>No bowel obstruction signs are present; the primary symptom is failure to void, not pass stool<br />
无肠梗阻征象；主要症状是无法排尿而非排便障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Prostatic adenocarcinoma<br />
D — 前列腺腺癌</td>
<td>Typically asymptomatic; may cause LUTS but rarely causes acute bladder outlet obstruction; DRE would show hard irregular nodule<br />
通常无症状；可引起下尿路症状但很少引起急性膀胱出口梗阻；直肠指检应触及质硬不规则结节</td>
<td>Smooth prostate on DRE argues against malignancy; acute obstruction is a BPH hallmark, not carcinoma<br />
直肠指检前列腺质地光滑不支持恶性肿瘤；急性梗阻是BPH特征而非癌症特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Sigmoid volvulus<br />
E — 乙状结肠扭转</td>
<td>Causes large bowel obstruction; "coffee-bean sign" on abdominal x-ray; no urinary symptoms<br />
引起大肠梗阻；腹部X线示"咖啡豆征"；无泌尿系症状</td>
<td>Bowel obstruction and urinary retention are distinct entities involving entirely different organ systems<br />
肠梗阻与尿潴留是累及完全不同器官系统的不同疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Urinary tract infection<br />
F — 尿路感染</td>
<td>UTI causes dysuria, frequency, urgency — but does NOT cause complete inability to void with bladder distension; may complicate BPH but is not the primary diagnosis here<br />
尿路感染引起排尿困难、尿频、尿急——但不引起完全性尿潴留伴膀胱膨胀；可并发BPH但非本题主要诊断</td>
<td>Complete retention with a palpably distended bladder indicates mechanical obstruction, not infection<br />
完全性尿潴留伴可触及的膀胱膨胀提示机械性梗阻，而非感染</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is Choice A (bacterial prostatitis) because it can cause urinary retention — the critical discriminator is the absence of fever, chills, and systemic infection signs, which are required to diagnose prostatitis.*

Choice A（细菌性前列腺炎）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因为它也可引起尿潴留——关键鉴别点在于本题无发热、寒战及全身感染表现，而这些是诊断前列腺炎的必要条件。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — BPH vs. Bacterial Prostatitis vs. Prostatic Adenocarcinoma / 良性前列腺增生 vs. 细菌性前列腺炎 vs. 前列腺腺癌

<table>
<colgroup>

<th><strong>BPH</strong><br />
<strong>良性前列腺增生</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bacterial Prostatitis</strong><br />
<strong>细菌性前列腺炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>Prostatic Adenocarcinoma</strong><br />
<strong>前列腺腺癌</strong></th>

<tr>
<td>Typical age<br />
典型年龄</td>

&gt;50岁，70岁高峰</td>

任何年龄，常见于年轻人</td>
<td>&gt;65, rare under 50<br />
&gt;65岁，50岁以下少见</td>
</tr>

发热/寒战</td>

无</td>

<td>Absent<br />

<tr>
<td>DRE findings<br />
直肠指检</td>
<td>Enlarged, smooth, rubbery, non-tender<br />
增大、光滑、橡皮样、无压痛</td>
<td>Boggy, exquisitely tender, warm<br />
柔软充血、极度压痛、局部热感</td>

质硬、不规则结节；不对称</td>

<tr>
<td>Acute urinary retention<br />
急性尿潴留</td>

常见——经典并发症</td>
<td>Possible but uncommon<br />
可能但不常见</td>
<td>Rare; only late-stage disease<br />
少见；仅见于晚期疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PSA level<br />
PSA水平</td>
<td>Mildly elevated (proportional to size)<br />
轻度升高（与腺体大小成比例）</td>
<td>Markedly elevated acutely<br />
急性期显著升高</td>
<td>Often markedly elevated; may be normal<br />
常显著升高；也可正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anatomic zone of origin<br />
起源解剖区带</td>
<td>Transition zone (periurethral)<br />
移行带（尿道周围）</td>
<td>Diffuse or any zone<br />
弥漫性或任何区带</td>
<td>Peripheral zone (70% of cases)<br />
外周带（占70%的病例）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Catheterization (acute); α-blockers, finasteride, TURP<br />
导尿（急性期）；α受体阻滞剂、非那雄胺、TURP</td>
<td>Fluoroquinolone antibiotics ×4–6 weeks<br />
氟喹诺酮类抗生素×4-6周</td>
<td>Surveillance, surgery, radiation, ADT<br />
主动监测、手术、放疗、雄激素剥夺治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An elderly man with acute inability to void, midline suprapubic fullness, and an enlarged smooth prostate on DRE has BPH causing acute urinary retention — treat immediately with urethral catheterization.**

**老年男性急性无法排尿、耻骨上中线区饱满感、直肠指检前列腺光滑增大，诊断为BPH导致的急性尿潴留——立即行尿道导尿治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BPH LUTS Mnemonic "FUNWI" / 记忆钩 — BPH下尿路症状助记词 "FUNWI":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>F</strong>requency — urinary frequency, voiding too often / 尿频，排尿次数过多<br />
• <strong>U</strong>rgency — sudden, compelling urge to void / 尿急，突然强烈的排尿冲动<br />
• <strong>N</strong>octuria — waking at night to urinate / 夜尿，夜间起床排尿<br />
• <strong>W</strong>eak stream — reduced force and caliber of urinary flow / 尿流弱，尿流力量和口径减小<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ncomplete emptying — post-void residual sensation / 排尿不尽感，排尿后仍有残余感</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Benign Prostatic Hyperplasia / 高频知识表 — 良性前列腺增生

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>5α-reductase converts testosterone → DHT; DHT drives transition zone hyperplasia → urethral compression → LUTS and urinary retention<br />
5α-还原酶将睾酮转化为DHT；DHT驱动移行带增生→尿道压迫→下尿路症状和尿潴留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physical exam in acute retention<br />
急性尿潴留体征</td>
<td>Inability to void + suprapubic pain + dull to percussion above pubic symphysis + palpably tense bladder extending toward umbilicus<br />
无法排尿+耻骨上疼痛+耻骨联合上方叩诊浊音+可触及向脐部延伸的紧张膀胱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Immediate management of acute retention<br />
急性尿潴留即刻处理</td>
<td>Urethral catheterization to decompress the bladder; prevents complications: bladder rupture, detrusor necrosis, hydroureter, hydronephrosis, postrenal AKI<br />
尿道导尿立即减压膀胱；预防并发症：膀胱破裂、逼尿肌坏死、输尿管积水、肾积水、肾后性急性肾损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>α-Blockers (tamsulosin)<br />
α受体阻滞剂（坦索罗辛）</td>
<td>Relax smooth muscle of prostate and bladder neck → improve urinary flow; rapid onset within days; first-line agent for LUTS<br />
松弛前列腺和膀胱颈平滑肌→改善尿流；数天内快速起效；下尿路症状的一线用药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5α-Reductase inhibitors (finasteride)<br />
5α-还原酶抑制剂（非那雄胺）</td>
<td>Block DHT synthesis → shrink prostate volume over months; preferred for large glands (&gt;40 g); reduce PSA by ~50% (important for PSA interpretation)<br />
阻断DHT合成→数月内缩小前列腺体积；适用于较大前列腺（&gt;40g）；使PSA降低约50%（对PSA解读至关重要）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical option: TURP<br />
手术选项：经尿道前列腺电切术</td>
<td>Gold standard for medically refractory BPH; removes obstructing tissue transurethrally; most common complication: retrograde ejaculation<br />
药物难治性BPH的金标准；经尿道切除梗阻性前列腺组织；最常见并发症：逆行射精</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-obstructive diuresis<br />
梗阻后利尿</td>
<td>After catheter placement for prolonged retention, expect brisk diuresis (&gt;200 mL/hr); replace urine output carefully to prevent dehydration and electrolyte disorders<br />
长期尿潴留置管后可出现大量利尿（&gt;200 mL/hr）；需仔细补充尿量，防止脱水和电解质紊乱</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Drugs that precipitate acute urinary retention in BPH:** Anticholinergics, alpha-agonists (decongestants like pseudoephedrine), TCAs, antihistamines, and opioids can all precipitate acute retention in men with underlying BPH by increasing bladder outlet resistance or reducing detrusor contractility\
  **可诱发BPH患者急性尿潴留的药物:** 抗胆碱能药、α受体激动剂（如伪麻黄碱等鼻减充血剂）、三环类抗抑郁药、抗组胺药和阿片类药物均可通过增加膀胱出口阻力或降低逼尿肌收缩力诱发急性尿潴留

- **PSA interpretation caveat with finasteride:** 5α-reductase inhibitors halve PSA levels within 6 months; a PSA that fails to decrease by ~50% after adequate treatment raises suspicion for concurrent prostate malignancy and warrants biopsy\
  **非那雄胺治疗中PSA解读注意事项:** 5α-还原酶抑制剂在6个月内使PSA减半；充分治疗后PSA未能下降约50%应高度怀疑并存前列腺恶性肿瘤，需行活检

- **BPH vs. prostate cancer on DRE — key distinction:** BPH → smooth, rubbery, symmetric enlargement; prostate cancer → hard, irregular, asymmetric nodule in the peripheral zone; both can coexist — biopsy is needed to exclude malignancy when PSA is disproportionately elevated\
  **BPH与前列腺癌直肠指检鉴别要点:** BPH→光滑、橡皮样、对称性增大；前列腺癌→外周带质硬、不规则、不对称结节；两者可共存——当PSA异常升高时需行活检排除恶性肿瘤

- **Relative contraindication of DRE in bacterial prostatitis:** Digital rectal examination is relatively contraindicated in acute bacterial prostatitis due to the theoretical risk of bacteremia from compressing an acutely infected, vascular gland — contrasting with BPH and adenocarcinoma where DRE is essential for diagnosis\
  **细菌性前列腺炎中直肠指检的相对禁忌:** 急性细菌性前列腺炎中直肠指检相对禁忌，因按压急性感染且血管丰富的腺体存在菌血症的理论风险——与BPH和腺癌中直肠指检对诊断至关重要形成对比

# Question 137 — Ewing Sarcoma / 尤文肉瘤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>6-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the emergency department by his parents because of a <strong>2-hour history of severe right leg pain</strong> and <strong>refusal to walk</strong>. They say he has <strong>intermittently reported pain in his leg during the past 2 weeks</strong>. He has no history of trauma or serious illness and receives no medications. Growth and development are appropriate for age. His <strong>temperature is 38.1°C (100.5°F)</strong>, pulse is 100/min, and blood pressure is 100/80 mm Hg. There is <strong>warmth and tenderness to palpation of the proximal aspect of the right tibia</strong> with an associated <strong>firm mass</strong>. Distal pulses are intact. Range of motion of the right knee is limited by pain. Muscle strength in the right lower extremity is 4/5 because of pain and 5/5 elsewhere. Sensation is intact. Laboratory studies show a hemoglobin concentration of 10 g/dL, leukocyte count of 20,000/mm3, and <strong>erythrocyte sedimentation rate of 10 mm/h</strong>. X-rays show a <strong>6-cm, poorly defined lytic lesion in the proximal tibial metadiaphysis</strong> with <strong>adjacent periosteal reaction</strong>. The results of a biopsy are shown. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acute lymphoblastic leukemia<br />
B) Eosinophilic granuloma<br />
C) Ewing sarcoma<br />
D) Osteoid osteoma<br />
E) Osteomyelitis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>6-year-old boy, 2 weeks of intermittent bone pain<br />
6岁男孩，2周间歇性骨痛</td>
<td>Ewing sarcoma peaks at age 5–25; insidious weeks-long onset distinguishes it from acute osteomyelitis<br />
尤文肉瘤好发5–25岁；隐匿性数周起病与急性骨髓炎不同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Firm mass + warmth at proximal tibia<br />
胫骨近端坚实肿块+皮温升高</td>
<td>Solid bone tumor with periosteal extension; warmth can falsely suggest infection<br />
实性骨肿瘤伴骨膜扩展；皮温升高可误导感染诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever (38.1°C) + leukocytosis (WBC 20,000/mm3)<br />
发热（38.1°C）+白细胞增多（20,000/mm3）</td>
<td>Ewing triggers systemic cytokine release, creating an infection-like picture<br />
尤文肉瘤引发全身细胞因子释放，临床表现类似感染</td>

<tr>

尽管发热/白细胞增多，正常ESR强烈反对骨髓炎（ESR通常&gt;50 mm/h）；支持恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>6-cm poorly defined lytic lesion in the metadiaphysis<br />
干骺端6cm边界不清溶骨性病变</td>
<td>Large, aggressive lytic lesion in the metadiaphysis is classic for Ewing sarcoma<br />
干骺端大型侵袭性溶骨性病变是尤文肉瘤的典型表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Adjacent periosteal reaction on X-ray<br />
X线邻近骨膜反应</td>
<td>"Onion-skin" layered periosteal reaction is the hallmark imaging finding of Ewing sarcoma<br />
"洋葱皮样"层状骨膜反应是尤文肉瘤的标志性影像表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biopsy shown (small round blue cells implied)<br />
活检结果显示（提示小圆蓝细胞）</td>
<td>Ewing sarcoma histology: sheets of undifferentiated small round blue cells, CD99+ on immunostaining<br />
尤文肉瘤组织学：成片未分化小圆蓝细胞，免疫染色CD99阳性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Ewing sarcoma** arises from **mesenchymal precursor cells** of bone and soft tissue, driven by a pathognomonic **t(11;22)(q24;q12) chromosomal translocation** that fuses the *EWS* gene to the *FLI1* transcription factor gene:

**尤文肉瘤**起源于骨和软组织的**间质前体细胞**，由特征性的**t(11;22)(q24;q12)染色体易位**驱动，将*EWS*基因与*FLI1*转录因子基因融合：

- The EWS-FLI1 fusion protein acts as an aberrant transcription factor, dysregulating genes controlling cell proliferation and apoptosis\
  EWS-FLI1融合蛋白作为异常转录因子，失调控制细胞增殖和凋亡的基因

- Rapid tumor growth stimulates periosteal reactive bone formation in concentric layers → classic "onion-skin" periosteal reaction on X-ray\
  肿瘤快速生长刺激骨膜产生同心层状反应性新骨→X线经典"洋葱皮样"骨膜反应

- Tumor necrosis and cytokine release cause fever, leukocytosis, and anemia, mimicking bacterial osteomyelitis\
  肿瘤坏死和细胞因子释放引起发热、白细胞增多和贫血，模拟细菌性骨髓炎

- ESR remains normal-to-low despite systemic inflammation because the acute-phase fibrinogen response is far less pronounced than in bacterial infection — this discordance is the pivotal diagnostic clue\
  尽管存在全身炎症，ESR仍正常至低水平，因为急性期纤维蛋白原反应远不如细菌感染显著——这种不一致是关键诊断线索

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Ewing favors the diaphysis/metadiaphysis of long bones (femur \#1, tibia \#2) and flat bones of the axial skeleton (pelvis, ribs, scapula); osteosarcoma favors the metaphysis immediately adjacent to the growth plate.

**解剖小窍门:** 尤文好发于长骨骨干/干骺端（股骨第一、胫骨第二）和中轴骨扁平骨（骨盆、肋骨、肩胛骨）；骨肉瘤好发于紧邻生长板的骨骺端。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Ewing Sarcoma / 正确答案 (C) — 尤文肉瘤

**Ewing sarcoma** is a high-grade primary bone malignancy of mesenchymal origin and the second most common primary bone tumor in children after osteosarcoma:

**尤文肉瘤**是间质来源的高级别原发性骨恶性肿瘤，是继骨肉瘤之后儿童中第二常见的原发性骨肿瘤：

- Age peak 5–25 years; male \> female; more common in White populations; very rare in Asian and Black populations\
  发病高峰5–25岁；男\>女；白人群体更常见；亚裔和黑人群体极少见

- Classic presentation: weeks-to-months of waxing-and-waning bone pain ± palpable soft tissue mass; constitutional symptoms (fever, weight loss) in ~30% of patients\
  典型表现：数周至数月起伏性骨痛±可触及软组织肿块；约30%患者有全身症状（发热、体重减轻）

- Biopsy hallmark: sheets of small, round, blue cells with scant cytoplasm and indistinct nucleoli; CD99 (MIC2) strongly positive on immunostaining\
  活检标志：成片小圆蓝细胞，胞质稀少，核仁不清；CD99（MIC2）免疫染色强阳性

- Confirmatory molecular finding: t(11;22) → EWS-FLI1 fusion detected in ~85% of cases by FISH or RT-PCR\
  确诊分子标志：约85%病例通过FISH或RT-PCR检测到t(11;22)→EWS-FLI1融合

**Diagnosis:** Clinical presentation + imaging (metadiaphyseal lytic lesion + onion-skin periosteal reaction) + biopsy (small round blue cells, CD99+) + cytogenetics/FISH confirming t(11;22)

**诊断:** 临床表现+影像学（干骺端溶骨性病变+洋葱皮样骨膜反应）+活检（小圆蓝细胞，CD99+）+细胞遗传学/FISH确认t(11;22)

**Treatment:** Multimodal — neoadjuvant chemotherapy (VDC/IE regimen: vincristine + doxorubicin + cyclophosphamide alternating with ifosfamide + etoposide), followed by local control (wide surgical resection ± radiation therapy), then adjuvant chemotherapy

**治疗:** 多模态——新辅助化疗（VDC/IE方案：长春新碱+多柔比星+环磷酰胺与异环磷酰胺+依托泊苷交替），之后局部控制（广泛手术切除±放疗），再行辅助化疗

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acute lymphoblastic leukemia<br />
A — 急性淋巴细胞白血病</td>
<td>Bone pain and leukocytosis can occur in ALL, but a discrete 6-cm lytic bone mass with periosteal reaction is atypical; expect lymphadenopathy, hepatosplenomegaly, circulating blast cells on peripheral smear<br />
ALL可有骨痛和白细胞增多，但6cm局灶溶骨肿块伴骨膜反应不典型；应有淋巴结肿大、肝脾肿大、外周血涂片幼稚细胞</td>
<td>ALL rarely forms a discrete bone mass with periosteal reaction; CBC in ALL would show circulating blasts, not isolated leukocytosis<br />
ALL极少形成局灶性骨肿块伴骨膜反应；ALL的CBC应显示循环幼稚细胞，而非单纯白细胞增多</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Eosinophilic granuloma<br />
B — 嗜酸性肉芽肿</td>
<td>Langerhans cell histiocytosis confined to bone; lytic lesions classically favor skull ("punched-out" lesion) and vertebrae ("vertebra plana"); rarely presents with a large soft-tissue mass or constitutional fever<br />
局限于骨的朗格汉斯细胞组织细胞增生症；溶骨病变经典好发颅骨（穿凿样病变）和椎体（扁平椎）；极少出现大软组织肿块或全身发热</td>
<td>Skull/vertebral location vs. long bone metadiaphysis; no onion-skin periosteal reaction; no firm palpable mass<br />
颅骨/椎体vs.长骨干骺端；无洋葱皮样骨膜反应；无可触及坚实肿块</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Ewing sarcoma ✓<br />
C — 尤文肉瘤 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Age 6, weeks of insidious bone pain, fever + leukocytosis with a strikingly low ESR, metadiaphyseal lytic lesion with onion-skin periosteal reaction, firm mass, and biopsy showing small round blue cells all converge on Ewing sarcoma<br />
正确——6岁、数周隐匿骨痛、发热+白细胞增多而ESR出人意料低、干骺端溶骨病变伴洋葱皮骨膜反应、坚实肿块、活检小圆蓝细胞，所有特征均指向尤文肉瘤</td>
<td>The discordantly low ESR (10 mm/h) despite systemic inflammation is the pivotal clue against osteomyelitis and toward malignancy<br />
全身炎症背景下ESR异常低（10 mm/h）是反对骨髓炎、支持恶性肿瘤的关键线索</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Osteoid osteoma<br />
D — 骨样骨瘤</td>
<td>Benign tumor; nidus is &lt;2 cm with surrounding osteosclerosis (not a 6-cm lytic mass); hallmark is night pain dramatically relieved by aspirin/NSAIDs; no fever, no firm mass, no constitutional symptoms<br />
良性肿瘤；病灶&lt;2cm伴周围骨硬化（非6cm溶骨肿块）；标志性表现为阿司匹林/NSAIDs显著缓解的夜间疼痛；无发热、无坚实肿块、无全身症状</td>
<td>Size (&lt;2 cm nidus vs. 6-cm lesion), osteosclerotic vs. lytic, and aspirin-responsive night pain vs. progressive pain with a mass<br />
大小（&lt;2cm病灶vs.6cm病变）、骨硬化性vs.溶骨性、阿司匹林反应夜间痛vs.进行性疼痛伴肿块</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Osteomyelitis<br />
E — 骨髓炎</td>
<td>Fever, bone pain, and leukocytosis overlap with Ewing, making this the classic distractor — but ESR in osteomyelitis is typically markedly elevated (&gt;50 mm/h, often &gt;100); no discrete firm mass; X-ray rarely shows a 6-cm lytic lesion with layered periosteal reaction<br />
发热、骨痛和白细胞增多与尤文重叠，使此为经典干扰项——但骨髓炎ESR通常明显升高（&gt;50 mm/h，常&gt;100）；无局灶坚实肿块；X线极少显示6cm溶骨性病变伴层状骨膜反应</td>
<td>ESR of 10 mm/h is the single most discriminating clue — incompatible with bacterial osteomyelitis; firm mass and large lytic lesion favor malignancy<br />
ESR 10 mm/h是最具鉴别力的单一线索——与细菌性骨髓炎不符；坚实肿块和大型溶骨性病变支持恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Osteomyelitis is the classic trap here because it shares fever, leukocytosis, and bone pain — but the strikingly low ESR (10 mm/h), the large firm mass on exam, and the aggressive periosteal reaction on X-ray collectively make osteomyelitis untenable and confirm malignancy.*

骨髓炎是此题的经典陷阱，因其共享发热、白细胞增多和骨痛——但出人意料的低ESR（10 mm/h）、查体坚实大肿块以及X线侵袭性骨膜反应共同使骨髓炎站不住脚，确认恶性肿瘤诊断。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Ewing Sarcoma vs. Osteosarcoma vs. Osteomyelitis / 尤文肉瘤 vs. 骨肉瘤 vs. 骨髓炎

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Ewing sarcoma presents in children and adolescents with weeks of insidious bone pain, a firm mass, fever and leukocytosis but a strikingly low ESR, a metadiaphyseal lytic lesion with onion-skin periosteal reaction on X-ray, and small round blue cells on biopsy, driven by the t(11;22) EWS-FLI1 translocation.**

**尤文肉瘤表现为儿童/青少年数周隐匿性骨痛、坚实肿块、发热和白细胞增多但ESR出人意料地低，X线示干骺端溶骨性病变伴洋葱皮样骨膜反应，活检见小圆蓝细胞，由t(11;22) EWS-FLI1易位驱动。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "EWING" Sarcoma Features / 记忆钩 — "EWING"尤文肉瘤特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>E</strong>xtremity long bones (femur, tibia) &amp; axial flat bones (pelvis, ribs) — classic locations / 四肢长骨（股骨、胫骨）及中轴扁平骨（骨盆、肋骨）——典型部位<br />
• <strong>W</strong>hite-to-blue small round cells on biopsy (CD99+) — histologic hallmark / 活检见小圆蓝细胞（CD99+）——组织学标志<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nsidious onset over weeks, mimicking infection — but ESR is discordantly low / 数周隐匿起病，模拟感染——但ESR不相称地低<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eocortex onion-skin layered periosteal reaction on X-ray — hallmark imaging finding / X线洋葱皮样层状骨膜反应——标志性影像表现<br />
• <strong>G</strong>ene translocation t(11;22) → EWS-FLI1 — confirmatory molecular finding / t(11;22)→EWS-FLI1基因易位——确诊分子标志</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Ewing Sarcoma & Pediatric Bone Tumors / 高频知识表 — 尤文肉瘤及儿童骨肿瘤

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>t(11;22) translocation<br />
t(11;22)易位</td>
<td>Present in ~85% of Ewing sarcoma; creates EWS-FLI1 oncogenic fusion protein; detected by FISH or RT-PCR on biopsy specimen; variant t(21;22) creates EWS-ERG fusion in ~10%<br />
约85%尤文肉瘤存在；产生EWS-FLI1致癌融合蛋白；通过FISH或RT-PCR在活检标本中检测；变异型t(21;22)产生EWS-ERG融合见于约10%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Small round blue cell tumors (SRBCT)<br />
小圆蓝细胞肿瘤（SRBCT）</td>
<td>Five SRBCTs in children: Ewing (CD99+, EWS-FLI1), neuroblastoma (NSE+, Homer-Wright rosettes), rhabdomyosarcoma (desmin+, myogenin+), ALL (TdT+, CD10+), Wilms tumor (WT1+); immunostaining panel is essential for discrimination<br />
儿童5种SRBCT：尤文（CD99+、EWS-FLI1）、神经母细胞瘤（NSE+、Homer-Wright菊形团）、横纹肌肉瘤（desmin+、肌原蛋白+）、ALL（TdT+、CD10+）、Wilms瘤（WT1+）；免疫染色组合是鉴别关键</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Periosteal reaction patterns<br />
骨膜反应类型</td>
<td>Onion-skin (concentric layers) = Ewing sarcoma; Sunburst pattern = osteosarcoma; Codman triangle (lifted periosteum at tumor margin) = seen in both aggressive tumors; all represent rapid periosteal elevation by tumor<br />
洋葱皮样（同心层状）=尤文肉瘤；日光放射状=骨肉瘤；Codman三角（肿瘤边缘骨膜抬高）=两种侵袭性肿瘤均可见；均代表肿瘤对骨膜的快速抬高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ESR as discriminator<br />
ESR作为鉴别指标</td>
<td>Ewing and osteosarcoma: ESR normal to mildly elevated despite systemic signs; bacterial osteomyelitis and septic arthritis: ESR typically &gt;50 mm/h, often &gt;100 mm/h — this is tested repeatedly on USMLE<br />
尤文和骨肉瘤：尽管有全身症状，ESR正常至轻度升高；细菌性骨髓炎和化脓性关节炎：ESR通常&gt;50 mm/h，常&gt;100 mm/h——此点在USMLE中反复考查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prognostic factors in Ewing<br />
尤文预后因素</td>
<td>Poor prognosis: older age at diagnosis, axial/pelvic location, tumor &gt;8 cm, metastases at presentation (most common: lung and bone marrow); 5-year survival ~70% for localized disease vs. ~30% with distant metastases<br />
预后差：诊断年龄较大、中轴/骨盆部位、肿瘤&gt;8cm、就诊时已转移（最常见：肺和骨髓）；局限性疾病5年生存率约70%，远处转移约30%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Metastatic workup<br />
转移评估</td>
<td>Chest CT (pulmonary mets most common site), whole-body PET or bone scan (skeletal mets), bilateral bone marrow biopsy (marrow involvement); staging determines treatment intensity<br />
胸部CT（肺转移最常见）、全身PET或骨扫描（骨骼转移）、双侧骨髓活检（骨髓受累）；分期决定治疗强度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Osteoid osteoma vs. Ewing<br />
骨样骨瘤vs.尤文</td>
<td>Osteoid osteoma: benign, &lt;2 cm radiolucent nidus with surrounding dense sclerosis, night pain dramatically relieved by aspirin, no systemic symptoms, diagnosed by CT; Ewing: malignant, &gt;2 cm lytic with periosteal reaction, progressive pain, systemic signs, biopsy required<br />
骨样骨瘤：良性，&lt;2cm透亮病灶伴致密硬化，阿司匹林显著缓解夜间痛，无全身症状，CT确诊；尤文：恶性，&gt;2cm溶骨伴骨膜反应，进行性疼痛，全身症状，需活检</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of SRBCT on biopsy:** Neuroblastoma (NSE+, chromogranin+, Homer-Wright rosettes, NMB gene amplification), rhabdomyosarcoma (desmin+, myogenin+, skeletal muscle differentiation), Ewing (CD99+, EWS-FLI1), ALL (TdT+, CD10+, lymphoid markers) — immunostaining plus molecular testing is required to distinguish these overlapping histologies\
  **活检SRBCT鉴别:** 神经母细胞瘤（NSE+、嗜铬粒蛋白+、Homer-Wright菊形团、MYCN扩增）、横纹肌肉瘤（desmin+、肌原蛋白+、骨骼肌分化）、尤文（CD99+、EWS-FLI1）、ALL（TdT+、CD10+、淋巴系标志）——需免疫染色加分子检测区分这些重叠组织学

- **Variant — extraosseous Ewing sarcoma:** ~15% of Ewing sarcoma arises in soft tissue without primary bone involvement; same t(11;22) translocation; commonly presents as a paravertebral or chest wall soft tissue mass in older adolescents\
  **变式——骨外尤文肉瘤:** 约15%尤文肉瘤起源于软组织而无原发骨受累；同样的t(11;22)易位；常表现为年长青少年椎旁或胸壁软组织肿块

- **Key complication — pathologic fracture:** Aggressive lytic cortical destruction can precipitate fracture through the tumor site; vertebral Ewing may cause sudden spinal cord compression — a surgical emergency\
  **主要并发症——病理性骨折:** 侵袭性溶骨皮质破坏可在肿瘤部位引发骨折；椎体尤文可引起急性脊髓压迫——外科急症

- **Epidemiologic pearl — racial disparity:** Ewing sarcoma is exceedingly rare in Asian and Black populations (incidence ~10-fold lower than in Whites); if a Black or Asian child presents with similar findings, osteosarcoma or osteomyelitis should rank higher before Ewing\
  **流行病学要点——种族差异:** 尤文肉瘤在亚裔和黑人群体中极为罕见（发病率约为白人的1/10）；若黑人或亚裔儿童出现类似表现，骨肉瘤或骨髓炎应在尤文之前排位更高

# Question 138 — South American Trypanosomiasis (Chagas Disease) / 南美锥虫病（恰加斯病）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>39-year-old man</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>1-month history</strong> of intermittent regurgitation and constipation. He has regurgitated <strong>undigested food</strong> four times weekly. He previously had daily bowel movements; during the past month, he has had a bowel movement <strong>every 3 to 4 days</strong>. He also has a <strong>1-year history of progressive difficulty swallowing</strong>. He says initially he had difficulty swallowing solids. He now also has <strong>difficulty swallowing liquids</strong>. When he eats, he occasionally has <strong>moderate pain in the lower sternal area</strong> that radiates upward. He <strong>emigrated from Brazil</strong> 5 years ago. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows no abnormalities. A chest x-ray shows a <strong>dilated esophagus with an air-fluid level</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Barrett esophagus<br />
B) Nutcracker esophagus<br />
C) Schatzki ring<br />
D) South American trypanosomiasis<br />
E) Systemic sclerosis (scleroderma)</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Progressive dysphagia: solids → liquids<br />
进行性吞咽困难：先固体，后液体</td>
<td>Complete loss of peristalsis, not a structural ring; Schatzki ring causes intermittent solid-only dysphagia<br />
提示蠕动完全丧失，而非结构性环；Schatzki环仅引起间歇性固体吞咽困难</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Emigrated from Brazil 5 years ago<br />
5年前从巴西移民</td>
<td>South America is endemic for T. cruzi; this single geographic clue is the strongest discriminator on this question<br />
南美洲是克氏锥虫流行区；这一地理线索是本题最强的鉴别依据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dilated esophagus with air-fluid level on CXR<br />
胸片示食管扩张伴气液平面</td>
<td>Megaesophagus — hallmark of Chagas disease; rules out Barrett, Schatzki ring, and scleroderma (which causes stricture not dilation)<br />
食管巨大症——Chagas病标志；可排除Barrett食管、Schatzki环和硬皮病（后者致狭窄而非扩张）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Regurgitation of undigested food<br />
反流未消化食物</td>
<td>Food retained proximal to a non-relaxing LES; distinguishes megaesophagus from GERD (which regurgitates digested/acidic content)<br />
食物滞留于不能舒张的LES近端；有别于GERD（后者反流已消化/酸性内容物）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Constipation (every 3–4 days)<br />
便秘（每3–4天一次）</td>
<td>Suggests megacolon — another GI manifestation of Chagas due to myenteric plexus destruction in the colon<br />
提示巨结肠——结肠肌间神经丛破坏所致的另一Chagas病消化道表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1-year progressive course with no exam abnormalities<br />
1年进行性病程且体检无异常</td>
<td>Slow neurodegeneration without structural lesion; scleroderma would show skin changes; no evidence of systemic disease<br />
缓慢神经退变而无结构性病变；硬皮病应有皮肤改变；无全身病变证据</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Trypanosoma cruzi** triggers immune-mediated destruction of the **myenteric (Auerbach's) plexus** neurons throughout the gastrointestinal tract:

**克氏锥虫（\*Trypanosoma cruzi\*）**通过免疫介导机制破坏胃肠道各段的**肌间（Auerbach）神经丛**神经元：

- Loss of inhibitory ganglionic neurons → failure of **lower esophageal sphincter (LES)** relaxation → functional obstruction identical to achalasia\
  抑制性神经节细胞丧失 → **食管下括约肌（LES）**舒张障碍 → 功能性梗阻，表现与贲门失弛缓症相同

- Food and secretion stasis → progressive **esophageal dilation** (megaesophagus) → air-fluid level visible on CXR\
  食物和分泌物潴留 → 进行性**食管扩张**（食管巨大症）→ 胸片可见气液平面

- Same neuronal destruction in colon → **megacolon** → severe constipation\
  结肠发生相同的神经元破坏 → **巨结肠** → 严重便秘

- Cardiac myenteric and conduction system involvement → **dilated cardiomyopathy**, arrhythmia, and apical aneurysm\
  心脏肌间神经丛及传导系统受累 → **扩张型心肌病**、心律失常和心尖部室壁瘤

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Chagas preferentially destroys inhibitory neurons of the Auerbach plexus, producing "mega" phenomena everywhere — megaesophagus, megacolon, and cardiomegaly.

**解剖小窍门:** Chagas病优先破坏Auerbach神经丛抑制性神经元，在全身产生"巨大"现象——食管巨大症、巨结肠和心脏扩大。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — South American Trypanosomiasis (Chagas Disease) / 正确答案 (D) — 南美锥虫病（恰加斯病）

**South American trypanosomiasis (Chagas disease)** is caused by the flagellate protozoan *Trypanosoma cruzi*, transmitted via the bite of Reduviidae (triatomine/"kissing") bugs endemic to Latin America:

**南美锥虫病（恰加斯病）**由鞭毛原虫*克氏锥虫（Trypanosoma cruzi）*引起，经拉丁美洲特有的锥蝽（猎蝽科/"接吻虫"）叮咬传播：

- Acute phase: mild fever, malaise, lymphadenopathy, Romaña sign (unilateral painless periorbital edema at bite site); resolves spontaneously in 1–2 months\
  急性期：轻度发热、乏力、淋巴结肿大、Romaña征（叮咬部位单侧无痛性眼眶周围水肿）；1–2个月内自行消退

- Chronic phase (years later): cardiac triad (dilated cardiomyopathy + arrhythmia + CHF) + GI triad (megaesophagus + megacolon + weight loss); NOT curable once established\
  慢性期（多年后）：心脏三联征（扩张型心肌病 + 心律失常 + 充血性心力衰竭）+ 消化道三联征（食管巨大症 + 巨结肠 + 体重下降）；进入慢性期后不可治愈

- Key imaging: CXR shows dilated esophagus with air-fluid level; echocardiogram shows cardiomegaly ± apical aneurysm\
  关键影像学：胸片显示食管扩张伴气液平面；超声心动图显示心脏扩大±心尖部室壁瘤

- Bugs are nocturnal, infest rural housing with thatched roofs or cracked walls; feed on sleeping human hosts\
  锥蝽为夜行性昆虫，栖息于茅草屋顶或墙缝农村房屋；在人类睡眠时叮咬吸血

**Diagnosis:** Acute phase — peripheral blood smear (extracellular trypomastigotes); Chronic phase — ELISA serology or PCR; CXR and ECG for organ involvement

**诊断:** 急性期——外周血涂片（胞外锥鞭毛体）；慢性期——ELISA血清学或PCR；胸片和心电图评估器官受累

**Treatment:** Nifurtimox or benznidazole (prolonged courses, curative if given in acute phase); chronic phase is managed supportively — cardiac (ICD, transplant) and GI (esophageal dilation, laxatives) complications

**治疗:** 硝呋替莫或苄硝唑（疗程较长，急性期给药可治愈）；慢性期支持治疗——心脏（ICD、移植）和消化道（食管扩张术、泻药）并发症管理

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Barrett esophagus<br />
A — Barrett食管</td>
<td>Intestinal metaplasia of distal esophagus from chronic GERD; presents with heartburn, not progressive dysphagia; esophageal dilation does not occur<br />
慢性GERD所致食管远端肠化生；表现为烧心而非进行性吞咽困难；不会出现食管扩张</td>
<td>No dilation on CXR; no long-standing heartburn history in stem<br />
胸片无扩张；题干无长期烧心病史</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Nutcracker esophagus<br />
B — 胡桃夹食管</td>
<td>Hypertensive peristalsis causing dysphagia and chest pain; does NOT produce esophageal dilation; manometry shows high-amplitude contractions<br />
高压蠕动引起吞咽困难和胸痛；不产生食管扩张；测压显示高幅收缩</td>
<td>No dilation; no geographic clue; chest pain alone insufficient<br />
无扩张；无地理线索；单纯胸痛不足以诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Schatzki ring<br />
C — Schatzki环</td>
<td>Mucosal ring at gastroesophageal junction; dysphagia is intermittent and limited to solids (steak-house syndrome); esophageal dilation does not occur<br />
胃食管交界处黏膜环；吞咽困难间歇性且仅限固体（牛排馆综合征）；不出现食管扩张</td>
<td>This patient has progressive dysphagia including liquids; CXR shows dilation<br />
本患者吞咽困难呈进行性且累及液体；胸片显示扩张</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — South American trypanosomiasis ✓<br />
D — 南美锥虫病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — T. cruzi destroys the myenteric plexus → megaesophagus + megacolon; Brazilian origin + dilation on CXR + progressive dysphagia + constipation = classic chronic Chagas<br />
正确——克氏锥虫破坏肌间神经丛 → 食管巨大症 + 巨结肠；巴西来源 + 胸片扩张 + 进行性吞咽困难 + 便秘 = 典型慢性Chagas病</td>
<td>All four pillars present: Latin America + megaesophagus + megacolon + progressive dysphagia (solids then liquids)<br />
四大支柱齐备：拉丁美洲 + 食管巨大症 + 巨结肠 + 进行性吞咽困难（先固体后液体）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Systemic sclerosis (scleroderma)<br />
E — 系统性硬化症（硬皮病）</td>
<td>Esophageal fibrosis causes hypomotility and stricture, NOT dilation; would expect taut skin, Raynaud's phenomenon, telangiectasias — all absent here<br />
食管纤维化导致低动力和狭窄，而非扩张；预期有皮肤绷紧、雷诺现象、毛细血管扩张——本例均无</td>
<td>"No abnormalities" on exam eliminates scleroderma; esophagus narrows in scleroderma, not dilates<br />
体检"无异常"排除硬皮病；硬皮病食管表现为狭窄而非扩张</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is scleroderma (E), which also causes esophageal dysmotility and progressive dysphagia; the decisive discriminators are the CXR showing dilation (scleroderma causes narrowing) and the complete absence of skin findings on exam.*

硬皮病（E）是最易混淆的干扰项，同样可致食管动力障碍和进行性吞咽困难；决定性鉴别要点是胸片显示食管扩张（硬皮病为狭窄）以及体检完全无皮肤改变。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A Brazilian immigrant with progressive dysphagia (solids then liquids), megaesophagus on CXR, regurgitation of undigested food, and constipation has chronic Chagas disease from T. cruzi infection destroying the myenteric plexus.**

**一名巴西移民出现进行性吞咽困难（先固体后液体）、胸片示食管巨大症、反流未消化食物及便秘，诊断为慢性Chagas病——由克氏锥虫感染破坏肌间神经丛所致。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — MEGA: Chronic Chagas Complications / 记忆钩 — MEGA：慢性Chagas病并发症:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>M</strong>egaesophagus — progressive dysphagia (solids → liquids), regurgitation of undigested food, air-fluid level on CXR / 食管巨大症——进行性吞咽困难（固体→液体）、反流未消化食物、胸片气液平面<br />
• <strong>E</strong>nlarged heart (dilated cardiomyopathy) — right bundle branch block, apical aneurysm, arrhythmia, sudden death / 心脏扩大（扩张型心肌病）——右束支传导阻滞、心尖部室壁瘤、心律失常、猝死<br />
• <strong>G</strong>ut (megacolon) — severe constipation, potential bowel obstruction / 巨肠（巨结肠）——严重便秘，可致肠梗阻<br />
• <strong>A</strong>uerbach plexus destroyed by T. cruzi in South <strong>A</strong>merica / 南美洲克氏锥虫破坏Auerbach神经丛</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Chagas Disease (South American Trypanosomiasis) / 高频知识表 — 恰加斯病（南美锥虫病）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Causative agent &amp; transmission<br />
病原体及传播方式</td>
<td>Trypanosoma cruzi (flagellate protozoan); transmitted by nocturnal Reduviidae (triatomine/"kissing") bugs that infest thatched-roof rural housing; also via blood transfusion, organ transplant, vertical (mother-to-child)<br />
克氏锥虫（鞭毛原虫）；经夜行性锥蝽（猎蝽科/"接吻虫"）传播，后者栖息于茅草屋顶农村房屋；也可经输血、器官移植、垂直传播</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute phase<br />
急性期</td>
<td>Mild fever, malaise, lymphadenopathy ± splenomegaly; Romaña sign (unilateral painless periorbital edema at bite site near eye); lasts 1–2 months, resolves spontaneously; CURABLE with nifurtimox or benznidazole<br />
轻度发热、乏力、淋巴结肿大±脾大；Romaña征（眼部附近叮咬处单侧无痛性眼眶周围水肿）；持续1–2个月，自行消退；硝呋替莫或苄硝唑可治愈</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic phase — cardiac<br />
慢性期——心脏</td>
<td>Dilated cardiomyopathy, right bundle branch block (classic ECG finding), apical left ventricular aneurysm, CHF, arrhythmia; leading cause of death in chronic Chagas<br />
扩张型心肌病、右束支传导阻滞（经典心电图表现）、左室心尖部室壁瘤、充血性心力衰竭、心律失常；慢性Chagas病主要死因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic phase — GI<br />
慢性期——消化道</td>
<td>Megaesophagus (dysphagia, regurgitation of undigested food, odynophagia, weight loss) + megacolon (constipation, obstruction); both due to myenteric plexus neuronal destruction<br />
食管巨大症（吞咽困难、反流未消化食物、吞咽痛、体重下降）+ 巨结肠（便秘、梗阻）；均由肌间神经丛神经元破坏所致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis by phase<br />
分期诊断方法</td>
<td>Acute: peripheral blood smear (extracellular trypomastigotes); Chronic: ELISA serology (gold standard), PCR; CXR shows dilated esophagus ± cardiomegaly; ECG for cardiac involvement<br />
急性期：外周血涂片（胞外锥鞭毛体）；慢性期：ELISA血清学（金标准）、PCR；胸片显示食管扩张±心脏扩大；心电图评估心脏受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Acute phase: nifurtimox or benznidazole (prolonged course, curative); Chronic phase: NOT curable — supportive management of cardiac (ICD, antiarrhythmics, transplant) and GI (esophageal pneumatic dilation, laxatives, surgery for megacolon) complications<br />
急性期：硝呋替莫或苄硝唑（疗程长，可治愈）；慢性期：不可治愈——支持管理心脏（ICD、抗心律失常药、移植）和消化道（食管气囊扩张、泻药、巨结肠手术）并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chagas vs. primary achalasia<br />
Chagas vs. 原发性贲门失弛缓症</td>
<td>Both cause megaesophagus and progressive dysphagia (solids → liquids); Chagas: Latin American origin + megacolon + dilated cardiomyopathy; Achalasia: no geographic clue, no cardiac or colonic involvement, bird-beak on barium swallow<br />
两者均致食管巨大症和进行性吞咽困难（固体→液体）；Chagas：拉丁美洲来源 + 巨结肠 + 扩张型心肌病；贲门失弛缓症：无地理线索，无心脏或结肠受累，钡餐显示鸟嘴征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why dilation, not stricture<br />
为何出现扩张而非狭窄</td>
<td>Myenteric plexus destruction → loss of inhibitory neurons → LES fails to relax → functional (not mechanical) obstruction → proximal dilation from back-pressure; scleroderma causes fibrosis → narrowing → stricture<br />
肌间神经丛破坏 → 抑制性神经元丧失 → LES不能舒张 → 功能性（非机械性）梗阻 → 近端因背压扩张；硬皮病为纤维化 → 管腔变窄 → 狭窄</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Romaña sign:** unilateral painless periorbital edema at the site of a conjunctival/eyelid bug bite during acute Chagas — rare but pathognomonic; test-takers should recognize it as distinct from cellulitis or angioedema\
  **Romaña征:** 急性Chagas病期间结膜/眼睑叮咬部位出现单侧无痛性眼眶周围水肿——罕见但具特征性；考生应将其与蜂窝织炎或血管性水肿区分

- **Achalasia look-alike:** Chagas and primary achalasia share megaesophagus, bird-beak LES on barium swallow, and progressive dysphagia; the exam will always embed a Latin American geographic clue to point to Chagas — never miss the travel/immigration history\
  **贲门失弛缓症拟似:** Chagas病与原发性贲门失弛缓症共享食管巨大症、钡餐鸟嘴征和进行性吞咽困难；考题中必然嵌入拉丁美洲地理线索以指向Chagas病——切勿遗漏旅行/移民史

- **Why chronic phase is incurable:** T. cruzi evades immune clearance and establishes latent intracellular infection; myenteric neurons and cardiomyocytes destroyed in chronic phase cannot regenerate; antiparasitics have no benefit once structural damage is established\
  **慢性期不可治愈的原因:** 克氏锥虫逃避免疫清除并建立潜伏性胞内感染；慢性期被破坏的肌间神经元和心肌细胞不可再生；一旦结构性损伤已建立，抗寄生虫药物无效

- **Key ECG finding:** right bundle branch block (RBBB) + left anterior fascicular block is the classic ECG pattern of chronic Chagas cardiomyopathy; combined with an apical aneurysm, it is nearly pathognomonic in a Latin American patient\
  **关键心电图表现:** 右束支传导阻滞（RBBB）+ 左前分支阻滞是慢性Chagas心肌病的经典心电图模式；结合心尖部室壁瘤，对于拉丁美洲患者几乎具有诊断意义

# Question 139 — Transfusion-Related Acute Lung Injury / 输血相关急性肺损伤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>hospitalized 27-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>sickle cell crisis</strong> has <strong>shortness of breath</strong> and <strong>nonproductive cough</strong> <strong>4 hours after transfusion</strong> of 1 unit of packed red blood cells. Her only medication is morphine. Her temperature is <strong>38°C (100.4°F)</strong>, pulse is <strong>126/min</strong>, respirations are <strong>28/min</strong>, and blood pressure is <strong>98/58 mm Hg</strong>. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of <strong>88%</strong>. Examination shows central cyanosis. <strong>Diffuse crackles are heard bilaterally</strong>. Heart sounds are normal. Arterial blood gas analysis on room air shows: pH 7.47, PCO2 38 mm Hg, PO2 55 mm Hg. A chest x-ray shows <strong>bilateral pulmonary infiltrates</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely cause of these findings?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of these findings?</strong></p>
<p>A) ABO incompatibility<br />
B) Anaphylactic transfusion reaction<br />
C) Fluid overload<br />
D) Hemolytic transfusion reaction<br />
E) Transfusion-related acute lung injury</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Onset 4 hours after transfusion<br />
输血后4小时发病</td>
<td>TRALI hallmark: onset during or within 6 hours of transfusion; distinguishes from delayed hemolytic reactions<br />
TRALI 标志：发生于输血后6小时内；有别于迟发性溶血反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral crackles + bilateral pulmonary infiltrates on CXR<br />
双侧湿啰音 + 胸片双肺浸润影</td>
<td>Non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema pattern; key diagnostic criterion for TRALI<br />
非心源性肺水肿表现；TRALI 的关键诊断标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypoxemia: SpO2 88%, PO2 55 mm Hg<br />
低氧血症：氧饱和度88%，PO2 55 mmHg</td>
<td>Severe hypoxemia unresponsive to small O2 supplementation; reflects massive V/Q mismatch from alveolar flooding<br />
严重低氧血症；反映肺泡积液引起的大量通气/血流失匹配</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypotension: BP 98/58 mm Hg<br />
低血压：血压98/58 mmHg</td>
<td>Hemodynamic compromise seen in TRALI due to inflammatory cytokine release; absent in simple fluid overload<br />
TRALI 中炎症细胞因子释放导致血流动力学障碍；单纯液体过负荷中不出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever: T 38°C<br />
发热：体温38°C</td>
<td>Fever accompanies TRALI due to neutrophil activation; helps distinguish from anaphylaxis (no fever)<br />
TRALI 中性粒细胞活化伴发热；有助于与过敏反应（无发热）区分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal heart sounds<br />
心音正常</td>
<td>Against cardiogenic pulmonary edema (no S3, no JVD, no displaced PMI); favors non-cardiogenic etiology<br />
排除心源性肺水肿（无S3奔马律、无颈静脉怒张）；支持非心源性病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**TRALI** is caused by **donor antibodies** (anti-HLA or anti-neutrophil antibodies) in the transfused product that bind to **recipient neutrophils** in the pulmonary microvasculature, triggering massive **inflammatory cascade**:

**TRALI** 由输血产品中的**供者抗体**（抗HLA抗体或抗中性粒细胞抗体）与受者**肺微血管内的中性粒细胞**结合，触发大规模**炎症级联反应**引起：

- Donor antibodies activate pulmonary neutrophils → degranulation + cytokine/ROS release\
  供者抗体激活肺内中性粒细胞 → 脱颗粒 + 细胞因子/活性氧释放

- Activated neutrophils damage alveolar-capillary membrane → massive capillary leak\
  活化的中性粒细胞损伤肺泡-毛细血管膜 → 大量毛细血管渗漏

- Protein-rich fluid floods alveoli → non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema → hypoxemia\
  富含蛋白质的液体涌入肺泡 → 非心源性肺水肿 → 低氧血症

- Inflammatory mediators cause systemic vasodilation → hypotension + fever\
  炎症介质导致全身血管扩张 → 低血压 + 发热

- Wedge pressure remains normal (PCWP \< 18 mmHg) — distinguishes from cardiogenic edema\
  肺毛细血管楔压保持正常（PCWP \< 18 mmHg）——与心源性水肿区分的关键

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** TRALI floods the alveoli WITHOUT raising left heart pressures — that's why the heart sounds are normal and the CXR shows infiltrates without cardiomegaly or Kerley B lines.

**解剖小窍门:** TRALI 淹没肺泡但不升高左心压力——这就是为什么心音正常，胸片显示浸润影但无心脏增大或Kerley B线。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Transfusion-Related Acute Lung Injury / 正确答案 (E) — 输血相关急性肺损伤

**Transfusion-Related Acute Lung Injury (TRALI)** is a life-threatening non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema occurring within 6 hours of transfusion, caused by donor antibody-mediated neutrophil activation in the pulmonary vasculature:

**输血相关急性肺损伤（TRALI）** 是发生于输血后6小时内的危及生命的非心源性肺水肿，由供者抗体介导的肺血管内中性粒细胞活化引起：

- Timing: during transfusion or within 6 hours (this patient: 4 hours — classic)\
  时间：输血中或6小时内（本例：4小时——典型）

- Blood products with highest risk: plasma \> platelets \> whole blood \> pRBCs\
  风险最高的血制品：血浆 \> 血小板 \> 全血 \> 浓缩红细胞

- Diagnosis requires: new acute hypoxemia + bilateral CXR infiltrates + temporal relation to transfusion + no pre-existing ALI\
  诊断要求：新发急性低氧血症 + 胸片双侧浸润影 + 与输血时间相关 + 无既存ALI

- TRALI is the leading cause of transfusion-related mortality in the US\
  TRALI 是美国输血相关死亡的首要原因

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis — fever, hypotension, hypoxemia (PO2/FiO2 \< 300), bilateral infiltrates, normal cardiac pressures, all within 6 hours of transfusion; no specific lab test confirms TRALI.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——输血6小时内出现发热、低血压、低氧血症（PO2/FiO2 \< 300）、双侧浸润影、心脏压力正常；无特异性实验室检查可确诊TRALI。

**Treatment:** Stop transfusion immediately; supplemental O2 (noninvasive positive pressure ventilation or intubation); hemodynamic support (IV fluids, vasopressors); do NOT use diuretics (worsens non-cardiogenic edema); most patients recover within 48–96 hours.

**治疗:** 立即停止输血；补充氧气（无创正压通气或气管插管）；血流动力学支持（静脉补液、血管升压药）；**禁用利尿剂**（会加重非心源性水肿）；多数患者48–96小时内恢复。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — ABO incompatibility<br />
A — ABO血型不合</td>
<td>Presents with fever, rigors, flank/back pain, hemoglobinuria, DIC — NOT bilateral pulmonary infiltrates or hypoxemia<br />
表现为发热、寒战、腰背痛、血红蛋白尿、DIC——不会出现双肺浸润影或低氧血症</td>
<td>No pulmonary infiltrates; hemolysis markers (hemoglobinuria, elevated LDH, positive DAT)<br />
无肺浸润影；溶血标志物（血红蛋白尿、LDH升高、直接抗球蛋白试验阳性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Anaphylactic transfusion reaction<br />
B — 过敏性输血反应</td>
<td>IgE-mediated; presents with urticaria, bronchospasm, angioedema, hypotension — no fever, no pulmonary infiltrates<br />
IgE介导；表现为荨麻疹、支气管痉挛、血管性水肿、低血压——无发热，无肺浸润影</td>
<td>No fever + no bilateral infiltrates + urticaria/wheezing pattern vs. this patient's crackles + CXR changes<br />
无发热 + 无双侧浸润影 + 荨麻疹/喘鸣模式，而本患者有湿啰音 + 胸片改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Fluid overload<br />
C — 液体过负荷</td>
<td>TACO (transfusion-associated circulatory overload) presents with hypertension (not hypotension), elevated BNP, JVD, peripheral edema<br />
TACO（输血相关循环过负荷）表现为高血压（非低血压）、BNP升高、颈静脉怒张、外周水肿</td>
<td>Hypotension rules out TACO; 1 unit pRBCs is too small to cause TACO in a normovolemic patient<br />
低血压排除TACO；正常容量患者输注1单位红细胞量太少无法引起TACO</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Hemolytic transfusion reaction<br />
D — 溶血性输血反应</td>
<td>Usually caused by ABO incompatibility; presents with fever, back pain, hematuria, hemolysis — not primarily a pulmonary syndrome<br />
通常由ABO不合引起；表现为发热、腰痛、血尿、溶血——不是主要的肺部综合征</td>
<td>Primary findings are hemolysis (elevated indirect bilirubin, hemoglobinuria), not bilateral pulmonary infiltrates<br />
主要表现为溶血（间接胆红素升高、血红蛋白尿），而非双肺浸润影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Transfusion-related acute lung injury ✓<br />
E — 输血相关急性肺损伤 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — classic TRALI: onset 4 h post-transfusion, fever, hypotension, hypoxemia (PO2 55), bilateral infiltrates, normal heart sounds<br />
正确——典型TRALI：输血后4小时发病，发热、低血压、低氧血症（PO2 55）、双侧浸润影、心音正常</td>
<td>All five TRALI criteria met; non-cardiogenic pattern confirmed by hypotension + normal heart sounds<br />
满足全部五项TRALI诊断标准；低血压 + 心音正常证实非心源性模式</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is fluid overload (TACO), but hypotension and the absence of elevated filling pressures decisively rule it out — TACO causes hypertension from volume excess, not hypotension.*

TACO（液体过负荷）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，但低血压和充盈压不高的表现可断然排除——TACO由容量过多引起高血压，而非低血压。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**TRALI = Transfusion within 6 hours + Fever + Hypotension + Hypoxemia + Bilateral infiltrates + Normal cardiac pressures → Stop transfusion, give O2, hemodynamic support.**

**TRALI = 输血6小时内 + 发热 + 低血压 + 低氧血症 + 双肺浸润影 + 心脏压力正常 → 停止输血、补氧、血流动力学支持。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — TRALI's "FHIB" / 记忆钩 — TRALI 的 "FHIB" 四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>F</strong>ever — always present, distinguishes TRALI from TACO / 发热——总是出现，区别于TACO<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ypotension — from systemic vasodilation (NOT volume overload) / 低血压——来自全身血管扩张（非容量过负荷）<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfiltrates bilateral — non-cardiogenic, wedge pressure normal / 双侧浸润影——非心源性，楔压正常<br />
• <strong>B</strong>lood product window — onset within 6 hours of any transfusion / 血制品窗口期——任何输血后6小时内发病</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>
