## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Developmental Anxiety and Object Permanence in Pediatrics / 高频知识表 — 儿科发育性焦虑与客体永久性

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Object permanence<br />
客体永久性</td>
<td>Develops fully by ~18–24 months (Piaget sensorimotor stage); before this, "out of sight = gone forever" underlies separation anxiety<br />
约 18~24 个月发育完善（皮亚杰感觉运动期）；此前"看不见=永远消失"是分离焦虑的认知基础</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal separation anxiety timeline<br />
正常分离焦虑时间轴</td>
<td>Begins ~6 months, peaks 18–24 months, resolves by age 3–4; persistence beyond age 6 suggests Separation Anxiety Disorder<br />
约 6 个月出现，18~24 个月达高峰，3~4 岁消退；6 岁后持续提示分离焦虑障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Stranger anxiety timeline<br />
陌生人焦虑时间轴</td>
<td>Peaks 9–12 months; part of normal secure attachment development (Bowlby/Ainsworth)<br />
高峰为 9~12 个月；属于正常安全型依恋发育的一部分（鲍尔比/安斯沃思理论）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Separation Anxiety Disorder (DSM-5)<br />
分离焦虑障碍（DSM-5）</td>
<td>Excessive fear of separation lasting ≥4 weeks in children, causing significant distress/impairment; most common anxiety disorder in children under 12<br />
儿童对分离的过度恐惧持续≥4 周，造成明显痛苦/功能损害；12 岁以下最常见的焦虑障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hospital management of separation anxiety<br />
住院环境中分离焦虑的处理</td>
<td>Allow parental presence during induction; child life specialists; minimize wait times; provide age-appropriate explanation<br />
允许父母陪伴至麻醉诱导；利用儿童生活专家；缩短等待时间；提供适合年龄的解释</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fear of mutilation<br />
肢体残缺恐惧</td>
<td>More characteristic of school-age children (6–12 years, concrete operations stage) who understand bodily integrity; not typical in toddlers<br />
更典型于学龄儿童（6~12 岁，具体运算期），已理解身体完整性概念；在幼儿中不典型</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of crying/clinging in toddlers:** Separation anxiety (primary caregiver threat), stranger anxiety (unfamiliar person present), pain (localized behavior, consolable with analgesia), hunger/fatigue (context-dependent)\
  **幼儿哭泣/依附的鉴别:** 分离焦虑（主要照料者威胁）、陌生人焦虑（陌生人出现）、疼痛（定位行为，镇痛可安抚）、饥饿/疲劳（情境依赖）

- **Developmental progression of fears:** Infancy → strangers; toddler → separation; preschool → monsters/dark; school-age → bodily harm, death; adolescence → social/panic\
  **儿童恐惧发育进程:** 婴儿期→陌生人；幼儿期→分离；学龄前→怪物/黑暗；学龄期→肢体伤害、死亡；青少年期→社交/惊恐

- **Key complication of untreated Separation Anxiety Disorder:** School refusal (school avoidance disorder), social isolation, risk factor for adult agoraphobia and panic disorder\
  **未治疗分离焦虑障碍的关键并发症:** 拒学（学校回避障碍）、社会隔离，成年后广场恐惧症和惊恐障碍的风险因素

- **Exam variant — adolescent presentation:** Separation Anxiety Disorder in teenagers may present as somatic complaints (headache, abdominal pain) to avoid school, not just clinging behavior\
  **题目变式——青少年表现:** 青少年分离焦虑障碍可表现为躯体主诉（头痛、腹痛）以回避上学，而非仅有依附行为

# Question 146 — Caustic Alkali Ingestion with Esophageal Injury / 强碱腐蚀性摄入致食管损伤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>19-year-old woman</strong> is brought to the emergency department by her mother <strong>30 minutes after ingesting an unknown liquid</strong> she found in her parents' utility room following an argument with her boyfriend. Immediately after swallowing the liquid, she telephoned her mother at work, who arrived at home 20 minutes later and found her daughter <strong>drooling</strong> and reporting <strong>severe upper chest pain</strong>. On arrival at the emergency department, the patient is in obvious distress and is <strong>drooling and unable to swallow</strong>. Temperature is 37.0°C (98.6°F), pulse is 120/min and regular, respirations are 20/min, and blood pressure is 148/90 mm Hg. Physical examination shows <strong>profuse clear drainage from the mouth</strong> and <strong>erythema and edema of the posterior oropharynx</strong>. Cardiopulmonary examination shows no abnormalities. Two large-bore intravenous catheters are inserted for fluid administration and a dose of intravenous hydromorphone is administered. The patient begins to feel more comfortable. Results of laboratory studies are within the reference ranges. Chest x-ray shows no abnormalities. Which of the following is the most appropriate management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Administration of activated charcoal<br />
B) Administration of oral bicarbonate<br />
C) Esophagogastroduodenoscopy<br />
D) Induction of vomiting<br />
E) Nasogastric tube placement</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Unknown liquid from utility room<br />
储藏室不明液体</td>
<td>High suspicion for caustic household chemical (drain cleaner = alkali); utility rooms store lye/bleach<br />
高度怀疑腐蚀性家用化学品（管道疏通剂 = 强碱）；储藏室常存放碱液/漂白剂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Drooling and unable to swallow<br />
流涎且无法吞咽</td>
<td>Oropharyngeal/esophageal injury disrupting swallowing reflex; also contraindicates oral interventions<br />
口咽/食管损伤破坏吞咽反射；同时禁忌口服干预措施</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Severe upper chest pain<br />
剧烈上胸痛</td>
<td>Esophageal chemical burn; raises concern for transmural injury or early perforation<br />
食管化学烧伤；提示跨壁损伤或早期穿孔风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Erythema and edema of posterior oropharynx<br />
口咽后壁红斑及水肿</td>
<td>Visible proximal injury = high likelihood of distal GI injury (esophagus, stomach)<br />
可见近端损伤 = 远端消化道损伤（食管、胃）高概率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia + hypertension<br />
心动过速 + 高血压</td>
<td>Sympathetic activation from pain/stress; also reflects systemic response to significant injury<br />
疼痛/应激交感激活；同时反映显著损伤的全身反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chest x-ray no abnormalities<br />
胸片无异常</td>
<td>Rules out free air (perforation) at this point; does NOT exclude mucosal injury requiring EGD<br />
此时排除游离气体（穿孔）；但不能排除需要 EGD 评估的黏膜损伤</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Caustic alkali** (e.g., sodium hydroxide in drain cleaners) acts as a **proton acceptor and strong nucleophile**, causing **liquefactive necrosis** — a uniquely penetrating form of tissue destruction distinct from acid burns:

**强碱**（如管道疏通剂中的氢氧化钠）作为**质子受体和强亲核试剂**，引发**液化性坏死** — 这是一种不同于酸烧伤的深度渗透性组织破坏：

- Alkali saponifies lipid membranes and denatures proteins → cells liquefy and injury penetrates deeply through tissue layers\
  碱液皂化脂质膜并使蛋白质变性 → 细胞液化，损伤深层渗透穿透组织各层

- Unlike acid burns (coagulative necrosis forms a protective eschar), alkali creates no barrier → deeper, more extensive damage\
  与酸烧伤（凝固性坏死形成保护性焦痂）不同，碱液无屏障形成 → 损伤更深、范围更广

- Esophagus is particularly vulnerable (squamous epithelium, no protective lumen); stomach injury also common\
  食管特别易受损（鳞状上皮，无保护性管腔）；胃损伤同样常见

- Visible oropharyngeal burns correlate strongly with distal esophageal/gastric injury\
  可见口咽部烧伤与远端食管/胃损伤强烈相关

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The esophagus is most at risk with alkali (slow transit), while the stomach is more at risk with acid (rapid transit past a closed pylorus).

**解剖小窍门:** 食管在强碱摄入时风险最高（通过缓慢），胃在强酸摄入时风险更高（通过幽门关闭后酸液潴留）。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Esophagogastroduodenoscopy / 正确答案 (C) — 食管胃十二指肠镜检查

**Esophagogastroduodenoscopy (EGD)** is the definitive procedure to evaluate the extent and severity of mucosal injury following caustic ingestion, and it directly guides subsequent management:

**食管胃十二指肠镜检查（EGD）**是腐蚀性摄入后评估黏膜损伤范围和严重程度的决定性手段，直接指导后续处理：

- EGD grades injury: Grade I (superficial) → conservative; Grade IIb-III (deep/circumferential) → high risk for stricture, perforation, surgery\
  EGD 分级损伤：I 级（浅表）→ 保守治疗；IIb-III 级（深层/环周）→ 狭窄、穿孔、手术风险高

- Performed within 12–24 hours of ingestion (not immediately — allow resuscitation; not delayed beyond 24h — edema obscures grading)\
  摄入后 12–24 小时内进行（不是立即——需先复苏；不超过 24 小时延迟——水肿影响分级评估）

- Visible oropharyngeal injury (as in this patient) increases probability of significant esophageal/gastric injury requiring endoscopic staging\
  可见口咽损伤（本例患者）增加显著食管/胃损伤需内镜分级的概率

**Diagnosis:** Caustic alkali ingestion with oropharyngeal burns and suspected esophageal injury, requiring EGD to grade mucosal damage before determining further treatment.

**诊断:** 强碱腐蚀性摄入伴口咽烧伤及疑似食管损伤，需 EGD 评估黏膜损伤程度后决定进一步治疗。

**Treatment:** Supportive care (IV fluids, IV opioid analgesia, NPO, airway monitoring) → EGD for staging → if high-grade: corticosteroids (controversial), antibiotics, surgery for perforation.

**治疗:** 支持治疗（静脉补液、静脉阿片类镇痛、禁食、气道监测）→ EGD 分级 → 高级别损伤：糖皮质激素（争议性）、抗生素、穿孔则手术干预。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Activated charcoal<br />
A — 活性炭</td>
<td>Contraindicated: patient cannot swallow and cannot protect airway → aspiration risk causes aspiration pneumonitis; also obscures EGD visualization<br />
禁忌：患者无法吞咽且无法保护气道 → 误吸风险导致吸入性肺炎；同时遮蔽 EGD 视野</td>
<td>Activated charcoal is for toxins with enterohepatic circulation; caustic agents are not adsorbed by charcoal and it adds harm<br />
活性炭用于肠肝循环毒物；腐蚀性物质不被活性炭吸附，反增加风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Oral bicarbonate<br />
B — 口服碳酸氢钠</td>
<td>Patient cannot swallow (dangerous); acid-base neutralization causes exothermic reaction → additional thermal injury<br />
患者无法吞咽（危险）；酸碱中和产生放热反应 → 额外热损伤</td>
<td>Never neutralize caustic ingestions chemically — generates heat and worsens injury<br />
切勿化学中和腐蚀性摄入——产热加重损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Esophagogastroduodenoscopy ✓<br />
C — 食管胃十二指肠镜检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — gold standard to assess mucosal injury extent, grade damage, and guide management<br />
正确——评估黏膜损伤范围、损伤分级和指导处理的金标准</td>
<td>Visible oropharyngeal injury with inability to swallow mandates EGD evaluation<br />
可见口咽损伤伴吞咽障碍，强制要求 EGD 评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Induction of vomiting<br />
D — 催吐</td>
<td>Causes re-exposure of alkali to esophageal mucosa; esophageal trauma from vomiting pressure; risk of Mallory-Weiss or perforation<br />
导致强碱再次接触食管黏膜；呕吐压力造成食管创伤；Mallory-Weiss 撕裂或穿孔风险</td>
<td>Never induce vomiting after caustic or petroleum distillate ingestion<br />
腐蚀性或石油馏出物摄入后切勿催吐</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Nasogastric tube placement<br />
E — 鼻胃管置入</td>
<td>Blind placement risks creating false passage through injured/perforated esophagus; causes further mechanical trauma to burned tissue<br />
盲目置入有穿透受损/穿孔食管形成假腔的风险；对烧伤组织造成进一步机械损伤</td>
<td>In caustic ingestion, NGT is contraindicated; EGD first establishes injury grade before any tube decisions<br />
腐蚀性摄入时禁忌鼻胃管；应先 EGD 确定损伤分级再决定置管</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (E) nasogastric tube — decompression seems intuitive, but blind tube passage through a potentially perforated esophagus is exactly the kind of intervention that converts a chemical burn into a surgical emergency.*

鼻胃管（E 项）是最具迷惑性的干扰项——胃减压看似合理，但在可能穿孔的食管中盲目通过管道，恰恰是将化学烧伤转变为外科急症的操作。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Alkali vs. Acid Caustic Ingestion / 强碱 vs. 强酸腐蚀性摄入对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Alkali (e.g., NaOH, drain cleaner)</strong><br />
<strong>强碱（如 NaOH、管道疏通剂）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Acid (e.g., HCl, battery acid)</strong><br />
<strong>强酸（如盐酸、电池酸液）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Necrosis type<br />
坏死类型</td>
<td>Liquefactive necrosis (no eschar → deep penetration)<br />
液化性坏死（无焦痂 → 深层渗透）</td>
<td>Coagulative necrosis (eschar limits penetration)<br />
凝固性坏死（焦痂限制渗透）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most injured site<br />
最易受损部位</td>
<td>Esophagus (slow transit)<br />
食管（通过缓慢）</td>
<td>Stomach/pylorus (pooling)<br />
胃/幽门（酸液积聚）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Depth of injury<br />
损伤深度</td>
<td>Typically deeper, transmural risk higher<br />
通常更深，跨壁风险更高</td>
<td>Relatively more superficial in esophagus<br />
在食管中相对较浅</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-term complication<br />
长期并发症</td>
<td>Esophageal stricture (weeks–months later)<br />
食管狭窄（数周至数月后）</td>
<td>Pyloric stenosis / gastric outlet obstruction<br />
幽门狭窄/胃出口梗阻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Oropharyngeal burns predictive?<br />
口咽烧伤是否预测远端损伤？</td>
<td>Yes — correlates with esophageal/gastric injury<br />
是——与食管/胃损伤相关</td>
<td>Less predictive (acid transits faster)<br />
预测性较低（酸通过更快）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Workup<br />
评估手段</td>
<td>EGD within 12–24 hours<br />
12–24 小时内 EGD</td>
<td>EGD within 12–24 hours<br />
12–24 小时内 EGD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Contraindicated interventions<br />
禁忌干预</td>
<td>Charcoal, NGT, vomiting induction, neutralization<br />
活性炭、鼻胃管、催吐、化学中和</td>
<td>Same contraindications<br />
相同禁忌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**After caustic alkali ingestion causing oropharyngeal burns and dysphagia, the next step is EGD to grade the extent of esophageal and gastric mucosal injury.**

**强碱腐蚀性摄入引起口咽烧伤和吞咽障碍后，下一步是 EGD 评估食管和胃黏膜损伤范围。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CAVE" for Caustic Ingestion Don'ts / 记忆钩 — 腐蚀性摄入禁忌"CAVE":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>harcoal — avoid (can't adsorb caustics, obscures EGD, aspiration risk) / 活性炭——禁用（无法吸附腐蚀剂，遮蔽EGD，误吸风险）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>cid-base neutralization — avoid (exothermic reaction = more burns) / 酸碱中和——禁用（放热反应 = 更多烧伤）<br />
• <strong>V</strong>omiting induction — avoid (re-exposes mucosa, pressure trauma, perforation) / 催吐——禁用（再次暴露黏膜，压力损伤，穿孔）<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ND everything with EGD — the one RIGHT answer (grade injury, guide management) / 一切以EGD收尾——唯一正确答案（损伤分级，指导处理）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Caustic Ingestion Management / 高频知识表 — 腐蚀性摄入处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>EGD timing<br />
EGD 时机</td>
<td>12–24 hours post-ingestion; too early (&lt; 6h) = edema makes grading unreliable; too late (&gt; 48h) = tissue softening increases perforation risk during scope<br />
摄入后 12–24 小时；过早（&lt; 6h）= 水肿影响分级；过晚（&gt; 48h）= 组织软化增加镜检穿孔风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Zargar EGD grading<br />
Zargar EGD 分级</td>
<td>Grade I: mucosal edema/erythema → good prognosis; Grade IIa: superficial ulcers; Grade IIb: deep/circumferential ulcers; Grade III: necrosis → perforation/stricture risk<br />
I 级：黏膜水肿/红斑 → 预后良好；IIa：浅表溃疡；IIb：深/环周溃疡；III 级：坏死 → 穿孔/狭窄风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Steroids in caustic injury<br />
腐蚀性损伤中的激素</td>
<td>Controversial; some use for Grade IIb to reduce stricture formation; NOT recommended for Grade III (perforation risk outweighs benefit)<br />
有争议；部分用于 IIb 级减少狭窄；III 级不推荐（穿孔风险超过获益）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Airway management priority<br />
气道管理优先级</td>
<td>Oropharyngeal edema can progress to airway compromise; early intubation or surgical airway if stridor or rapidly expanding edema<br />
口咽水肿可进展为气道受损；若有喘鸣或迅速扩展的水肿需早期插管或外科气道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Late complication: esophageal stricture<br />
晚期并发症：食管狭窄</td>
<td>Develops weeks to months post-injury in severe cases; presents with progressive dysphagia; treated with serial endoscopic dilation<br />
重度损伤后数周至数月出现；表现为进行性吞咽困难；通过序列内镜扩张治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Psychiatric follow-up<br />
精神科随访</td>
<td>Intentional ingestion (as in this case — argument with boyfriend) requires psychiatric evaluation before discharge<br />
蓄意摄入（本例——与男友争吵后）需出院前精神科评估</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of corrosive ingestion agents:** Alkalis include NaOH (drain cleaner/lye), KOH, bleach (NaOCl); acids include HCl (pool cleaner), H₂SO₄ (battery acid) — alkalis cause more severe esophageal injury\
  **腐蚀性摄入物鉴别:** 强碱包括 NaOH（管道疏通剂/碱液）、KOH、漂白剂（NaOCl）；强酸包括盐酸（泳池清洁剂）、硫酸（电池酸液）——强碱造成更严重的食管损伤

- **Key complication — perforation signs:** Free air on imaging, mediastinitis (fever, chest pain, crepitus), or peritonitis indicate perforation requiring emergent surgery\
  **关键并发症——穿孔征象:** 影像学游离气体、纵隔炎（发热、胸痛、捻发音）或腹膜炎提示穿孔，需急诊手术

- **Variant — pediatric accidental ingestion:** Children often ingest small quantities with less severe injury (brief contact vs. intentional adult ingestion); management algorithm same but lower threshold for observation without EGD if asymptomatic\
  **题目变式——儿童意外摄入:** 儿童通常摄入量少，损伤较轻（短暂接触 vs. 成人蓄意摄入）；处理流程相同，但无症状者可酌情观察而非强制 EGD

- **Cause of death in severe cases:** Esophageal or gastric perforation leading to mediastinitis, sepsis, or fistula formation (tracheoesophageal or aortoesophageal) are the most feared lethal complications\
  **严重病例死亡原因:** 食管或胃穿孔导致纵隔炎、脓毒症或瘘管形成（气管食管瘘或主动脉食管瘘）是最危险的致死性并发症

# Question 147 — Post-Splenectomy Vaccination Against Encapsulated Bacteria / 脾切除术后针对荚膜菌疫苗接种

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>23-year-old male</strong> college student comes to the clinic for a follow-up visit <strong>14 days after undergoing emergent splenectomy</strong> following a <strong>motor vehicle collision</strong>. The patient has resumed his regular diet and is ambulating normally. Medical history otherwise is unremarkable, and his only medication is acetaminophen as needed. The patient <strong>completed his Haemophilus influenzae type b vaccinations by age 18 months</strong> and his varicella, polio, and measles-mumps-rubella vaccinations by age 5 years; he received a human papillomavirus vaccination at age 11 years. Temperature is 37.0°C (98.6°F), pulse is 82/min, and blood pressure is 116/54 mm Hg. Abdominal examination shows a <strong>well-healing midline incision</strong>. Which of the following vaccinations is most appropriate to administer to this patient today?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following vaccinations is most appropriate to administer to this patient today?</strong></p>
<p>A) Haemophilus influenzae type b<br />
B) Human papillomavirus<br />
C) Inactivated poliovirus<br />
D) Measles, mumps, rubella<br />
E) Varicella<br />
F) No vaccine is indicated at this time</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Emergent splenectomy, 14 days ago<br />
14 天前急诊脾切除</td>
<td>Asplenia eliminates splenic filtration of encapsulated bacteria, permanently and dramatically increasing infection risk<br />
无脾状态永久消除脾脏对荚膜菌的过滤功能，感染风险大幅升高</td>
</tr>

外伤性脾切除 = 手术性无脾；患者对荚膜菌永久免疫受损</td>

</tr>

病史中未提及肺炎球菌或脑膜炎球菌疫苗</td>
<td>These are also mandatory for asplenic patients; the question tests the underlying principle of encapsulated bacteria risk<br />
这些疫苗同样是无脾患者的必须项；题目考查荚膜菌风险的基本原则</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **spleen** is the primary organ for clearing **opsonized encapsulated bacteria** from the bloodstream via three synergistic mechanisms:

**脾脏**通过三种协同机制清除血液中**被调理素包被的荚膜菌**，是这一过程的核心器官：

- The splenic sinusoids physically trap **opsonized pathogens** through slow-flow mechanical filtration even before antibody response is mounted\
  脾窦通过低流速机械过滤物理捕获**被调理素包被的病原体**，甚至在抗体应答启动前即可发挥作用

- Splenic **macrophages** phagocytose opsonized bacteria via Fc and complement receptors, providing rapid innate clearance\
  脾脏**巨噬细胞**通过 Fc 受体和补体受体吞噬调理素包被的细菌，提供快速先天性清除

- Splenic **marginal zone B cells** produce **IgM** against T-independent polysaccharide antigens (the bacterial capsule) within days\
  脾脏**边缘区 B 细胞**在数天内针对 T 非依赖性多糖抗原（荚膜）产生 **IgM**

- Without a spleen, **encapsulated organisms** evade all three mechanisms → fulminant bacteremia → **overwhelming post-splenectomy infection (OPSI)**\
  缺乏脾脏，**荚膜菌**逃脱上述三种机制 → 暴发性菌血症 → **脾切除术后暴发性感染（OPSI）**

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Encapsulated bacteria resist phagocytosis by shielding their surface antigens under a polysaccharide capsule; the spleen is uniquely able to clear them even without pre-formed antibody, which is precisely why its absence is selectively lethal for these organisms and not for viruses.

**解剖小窍门:** 荚膜菌通过多糖荚膜覆盖表面抗原来抵抗吞噬；脾脏即使在无预存抗体的情况下也能清除荚膜菌，这正是无脾状态对这类细菌（而非病毒）选择性致命的原因。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Haemophilus influenzae type b Vaccine / 正确答案 (A) — b 型流感嗜血杆菌疫苗

**Haemophilus influenzae type b (Hib)** is an encapsulated gram-negative coccobacillus that requires intact splenic function for adequate clearance from the bloodstream:

**b 型流感嗜血杆菌（Hib）** 是一种有荚膜的革兰阴性球杆菌，需要完整的脾脏功能才能从血液中充分清除：

- Hib possesses a **polyribosylribitol phosphate (PRP) capsule** that directly resists complement-mediated lysis and unaugmented phagocytosis\
  Hib 具有**聚核糖磷酸核糖醇（PRP）荚膜**，可直接抵抗补体介导的溶解和未增强的吞噬作用

- Asplenic patients face dramatically elevated risk for **invasive Hib disease**: bacteremia, meningitis, septic arthritis\
  无脾患者面临**侵袭性 Hib 疾病**（菌血症、脑膜炎、化脓性关节炎）风险显著升高

- Despite completing the childhood Hib series, **asplenic adults require a single booster dose** — the vaccination history does not override the asplenia indication\
  尽管已完成儿童期 Hib 系列接种，**无脾成人仍需单次加强剂量**——接种史不能覆盖无脾适应证

**Diagnosis:** The core insight is that post-splenectomy asplenia permanently eliminates the key clearance mechanism for encapsulated bacteria; prior Hib vaccination does not confer adequate protection when the splenic filter is absent.

**诊断:** 核心认识是脾切除术后无脾状态永久消除了荚膜菌的关键清除机制；当脾脏过滤器缺失时，既往 Hib 疫苗接种不能提供足够的保护。

**Treatment:** Administer Hib vaccine (one dose for previously vaccinated adults); also complete pneumococcal (PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23) and meningococcal (MenACWY + MenB) vaccines; consider prophylactic amoxicillin or penicillin V for 2–5 years post-splenectomy.

**治疗:** 接种 Hib 疫苗（既往已接种成人给单剂）；同时完成肺炎球菌（PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23）和脑膜炎球菌（MenACWY + MenB）疫苗；考虑脾切除后 2-5 年预防性使用阿莫西林或青霉素 V。

MMR 针对病毒性病原体；脾脏缺失不会特别增加麻疹、腮腺炎或风疹易感性；5 岁前已完成接种</td>
<td>Live-attenuated viral vaccine; no asplenia-specific indication<br />
减毒活病毒疫苗；无无脾特异性接种指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Varicella<br />
E — 水痘</td>
<td>Varicella (VZV) is a herpesvirus; asplenia does not specifically increase VZV risk; series was completed by age 5<br />
水痘（VZV）是疱疹病毒；无脾不会特异性增加 VZV 风险；5 岁前已完成接种</td>
<td>Live-attenuated viral vaccine; no asplenia-specific indication<br />
减毒活病毒疫苗；无无脾特异性接种指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — No vaccine is indicated at this time<br />
F — 目前无需接种疫苗</td>
<td>Incorrect; asplenic patients have permanent, lifelong elevated risk for invasive encapsulated bacterial disease and require specific re-vaccination<br />
错误；无脾患者对荚膜菌侵袭性疾病具有永久性终身风险，需要特定的重新接种</td>
<td>Asplenia = permanent loss of encapsulated bacteria clearance = vaccination is mandatory<br />
无脾 = 荚膜菌清除功能永久丧失 = 必须接种疫苗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is (F) "no vaccine indicated," which exploits the fact that the patient already received Hib in childhood — the key distinction is that post-splenectomy status mandates re-vaccination for encapsulated bacterial vaccines regardless of prior immunization history.*

最危险的干扰项是 F「目前无需接种」，该选项利用了患者儿童期已接种 Hib 这一事实——关键区别在于，脾切除术后状态对荚膜菌疫苗的接种要求无论既往免疫接种史如何均不可免除。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Asplenia-Specific Vaccines vs. Standard Schedule Vaccines / 无脾特异性疫苗 vs. 常规计划疫苗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Asplenia-Specific Vaccines (Encapsulated Bacteria)</strong><br />
<strong>无脾特异性疫苗（荚膜菌）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Standard Schedule Vaccines (Viral, Not Asplenia-Specific)</strong><br />
<strong>常规计划疫苗（病毒性，非无脾特异）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Target pathogens<br />
目标病原体</td>
<td>S. pneumoniae, H. influenzae type b, N. meningitidis<br />
肺炎链球菌、b 型流感嗜血杆菌、脑膜炎奈瑟菌</td>
<td>HPV, poliovirus, measles, mumps, rubella, varicella<br />
HPV、脊髓灰质炎病毒、麻疹、腮腺炎、风疹、水痘</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism of immune evasion<br />
免疫逃避机制</td>
<td>Polysaccharide capsule resists phagocytosis without opsonization; requires splenic marginal zone B cells for IgM<br />
多糖荚膜在无调理素化时抵抗吞噬；需脾脏边缘区 B 细胞产生 IgM</td>
<td>Intracellular replication; neutralized by circulating antibodies and T-cell immunity via lymph nodes<br />
细胞内复制；被循环抗体和淋巴结 T 细胞免疫中和</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why asplenia specifically matters<br />
无脾特别重要的原因</td>
<td>Spleen is the PRIMARY mechanical and immunologic clearance site for encapsulated bacteria<br />
脾脏是荚膜菌的主要机械和免疫学清除部位</td>
<td>Viral clearance depends on T-cell immunity and lymph nodes, not splenic filtration<br />
病毒清除依赖 T 细胞免疫和淋巴结，不特别依赖脾脏过滤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Re-vaccination after splenectomy<br />
脾切除后重新接种要求</td>
<td>Required: PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23, MenACWY, MenB, Hib (one booster even if prior series complete)<br />
必须：PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23、MenACWY、MenB、Hib（即使既往已完成接种系列也需单次加强）</td>
<td>Not specifically required due to asplenia; follow routine adult immunization schedule<br />
无脾状态无特定重新接种要求；遵循常规成人免疫接种计划</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Timing post-splenectomy<br />
脾切除后接种时机</td>
<td>Ideally ≥2 weeks before elective surgery; ASAP at first post-op visit for emergent cases (as in this question)<br />
选择性手术理想情况下提前 ≥2 周；急诊手术在首次术后随访时尽快接种（如本题）</td>
<td>Per routine schedule; no urgency related to splenectomy<br />
按常规计划；与脾切除无关的紧迫性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Consequence if missed<br />
漏接种的后果</td>
<td>OPSI: rapidly fatal sepsis, 50–70% mortality, can progress from symptom onset to death in &lt;24 hours<br />
OPSI：快速致死性败血症，死亡率 50-70%，可在 24 小时内从症状发作到死亡</td>
<td>Standard vaccine-preventable illness; not specifically amplified by asplenia<br />
标准疫苗可预防疾病；无脾状态不会特别放大</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**After splenectomy, the patient loses the primary clearance mechanism for encapsulated bacteria, making vaccination against H. influenzae, S. pneumoniae, and N. meningitidis mandatory regardless of prior immunization history.**

**脾切除术后患者丧失荚膜菌的主要清除机制，因此无论既往接种史如何，必须接种针对流感嗜血杆菌、肺炎链球菌和脑膜炎奈瑟菌的疫苗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SHiN" for Post-Splenectomy Mandatory Vaccines / 记忆钩 — "SHiN" 记住脾切除后必须接种的疫苗:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>treptococcus pneumoniae — #1 cause of OPSI; give PCV + PPSV23 / 肺炎链球菌——OPSI 首要病原；接种 PCV + PPSV23<br />
• <strong>H</strong>aemophilus influenzae type b — re-vaccinate post-splenectomy even if childhood series was completed / b 型流感嗜血杆菌——脾切除后需重新接种，即使儿童期已完成系列接种<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eisseria meningitidis — (the "iN" in SHiN); give MenACWY + MenB / 脑膜炎奈瑟菌——（SHiN 中的"iN"）；接种 MenACWY + MenB</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Post-Splenectomy Management / 高频知识表 — 脾切除术后管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Encapsulated organisms (USMLE core list)<br />
荚膜菌（USMLE 核心清单）</td>
<td>S. pneumoniae, H. influenzae type b, N. meningitidis, Klebsiella pneumoniae, E. coli, Salmonella typhi, group B Strep — mnemonic "SHiNe KESs"<br />
肺炎链球菌、b 型流感嗜血杆菌、脑膜炎奈瑟菌、肺炎克雷伯菌、大肠杆菌、伤寒沙门菌、B 组链球菌——记忆口诀"SHiNe KESs"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Overwhelming Post-Splenectomy Infection (OPSI)<br />
脾切除术后暴发性感染（OPSI）</td>
<td>Rapidly fatal sepsis most commonly from S. pneumoniae; mortality 50–70%; can progress to death in &lt;24 hours; highest risk in first 2 years post-splenectomy<br />
最常由肺炎链球菌引起的快速致死性败血症；死亡率 50-70%；可在 24 小时内死亡；脾切除后前 2 年风险最高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Required vaccines post-splenectomy<br />
脾切除后必须接种的疫苗</td>
<td>Pneumococcal (PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23), Meningococcal (MenACWY + MenB), Haemophilus influenzae type b (one booster dose)<br />
肺炎球菌（PCV15/PCV20 + PPSV23）、脑膜炎球菌（MenACWY + MenB）、b 型流感嗜血杆菌（单次加强剂量）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Optimal timing of vaccination<br />
最佳接种时机</td>
<td>Elective splenectomy: vaccinate ≥2 weeks before surgery; emergent splenectomy: vaccinate at first post-op clinic visit (≥2 weeks post-op)<br />
择期脾切除：术前 ≥2 周接种；急诊脾切除：在首次术后门诊随访时（术后 ≥2 周）接种</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
预防性抗生素</td>
<td>Amoxicillin or penicillin V for 2–5 years post-splenectomy (some guidelines recommend lifelong in high-risk patients, e.g., sickle cell disease)<br />
脾切除后 2-5 年使用阿莫西林或青霉素 V（部分指南建议高危患者，如镰刀细胞病，终身使用）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Howell-Jolly bodies<br />
Howell-Jolly 小体</td>
<td>Nuclear remnants in RBCs on peripheral blood smear = functional asplenia; seen post-splenectomy and in sickle cell disease (autosplenectomy)<br />
外周血涂片红细胞内核残余 = 功能性无脾；见于脾切除术后及镰刀细胞病（自体脾切除）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sickle cell disease parallel<br />
镰刀细胞病类比</td>
<td>Repeated splenic infarction → autosplenectomy by age ~5; same "SHiN" vaccination requirements apply; prophylactic penicillin started at diagnosis<br />
反复脾梗死 → 约 5 岁时自体脾切除；适用相同的"SHiN"疫苗接种要求；诊断时开始预防性青霉素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Functional vs. Anatomic Asplenia:** Both surgical splenectomy and autosplenectomy (sickle cell disease, celiac disease, bone marrow transplant) confer identical encapsulated bacterial infection risk; the same "SHiN" vaccination protocol applies to all\
  **功能性 vs 解剖性无脾:** 手术脾切除和自体脾切除（镰刀细胞病、乳糜泻、骨髓移植）均带来相同的荚膜菌感染风险；相同的"SHiN"疫苗接种方案适用于所有情况

- **Childhood Vaccination History Does Not Exempt Asplenic Adults:** A deliberate trap in this question — the patient completed Hib in childhood; the test-taker must recognize that asplenia re-sets the vaccination requirement for all three encapsulated bacterial vaccines\
  **儿童期接种史不能豁免无脾成人:** 本题故意设置的陷阱——患者儿童期完成了 Hib 接种；考生必须认识到无脾状态会重置所有三种荚膜菌疫苗的接种要求

- **Timing of This Case:** The 14-day post-operative follow-up visit is the textbook-perfect moment to initiate vaccinations for emergent splenectomy; pre-op vaccination was impossible given the trauma context\
  **本病例的时机:** 术后 14 天随访恰好是急诊脾切除后启动疫苗接种的教科书级完美时机；外伤情况下术前接种不可行

- **Differential of Causes Requiring Same Prophylaxis:** Post-traumatic splenectomy, elective splenectomy (ITP, hereditary spherocytosis), sickle cell autosplenectomy, functional asplenia from radiation or infiltration — all require encapsulated organism vaccines and penicillin prophylaxis\
  **需要相同预防措施的病因鉴别:** 外伤后脾切除、择期脾切除（ITP、遗传性球形红细胞增多症）、镰刀细胞病自体脾切除、放射或浸润导致的功能性无脾——均需荚膜菌疫苗和青霉素预防

# Question 148 — Ruptured Ectopic Pregnancy with Hemorrhagic Shock / 破裂性异位妊娠合并失血性休克

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 19-year-old college student</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>3-day history of lower abdominal pain and vaginal spotting</strong>. Menses usually occur at regular 28-day intervals, but she <strong>cannot recall the date of her last menstrual period</strong>. She takes no medications. She is <strong>sexually active and uses condoms inconsistently</strong>. She appears <strong>pale</strong> but is alert and answers questions appropriately. Her <strong>pulse is 110/min</strong>, respirations are 22/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 80/50 mm Hg</strong>. Abdominal examination shows <strong>lower quadrant tenderness with marked guarding</strong>. Pelvic examination shows a <strong>soft uterus and adnexal tenderness greater on the right than on the left</strong>. Her <strong>hemoglobin concentration is 6.2 g/dL</strong>, hematocrit is 18%, and <strong>serum β-hCG concentration is 6645 mIU/mL</strong>. Urinalysis shows no abnormalities.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Observation only<br />
B) CT scan of the abdomen<br />
C) Intravenous antibiotic therapy<br />
D) Culdocentesis<br />
E) Exploratory laparotomy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sexually active, inconsistent condom use, unknown LMP<br />
有性生活、避孕不一致、末次月经不详</td>
<td>Risk profile for unintended pregnancy; unknown LMP suggests possible missed period / 异位妊娠高风险因素，末次月经不详提示可能已停经</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>β-hCG 6645 mIU/mL<br />
β-hCG 6645 mIU/mL</td>
<td>Confirms intrauterine or ectopic pregnancy; no gestational sac on exam implies ectopic / 确认妊娠存在；宫腔未见孕囊提示异位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 80/50, HR 110/min<br />
血压 80/50，心率 110 次/分</td>
<td>Hemorrhagic shock (Class III–IV) — demands emergent surgical intervention / 失血性休克，需立即手术干预</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hemoglobin 6.2 g/dL, Hct 18%<br />
血红蛋白 6.2 g/dL，红细胞压积 18%</td>
<td>Severe acute blood loss anemia consistent with hemoperitoneum / 提示大量腹腔内出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Marked abdominal guarding<br />
明显腹肌紧张</td>
<td>Peritoneal irritation from hemoperitoneum — sign of rupture / 腹腔积血刺激腹膜，为破裂体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Adnexal tenderness greater on right<br />
右侧附件区压痛更明显</td>
<td>Localizes ectopic implantation site to right fallopian tube / 提示右侧输卵管为异位种植部位</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Ectopic pregnancy** occurs when a **fertilized ovum implants outside the endometrial cavity**, most commonly in the **ampulla of the fallopian tube**. The trophoblastic tissue invades the thin tubal wall, and as the conceptus grows, the tube eventually **ruptures**:

**异位妊娠**是指**受精卵在子宫内膜腔以外部位种植**，最常见于**输卵管壶腹部**。滋养细胞侵入薄壁输卵管，随着胚胎生长，输卵管最终**破裂**：

- Tubal rupture tears highly vascular trophoblastic tissue → torrential hemorrhage into the peritoneal cavity\
  输卵管破裂撕裂高度血管化的滋养细胞组织 → 大量出血进入腹腔

- Hemoperitoneum irritates the peritoneum → rebound tenderness and guarding\
  腹腔积血刺激腹膜 → 反跳痛和肌紧张

- Rapid blood loss → distributive/hypovolemic shock: tachycardia, hypotension, pallor, anemia\
  快速失血 → 低血容量性休克：心动过速、低血压、苍白、贫血

- β-hCG remains elevated because trophoblastic tissue is still viable at time of rupture\
  破裂时滋养细胞仍存活，故 β-hCG 持续升高

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The fallopian tube lacks the distensibility of the uterus — once the gestational sac exceeds ~3–4 cm, rupture is inevitable without intervention.

**解剖小窍门:** 输卵管缺乏子宫的延展性——孕囊超过约 3–4 cm 而未干预时，破裂不可避免。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Emergent Exploratory Laparotomy / 正确答案 (E) — 急诊剖腹探查术

**Exploratory laparotomy** is the definitive treatment for a **ruptured ectopic pregnancy** with hemodynamic instability:

**剖腹探查术**是**破裂性异位妊娠**合并血流动力学不稳定的确定性治疗方法：

- Permits direct visualization and control of the bleeding source (salpingectomy or salpingostomy)\
  可直视并控制出血来源（输卵管切除或保守切开）

- Allows simultaneous peritoneal lavage and clot evacuation\
  可同时进行腹腔灌洗和血凝块清除

- Must be accompanied by aggressive IV fluid resuscitation and packed red blood cell transfusion\
  须同步积极静脉补液及红细胞输血

**Diagnosis:** Ruptured ectopic pregnancy is a clinical diagnosis made at the bedside — positive β-hCG + hemodynamic instability + peritoneal signs = operate immediately; imaging delays are lethal.

**诊断:** 破裂性异位妊娠为床旁临床诊断——β-hCG 阳性 + 血流动力学不稳定 + 腹膜刺激征 = 立即手术；等待影像学会导致死亡。

**Treatment:** Emergent exploratory laparotomy (or laparoscopy if stable enough) + salpingectomy of affected tube + concurrent blood product resuscitation.

**治疗:** 急诊剖腹探查（若生命体征稍稳可考虑腹腔镜）+ 患侧输卵管切除术 + 同步输血复苏。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Observation only<br />
A — 仅观察</td>
<td>Inappropriate — this patient is in hemorrhagic shock; observation = death<br />
不恰当——患者处于失血性休克，仅观察等于放任死亡</td>
<td>Hemodynamic instability mandates action<br />
血流动力学不稳定必须立即处置</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — CT scan of the abdomen<br />
B — 腹部 CT</td>
<td>Delays definitive surgery in an unstable patient; imaging does not stop bleeding<br />
延误不稳定患者的手术时机；影像无法止血</td>
<td>"Treat, don't image" in hemorrhagic shock<br />
失血性休克原则：先治疗，不先影像</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Intravenous antibiotic therapy<br />
C — 静脉抗生素治疗</td>
<td>For tubo-ovarian abscess (fever, purulent discharge, WBC elevation) — not present here; antibiotics do not stop hemorrhage<br />
适用于输卵管卵巢脓肿（发热、脓性分泌物、白细胞升高）——本例均无；抗生素无法止血</td>
<td>No fever, no purulence; profound anemia points to bleeding not infection<br />
无发热无脓性分泌物；重度贫血指向出血非感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Culdocentesis<br />
D — 后穹窿穿刺</td>
<td>Historically used to detect hemoperitoneum, but is outdated and adds no management value when diagnosis is already clear<br />
历史上用于检测腹腔积血，但诊断已明确时不增加处置价值且耽误时间</td>
<td>Culdocentesis confirms blood but doesn't treat it; wastes critical minutes<br />
穿刺只能确认积血，不能止血；浪费宝贵时间</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Exploratory laparotomy ✓<br />
E — 剖腹探查术 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — only intervention that controls the hemorrhage and addresses the ruptured ectopic<br />
正确——唯一能控制出血并处理破裂异位妊娠的干预手段</td>
<td>Hemodynamic instability + positive β-hCG + peritoneal signs = OR now<br />
血流动力学不稳 + β-hCG 阳性 + 腹膜刺激征 = 立即手术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is D (culdocentesis) — it does detect hemoperitoneum, but in a patient already crashing, spending time on a confirmatory procedure rather than going to the OR is a fatal error.*

本题最具迷惑性的干扰项是 D（后穹窿穿刺）——虽然确能检测腹腔积血，但对已处于休克状态的患者而言，花时间做确认性操作而非直接手术是致命错误。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Ruptured vs. Unruptured Ectopic Pregnancy Management / 破裂性 vs 未破裂异位妊娠处理对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Unruptured Ectopic</strong><br />
<strong>未破裂异位妊娠</strong></th>
<th><strong>Ruptured Ectopic</strong><br />
<strong>破裂性异位妊娠</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Hemodynamic status<br />
血流动力学</td>
<td>Stable<br />
稳定</td>
<td>Unstable (shock)<br />
不稳定（休克）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abdominal exam<br />
腹部检查</td>
<td>Mild tenderness, no guarding<br />
轻压痛，无肌紧张</td>
<td>Marked guarding, rebound<br />
明显肌紧张、反跳痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anemia<br />
贫血</td>
<td>None or mild<br />
无或轻度</td>
<td>Severe (Hgb &lt;7)<br />
重度（Hgb &lt;7）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>β-hCG trend<br />
β-hCG 趋势</td>
<td>Plateau or slow rise<br />
平台期或缓慢升高</td>
<td>Elevated at time of rupture<br />
破裂时升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>Methotrexate (if criteria met) or laparoscopy<br />
甲氨蝶呤（符合条件者）或腹腔镜</td>
<td>Emergent laparotomy/laparoscopy + resuscitation<br />
急诊开腹/腹腔镜 + 复苏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Methotrexate eligible?<br />
可用甲氨蝶呤？</td>
<td>Yes (if stable, β-hCG &lt;5000, no cardiac activity)<br />
可以（稳定、β-hCG &lt;5000、无胎心）</td>
<td>Contraindicated<br />
禁忌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A young woman with a positive β-hCG, hemorrhagic shock, and peritoneal signs has a ruptured ectopic pregnancy until proven otherwise — go straight to the OR.**

**育龄女性出现 β-hCG 阳性、失血性休克及腹膜刺激征，在排除前首先考虑破裂性异位妊娠——直接送手术室。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SHOCK = Ruptured Ectopic / 记忆钩 — SHOCK 五字诀判断破裂性异位妊娠:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>potting/pain — vaginal bleeding + lower abdominal pain / 阴道出血 + 下腹痛<br />
• <strong>H</strong>CG positive — confirms pregnancy outside uterus / β-hCG 阳性确认妊娠<br />
• <strong>O</strong>pen abdomen findings — guarding, rebound tenderness / 腹膜刺激征（肌紧张、反跳痛）<br />
• <strong>C</strong>rash vitals — HR↑, BP↓ (hemorrhagic shock) / 生命体征崩溃（心率↑、血压↓）<br />
• <strong>K</strong>nife now — emergent laparotomy, no time for imaging / 立即手术，无需等待影像</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Ectopic Pregnancy / 高频知识表 — 异位妊娠

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common site<br />
最常见部位</td>
<td>Ampulla of fallopian tube (70%); also isthmus, fimbria, cornua, ovary, abdominal cavity<br />
输卵管壶腹部（70%）；其次峡部、伞端、间质部、卵巢、腹腔</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Prior PID/STI, prior ectopic, tubal surgery, IUD use, ART, smoking<br />
既往盆腔炎/性传播感染、既往异位妊娠史、输卵管手术、宫内节育器、辅助生殖、吸烟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Methotrexate criteria<br />
甲氨蝶呤适应证</td>
<td>Hemodynamically stable + β-hCG &lt;5000 + no fetal cardiac activity + no rupture + mass &lt;3.5 cm<br />
血流动力学稳定 + β-hCG &lt;5000 + 无胎心 + 无破裂 + 包块 &lt;3.5 cm</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Discriminatory zone<br />
鉴别区</td>
<td>β-hCG &gt;1500–2000 mIU/mL: intrauterine gestational sac should be visible on transvaginal US; absence suggests ectopic<br />
β-hCG &gt;1500–2000：经阴道超声应可见宫内孕囊；未见则提示异位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Culdocentesis<br />
后穹窿穿刺</td>
<td>Historically used to detect hemoperitoneum (non-clotting blood = positive); largely replaced by transvaginal ultrasound<br />
历史上用于检测腹腔积血（不凝血 = 阳性）；已基本被经阴道超声取代</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Contraindication to methotrexate<br />
甲氨蝶呤禁忌证</td>
<td>Hemodynamic instability, ruptured ectopic, hepatic/renal disease, immunodeficiency, breastfeeding<br />
血流动力学不稳定、破裂性异位、肝肾疾病、免疫缺陷、哺乳期</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-treatment monitoring<br />
治疗后监测</td>
<td>β-hCG levels every 48 hours until undetectable; rising levels after methotrexate may indicate treatment failure requiring surgery<br />
β-hCG 每 48 小时复查直至转阴；甲氨蝶呤后 β-hCG 上升提示治疗失败需手术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of positive β-hCG + abdominal pain:** ruptured ectopic, threatened/inevitable abortion, ovarian torsion with pregnancy, appendicitis in pregnancy — ectopic tops list when hemodynamically unstable\
  **妊娠合并腹痛的鉴别:** 破裂性异位妊娠、先兆/难免流产、妊娠合并卵巢扭转、妊娠合并阑尾炎——血流动力学不稳定时异位妊娠首先考虑

- **Variant — interstitial (cornual) ectopic:** implants in the intramural portion of tube; presents later (8–16 wks) with higher rupture risk and greater hemorrhage due to rich myometrial blood supply; often requires cornual resection\
  **间质部（宫角）异位妊娠变式:** 种植于输卵管壁内段；发现较晚（8–16 周），因宫角血供丰富出血更猛烈；常需宫角切除

- **Key complication of missed diagnosis:** exsanguination and death — ruptured ectopic is a leading cause of first-trimester maternal mortality in the United States\
  **漏诊的关键并发症:** 失血死亡——破裂性异位妊娠是美国妊娠早期孕产妇死亡的主要原因之一

- **Rh status consideration:** Rh-negative patients with ectopic pregnancy (ruptured or not) should receive Rh(D) immunoglobulin (RhoGAM) to prevent alloimmunization in future pregnancies\
  **Rh 血型注意事项:** Rh 阴性患者发生异位妊娠（无论破裂与否）均应注射 Rh(D) 免疫球蛋白（RhoGAM），防止后续妊娠同种免疫反应

# Question 149 — Alcohol Use Disorder / 酒精使用障碍

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>17-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the office by his parents because of changes in his behavior during the past 6 months. They say he has become <strong>withdrawn and moody</strong> and that his <strong>grades have declined</strong>. He has returned home from parties <strong>intoxicated three times during the past month</strong>. During a wedding reception 3 weeks ago, he was <strong>delirious, incoherent, and imbalanced</strong>. The patient says he drinks alcohol but that <strong>his drinking is not a problem</strong> and <strong>he can stop drinking whenever he wants</strong>. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, he is calm and cooperative. He reports no insomnia, hypersomnia, or suicidal ideation. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Alcohol use disorder<br />
B) Conduct disorder<br />
C) Major depressive disorder<br />
D) Normal adolescent behavior<br />
E) Recreational alcohol use</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Intoxicated three times in past month<br />
过去一个月三次醉酒</td>
<td>Repeated intoxication = pattern of harmful use, not isolated experimentation<br />
反复醉酒提示行为模式，而非偶然尝试</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Delirious, incoherent, imbalanced at wedding<br />
婚礼上谵妄、语无伦次、步态不稳</td>
<td>Evidence of significant intoxication causing functional impairment<br />
严重醉酒导致功能损害的直接证据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Grades declined; withdrawn and moody<br />
成绩下降；孤僻、情绪不稳定</td>
<td>Negative academic and social consequences — DSM-5 AUD criteria<br />
负面学业和社交后果——DSM-5 AUD 诊断标准之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Drinking is not a problem" / "can stop whenever he wants"<br />
"饮酒不成问题" / "随时可以停"</td>
<td>Classic denial — impaired control is a hallmark DSM-5 criterion; denial does not rule out AUD, it confirms it<br />
典型否认——控制缺失是 DSM-5 核心标准；否认不能排除 AUD，反而印证诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>17-year-old (underage)<br />
17 岁（未成年）</td>
<td>AUD can and does occur in adolescents; underage drinking is not recreational by legal or clinical definition<br />
AUD 可发生于青少年；未成年饮酒在法律和临床上均不属于"休闲饮酒"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No insomnia, hypersomnia, or suicidal ideation<br />
无失眠、嗜睡或自杀意念</td>
<td>Argues against major depressive disorder as primary diagnosis<br />
不支持重度抑郁障碍作为首要诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Alcohol use disorder (AUD)** is a maladaptive pattern of alcohol use causing clinically significant impairment, diagnosed when **≥2 of 11 DSM-5 criteria** are met within any 12-month period across four domains:

**酒精使用障碍（AUD）**是导致临床上显著功能损害的酒精使用适应不良模式，当在任意12个月内满足 **11 条 DSM-5 标准中的 ≥2 条**时即可诊断，涉及四个领域：

- Impaired control: drinking more/longer than intended; persistent desire or failed efforts to cut down; spending excessive time obtaining/using alcohol; craving\
  控制缺失：饮酒量/时间超出预期；持续想减少饮酒但努力失败；花费大量时间获取/使用酒精；渴求

- Social impairment: failure to fulfill major role obligations (school, work); continued use despite social/interpersonal problems; reduced important activities\
  社会功能损害：无法履行主要职责（学业、工作）；尽管社交/人际问题持续饮酒；减少重要活动

- Risky use: recurrent use in physically hazardous situations; continued use despite physical or psychological harm\
  高风险使用：反复在身体危险情况下饮酒；尽管存在躯体或心理伤害仍继续

- Pharmacological criteria: tolerance (needing more for same effect); withdrawal symptoms\
  药理学标准：耐受性（需要更多量才能达到同等效果）；戒断症状

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The **mesolimbic dopamine pathway** (VTA → nucleus accumbens) mediates alcohol's rewarding and reinforcing effects, driving compulsive use despite mounting negative consequences.

**解剖小窍门:** **中脑边缘多巴胺通路**（腹侧被盖区 → 伏隔核）介导酒精的奖励和强化效应，驱动尽管负面后果不断积累仍强迫性使用。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Alcohol Use Disorder / 正确答案 (A) — 酒精使用障碍

**Alcohol use disorder** is diagnosed by the presence of ≥2 DSM-5 criteria causing clinically significant impairment — the patient's self-assessment is irrelevant to the diagnosis:

**酒精使用障碍**通过存在 ≥2 条 DSM-5 标准导致临床上显著损害来诊断——患者的自我评估与诊断无关：

- This patient meets multiple criteria: repeated intoxication (risky use), academic decline (role obligation failure), social withdrawal (social impairment), and denial with stated inability to see a problem (impaired control)\
  本患者满足多条标准：反复醉酒（高风险使用）、成绩下降（职责履行失败）、社会退缩（社会功能损害）、否认并声称看不出问题（控制缺失）

- Severity is classified as: mild (2–3 criteria), moderate (4–5 criteria), severe (≥6 criteria)\
  严重程度分类：轻度（2–3 条标准）、中度（4–5 条）、重度（≥6 条）

- AUD in adolescents carries additional risks beyond adults: MVA, high-risk sexual behavior, suicide; early-onset worsens long-term prognosis\
  青少年 AUD 比成人承担额外风险：交通事故、高风险性行为、自杀；起病越早长期预后越差

**Diagnosis:** AUD is a clinical diagnosis based on behavioral patterns and functional consequences — laboratory findings (GGT, MCV, LFTs) may support but are not required.

**诊断:** AUD 是基于行为模式和功能后果的临床诊断——实验室检查（GGT、MCV、肝功能）可支持诊断但非必需。

**Treatment:** Brief motivational interviewing as first-line; pharmacotherapy for moderate–severe AUD includes naltrexone (reduces craving), acamprosate (reduces withdrawal), or disulfiram (aversion); refer to addiction specialist.

**治疗:** 简短动机性访谈为一线干预；中重度 AUD 药物治疗包括纳曲酮（降低渴求）、阿坎酸（减轻戒断）或双硫仑（厌恶疗法）；转介成瘾专科。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Alcohol use disorder ✓<br />
A — 酒精使用障碍 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — meets ≥2 DSM-5 criteria: risky use, social/academic impairment, impaired control with denial<br />
正确——满足 ≥2 条 DSM-5 标准：高风险使用、社会/学业损害、伴否认的控制缺失</td>
<td>Repeated intoxication + negative consequences + denial = AUD<br />
反复醉酒 + 负面后果 + 否认 = AUD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Conduct disorder<br />
B — 品行障碍</td>
<td>Requires persistent violation of others' rights (aggression, theft, destruction, deceit) — none present here; excessive drinking alone does not constitute conduct disorder<br />
需要持续侵犯他人权利（攻击、盗窃、破坏、欺骗）——本例均无；单纯过度饮酒不构成品行障碍</td>
<td>No aggression, theft, or violation of others' rights beyond underage drinking<br />
除未成年饮酒外，无攻击、盗窃或侵犯他人权利的行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Major depressive disorder<br />
C — 重度抑郁障碍</td>
<td>MDD requires ≥5 symptoms for ≥2 weeks including depressed mood or anhedonia; patient denies neurovegetative symptoms; mood/behavioral changes are better explained by alcohol use<br />
MDD 需要 ≥2 周内 ≥5 种症状包括抑郁情绪或快感缺失；患者否认神经植物性症状；情绪/行为变化可由酒精使用更好解释</td>
<td>Alcohol use precedes and accounts for all mood and social changes<br />
酒精使用先于并解释所有情绪和社交变化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Normal adolescent behavior<br />
D — 正常青少年行为</td>
<td>Normal experimentation is occasional and does not cause repeated delirium, functional impairment, or academic decline; this patient has a pervasive pattern with negative consequences<br />
正常尝试是偶尔的，不会导致反复谵妄、功能损害或成绩下滑；本患者有伴负面后果的普遍性行为模式</td>
<td>Pattern + negative consequences + denial distinguish AUD from adolescent experimentation<br />
行为模式 + 负面后果 + 否认将 AUD 与青少年尝试性饮酒区分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Recreational alcohol use<br />
E — 休闲饮酒</td>
<td>Recreational use implies moderate consumption, maintained control, and absence of negative consequences; this patient has clear academic/social impairment and loss of control<br />
休闲饮酒意指适量消费、控制正常、无负面后果；本患者有明确学业/社交损害和控制缺失</td>
<td>Negative consequences + impaired control + underage status rule out recreational use<br />
负面后果 + 控制缺失 + 未成年身份排除休闲饮酒</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (E) Recreational alcohol use — the critical distinction is that negative consequences (academic decline, social withdrawal) and impaired control (repeated intoxication despite harm, denial) categorically satisfy DSM-5 AUD criteria regardless of the patient's self-report.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是 (E) 休闲饮酒——关键区别在于负面后果（成绩下降、社会退缩）和控制缺失（尽管有伤害仍反复醉酒、否认）明确满足 DSM-5 AUD 标准，无论患者如何自我报告。

反复醉酒、否认、职责失履</td>
<td>None; behavior is contextually appropriate<br />
无；行为在情境中适当</td>

教育、减少伤害</td>
<td>CBT, family therapy, social skills training<br />
认知行为治疗、家庭治疗、社交技能训练</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A teenager with repeated intoxication, academic and social decline, and denial of a drinking problem meets ≥2 DSM-5 criteria for alcohol use disorder — denial does not rule it out, it is itself a criterion.**

**一名青少年反复醉酒、学业和社交功能下降并否认饮酒是问题，满足酒精使用障碍 ≥2 条 DSM-5 标准——否认不能排除诊断，否认本身就是诊断标准之一。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — DRANK (AUD Core Features) / 记忆钩 — DRANK（AUD 核心特征）:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>enial — "I can stop anytime" is the textbook impaired control criterion / 否认——"我随时可以停"是控制缺失标准的教科书式表现<br />
• <strong>R</strong>epeated intoxication despite known consequences / 尽管已知有后果，仍反复醉酒<br />
• <strong>A</strong>cademic/occupational decline (failure to fulfill role obligations) / 学业/职业下降（无法履行职责）<br />
• <strong>N</strong>egative social consequences (withdrawal, relationship problems) / 负面社交后果（社会退缩、人际问题）<br />
• <strong>K</strong>eeping on drinking despite harm = ≥2 criteria met = AUD diagnosis / 不顾伤害继续饮酒 = 满足 ≥2 条标准 = AUD 诊断</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Alcohol Use Disorder in Adolescents / 高频知识表 — 青少年酒精使用障碍

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 AUD severity classification<br />
DSM-5 AUD 严重程度分类</td>
<td>11 criteria assessed over 12 months; mild = 2–3, moderate = 4–5, severe ≥6; severity guides treatment intensity<br />
评估 12 个月内的 11 条标准；轻度 = 2–3 条，中度 = 4–5 条，重度 ≥6 条；严重程度指导治疗强度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Denial as a DSM-5 criterion<br />
否认作为 DSM-5 标准</td>
<td>Denial is part of impaired control domain; patient's self-report of "no problem" is clinically irrelevant — diagnosis is based on observable behavioral criteria<br />
否认属于控制缺失领域；患者自述"没问题"在临床上无关紧要——诊断基于可观察的行为标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Adolescent-specific risks of AUD<br />
青少年 AUD 特异性风险</td>
<td>Academic failure, high-risk sexual behavior, motor vehicle accidents, suicide; earlier onset → worse long-term prognosis and higher rate of adult AUD<br />
学业失败、高风险性行为、交通事故、自杀；起病越早→长期预后越差，成年后 AUD 发生率越高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CRAFFT screening tool (adolescents)<br />
CRAFFT 筛查工具（青少年）</td>
<td>Car, Relax, Alone, Forget, Friends, Trouble; preferred over CAGE/AUDIT in patients &lt;21; ≥2 positive = positive screen<br />
汽车、放松、独处、遗忘、朋友、麻烦；在 &lt;21 岁患者中优于 CAGE/AUDIT；≥2 项阳性 = 筛查阳性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pharmacotherapy for AUD<br />
AUD 药物治疗</td>
<td>Naltrexone (μ-opioid antagonist — reduces euphoria and craving); acamprosate (reduces glutamate-mediated withdrawal discomfort); disulfiram (inhibits ALDH — acetaldehyde accumulation causes aversion)<br />
纳曲酮（μ-阿片拮抗剂——降低欣快感和渴求）；阿坎酸（减少谷氨酸介导的戒断不适）；双硫仑（抑制 ALDH——乙醛积累引起厌恶反应）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Alcohol withdrawal timeline<br />
酒精戒断时间轴</td>
<td>6–24h: tremor, anxiety, diaphoresis, tachycardia; 24–48h: seizures; 48–72h: delirium tremens (DTs); treatment = benzodiazepines (CIWA protocol)<br />
6–24小时：震颤、焦虑、出汗、心动过速；24–48小时：癫痫发作；48–72小时：震颤性谵妄；治疗 = 苯二氮䓬类（CIWA 方案）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AUD vs. MDD in adolescents<br />
青少年 AUD vs. MDD</td>
<td>Both cause mood changes and social withdrawal; temporal relationship is key — if alcohol use precedes and accounts for all mood/behavioral changes, AUD is primary; screen for comorbid MDD separately<br />
两者均可引起情绪变化和社会退缩；时间关系是关键——若酒精使用先于并解释所有情绪/行为变化，则 AUD 为首要诊断；应单独筛查共病 MDD</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **AUD and conduct disorder comorbidity:** Both diagnoses frequently co-occur in adolescents and are not mutually exclusive — if criteria for both are independently met, both are diagnosed; substance use often precedes conduct disorder onset\
  **AUD 与品行障碍共病:** 两种诊断在青少年中频繁共存且互不排斥——若两者均独立满足诊断标准，则同时诊断；物质使用通常先于品行障碍发生

- **Delirium at the wedding (acute intoxication vs. DTs):** The episode represents acute alcohol intoxication — cerebellar signs (ataxia) and encephalopathy from high BAL; delirium tremens occurs during withdrawal (48–72h after last drink), not during active intoxication\
  **婚礼上的谵妄（急性中毒 vs. 震颤性谵妄）:** 该发作代表急性酒精中毒——高血液酒精浓度导致小脑体征（共济失调）和脑病；震颤性谵妄发生于戒断期（最后一次饮酒后48–72小时），而非主动醉酒期间

- **Screening in primary care:** SBIRT (Screening, Brief Intervention, Referral to Treatment) is the recommended framework for adolescent substance use; even a 5-minute brief intervention reduces drinking in adolescents\
  **初级保健中的筛查:** SBIRT（筛查、简短干预、转介治疗）是青少年物质使用的推荐框架；即使是5分钟的简短干预也能减少青少年饮酒

- **Legal context reinforcing diagnosis:** In the US, any alcohol use by those \<21 is illegal; "recreational alcohol use" as a diagnosis for underage individuals is clinically and legally untenable — the correct minimum diagnosis is alcohol use (misuse), and AUD applies when criteria are met\
  **强化诊断的法律背景:** 在美国，21 岁以下任何饮酒均属违法；将"休闲饮酒"作为未成年人的诊断在临床和法律上均站不住脚——正确的最低诊断是酒精使用（滥用），满足标准时适用 AUD

# Question 150 — Menopausal Hormone Therapy / 绝经期激素治疗

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>47-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>9-month history of hot flashes, night sweats, and pain during sexual intercourse</strong>. Her <strong>last menstrual period was 1 year ago</strong>. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. Pelvic examination shows <strong>vaginal atrophy</strong> and <strong>no cervical mucus</strong>. A Pap smear and mammography show no abnormalities. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Pregnancy test<br />
B) Measurement of serum luteinizing hormone concentration<br />
C) Hormone therapy<br />
D) Levothyroxine therapy<br />
E) Vaginal corticosteroid therapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>47-year-old woman<br />
47 岁女性</td>
<td>Perimenopause/menopause typically occurs around age 50; consistent with expected age range<br />
围绝经期/绝经期通常发生在 50 岁左右，与预期年龄范围一致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Last menstrual period 1 year ago<br />
末次月经 1 年前</td>
<td>Menopause is defined as ≥12 months of amenorrhea; this patient meets the clinical definition<br />
绝经定义为闭经≥12 个月，该患者符合临床诊断标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hot flashes and night sweats<br />
潮热和盗汗</td>
<td>Classic vasomotor symptoms of estrogen deficiency; cardinal features of menopause<br />
雌激素缺乏的经典血管舒缩症状，是绝经期的主要表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain during sexual intercourse<br />
性交疼痛（性交困难）</td>
<td>Dyspareunia caused by vaginal atrophy and dryness from reduced estrogen<br />
由雌激素减少导致阴道萎缩和干燥引起的性交困难</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vaginal atrophy, no cervical mucus<br />
阴道萎缩，无宫颈黏液</td>
<td>Objective findings confirming genitourinary syndrome of menopause (GSM) from estrogen loss<br />
证实绝经期泌尿生殖综合征（GSM）的客观发现，源于雌激素丢失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal Pap smear and mammography<br />
宫颈涂片及乳腺钼靶正常</td>
<td>Screens out malignancy, establishing safety profile before initiating hormone therapy<br />
排除恶性肿瘤，为启动激素治疗前建立安全基线</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Estrogen deficiency** drives all symptoms in menopause: as **ovarian follicle reserve** is exhausted, **estradiol** levels fall, removing negative feedback on the hypothalamic-pituitary axis:

**雌激素缺乏**是绝经期所有症状的根本驱动因素：随着**卵巢卵泡储备**耗尽，**雌二醇**水平下降，解除了对下丘脑-垂体轴的负反馈：

- Elevated GnRH pulsatility → elevated FSH and LH (FSH rises more markedly)\
  GnRH 脉冲频率增加 → FSH 和 LH 升高（FSH 升高更为显著）

- Loss of estrogen → dysregulation of thermoregulatory set point → vasomotor instability (hot flashes, night sweats)\
  雌激素丢失 → 体温调节设定点失调 → 血管舒缩不稳定（潮热、盗汗）

- Reduced estrogen in genitourinary tissue → thinning of vaginal epithelium, decreased lubrication → atrophy and dyspareunia\
  泌尿生殖组织雌激素减少 → 阴道上皮变薄、润滑减少 → 萎缩和性交困难

- Chronic estrogen deficiency → decreased bone mineral density → osteoporosis risk\
  长期雌激素缺乏 → 骨矿物质密度降低 → 骨质疏松风险

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** FSH rises before LH in menopause because FSH is more sensitive to the loss of inhibin B (produced by granulosa cells), not just estradiol feedback.

**解剖小窍门:** 绝经期 FSH 比 LH 升高更早，是因为 FSH 对颗粒细胞产生的抑制素 B（inhibin B）的丢失更加敏感，而不仅仅是雌二醇反馈。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Menopausal Hormone Therapy / 正确答案 (C) — 绝经期激素治疗

**Hormone therapy (HT)** is the most effective treatment for menopausal vasomotor symptoms and genitourinary syndrome when the patient has no contraindications:

**激素治疗（HT）**是治疗绝经期血管舒缩症状和泌尿生殖综合征最有效的方法，前提是患者无禁忌证：

- Exogenous estrogen replaces endogenous deficiency, directly addressing the root cause of all symptoms\
  外源性雌激素补充内源性雌激素不足，直接解决所有症状的根本原因

- Women with intact uterus must receive combined estrogen + progestogen to prevent unopposed estrogen-induced endometrial hyperplasia/cancer\
  保留子宫的女性必须接受雌激素+孕激素联合治疗，以防止单纯雌激素引起子宫内膜增生/癌

- Risks include breast cancer, VTE, cardiovascular disease, stroke — use should be limited to shortest effective duration (3–5 years)\
  风险包括乳腺癌、静脉血栓栓塞、心血管疾病、卒中——应限于最短有效疗程（3～5 年）

- This patient has normal Pap and mammography, making her a reasonable candidate for HT\
  该患者宫颈涂片和乳腺钼靶正常，是接受 HT 的合理候选人

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis — menopause defined as 12 consecutive months of amenorrhea in a woman of appropriate age with vasomotor symptoms and vaginal atrophy; lab confirmation (FSH, estradiol) not required when presentation is classic.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——绝经期定义为适龄女性连续 12 个月闭经，伴血管舒缩症状和阴道萎缩；典型表现时无需实验室检查（FSH、雌二醇）确认。

**Treatment:** Systemic hormone therapy (estrogen + progestogen for women with intact uterus); local vaginal estrogen is an alternative for isolated genitourinary symptoms; duration limited to 3–5 years.

**治疗:** 系统性激素治疗（保留子宫者用雌激素+孕激素联合方案）；局部阴道雌激素可用于单纯泌尿生殖症状；疗程限制在 3～5 年。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Pregnancy test<br />
A — 妊娠试验</td>
<td>No menstrual period for 12 months with full menopausal symptom complex makes pregnancy extremely unlikely; not the appropriate next step<br />
闭经 12 个月伴完整绝经期症状群，妊娠极不可能；不是合适的下一步</td>
<td>Age + 12 months amenorrhea + vasomotor symptoms = clinical menopause, not pregnancy<br />
年龄 + 12 个月闭经 + 血管舒缩症状 = 临床绝经，而非妊娠</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Measurement of serum LH concentration<br />
B — 血清黄体生成素测定</td>
<td>Menopause is a clinical diagnosis; labs (FSH, LH) only needed when diagnosis is uncertain (e.g., &lt;12 months, atypical age); this patient meets full clinical criteria<br />
绝经期是临床诊断；只有诊断不明时（如&lt;12 个月、年龄不典型）才需要实验室检查；该患者符合完整临床标准</td>
<td>Clinical diagnosis does not require lab confirmation when criteria are met<br />
符合标准时临床诊断不需实验室确认</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hormone therapy ✓<br />
C — 激素治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — addresses the root cause (estrogen deficiency) and directly treats all three complaints: hot flashes, night sweats, and dyspareunia<br />
正确——针对根本原因（雌激素缺乏），直接治疗三大主诉：潮热、盗汗和性交困难</td>
<td>Only treatment that addresses vasomotor + genitourinary symptoms simultaneously<br />
唯一能同时解决血管舒缩症状和泌尿生殖症状的治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Levothyroxine therapy<br />
D — 左甲状腺素治疗</td>
<td>Levothyroxine treats hypothyroidism (weight gain, cold intolerance, constipation, fatigue, bradycardia); this patient has no such symptoms<br />
左甲状腺素用于治疗甲状腺功能减退（体重增加、畏寒、便秘、乏力、心动过缓）；该患者无此类症状</td>
<td>Hypothyroid amenorrhea is accompanied by cold intolerance and weight gain, not hot flashes<br />
甲减性闭经伴畏寒和体重增加，而非潮热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Vaginal corticosteroid therapy<br />
E — 阴道糖皮质激素治疗</td>
<td>Corticosteroids treat inflammatory dermatoses (lichen planus, lichen sclerosus); atrophy here is from estrogen deficiency, not inflammation<br />
糖皮质激素治疗炎症性皮肤病（扁平苔藓、硬化性苔藓）；此处萎缩源于雌激素缺乏，而非炎症</td>
<td>Vaginal atrophy caused by estrogen deficiency responds to estrogen, not steroids<br />
雌激素缺乏引起的阴道萎缩对雌激素有效，对糖皮质激素无效</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractor is Choice B — many test-takers confuse "confirm the diagnosis with labs" with "treat the patient"; because menopause is a clinical diagnosis when criteria are met, the next step is management, not further workup.*

最强干扰项是选项 B——许多考生将"用实验室检查确认诊断"与"治疗患者"混淆；当临床标准满足时，绝经期即为临床诊断，下一步应是处理而非进一步检查。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A woman with 12+ months of amenorrhea, vasomotor symptoms, and vaginal atrophy has clinical menopause and should be offered hormone therapy to replace the estrogen her ovaries no longer produce.**

**闭经超过 12 个月、伴血管舒缩症状和阴道萎缩的女性为临床绝经期，应给予激素治疗以补充卵巢不再分泌的雌激素。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ESTROGEN Rules Menopause / 记忆钩 — ESTROGEN 统领绝经期:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>E</strong>ndometrial protection — always add progestogen if uterus intact / 子宫内膜保护——保留子宫必须联用孕激素<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ymptoms relieved — hot flashes, night sweats, dyspareunia all respond / 症状缓解——潮热、盗汗、性交困难均有效<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hree-to-five years — limit duration to reduce cancer and CVD risk / 3～5 年——限制疗程以降低癌症和心血管风险<br />
• <strong>R</strong>isk stratify first — screen with Pap + mammography before prescribing / 先评估风险——处方前先行宫颈涂片和乳腺钼靶筛查<br />
• <strong>O</strong>steoporosis prevention — a secondary benefit of systemic HT / 骨质疏松预防——系统性 HT 的附加获益</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Menopause Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 绝经期诊断与管理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of menopause<br />
绝经定义</td>
<td>≥12 consecutive months of amenorrhea due to ovarian failure; average age ~51 in the US<br />
因卵巢功能衰竭导致连续≥12 个月闭经；美国平均年龄约 51 岁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lab findings in menopause<br />
绝经期实验室检查</td>
<td>↑FSH (&gt;40 mIU/mL), ↑LH, ↓estradiol; inhibin B falls earliest; labs not required for clinical diagnosis<br />
FSH 升高（&gt;40 mIU/mL）、LH 升高、雌二醇降低；抑制素 B 最早下降；临床诊断无需实验室检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vasomotor symptoms<br />
血管舒缩症状</td>
<td>Hot flashes and night sweats; caused by thermoregulatory instability from estrogen withdrawal; most effectively treated with HT<br />
潮热和盗汗；由雌激素撤退引起的体温调节不稳定所致；最有效的治疗为 HT</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Genitourinary syndrome of menopause (GSM)<br />
绝经期泌尿生殖综合征</td>
<td>Vaginal dryness, atrophy, dyspareunia, urinary symptoms; treated with local or systemic estrogen<br />
阴道干燥、萎缩、性交困难、泌尿系统症状；用局部或系统性雌激素治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hormone therapy risks<br />
激素治疗风险</td>
<td>Breast cancer, endometrial cancer (if unopposed estrogen), VTE, stroke; risk-benefit balance guides prescribing<br />
乳腺癌、子宫内膜癌（单用雌激素时）、VTE、卒中；风险-获益权衡指导处方</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-hormonal alternatives<br />
非激素替代方案</td>
<td>SSRIs/SNRIs (paroxetine FDA-approved), gabapentin, clonidine for vasomotor symptoms in those who cannot use HT<br />
SSRIs/SNRIs（帕罗西汀经 FDA 批准）、加巴喷丁、可乐定用于不能使用 HT 者的血管舒缩症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Contraindications to systemic HT<br />
系统性 HT 禁忌证</td>
<td>Active/history of breast or endometrial cancer, unexplained vaginal bleeding, active VTE, CAD, stroke<br />
活动性/既往乳腺癌或子宫内膜癌、不明原因阴道出血、活动性 VTE、冠心病、卒中</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of secondary amenorrhea:** Pregnancy (most common), hypothyroidism, hyperprolactinemia, PCOS, premature ovarian insufficiency (POI if \<40 y/o), and menopause — always rule out pregnancy first\
  **继发性闭经鉴别诊断:** 妊娠（最常见）、甲状腺功能减退、高泌乳素血症、PCOS、早发性卵巢功能不全（\<40 岁为 POI）和绝经——始终首先排除妊娠

- **Premature ovarian insufficiency (POI):** Menopause \<40 years; requires HT until average menopausal age (~51) for bone and cardiovascular protection regardless of symptom severity\
  **早发性卵巢功能不全（POI）:** 40 岁前绝经；无论症状严重程度，均需 HT 至平均绝经年龄（约 51 岁）以保护骨骼和心血管

- **Key complication of unopposed estrogen:** Endometrial hyperplasia progressing to endometrial adenocarcinoma; progestogen (e.g., medroxyprogesterone) added to estrogen prevents this in women with intact uterus\
  **单用雌激素的关键并发症:** 子宫内膜增生进展为子宫内膜腺癌；保留子宫的女性加用孕激素（如甲羟孕酮）可预防此并发症

- **Lichen sclerosus vs. atrophic vaginitis:** Both cause vulvovaginal symptoms, but lichen sclerosus shows white, wrinkled, "cigarette paper" skin and is treated with topical corticosteroids, not estrogen\
  **硬化性苔藓 vs. 萎缩性阴道炎:** 两者均引起外阴阴道症状，但硬化性苔藓表现为白色皱缩"卷烟纸"样皮肤，用局部糖皮质激素治疗，而非雌激素
